Oducedpray ybay Avidday Idgerway

Ybay Arkmay Aintway 

(Amuelsay Anghornelay Emensclay)

Elicityfay--Commission andway Omissionway

Uperintendentsay--"Showing offway"--Tom Ionizedlay

APTERCHAY IVXAY. Ampcay-Life--A Ensationsay--Tom Ealsstay Awayway omfray Ampcay 

APTERCHAY XVAY. Omtay Econnoitersray--Learns ethay Ituationsay--Reports atway Ampcay

Essonlay--A Ightnay Urprisesay--An Indianway Arway

APTERCHAY IXXXAY. Anway Exploringway Expeditionway--Trouble Ommencescay--Lost inway ethay

APTERCHAY IIXXXAY. Omtay ellstay ethay Orystay ofway eirthay Escapeway--Tom's Enemyway inway Afesay 
Uartersqay 

APTERCHAY IIIXXXAY. Ethay Atefay ofway Injunway Oejay--Huck andway Omtay Omparecay Otesnay 
--Anway Expeditionway otay ethay Avecay--Protection Againstway Ostsghay--"An Awfulway Ugsnay

EFACEPRAY 

Ostmay ofway ethay adventuresway ecordedray inway isthay ookbay eallyray occurredway; oneway orway otway 
ereway experiencesway ofway ymay ownway, ethay estray osethay ofway oysbay owhay ereway oolmatesschay 
ofway inemay. Uckhay Innfay isway awndray omfray ifelay; Omtay Awyersay alsoway, utbay otnay omfray anway 
individualway--he isway away ombinationcay ofway ethay aracteristicschay ofway eethray oysbay omwhay 
Iway ewknay, andway ereforethay elongsbay otay ethay ompositecay orderway ofway architectureway. 

Ethay oddway uperstitionssay ouchedtay uponway ereway allway evalentpray amongway ildrenchay andway 
avesslay inway ethay Estway atway ethay eriodpay ofway isthay orystay--that isway otay aysay, irtythay orway 
ortyfay yearsway agoway. 

Althoughway ymay ookbay isway intendedway ainlymay orfay ethay entertainmentway ofway oysbay andway 
irlsgay, Iway opehay itway illway otnay ebay unnedshay ybay enmay andway omenway onway atthay accountway, 
orfay artpay ofway ymay anplay ashay eenbay otay ytray otay easantlyplay emindray adultsway ofway atwhay 
eythay onceway ereway emselvesthay, andway ofway owhay eythay eltfay andway oughtthay andway alkedtay, 
andway atwhay ueerqay enterprisesway eythay ometimessay engagedway inway. 

ETHAY AUTHORWAY. 

ARTFORDHAY, 1876. 




APTERCHAY Iway 

"OMTAY!" 

Onay answerway. 

"OMTAY!" 

Onay answerway. 

"Atwhay's onegay ithway atthay oybay, Iway onderway? Youway OMTAY!" 

Onay answerway. 

Ethay oldway adylay ulledpay erhay ectaclesspay ownday andway ookedlay overway emthay aboutway ethay 
oomray; enthay eshay utpay emthay upway andway ookedlay outway underway emthay. Eshay eldomsay orway 
evernay ookedlay _oughthray_ emthay orfay osay allsmay away ingthay asway away oybay; eythay ereway 
erhay atestay airpay, ethay idepray ofway erhay earthay, andway ereway uiltbay orfay "ylestay," otnay 
ervicesay--she ouldcay avehay eensay oughthray away airpay ofway ovestay-lids ustjay asway ellway. 
Eshay ookedlay erplexedpay orfay away omentmay, andway enthay aidsay, otnay iercelyfay, utbay 
illstay oudlay enoughway orfay ethay urniturefay otay earhay: 

"Ellway, Iway aylay ifway Iway etgay oldhay ofway youway Iway'll--" 

Eshay idday otnay inishfay, orfay ybay isthay imetay eshay asway endingbay ownday andway unchingpay 
underway ethay edbay ithway ethay oombray, andway osay eshay eedednay eathbray otay unctuatepay ethay 
unchespay ithway. Eshay esurrectedray othingnay utbay ethay atcay. 

"Iway evernay idday eesay ethay eatbay ofway atthay oybay!" 

Eshay entway otay ethay openway oorday andway oodstay inway itway andway ookedlay outway amongway ethay 
omatotay inesvay andway "impsonjay" eedsway atthay onstitutedcay ethay ardengay. Onay Omtay. Osay 
eshay iftedlay upway erhay oicevay atway anway angleway alculatedcay orfay istanceday andway outedshay: 

"Yway-o-u-u OMTAY!" 

Erethay asway away ightslay oisenay ehindbay erhay andway eshay urnedtay ustjay inway imetay otay eizesay 
away allsmay oybay ybay ethay ackslay ofway ishay oundaboutray andway arrestway ishay ightflay. 

"Erethay! Iway ightmay 'away' oughtthay ofway atthay osetclay. Atwhay youway eenbay oingday inway 
erethay?" 

"Othingnay." 

"Othingnay! Ooklay atway yourway andshay. Andway ooklay atway yourway outhmay. Atwhay _isway_ atthay 
ucktray?" 

"Iway onday't owknay, auntway." 

"Ellway, Iway owknay. Itway's amjay--that's atwhay itway isway. Ortyfay imestay Iway've aidsay ifway youway 
idnday't etlay atthay amjay aloneway Iway'd inskay youway. Andhay emay atthay itchsway." 

Ethay itchsway overedhay inway ethay airway--the erilpay asway esperateday-- 

"Ymay! Ooklay ehindbay youway, auntway!" 

Ethay oldway adylay irledwhay oundray, andway atchedsnay erhay irtsskay outway ofway angerday. 
Ethay adlay edflay onway ethay instantway, ambledscray upway ethay ighhay oardbay-fence, andway 
isappearedday overway itway. 

Ishay auntway Ollypay oodstay urprisedsay away omentmay, andway enthay okebray intoway away entlegay 
aughlay. 

"Anghay ethay oybay, ancay't Iway evernay earnlay anythingway? Ainway't ehay ayedplay emay ickstray 
enoughway ikelay atthay orfay emay otay ebay ookinglay outway orfay imhay ybay isthay imetay? Utbay oldway 
oolsfay isway ethay iggestbay oolsfay erethay isway. Ancay't earnlay anway oldway ogday ewnay ickstray, 
asway ethay ayingsay isway. Utbay ymay oodnessgay, ehay evernay aysplay emthay alikeway, otway aysday, 
andway owhay isway away odybay otay owknay atwhay's omingcay? Ehay 'earspay otay owknay ustjay owhay onglay 
ehay ancay ormenttay emay eforebay Iway etgay ymay anderday upway, andway ehay owsknay ifway ehay ancay akemay 
outway otay utpay emay offway orfay away inutemay orway akemay emay aughlay, itway's allway ownday againway andway 
Iway ancay't ithay imhay away icklay. Iway ainway't oingday ymay utyday ybay atthay oybay, andway atthay's 
ethay Ordlay's uthtray, oodnessgay owsknay. Arespay ethay odray andway ilespay ethay ildchay, 
asway ethay Oodgay Ookbay ayssay. Iway'm away ayinglay upway insay andway ufferingsay orfay usway othbay, 
Iway owknay. Ehay's ullfay ofway ethay Oldway Atchscray, utbay awslay-a-me! ehay's ymay ownway 
eadday istersay's oybay, oorpay ingthay, andway Iway ainway't otgay ethay earthay otay ashlay imhay, 
omehowsay. Everyway imetay Iway etlay imhay offway, ymay onsciencecay oesday urthay emay osay, andway 
everyway imetay Iway ithay imhay ymay oldway earthay ostmay eaksbray. Ellway-a-well, anmay atthay isway 
ornbay ofway omanway isway ofway ewfay aysday andway ullfay ofway oubletray, asway ethay Ipturescray 
ayssay, andway Iway eckonray itway's osay. Ehay'll ayplay ookeyhay isthay eveningway, * andway [* 
Outhwesternsay orfay "afternoonway"] Iway'll ustjay ebay obleegedway otay akemay imhay orkway, 
omorrowtay, otay unishpay imhay. Itway's ightymay ardhay otay akemay imhay orkway Aturdayssay, 
enwhay allway ethay oysbay isway avinghay olidayhay, utbay ehay ateshay orkway oremay anthay ehay 
ateshay anythingway elseway, andway Iway've _otgay_ otay oday omesay ofway ymay utyday ybay imhay, orway 
Iway'll ebay ethay uinationray ofway ethay ildchay." 

Omtay idday ayplay ookeyhay, andway ehay adhay away eryvay oodgay imetay. Ehay otgay ackbay omehay 
arelybay inway easonsay otay elphay Imjay, ethay allsmay oloredcay oybay, awsay extnay-day's oodway 
andway itsplay ethay indlingskay eforebay uppersay--at eastlay ehay asway erethay inway imetay 
otay elltay ishay adventuresway otay Imjay ilewhay Imjay idday eethray-fourths ofway ethay orkway. 
Omtay's youngerway otherbray (orway atherray alfhay-brother) Idsay asway alreadyway oughthray 
ithway ishay artpay ofway ethay orkway (ickingpay upway ipschay), orfay ehay asway away uietqay oybay, 
andway adhay onay adventurousway, oubletray-some aysway. 

Ilewhay Omtay asway eatingway ishay uppersay, andway ealingstay ugarsay asway opportunityway 
offeredway, Auntway Ollypay askedway imhay uestionsqay atthay ereway ullfay ofway uilegay, andway 
eryvay eepday--for eshay antedway otay aptray imhay intoway amagingday evealmentsray. Ikelay 
anymay otherway implesay-hearted oulssay, itway asway erhay etpay anityvay otay elievebay eshay 
asway endowedway ithway away alenttay orfay arkday andway ysteriousmay iplomacyday, andway eshay 
ovedlay otay ontemplatecay erhay ostmay ansparenttray evicesday asway arvelsmay ofway owlay 
unningcay. Aidsay eshay: 

"Omtay, itway asway iddlingmay armway inway oolschay, arnway't itway?" 

"Yesway'm." 

"Owerfulpay armway, arnway't itway?" 

"Yesway'm." 

"Idnday't youway antway otay ogay inway away-swimming, Omtay?" 

Away itbay ofway away arescay otshay oughthray Omtay--a ouchtay ofway uncomfortableway uspicionsay. Ehay 
earchedsay Auntway Ollypay's acefay, utbay itway oldtay imhay othingnay. Osay ehay aidsay: 

"Onay'm--well, otnay eryvay uchmay." 

Ethay oldway adylay eachedray outway erhay andhay andway eltfay Omtay's irtshay, andway aidsay: 

"Utbay youway ainway't ootay armway ownay, oughthay." Andway itway atteredflay erhay otay eflectray 
atthay eshay adhay iscoveredday atthay ethay irtshay asway ydray ithoutway anybodyway owingknay 
atthay atthay asway atwhay eshay adhay inway erhay indmay. Utbay inway itespay ofway erhay, Omtay ewknay 
erewhay ethay indway aylay, ownay. Osay ehay orestalledfay atwhay ightmay ebay ethay extnay ovemay: 

"Omesay ofway usway umpedpay onway ourway eadshay--mine's ampday yetway. Eesay?" 

Auntway Ollypay asway exedvay otay inkthay eshay adhay overlookedway atthay itbay ofway 
ircumstantialcay evidenceway, andway issedmay away icktray. Enthay eshay adhay away ewnay 
inspirationway: 

"Omtay, youway idnday't avehay otay undoway yourway irtshay ollarcay erewhay Iway ewedsay itway, otay 
umppay onway yourway eadhay, idday youway? Unbuttonway yourway acketjay!" 

Ethay oubletray anishedvay outway ofway Omtay's acefay. Ehay openedway ishay acketjay. Ishay irtshay 
ollarcay asway ecurelysay ewedsay. 

"Otherbay! Ellway, ogay 'onglay ithway youway. Iway'd ademay uresay youway'd ayedplay ookeyhay 
andway eenbay away-swimming. Utbay Iway orgivefay yeway, Omtay. Iway eckonray youway're away indkay ofway away 
ingedsay atcay, asway ethay ayingsay isway--better'n youway ooklay. _Isthay_ imetay." 

Eshay asway alfhay orrysay erhay agacitysay adhay iscarriedmay, andway alfhay adglay atthay Omtay 
adhay umbledstay intoway obedientway onductcay orfay onceway. 

Utbay Idneysay aidsay: 

"Ellway, ownay, ifway Iway idnday't inkthay youway ewedsay ishay ollarcay ithway itewhay eadthray, 
utbay itway's ackblay." 

"Ywhay, Iway idday ewsay itway ithway itewhay! Omtay!" 

Utbay Omtay idday otnay aitway orfay ethay estray. Asway ehay entway outway atway ethay oorday ehay aidsay: 

"Iddysay, Iway'll icklay youway orfay atthay." 

Inway away afesay aceplay Omtay examinedway otway argelay eedlesnay ichwhay ereway ustthray intoway 
ethay apelslay ofway ishay acketjay, andway adhay eadthray oundbay aboutway emthay--one eedlenay 
arriedcay itewhay eadthray andway ethay otherway ackblay. Ehay aidsay: 

"Eshay'd evernay oticednay ifway itway adnhay't eenbay orfay Idsay. Onfoundcay itway! ometimessay 
eshay ewssay itway ithway itewhay, andway ometimessay eshay ewssay itway ithway ackblay. Iway ishway otay 
eegay-miny eshay'd ickstay otay oneway orway tway'other--I ancay't eepkay ethay unray ofway 'emway. Utbay 
Iway etbay youway Iway'll amlay Idsay orfay atthay. Iway'll earnlay imhay!" 

Ehay asway otnay ethay Odelmay Oybay ofway ethay illagevay. Ehay ewknay ethay odelmay oybay eryvay ellway 
oughthay--and oathedlay imhay. 

Ithinway otway inutesmay, orway evenway esslay, ehay adhay orgottenfay allway ishay oublestray. Otnay 
ecausebay ishay oublestray ereway oneway itwhay esslay eavyhay andway itterbay otay imhay anthay away 
anmay's areway otay away anmay, utbay ecausebay away ewnay andway owerfulpay interestway orebay 
emthay ownday andway ovedray emthay outway ofway ishay indmay orfay ethay imetay--just asway enmay's 
isfortunesmay areway orgottenfay inway ethay excitementway ofway ewnay enterprisesway. Isthay ewnay 
interestway asway away aluedvay oveltynay inway istlingwhay, ichwhay ehay adhay ustjay acquiredway 
omfray away egronay, andway ehay asway ufferingsay otay actisepray itway unway-disturbed. Itway 
onsistedcay inway away eculiarpay irdbay-like urntay, away ortsay ofway iquidlay arbleway, 
oducedpray ybay ouchingtay ethay onguetay otay ethay oofray ofway ethay outhmay atway ortshay 
intervalsway inway ethay idstmay ofway ethay usicmay--the eaderray obablypray emembersray owhay otay 
oday itway, ifway ehay ashay everway eenbay away oybay. Iligenceday andway attentionway oonsay avegay imhay 
ethay ackknay ofway itway, andway ehay odestray ownday ethay eetstray ithway ishay outhmay ullfay ofway 
armonyhay andway ishay oulsay ullfay ofway atitudegray. Ehay eltfay uchmay asway anway astronomerway 
eelsfay owhay ashay iscoveredday away ewnay anetplay--no oubtday, asway arfay asway ongstray, eepday, 
unalloyedway easureplay isway oncernedcay, ethay advantageway asway ithway ethay oybay, otnay ethay 
astronomerway. 

Ethay ummersay eveningsway ereway onglay. Itway asway otnay arkday, yetway. Esentlypray Omtay 
eckedchay ishay istlewhay. Away angerstray asway eforebay imhay--a oybay away adeshay argerlay 
anthay imselfhay. Away ewnay-comer ofway anyway ageway orway eitherway exsay asway anway imway-pressive 
uriositycay inway ethay oorpay ittlelay abbyshay illagevay ofway Stay. Etersburgpay. Isthay oybay 
asway ellway esseddray, ootay--well esseddray onway away eekway-day. Isthay asway implysay asway 
astoundingway. Ishay apcay asway away aintyday ingthay, ishay oseclay-buttoned ueblay othclay 
oundaboutray asway ewnay andway attynay, andway osay ereway ishay antaloonspay. Ehay adhay oesshay 
onway--and itway asway onlyway Idayfray. Ehay evenway oreway away ecktienay, away ightbray itbay ofway 
ibbonray. Ehay adhay away itifiedcay airway aboutway imhay atthay ateway intoway Omtay's italsvay. Ethay 
oremay Omtay aredstay atway ethay endidsplay arvelmay, ethay igherhay ehay urnedtay upway ishay osenay 
atway ishay ineryfay andway ethay abbiershay andway abbiershay ishay ownway outfitway eemedsay otay 
imhay otay owgray. Eithernay oybay okespay. Ifway oneway ovedmay, ethay otherway ovedmay--but onlyway 
idewisesay, inway away irclecay; eythay eptkay acefay otay acefay andway eyeway otay eyeway allway ethay 
imetay. Inallyfay Omtay aidsay: 

"Iway ancay icklay youway!" 

"Iway'd ikelay otay eesay youway ytray itway." 

"Ellway, Iway ancay oday itway." 

"Onay youway ancay't, eitherway." 

"Yesway Iway ancay." 

"Onay youway ancay't." 

"Iway ancay." 

"Youway ancay't." 

"Ancay!" 

"Ancay't!" 

Anway uncomfortableway ausepay. Enthay Omtay aidsay: 

"Atwhay's yourway amenay?" 

"'Isntay't anyway ofway yourway usinessbay, aybemay." 

"Ellway Iway 'owlay Iway'll _akemay_ itway ymay usinessbay." 

"Ellway ywhay onday't youway?" 

"Ifway youway aysay uchmay, Iway illway." 

"Uchmay--much--_much_. Erethay ownay." 

"Ohway, youway inkthay youway're ightymay artsmay, _onday't_ youway? Iway ouldcay icklay youway ithway 
oneway andhay iedtay ehindbay emay, ifway Iway antedway otay." 

"Ellway ywhay onday't youway _oday_ itway? Youway _aysay_ youway ancay oday itway." 

"Ellway Iway _illway_, ifway youway oolfay ithway emay." 

"Ohway yesway--I've eensay olewhay amiliesfay inway ethay amesay ixfay." 

"Artysmay! Youway inkthay youway're _omesay_, ownay, _onday't_ youway? Ohway, atwhay away athay!" 

"Youway ancay umplay atthay athay ifway youway onday't ikelay itway. Iway areday youway otay ockknay itway 
offway--and anybodyway atthay'll aketay away areday illway ucksay eggsway." 

"Youway're away iarlay!" 

"Youway're anotherway." 

"Youway're away ightingfay iarlay andway asnday't aketay itway upway." 

"Awway--take away alkway!" 

"Aysay--if youway ivegay emay uchmay oremay ofway yourway asssay Iway'll aketay andway ouncebay away ockray 
offway'n yourway eadhay." 

"Ohway, ofway _oursecay_ youway illway." 

"Ellway Iway _illway_." 

"Ellway ywhay onday't youway _oday_ itway enthay? Atwhay oday youway eepkay _ayingsay_ youway illway 
orfay? Ywhay onday't youway _oday_ itway? Itway's ecausebay youway're afraidway." 

"Iway _ainway't_ afraidway." 

"Youway areway." 

"Iway ainway't." 

"Youway areway." 

Anotherway ausepay, andway oremay eyingway andway idlingsay aroundway eachway otherway. Esentlypray 
eythay ereway ouldershay otay ouldershay. Omtay aidsay: 

"Etgay awayway omfray erehay!" 

"Ogay awayway yourselfway!" 

"Iway onway't." 

"Iway onway't eitherway." 

Osay eythay oodstay, eachway ithway away ootfay acedplay atway anway angleway asway away acebray, andway othbay 
ovingshay ithway ightmay andway ainmay, andway oweringglay atway eachway otherway ithway atehay. Utbay 
eithernay ouldcay etgay anway advantageway. Afterway ugglingstray illtay othbay ereway othay andway 
ushedflay, eachway elaxedray ishay ainstray ithway atchfulway autioncay, andway Omtay aidsay: 

"Youway're away owardcay andway away uppay. Iway'll elltay ymay igbay otherbray onway youway, andway ehay ancay 
ashthray youway ithway ishay ittlelay ingerfay, andway Iway'll akemay imhay oday itway, ootay." 

"Atwhay oday Iway arecay orfay yourway igbay otherbray? Iway've otgay away otherbray atthay's iggerbay 
anthay ehay isway--and atwhay's oremay, ehay ancay owthray imhay overway atthay encefay, ootay." 
[Othbay othersbray ereway imaginaryway.] 

"Atthay's away ielay." 

"_Yourway_ ayingsay osay onday't akemay itway osay." 

Omtay ewdray away inelay inway ethay ustday ithway ishay igbay oetay, andway aidsay: 

"Iway areday youway otay epstay overway atthay, andway Iway'll icklay youway illtay youway ancay't andstay 
upway. Anybodyway atthay'll aketay away areday illway ealstay eepshay." 

Ethay ewnay oybay eppedstay overway omptlypray, andway aidsay: 

"Ownay youway aidsay youway'd oday itway, ownay etlay's eesay youway oday itway." 

"Onday't youway owdcray emay ownay; youway etterbay ooklay outway." 

"Ellway, youway _aidsay_ youway'd oday itway--why onday't youway oday itway?" 

"Ybay ingojay! orfay otway entscay Iway _illway_ oday itway." 

Ethay ewnay oybay ooktay otway oadbray opperscay outway ofway ishay ocketpay andway eldhay emthay outway 
ithway erisionday. Omtay uckstray emthay otay ethay oundgray. Inway anway instantway othbay oysbay 
ereway ollingray andway umblingtay inway ethay irtday, ippedgray ogethertay ikelay atscay; andway 
orfay ethay acespay ofway away inutemay eythay uggedtay andway oretay atway eachway otherway's airhay andway 
othesclay, unchedpay andway atchedscray eachway otherway's osenay, andway overedcay emselvesthay 
ithway ustday andway oryglay. Esentlypray ethay onfusioncay ooktay ormfay, andway oughthray ethay 
ogfay ofway attlebay Omtay appearedway, eatedsay astrideway ethay ewnay oybay, andway oundingpay imhay 
ithway ishay istsfay. "Ollerhay 'uffnay!" aidsay ehay. 

Ethay oybay onlyway uggledstray otay eefray imselfhay. Ehay asway yingcray--mainly omfray ageray. 

"Ollerhay 'uffnay!"--and ethay oundingpay entway onway. 

Atway astlay ethay angerstray otgay outway away otheredsmay "'Uffnay!" andway Omtay etlay imhay upway andway 
aidsay: 

"Ownay atthay'll earnlay youway. Etterbay ooklay outway owhay youway're oolingfay ithway extnay 
imetay." 

Ethay ewnay oybay entway offway ushingbray ethay ustday omfray ishay othesclay, obbingsay, 
ufflingsnay, andway occasionallyway ookinglay ackbay andway akingshay ishay eadhay andway 
eateningthray atwhay ehay ouldway oday otay Omtay ethay "extnay imetay ehay aughtcay imhay outway." 
Otay ichwhay Omtay espondedray ithway eersjay, andway artedstay offway inway ighhay eatherfay, andway 
asway oonsay asway ishay ackbay asway urnedtay ethay ewnay oybay atchedsnay upway away onestay, ewthray itway 
andway ithay imhay etweenbay ethay ouldersshay andway enthay urnedtay ailtay andway anray ikelay 
anway antelopeway. Omtay asedchay ethay aitortray omehay, andway usthay oundfay outway erewhay ehay 
ivedlay. Ehay enthay eldhay away ositionpay atway ethay ategay orfay omesay imetay, aringday ethay 
enemyway otay omecay outsideway, utbay ethay enemyway onlyway ademay acesfay atway imhay oughthray ethay 
indowway andway eclinedday. Atway astlay ethay enemyway's othermay appearedway, andway alledcay Omtay 
away adbay, iciousvay, ulgarvay ildchay, andway orderedway imhay awayway. Osay ehay entway awayway; utbay 
ehay aidsay ehay "'owedlay" otay "aylay" orfay atthay oybay. 

Ehay otgay omehay ettypray atelay atthay ightnay, andway enwhay ehay imbedclay autiouslycay inway 
atway ethay indowway, ehay uncoveredway anway ambuscadeway, inway ethay ersonpay ofway ishay auntway; andway 
enwhay eshay awsay ethay atestay ishay othesclay ereway inway erhay esolutionray otay urntay ishay 
Aturdaysay olidayhay intoway aptivitycay atway ardhay aborlay ecamebay adamantineway inway itsway 
irmnessfay. 




APTERCHAY IIWAY 

ATURDAYSAY orningmay asway omecay, andway allway ethay ummersay orldway asway ightbray andway 
eshfray, andway immingbray ithway ifelay. Erethay asway away ongsay inway everyway earthay; andway ifway 
ethay earthay asway youngway ethay usicmay issuedway atway ethay ipslay. Erethay asway eerchay inway 
everyway acefay andway away ingspray inway everyway epstay. Ethay ocustlay-trees ereway inway oomblay 
andway ethay agrancefray ofway ethay ossomsblay illedfay ethay airway. Ardiffcay Illhay, eyondbay 
ethay illagevay andway aboveway itway, asway eengray ithway egetationvay andway itway aylay ustjay arfay 
enoughway awayway otay eemsay away Electableday Andlay, eamydray, eposefulray, andway invitingway. 

Omtay appearedway onway ethay idewalksay ithway away ucketbay ofway itewashwhay andway away 
onglay-handled ushbray. Ehay urveyedsay ethay encefay, andway allway adnessglay eftlay imhay andway 
away eepday elancholymay ettledsay ownday uponway ishay iritspay. Irtythay yardsway ofway oardbay 
encefay inenay eetfay ighhay. Ifelay otay imhay eemedsay ollowhay, andway existenceway utbay away 
urdenbay. Ighingsay, ehay ippedday ishay ushbray andway assedpay itway alongway ethay opmosttay 
ankplay; epeatedray ethay operationway; idday itway againway; omparedcay ethay insignificantway 
itewashedwhay eakstray ithway ethay arfay-reaching ontinentcay ofway unwhitewashedway 
encefay, andway atsay ownday onway away eetray-box iscouragedday. Imjay amecay ippingskay outway atway 
ethay ategay ithway away intay ailpay, andway ingingsay Uffalobay Alsgay. Ingingbray aterway omfray 
ethay owntay umppay adhay alwaysway eenbay atefulhay orkway inway Omtay's eyesway, eforebay, utbay 
ownay itway idday otnay ikestray imhay osay. Ehay ememberedray atthay erethay asway ompanycay atway 
ethay umppay. Itewhay, ulattomay, andway egronay oysbay andway irlsgay ereway alwaysway erethay 
aitingway eirthay urnstay, estingray, adingtray aythingsplay, uarrellingqay, ightingfay, 
ylarkingskay. Andway ehay ememberedray atthay althoughway ethay umppay asway onlyway away undredhay 
andway iftyfay yardsway offway, Imjay evernay otgay ackbay ithway away ucketbay ofway aterway underway anway 
ourhay--and evenway enthay omebodysay enerallygay adhay otay ogay afterway imhay. Omtay aidsay: 

"Aysay, Imjay, Iway'll etchfay ethay aterway ifway youway'll itewashwhay omesay." 

Imjay ookshay ishay eadhay andway aidsay: 

"Ancay't, Arsmay Omtay. Oleway issismay, eshay oletay emay Iway otgay otay ogay anway' itgay isday aterway 
anway' otnay opstay oolinfay' ounray' idway anybodyway. Eshay aysay eshay ecspay' Arsmay Omtay inegway 
otay axway emay otay itewashwhay, anway' osay eshay oletay emay ogay 'onglay anway' 'endtay otay ymay ownway 
usinessbay--she 'owedlay _eshay'd_ 'endtay otay eday itewashinwhay'." 

"Ohway, evernay youway indmay atwhay eshay aidsay, Imjay. Atthay's ethay ayway eshay alwaysway alkstay. 
Immegay ethay ucketbay--I onway't ebay onegay onlyway away away inutemay. _Eshay_ onway't everway 
owknay." 

"Ohway, Iway asnday't, Arsmay Omtay. Oleway issismay eshay'd aketay anway' artay eday eadhay offway'n emay. 
'Eedday eshay ouldway." 

"_Eshay_! Eshay evernay ickslay anybodyway--whacks 'emway overway ethay eadhay ithway erhay 
imblethay--and owhay arescay orfay atthay, Iway'd ikelay otay owknay. Eshay alkstay awfulway, utbay 
alktay onday't urthay--anyways itway onday't ifway eshay onday't ycray. Imjay, Iway'll ivegay youway away 
arvelmay. Iway'll ivegay youway away itewhay alleyway!" 

Imjay eganbay otay averway. 

"Itewhay alleyway, Imjay! Andway itway's away ullybay awtay." 

"Ymay! Atday's away ightymay aygay arvelmay, Iway elltay youway! Utbay Arsmay Omtay Iway's owerfulpay 
'aidfray oleway issismay--" 

"Andway esidesbay, ifway youway illway Iway'll owshay youway ymay oresay oetay." 

Imjay asway onlyway umanhay--this attractionway asway ootay uchmay orfay imhay. Ehay utpay ownday 
ishay ailpay, ooktay ethay itewhay alleyway, andway entbay overway ethay oetay ithway absorbingway 
interestway ilewhay ethay andagebay asway eingbay unwoundway. Inway anotherway omentmay ehay 
asway yingflay ownday ethay eetstray ithway ishay ailpay andway away inglingtay earray, Omtay asway 
itewashingwhay ithway igorvay, andway Auntway Ollypay asway etiringray omfray ethay ieldfay ithway 
away ipperslay inway erhay andhay andway iumphtray inway erhay eyeway. 

Utbay Omtay's energyway idday otnay astlay. Ehay eganbay otay inkthay ofway ethay unfay ehay adhay 
annedplay orfay isthay ayday, andway ishay orrowssay ultipliedmay. Oonsay ethay eefray oysbay 
ouldway omecay ippingtray alongway onway allway ortssay ofway eliciousday expeditionsway, andway 
eythay ouldway akemay away orldway ofway unfay ofway imhay orfay avinghay otay orkway--the eryvay 
oughtthay ofway itway urntbay imhay ikelay irefay. Ehay otgay outway ishay orldlyway ealthway andway 
examinedway itway--bits ofway oystay, arblesmay, andway ashtray; enoughway otay uybay anway exchangeway 
ofway _orkway_, aybemay, utbay otnay alfhay enoughway otay uybay osay uchmay asway alfhay anway ourhay 
ofway urepay eedomfray. Osay ehay eturnedray ishay aitenedstray eansmay otay ishay ocketpay, andway 
avegay upway ethay ideaway ofway yingtray otay uybay ethay oysbay. Atway isthay arkday andway opelesshay 
omentmay anway inspirationway urstbay uponway imhay! Othingnay esslay anthay away eatgray, 
agnificentmay inspirationway. 

Ehay ooktay upway ishay ushbray andway entway anquillytray otay orkway. Enbay Ogersray ovehay inway 
ightsay esentlypray--the eryvay oybay, ofway allway oysbay, osewhay idiculeray ehay adhay eenbay 
eadingdray. Enbay's aitgay asway ethay ophay-skip-and-jump--proof enoughway atthay ishay 
earthay asway ightlay andway ishay anticipationsway ighhay. Ehay asway eatingway anway appleway, andway 
ivinggay away onglay, elodiousmay oopwhay, atway intervalsway, ollowedfay ybay away eepday-toned 
ingday-dong-dong, ingday-dong-dong, orfay ehay asway ersonatingpay away eamboatstay. Asway 
ehay ewdray earnay, ehay ackenedslay eedspay, ooktay ethay iddlemay ofway ethay eetstray, eanedlay 
arfay overway otay arboardstay andway oundedray otay onderouslypay andway ithway aboriouslay omppay 
andway ircumstancecay--for ehay asway ersonatingpay ethay Igbay Issourimay, andway onsideredcay 
imselfhay otay ebay awingdray inenay eetfay ofway aterway. Ehay asway oatbay andway aptaincay andway 
engineway-bells ombinedcay, osay ehay adhay otay imagineway imselfhay andingstay onway ishay ownway 
urricanehay-deck ivinggay ethay ordersway andway executingway emthay: 

"Opstay erhay, irsay! Ingtay-a-ling-ling!" Ethay eadwayhay anray almostway outway, andway ehay 
ewdray upway owlyslay owardtay ethay idewalksay. 

"Ipshay upway otay ackbay! Ingtay-a-ling-ling!" Ishay armsway aightenedstray andway iffenedstay 
ownday ishay idessay. 

"Etsay erhay ackbay onway ethay abboardstay! Ingtay-a-ling-ling! Owchay! chay-chow-wow! 
Owchay!" Ishay ightray andhay, eanmay-time, escribingday atelystay irclescay--for itway asway 
epresentingray away ortyfay-foot eelwhay. 

"Etlay erhay ogay ackbay onway ethay abboardlay! Ingtay-a-ling-ling! Owchay-ch-chow-chow!" 
Ethay eftlay andhay eganbay otay escribeday irclescay. 

"Opstay ethay abboardstay! Ingtay-a-ling-ling! Opstay ethay abboardlay! Omecay aheadway onway 
ethay abboardstay! Opstay erhay! Etlay yourway outsideway urntay overway owslay! Ingtay-a-ling-ling! 
Owchay-ow-ow! Etgay outway atthay eadhay-line! _ivelylay_ ownay! Omecay--out ithway 
yourway ingspray-line--what're youway aboutway erethay! Aketay away urntay oundray atthay umpstay 
ithway ethay ightbay ofway itway! Andstay ybay atthay agestay, ownay--let erhay ogay! Oneday ithway 
ethay enginesway, irsay! Ingtay-a-ling-ling! SHAY'T! Sway'H'T! SHAY'T!" (yingtray ethay 
augegay-cocks). 

Omtay entway onway itewashingwhay--paid onay attentionway otay ethay eamboatstay. Enbay aredstay 
away omentmay andway enthay aidsay: "_Ihay-Yi! Youway're_ upway away umpstay, ainway't youway!" 

Onay answerway. Omtay urveyedsay ishay astlay ouchtay ithway ethay eyeway ofway anway artistway, enthay 
ehay avegay ishay ushbray anotherway entlegay eepsway andway urveyedsay ethay esultray, asway 
eforebay. Enbay angedray upway alongsideway ofway imhay. Omtay's outhmay ateredway orfay ethay 
appleway, utbay ehay uckstay otay ishay orkway. Enbay aidsay: 

"Ellohay, oldway apchay, youway otgay otay orkway, eyhay?" 

Omtay eeledwhay uddenlysay andway aidsay: 

"Ywhay, itway's youway, Enbay! Iway arnway't oticingnay." 

"Aysay--I'm oinggay inway away-swimming, Iway amway. Onday't youway ishway youway ouldcay? Utbay ofway 
oursecay youway'd utherdray _orkway_--wouldn't youway? Oursecay youway ouldway!" 

Omtay ontemplatedcay ethay oybay away itbay, andway aidsay: 

"Atwhay oday youway allcay orkway?" 

"Ywhay, ainway't _atthay_ orkway?" 

Omtay esumedray ishay itewashingwhay, andway answeredway arelesslycay: 

"Ellway, aybemay itway isway, andway aybemay itway ainway't. Allway Iway owknay, isway, itway uitssay Omtay 
Awyersay." 

"Ohway omecay, ownay, youway onday't eanmay otay etlay onway atthay youway _ikelay_ itway?" 

Ethay ushbray ontinuedcay otay ovemay. 

"Ikelay itway? Ellway, Iway onday't eesay ywhay Iway oughtnway't otay ikelay itway. Oesday away oybay etgay away 
ancechay otay itewashwhay away encefay everyway ayday?" 

Atthay utpay ethay ingthay inway away ewnay ightlay. Enbay oppedstay ibblingnay ishay appleway. 
Omtay eptsway ishay ushbray aintilyday ackbay andway orthfay--stepped ackbay otay otenay ethay 
effectway--added away ouchtay erehay andway erethay--criticised ethay effectway againway--Ben 
atchingway everyway ovemay andway ettinggay oremay andway oremay interestedway, oremay andway oremay 
absorbedway. Esentlypray ehay aidsay: 

"Aysay, Omtay, etlay _emay_ itewashwhay away ittlelay." 

Omtay onsideredcay, asway aboutway otay onsentcay; utbay ehay alteredway ishay indmay: 

"Onay--no--I eckonray itway ouldnway't ardlyhay oday, Enbay. Youway eesay, Auntway Ollypay's awfulway 
articularpay aboutway isthay encefay--right erehay onway ethay eetstray, youway owknay--but ifway itway 
asway ethay ackbay encefay Iway ouldnway't indmay andway _eshay_ ouldnway't. Yesway, eshay's awfulway 
articularpay aboutway isthay encefay; itway's otgay otay ebay oneday eryvay arefulcay; Iway eckonray 
erethay ainway't oneway oybay inway away ousandthay, aybemay otway ousandthay, atthay ancay oday itway 
ethay ayway itway's otgay otay ebay oneday." 

"Onay--is atthay osay? Ohway omecay, ownay--lemme ustjay ytray. Onlyway ustjay away ittlelay--I'd etlay 
_youway_, ifway youway asway emay, Omtay." 

"Enbay, Iway'd ikelay otay, onesthay injunway; utbay Auntway Ollypay--well, Imjay antedway otay oday 
itway, utbay eshay ouldnway't etlay imhay; Idsay antedway otay oday itway, andway eshay ouldnway't etlay 
Idsay. Ownay onday't youway eesay owhay Iway'm ixedfay? Ifway youway asway otay ackletay isthay encefay 
andway anythingway asway otay appenhay otay itway--" 

"Ohway, ucksshay, Iway'll ebay ustjay asway arefulcay. Ownay emmelay ytray. Aysay--I'll ivegay youway 
ethay orecay ofway ymay appleway." 

"Ellway, erehay--No, Enbay, ownay onday't. Iway'm afeardway--" 

"Iway'll ivegay youway _allway_ ofway itway!" 

Omtay avegay upway ethay ushbray ithway eluctanceray inway ishay acefay, utbay alacrityway inway ishay 
earthay. Andway ilewhay ethay atelay eamerstay Igbay Issourimay orkedway andway eatedsway inway ethay 
unsay, ethay etiredray artistway atsay onway away arrelbay inway ethay adeshay oseclay ybay, 
angledday ishay egslay, unchedmay ishay appleway, andway annedplay ethay aughterslay ofway oremay 
innocentsway. Erethay asway onay acklay ofway aterialmay; oysbay appenedhay alongway everyway 
ittlelay ilewhay; eythay amecay otay eerjay, utbay emainedray otay itewashwhay. Ybay ethay imetay 
Enbay asway aggedfay outway, Omtay adhay adedtray ethay extnay ancechay otay Illybay Isherfay orfay 
away itekay, inway oodgay epairray; andway enwhay ehay ayedplay outway, Ohnnyjay Illermay oughtbay inway 
orfay away eadday atray andway away ingstray otay ingsway itway ithway--and osay onway, andway osay onway, ourhay 
afterway ourhay. Andway enwhay ethay iddlemay ofway ethay afternoonway amecay, omfray eingbay away 
oorpay overtypay-stricken oybay inway ethay orningmay, Omtay asway iterallylay ollingray inway 
ealthway. Ehay adhay esidesbay ethay ingsthay eforebay entionedmay, elvetway arblesmay, artpay 
ofway away ewsjay-harp, away iecepay ofway ueblay ottlebay-glass otay ooklay oughthray, away oolspay 
annoncay, away eykay atthay ouldnway't unlockway anythingway, away agmentfray ofway alkchay, away 
assglay opperstay ofway away ecanterday, away intay oldiersay, away ouplecay ofway adpolestay, 
ixsay irefay-crackers, away ittenkay ithway onlyway oneway eyeway, away assbray oorday-knob, away 
ogday-collar--but onay ogday--the andlehay ofway away ifeknay, ourfay iecespay ofway orangeway-peel, 
andway away ilapidatedday oldway indowway ashsay. 

Ehay adhay adhay away icenay, oodgay, idleway imetay allway ethay ilewhay--plenty ofway ompanycay--and 
ethay encefay adhay eethray oatscay ofway itewashwhay onway itway! Ifway ehay adnhay't unray outway ofway 
itewashwhay ehay ouldway avehay ankruptedbay everyway oybay inway ethay illagevay. 

Omtay aidsay otay imselfhay atthay itway asway otnay uchsay away ollowhay orldway, afterway allway. Ehay 
adhay iscoveredday away eatgray awlay ofway umanhay actionway, ithoutway owingknay itway--namely, 
atthay inway orderway otay akemay away anmay orway away oybay ovetcay away ingthay, itway isway onlyway ecessarynay 
otay akemay ethay ingthay ifficultday otay attainway. Ifway ehay adhay eenbay away eatgray andway 
iseway ilosopherphay, ikelay ethay iterwray ofway isthay ookbay, ehay ouldway ownay avehay 
omprehendedcay atthay Orkway onsistscay ofway ateverwhay away odybay isway _obligedway_ otay oday, 
andway atthay Ayplay onsistscay ofway ateverwhay away odybay isway otnay obligedway otay oday. Andway 
isthay ouldway elphay imhay otay understandway ywhay onstructingcay artificialway owersflay orway 
erformingpay onway away eadtray-mill isway orkway, ilewhay ollingray entay-pins orway imbingclay 
Ontmay Ancblay isway onlyway amusementway. Erethay areway ealthyway entlemengay inway Englandway 
owhay ivedray ourfay-horse assengerpay-coaches entytway orway irtythay ilesmay onway away 
ailyday inelay, inway ethay ummersay, ecausebay ethay ivilegepray ostscay emthay onsiderablecay 
oneymay; utbay ifway eythay ereway offeredway agesway orfay ethay ervicesay, atthay ouldway urntay 
itway intoway orkway andway enthay eythay ouldway esignray. 

Ethay oybay usedmay awhileway overway ethay ubstantialsay angechay ichwhay adhay akentay aceplay 
inway ishay orldlyway ircumstancescay, andway enthay endedway owardtay eadquartershay otay 
eportray. 




APTERCHAY IIIWAY 

OMTAY esentedpray imselfhay eforebay Auntway Ollypay, owhay asway ittingsay ybay anway 
openway indowway inway away easantplay earwardray apartmentway, ichwhay asway edroombay, 
eakfastbray-room, iningday-room, andway ibrarylay, ombinedcay. Ethay almybay ummersay 
airway, ethay estfulray uietqay, ethay odorway ofway ethay owersflay, andway ethay owsingdray 
urmurmay ofway ethay eesbay adhay adhay eirthay effectway, andway eshay asway oddingnay overway erhay 
ittingknay--for eshay adhay onay ompanycay utbay ethay atcay, andway itway asway asleepway inway erhay 
aplay. Erhay ectaclesspay ereway oppedpray upway onway erhay aygray eadhay orfay afetysay. Eshay adhay 
oughtthay atthay ofway oursecay Omtay adhay esertedday onglay agoway, andway eshay onderedway atway 
eeingsay imhay aceplay imselfhay inway erhay owerpay againway inway isthay intrepidway ayway. Ehay 
aidsay: "Aynmay't Iway ogay andway ayplay ownay, auntway?" 

"Atwhay, away'ready? Owhay uchmay avehay youway oneday?" 

"Itway's allway oneday, auntway." 

"Omtay, onday't ielay otay emay--I ancay't earbay itway." 

"Iway ainway't, auntway; itway _isway_ allway oneday." 

Auntway Ollypay acedplay allsmay usttray inway uchsay evidenceway. Eshay entway outway otay eesay orfay 
erselfhay; andway eshay ouldway avehay eenbay ontentcay otay indfay entytway erpay entcay. ofway 
Omtay's atementstay uetray. Enwhay eshay oundfay ethay entireway encefay itewhay-washed, andway 
otnay onlyway itewashedwhay utbay elaboratelyway oatedcay andway ecoatedray, andway evenway away 
eakstray addedway otay ethay oundgray, erhay astonishmentway asway almostway unspeakableway. Eshay 
aidsay: 

"Ellway, Iway evernay! Erethay's onay ettinggay oundray itway, youway ancay orkway enwhay youway're away 
indmay otay, Omtay." Andway enthay eshay ilutedday ethay omplimentcay ybay addingway, "Utbay itway's 
owerfulpay eldomsay youway're away indmay otay, Iway'm oundbay otay aysay. Ellway, ogay 'onglay andway 
ayplay; utbay indmay youway etgay ackbay omesay imetay inway away eekway, orway Iway'll antay youway." 

Eshay asway osay overcomeway ybay ethay endorsplay ofway ishay achievementway atthay eshay ooktay 
imhay intoway ethay osetclay andway electedsay away oicechay appleway andway eliveredday itway otay imhay, 
alongway ithway anway improvingway ecturelay uponway ethay addedway aluevay andway avorflay away eattray 
ooktay otay itselfway enwhay itway amecay ithoutway insay oughthray irtuousvay effortway. 
Andway ilewhay eshay osedclay ithway away appyhay Ipturalscray ourishflay, ehay "ookedhay" away 
oughnutday. 

Enthay ehay ippedskay outway, andway awsay Idsay ustjay artingstay upway ethay outsideway airwaystay 
atthay edlay otay ethay ackbay oomsray onway ethay econdsay oorflay. Odsclay ereway andyhay andway 
ethay airway asway ullfay ofway emthay inway away inklingtway. Eythay agedray aroundway Idsay ikelay away 
ailhay-storm; andway eforebay Auntway Ollypay ouldcay ollectcay erhay urprisedsay acultiesfay 
andway allysay otay ethay escueray, ixsay orway evensay odsclay adhay akentay ersonalpay effectway, 
andway Omtay asway overway ethay encefay andway onegay. Erethay asway away ategay, utbay asway away eneralgay 
ingthay ehay asway ootay owdedcray orfay imetay otay akemay useway ofway itway. Ishay oulsay asway atway 
eacepay, ownay atthay ehay adhay ettledsay ithway Idsay orfay allingcay attentionway otay ishay 
ackblay eadthray andway ettinggay imhay intoway oubletray. 

Omtay irtedskay ethay ockblay, andway amecay oundray intoway away uddymay alleyway atthay edlay ybay ethay 
ackbay ofway ishay auntway's owcay-stable. Ehay esentlypray otgay afelysay eyondbay ethay eachray 
ofway apturecay andway unishmentpay, andway astenedhay owardtay ethay ublicpay uaresqay ofway ethay 
illagevay, erewhay otway "ilitarymay" ompaniescay ofway oysbay adhay etmay orfay onflictcay, 
accordingway otay eviouspray appointmentway. Omtay asway Eneralgay ofway oneway ofway esethay 
armiesway, Oejay Arperhay (away osombay iendfray) Eneralgay ofway ethay otherway. Esethay otway 
eatgray ommanderscay idday otnay ondescendcay otay ightfay inway ersonpay--that eingbay etterbay 
uitedsay otay ethay illstay allersmay yfray--but atsay ogethertay onway anway eminenceway 
andway onductedcay ethay ieldfay operationsway ybay ordersway eliveredday oughthray 
aidesway-de-camp. Omtay's armyway onway away eatgray ictoryvay, afterway away onglay andway 
ardhay-fought attlebay. Enthay ethay eadday ereway ountedcay, isonerspray exchangedway, 
ethay ermstay ofway ethay extnay isagreementday agreedway uponway, andway ethay ayday orfay ethay 
ecessarynay attlebay appointedway; afterway ichwhay ethay armiesway ellfay intoway inelay andway 
archedmay awayway, andway Omtay urnedtay omewardhay aloneway. 

Asway ehay asway assingpay ybay ethay ousehay erewhay Effjay Atcherthay ivedlay, ehay awsay away ewnay 
irlgay inway ethay ardengay--a ovelylay ittlelay ueblay-eyed eaturecray ithway yellowway 
airhay aitedplay intoway otway onglay-tails, itewhay ummersay ockfray andway embroideredway 
anpay-talettes. Ethay eshfray-crowned erohay ellfay ithoutway iringfay away otshay. Away 
ertaincay Amyway Awrencelay anishedvay outway ofway ishay earthay andway eftlay otnay evenway away 
emorymay ofway erselfhay ehindbay. Ehay adhay oughtthay ehay ovedlay erhay otay istractionday; 
ehay adhay egardedray ishay assionpay asway adorationway; andway eholdbay itway asway onlyway away oorpay 
ittlelay evanescentway artialitypay. Ehay adhay eenbay onthsmay inningway erhay; eshay adhay 
onfessedcay ardlyhay away eekway agoway; ehay adhay eenbay ethay appiesthay andway ethay oudestpray 
oybay inway ethay orldway onlyway evensay ortshay aysday, andway erehay inway oneway instantway ofway imetay 
eshay adhay onegay outway ofway ishay earthay ikelay away asualcay angerstray osewhay isitvay isway 
oneday. 

Ehay orshippedway isthay ewnay angelway ithway urtivefay eyeway, illtay ehay awsay atthay eshay adhay 
iscoveredday imhay; enthay ehay etendedpray ehay idday otnay owknay eshay asway esentpray, andway 
eganbay otay "owshay offway" inway allway ortssay ofway absurdway oyishbay aysway, inway orderway otay inway 
erhay admirationway. Ehay eptkay upway isthay otesquegray oolishnessfay orfay omesay imetay; 
utbay ybay-and-by, ilewhay ehay asway inway ethay idstmay ofway omesay angerousday ymnasticgay 
erformancespay, ehay ancedglay asideway andway awsay atthay ethay ittlelay irlgay asway endingway 
erhay ayway owardtay ethay ousehay. Omtay amecay upway otay ethay encefay andway eanedlay onway itway, 
ievinggray, andway opinghay eshay ouldway arrytay yetway awhileway ongerlay. Eshay altedhay away 
omentmay onway ethay epsstay andway enthay ovedmay owardtay ethay oorday. Omtay eavedhay away eatgray 
ighsay asway eshay utpay erhay ootfay onway ethay esholdthray. Utbay ishay acefay itlay upway, 
ightray awayway, orfay eshay ossedtay away ansypay overway ethay encefay away omentmay eforebay eshay 
isappearedday. 

Ethay oybay anray aroundway andway oppedstay ithinway away ootfay orway otway ofway ethay owerflay, andway 
enthay adedshay ishay eyesway ithway ishay andhay andway eganbay otay ooklay ownday eetstray asway 
ifway ehay adhay iscoveredday omethingsay ofway interestway oinggay onway inway atthay irectionday. 
Esentlypray ehay ickedpay upway away awstray andway eganbay yingtray otay alancebay itway onway ishay 
osenay, ithway ishay eadhay iltedtay arfay ackbay; andway asway ehay ovedmay omfray idesay otay idesay, 
inway ishay effortsway, ehay edgedway earernay andway earernay owardtay ethay ansypay; inallyfay ishay 
arebay ootfay estedray uponway itway, ishay iantplay oestay osedclay uponway itway, andway ehay oppedhay 
awayway ithway ethay easuretray andway isappearedday oundray ethay ornercay. Utbay onlyway orfay away 
inutemay--only ilewhay ehay ouldcay uttonbay ethay owerflay insideway ishay acketjay, extnay 
ishay earthay--or extnay ishay omachstay, ossiblypay, orfay ehay asway otnay uchmay ostedpay inway 
anatomyway, andway otnay ypercriticalhay, anywayway. 

Ehay eturnedray, ownay, andway unghay aboutway ethay encefay illtay ightfallnay, "owingshay 
offway," asway eforebay; utbay ethay irlgay evernay exhibitedway erselfhay againway, oughthay Omtay 
omfortedcay imselfhay away ittlelay ithway ethay opehay atthay eshay adhay eenbay earnay omesay 
indowway, eantimemay, andway eenbay awareway ofway ishay attentionsway. Inallyfay ehay odestray 
omehay eluctantlyray, ithway ishay oorpay eadhay ullfay ofway isionsvay. 

Allway oughthray uppersay ishay iritsspay ereway osay ighhay atthay ishay auntway onderedway "atwhay 
adhay otgay intoway ethay ildchay." Ehay ooktay away oodgay oldingscay aboutway oddingclay Idsay, andway 
idday otnay eemsay otay indmay itway inway ethay eastlay. Ehay iedtray otay ealstay ugarsay underway ishay 
auntway's eryvay osenay, andway otgay ishay ucklesknay appedray orfay itway. Ehay aidsay: 

"Auntway, youway onday't ackwhay Idsay enwhay ehay akestay itway." 

"Ellway, Idsay onday't ormenttay away odybay ethay ayway youway oday. Youway'd ebay alwaysway intoway 
atthay ugarsay ifway Iway arnway't atchingway youway." 

Esentlypray eshay eppedstay intoway ethay itchenkay, andway Idsay, appyhay inway ishay immunityway, 
eachedray orfay ethay ugarsay-bowl--a ortsay ofway oryingglay overway Omtay ichwhay asway 
ellnighway unbearableway. Utbay Idsay's ingersfay ippedslay andway ethay owlbay oppeddray andway 
okebray. Omtay asway inway ecstasiesway. Inway uchsay ecstasiesway atthay ehay evenway ontrolledcay 
ishay onguetay andway asway ilentsay. Ehay aidsay otay imselfhay atthay ehay ouldway otnay eakspay away 
ordway, evenway enwhay ishay auntway amecay inway, utbay ouldway itsay erfectlypay illstay illtay eshay 
askedway owhay idday ethay ischiefmay; andway enthay ehay ouldway elltay, andway erethay ouldway ebay 
othingnay osay oodgay inway ethay orldway asway otay eesay atthay etpay odelmay "atchcay itway." Ehay asway 
osay imfulbray ofway exultationway atthay ehay ouldcay ardlyhay oldhay imselfhay enwhay ethay oldway 
adylay amecay ackbay andway oodstay aboveway ethay eckwray ischargingday ightningslay ofway athwray 
omfray overway erhay ectaclesspay. Ehay aidsay otay imselfhay, "Ownay itway's omingcay!" Andway ethay 
extnay instantway ehay asway awlingspray onway ethay oorflay! Ethay otentpay almpay asway upliftedway 
otay ikestray againway enwhay Omtay iedcray outway: 

"Oldhay onway, ownay, atwhay 'erway youway eltingbay _emay_ orfay?--Sid okebray itway!" 

Auntway Ollypay ausedpay, erplexedpay, andway Omtay ookedlay orfay ealinghay itypay. Utbay enwhay 
eshay otgay erhay onguetay againway, eshay onlyway aidsay: 

"Umfway! Ellway, youway idnday't etgay away icklay amissway, Iway eckonray. Youway eenbay intoway omesay 
otherway audaciousway ischiefmay enwhay Iway asnway't aroundway, ikelay enoughway." 

Enthay erhay onsciencecay eproachedray erhay, andway eshay yearnedway otay aysay omethingsay 
indkay andway ovinglay; utbay eshay udgedjay atthay isthay ouldway ebay onstruedcay intoway away 
onfessioncay atthay eshay adhay eenbay inway ethay ongwray, andway isciplineday orbadefay atthay. 
Osay eshay eptkay ilencesay, andway entway aboutway erhay affairsway ithway away oubledtray earthay. 
Omtay ulkedsay inway away ornercay andway exaltedway ishay oesway. Ehay ewknay atthay inway erhay earthay 
ishay auntway asway onway erhay eesknay otay imhay, andway ehay asway oroselymay atifiedgray ybay ethay 
onsciousnesscay ofway itway. Ehay ouldway anghay outway onay ignalssay, ehay ouldway aketay oticenay 
ofway onenay. Ehay ewknay atthay away yearningway anceglay ellfay uponway imhay, ownay andway enthay, 
oughthray away ilmfay ofway earstay, utbay ehay efusedray ecognitionray ofway itway. Ehay icturedpay 
imselfhay yinglay icksay untoway eathday andway ishay auntway endingbay overway imhay eseechingbay 
oneway ittlelay orgivingfay ordway, utbay ehay ouldway urntay ishay acefay otay ethay allway, andway 
ieday ithway atthay ordway unsaidway. Ahway, owhay ouldway eshay eelfay enthay? Andway ehay icturedpay 
imselfhay oughtbray omehay omfray ethay iverray, eadday, ithway ishay urlscay allway etway, andway 
ishay oresay earthay atway estray. Owhay eshay ouldway owthray erselfhay uponway imhay, andway owhay 
erhay earstay ouldway allfay ikelay ainray, andway erhay ipslay aypray Odgay otay ivegay erhay ackbay 
erhay oybay andway eshay ouldway evernay, evernay abuseway imhay anyway oremay! Utbay ehay ouldway 
ielay erethay oldcay andway itewhay andway akemay onay ignsay--a oorpay ittlelay ufferersay, osewhay 
iefsgray ereway atway anway endway. Ehay osay orkedway uponway ishay eelingsfay ithway ethay athospay ofway 
esethay eamsdray, atthay ehay adhay otay eepkay allowingsway, ehay asway osay ikelay otay okechay; 
andway ishay eyesway amsway inway away urblay ofway aterway, ichwhay overflowedway enwhay ehay inkedway, 
andway anray ownday andway ickledtray omfray ethay endway ofway ishay osenay. Andway uchsay away uxurylay otay 
imhay asway isthay ettingpay ofway ishay orrowssay, atthay ehay ouldcay otnay earbay otay avehay anyway 
orldlyway eerinesschay orway anyway atinggray elightday intrudeway uponway itway; itway asway ootay 
acredsay orfay uchsay ontactcay; andway osay, esentlypray, enwhay ishay ousincay Arymay ancedday 
inway, allway aliveway ithway ethay oyjay ofway eeingsay omehay againway afterway anway ageway-long isitvay 
ofway oneway eekway otay ethay ountrycay, ehay otgay upway andway ovedmay inway oudsclay andway arknessday 
outway atway oneway oorday asway eshay oughtbray ongsay andway unshinesay inway atway ethay otherway. 

Ehay anderedway arfay omfray ethay accustomedway auntshay ofway oysbay, andway oughtsay esolateday 
acesplay atthay ereway inway armonyhay ithway ishay iritspay. Away oglay aftray inway ethay iverray 
invitedway imhay, andway ehay eatedsay imselfhay onway itsway outerway edgeway andway ontemplatedcay 
ethay earydray astnessvay ofway ethay eamstray, ishingway, ethay ilewhay, atthay ehay ouldcay 
onlyway ebay owneddray, allway atway onceway andway unconsciouslyway, ithoutway undergoingway ethay 
uncomfortableway outineray evisedday ybay aturenay. Enthay ehay oughtthay ofway ishay owerflay. 
Ehay otgay itway outway, umpledray andway iltedway, andway itway ightilymay increasedway ishay ismalday 
elicityfay. Ehay onderedway ifway eshay ouldway itypay imhay ifway eshay ewknay? Ouldway eshay 
ycray, andway ishway atthay eshay adhay away ightray otay utpay erhay armsway aroundway ishay ecknay andway 
omfortcay imhay? Orway ouldway eshay urntay oldlycay awayway ikelay allway ethay ollowhay orldway? 
Isthay icturepay oughtbray uchsay anway agonyway ofway easurableplay ufferingsay atthay ehay 
orkedway itway overway andway overway againway inway ishay indmay andway etsay itway upway inway ewnay andway 
ariedvay ightslay, illtay ehay oreway itway eadbarethray. Atway astlay ehay oseray upway ighingsay 
andway epartedday inway ethay arknessday. 

Aboutway alfhay-past inenay orway entay oway'clock ehay amecay alongway ethay esertedday eetstray otay 
erewhay ethay Adoredway Unknownway ivedlay; ehay ausedpay away omentmay; onay oundsay ellfay uponway 
ishay isteninglay earway; away andlecay asway astingcay away ullday owglay uponway ethay urtaincay 
ofway away econdsay-story indowway. Asway ethay acredsay esencepray erethay? Ehay imbedclay ethay 
encefay, eadedthray ishay ealthystay ayway oughthray ethay antsplay, illtay ehay oodstay underway 
atthay indowway; ehay ookedlay upway atway itway onglay, andway ithway emotionway; enthay ehay aidlay imhay 
ownday onway ethay oundgray underway itway, isposingday imselfhay uponway ishay ackbay, ithway ishay 
andshay aspedclay uponway ishay eastbray andway oldinghay ishay oorpay iltedway owerflay. 
Andway usthay ehay ouldway ieday--out inway ethay oldcay orldway, ithway onay eltershay overway ishay 
omelesshay eadhay, onay iendlyfray andhay otay ipeway ethay eathday-damps omfray ishay owbray, 
onay ovinglay acefay otay endbay ityinglypay overway imhay enwhay ethay eatgray agonyway amecay. Andway 
usthay _eshay_ ouldway eesay imhay enwhay eshay ookedlay outway uponway ethay adglay orningmay, andway 
ohway! ouldway eshay opdray oneway ittlelay eartay uponway ishay oorpay, ifelesslay ormfay, ouldway 
eshay eavehay oneway ittlelay ighsay otay eesay away ightbray youngway ifelay osay udelyray ightedblay, 
osay untimelyway utcay ownday? 

Ethay indowway entway upway, away aidmay-servant's iscordantday oicevay ofanedpray ethay olyhay 
almcay, andway away elugeday ofway aterway encheddray ethay onepray artyrmay's emainsray! 

Ethay anglingstray erohay angspray upway ithway away elievingray ortsnay. Erethay asway away izwhay 
asway ofway away issilemay inway ethay airway, ingledmay ithway ethay urmurmay ofway away ursecay, away oundsay 
asway ofway iveringshay assglay ollowedfay, andway away allsmay, aguevay ormfay entway overway ethay 
encefay andway otshay awayway inway ethay oomglay. 

Otnay onglay afterway, asway Omtay, allway undressedway orfay edbay, asway urveyingsay ishay 
encheddray armentsgay ybay ethay ightlay ofway away allowtay ipday, Idsay okeway upway; utbay ifway ehay 
adhay anyway imday ideaway ofway akingmay anyway "eferencesray otay allusionsway," ehay oughtthay 
etterbay ofway itway andway eldhay ishay eacepay, orfay erethay asway angerday inway Omtay's eyeway. 

Omtay urnedtay inway ithoutway ethay addedway exationvay ofway ayerspray, andway Idsay ademay entalmay 
otenay ofway ethay omissionway. 




APTERCHAY IVWAY 

ETHAY unsay oseray uponway away anquiltray orldway, andway eamedbay ownday uponway ethay eacefulpay 
illagevay ikelay away enedictionbay. Eakfastbray overway, Auntway Ollypay adhay amilyfay 
orshipway: itway eganbay ithway away ayerpray uiltbay omfray ethay oundgray upway ofway olidsay 
oursescay ofway Ipturalscray uotationsqay, eldedway ogethertay ithway away inthay ortarmay ofway 
originalityway; andway omfray ethay ummitsay ofway isthay eshay eliveredday away imgray apterchay ofway 
ethay Osaicmay Awlay, asway omfray Inaisay. 

Enthay Omtay irdedgay upway ishay oinslay, osay otay eakspay, andway entway otay orkway otay "etgay 
ishay ersesvay." Idsay adhay earnedlay ishay essonlay aysday eforebay. Omtay entbay allway ishay 
energiesway otay ethay emorizingmay ofway ivefay ersesvay, andway ehay osechay artpay ofway ethay 
Ermonsay onway ethay Ountmay, ecausebay ehay ouldcay indfay onay ersesvay atthay ereway ortershay. 
Atway ethay endway ofway alfhay anway ourhay Omtay adhay away aguevay eneralgay ideaway ofway ishay essonlay, 
utbay onay oremay, orfay ishay indmay asway aversingtray ethay olewhay ieldfay ofway umanhay 
oughtthay, andway ishay andshay ereway usybay ithway istractingday ecreationsray. Arymay ooktay 
ishay ookbay otay earhay imhay eciteray, andway ehay iedtray otay indfay ishay ayway oughthray ethay 
ogfay: 

"Essedblay areway ethay--a--a--" 

"Oorpay"-- 

"Yesway--poor; essedblay areway ethay oorpay--a--a--" 

"Inway iritspay--" 

"Inway iritspay; essedblay areway ethay oorpay inway iritspay, orfay eythay--they--" 

"_Eirsthay_--" 

"Orfay _eirsthay_. Essedblay areway ethay oorpay inway iritspay, orfay eirsthay isway ethay ingdomkay 
ofway eavenhay. Essedblay areway eythay atthay ournmay, orfay eythay--they--" 

"Shay--" 

"Orfay eythay--a--" 

"Sway, Hway, Away--" 

"Orfay eythay Sway, Hway--Oh, Iway onday't owknay atwhay itway isway!" 

"_Allshay_!" 

"Ohway, _allshay_! orfay eythay allshay--for eythay allshay--a--a--shall ournmay--a--a--blessed 
areway eythay atthay allshay--they atthay--a--they atthay allshay ournmay, orfay eythay 
allshay--a--shall _atwhay_? Ywhay onday't youway elltay emay, Arymay?--what oday youway antway otay 
ebay osay eanmay orfay?" 

"Ohway, Omtay, youway oorpay ickthay-headed ingthay, Iway'm otnay easingtay youway. Iway ouldnway't 
oday atthay. Youway ustmay ogay andway earnlay itway againway. Onday't youway ebay iscouragedday, Omtay, 
youway'll anagemay itway--and ifway youway oday, Iway'll ivegay youway omethingsay everway osay icenay. 
Erethay, ownay, atthay's away oodgay oybay." 

"Allway ightray! Atwhay isway itway, Arymay, elltay emay atwhay itway isway." 

"Evernay youway indmay, Omtay. Youway owknay ifway Iway aysay itway's icenay, itway isway icenay." 

"Youway etbay youway atthay's osay, Arymay. Allway ightray, Iway'll ackletay itway againway." 

Andway ehay idday "ackletay itway againway"--and underway ethay oubleday essurepray ofway uriositycay 
andway ospectivepray aingay ehay idday itway ithway uchsay iritspay atthay ehay accomplishedway away 
iningshay uccesssay. Arymay avegay imhay away andbray-new "Arlowbay" ifeknay orthway elvetway 
andway away alfhay entscay; andway ethay onvulsioncay ofway elightday atthay eptsway ishay ystemsay 
ookshay imhay otay ishay oundationsfay. Uetray, ethay ifeknay ouldway otnay utcay anythingway, 
utbay itway asway away "uresay-enough" Arlowbay, andway erethay asway inconceivableway andeurgray 
inway atthay--though erewhay ethay Esternway oysbay everway otgay ethay ideaway atthay uchsay away 
eaponway ouldcay ossiblypay ebay ounterfeitedcay otay itsway injuryway isway anway imposingway 
ysterymay andway illway alwaysway emainray osay, erhapspay. Omtay ontrivedcay otay arifyscay ethay 
upboardcay ithway itway, andway asway arrangingway otay eginbay onway ethay ureaubay, enwhay ehay asway 
alledcay offway otay essdray orfay Undaysay-school. 

Arymay avegay imhay away intay asinbay ofway aterway andway away iecepay ofway oapsay, andway ehay entway 
outsideway ethay oorday andway etsay ethay asinbay onway away ittlelay enchbay erethay; enthay ehay 
ippedday ethay oapsay inway ethay aterway andway aidlay itway ownday; urnedtay upway ishay eevesslay; 
ouredpay outway ethay aterway onway ethay oundgray, entlygay, andway enthay enteredway ethay itchenkay 
andway eganbay otay ipeway ishay acefay iligentlyday onway ethay oweltay ehindbay ethay oorday. Utbay 
Arymay emovedray ethay oweltay andway aidsay: 

"Ownay ainway't youway ashamedway, Omtay. Youway ustnmay't ebay osay adbay. Aterway onway't urthay 
youway." 

Omtay asway away ifletray isconcertedday. Ethay asinbay asway efilledray, andway isthay imetay ehay 
oodstay overway itway away ittlelay ilewhay, atheringgay esolutionray; ooktay inway away igbay eathbray 
andway eganbay. Enwhay ehay enteredway ethay itchenkay esentlypray, ithway othbay eyesway utshay 
andway opinggray orfay ethay oweltay ithway ishay andshay, anway onorablehay estimonytay ofway 
udssay andway aterway asway ippingdray omfray ishay acefay. Utbay enwhay ehay emergedway omfray 
ethay oweltay, ehay asway otnay yetway atisfactorysay, orfay ethay eanclay erritorytay oppedstay 
ortshay atway ishay inchay andway ishay awsjay, ikelay away askmay; elowbay andway eyondbay isthay inelay 
erethay asway away arkday expanseway ofway unirrigatedway oilsay atthay eadspray ownwardday inway 
ontfray andway ackwardbay aroundway ishay ecknay. Arymay ooktay imhay inway andhay, andway enwhay eshay 
asway oneday ithway imhay ehay asway away anmay andway away otherbray, ithoutway istinctionday ofway 
olorcay, andway ishay aturatedsay airhay asway eatlynay ushedbray, andway itsway ortshay urlscay 
oughtwray intoway away aintyday andway ymmetricalsay eneralgay effectway. [Ehay ivatelypray 
oothedsmay outway ethay urlscay, ithway aborlay andway ifficultyday, andway asteredplay ishay 
airhay oseclay ownday otay ishay eadhay; orfay ehay eldhay urlscay otay ebay effeminateway, andway ishay 
ownway illedfay ishay ifelay ithway itternessbay.] Enthay Arymay otgay outway away uitsay ofway ishay 
othingclay atthay adhay eenbay usedway onlyway onway Undayssay uringday otway yearsway--they ereway 
implysay alledcay ishay "otherway othesclay"--and osay ybay atthay eway owknay ethay izesay ofway ishay 
ardrobeway. Ethay irlgay "utpay imhay otay ightsray" afterway ehay adhay esseddray imselfhay; 
eshay uttonedbay ishay eatnay oundaboutray upway otay ishay inchay, urnedtay ishay astvay irtshay 
ollarcay ownday overway ishay ouldersshay, ushedbray imhay offway andway ownedcray imhay ithway 
ishay eckledspay awstray athay. Ehay ownay ookedlay exceedinglyway improvedway andway 
uncomfortableway. Ehay asway ullyfay asway uncomfortableway asway ehay ookedlay; orfay erethay 
asway away estraintray aboutway olewhay othesclay andway eanlinessclay atthay alledgay imhay. Ehay 
opedhay atthay Arymay ouldway orgetfay ishay oesshay, utbay ethay opehay asway ightedblay; eshay 
oatedcay emthay oroughlythay ithway allowtay, asway asway ethay ustomcay, andway oughtbray 
emthay outway. Ehay ostlay ishay empertay andway aidsay ehay asway alwaysway eingbay ademay otay oday 
everythingway ehay idnday't antway otay oday. Utbay Arymay aidsay, ersuasivelypay: 

"Easeplay, Omtay--that's away oodgay oybay." 

Osay ehay otgay intoway ethay oesshay arlingsnay. Arymay asway oonsay eadyray, andway ethay eethray 
ildrenchay etsay outway orfay Undaysay-school--a aceplay atthay Omtay atedhay ithway ishay olewhay 
earthay; utbay Idsay andway Arymay ereway ondfay ofway itway. 

Abbathsay-school ourshay ereway omfray inenay otay alfhay-past entay; andway enthay urchchay 
ervicesay. Otway ofway ethay ildrenchay alwaysway emainedray orfay ethay ermonsay oluntarilyvay, 
andway ethay otherway alwaysway emainedray ootay--for ongerstray easonsray. Ethay urchchay's 
ighhay-backed, uncushionedway ewspay ouldway eatsay aboutway eethray undredhay ersonspay; 
ethay edificeway asway utbay away allsmay, ainplay affairway, ithway away ortsay ofway inepay oardbay 
eetray-box onway optay ofway itway orfay away eeplestay. Atway ethay oorday Omtay oppeddray ackbay away epstay 
andway accostedway away Undaysay-dressed omradecay: 

"Aysay, Illybay, otgay away yallerway ickettay?" 

"Yesway." 

"Atwhay'll youway aketay orfay erhay?" 

"Atwhay'll youway ivegay?" 

"Iecepay ofway ickrishlay andway away ishfay-hook." 

"Esslay eesay 'emway." 

Omtay exhibitedway. Eythay ereway atisfactorysay, andway ethay opertypray angedchay andshay. 
Enthay Omtay adedtray away ouplecay ofway itewhay alleysway orfay eethray edray icketstay, andway omesay 
allsmay ifletray orway otherway orfay away ouplecay ofway ueblay onesway. Ehay aylaidway otherway 
oysbay asway eythay amecay, andway entway onway uyingbay icketstay ofway ariousvay olorscay entay 
orway ifteenfay inutesmay ongerlay. Ehay enteredway ethay urchchay, ownay, ithway away armsway 
ofway eanclay andway oisynay oysbay andway irlsgay, oceededpray otay ishay eatsay andway artedstay 
away uarrelqay ithway ethay irstfay oybay atthay amecay andyhay. Ethay eachertay, away avegray, 
elderlyway anmay, interferedway; enthay urnedtay ishay ackbay away omentmay andway Omtay ulledpay away 
oybay's airhay inway ethay extnay enchbay, andway asway absorbedway inway ishay ookbay enwhay ethay oybay 
urnedtay aroundway; uckstay away inpay inway anotherway oybay, esentlypray, inway orderway otay earhay 
imhay aysay "Ouchway!" andway otgay away ewnay eprimandray omfray ishay eachertay. Omtay's olewhay 
assclay ereway ofway away atternpay--restless, oisynay, andway oublesometray. Enwhay eythay amecay 
otay eciteray eirthay essonslay, otnay oneway ofway emthay ewknay ishay ersesvay erfectlypay, utbay 
adhay otay ebay omptedpray allway alongway. Oweverhay, eythay orriedway oughthray, andway eachway 
otgay ishay ewardray--in allsmay ueblay icketstay, eachway ithway away assagepay ofway Ipturescray 
onway itway; eachway ueblay ickettay asway aypay orfay otway ersesvay ofway ethay ecitationray. Entay 
ueblay icketstay equalledway away edray oneway, andway ouldcay ebay exchangedway orfay itway; entay edray 
icketstay equalledway away yellowway oneway; orfay entay yellowway icketstay ethay uperintendentsay 
avegay away eryvay ainlyplay oundbay Iblebay (orthway ortyfay entscay inway osethay easyway 
imestay) otay ethay upilpay. Owhay anymay ofway ymay eadersray ouldway avehay ethay industryway andway 
applicationway otay emorizemay otway ousandthay ersesvay, evenway orfay away Oreday Iblebay? Andway 
yetway Arymay adhay acquiredway otway Iblesbay inway isthay ayway--it asway ethay atientpay orkway ofway 
otway yearsway--and away oybay ofway Ermangay arentagepay adhay onway ourfay orway ivefay. Ehay onceway 
ecitedray eethray ousandthay ersesvay ithoutway oppingstay; utbay ethay ainstray uponway ishay 
entalmay acultiesfay asway ootay eatgray, andway ehay asway ittlelay etterbay anthay anway idiotway 
omfray atthay ayday orthfay--a ievousgray isfortunemay orfay ethay oolschay, orfay onway eatgray 
occasionsway, eforebay ompanycay, ethay uperintendentsay (asway Omtay expressedway itway) 
adhay alwaysway ademay isthay oybay omecay outway andway "eadspray imselfhay." Onlyway ethay olderway 
upilspay anagedmay otay eepkay eirthay icketstay andway ickstay otay eirthay edioustay orkway 
onglay enoughway otay etgay away Iblebay, andway osay ethay eliveryday ofway oneway ofway esethay izespray 
asway away areray andway oteworthynay ircumstancecay; ethay uccessfulsay upilpay asway osay 
eatgray andway onspicuouscay orfay atthay ayday atthay onway ethay otspay everyway olarschay's 
earthay asway iredfay ithway away eshfray ambitionway atthay oftenway astedlay away ouplecay 
ofway eeksway. Itway isway ossiblepay atthay Omtay's entalmay omachstay adhay evernay eallyray 
ungeredhay orfay oneway ofway osethay izespray, utbay unquestionablyway ishay entireway eingbay 
adhay orfay anymay away ayday ongedlay orfay ethay oryglay andway ethay eclatway atthay amecay ithway itway. 

Inway ueday oursecay ethay uperintendentsay oodstay upway inway ontfray ofway ethay ulpitpay, ithway 
away osedclay ymnhay-book inway ishay andhay andway ishay orefingerfay insertedway etweenbay itsway 
eaveslay, andway ommandedcay attentionway. Enwhay away Undaysay-school uperintendentsay 
akesmay ishay ustomarycay ittlelay eechspay, away ymnhay-book inway ethay andhay isway asway 
ecessarynay asway isway ethay inevitableway eetshay ofway usicmay inway ethay andhay ofway away ingersay 
owhay andsstay orwardfay onway ethay atformplay andway ingssay away olosay atway away oncertcay--though 
ywhay, isway away ysterymay: orfay eithernay ethay ymnhay-book ornay ethay eetshay ofway usicmay 
isway everway eferredray otay ybay ethay ufferersay. Isthay uperintendentsay asway away imslay 
eaturecray ofway irtythay-five, ithway away andysay oateegay andway ortshay andysay airhay; ehay 
oreway away iffstay andingstay-collar osewhay upperway edgeway almostway eachedray ishay earsway 
andway osewhay arpshay ointspay urvedcay orwardfay abreastway ethay ornerscay ofway ishay outhmay--a 
encefay atthay ompelledcay away aightstray ookoutlay aheadway, andway away urningtay ofway ethay 
olewhay odybay enwhay away idesay iewvay asway equiredray; ishay inchay asway oppedpray onway away 
eadingspray avatcray ichwhay asway asway oadbray andway asway onglay asway away ankbay-note, andway adhay 
ingedfray endsway; ishay ootbay oestay ereway urnedtay arplyshay upway, inway ethay ashionfay 
ofway ethay ayday, ikelay eighslay-runners--an effectway atientlypay andway aboriouslylay 
oducedpray ybay ethay youngway enmay ybay ittingsay ithway eirthay oestay essedpray againstway away 
allway orfay ourshay ogethertay. Mray. Altersway asway eryvay earnestway ofway ienmay, andway eryvay 
inceresay andway onesthay atway earthay; andway ehay eldhay acredsay ingsthay andway acesplay 
inway uchsay everenceray, andway osay eparatedsay emthay omfray orldlyway attersmay, atthay 
unconsciouslyway otay imselfhay ishay Undaysay-school oicevay adhay acquiredway away eculiarpay 
intonationway ichwhay asway ollywhay absentway onway eekway-days. Ehay eganbay afterway isthay 
ashionfay: 

"Ownay, ildrenchay, Iway antway youway allway otay itsay upway ustjay asway aightstray andway ettypray asway 
youway ancay andway ivegay emay allway yourway attentionway orfay away inutemay orway otway. Erethay--that 
isway itway. Atthay isway ethay ayway oodgay ittlelay oysbay andway irlsgay ouldshay oday. Iway eesay oneway 
ittlelay irlgay owhay isway ookinglay outway ofway ethay indowway--I amway afraidway eshay inksthay Iway 
amway outway erethay omewheresay--perhaps upway inway oneway ofway ethay eestray akingmay away eechspay 
otay ethay ittlelay irdsbay. [Applausiveway ittertay.] Iway antway otay elltay youway owhay oodgay itway 
akesmay emay eelfay otay eesay osay anymay ightbray, eanclay ittlelay acesfay assembledway inway away 
aceplay ikelay isthay, earninglay otay oday ightray andway ebay oodgay." Andway osay orthfay andway osay 
onway. Itway isway otnay ecessarynay otay etsay ownday ethay estray ofway ethay orationway. Itway asway ofway away 
atternpay ichwhay oesday otnay aryvay, andway osay itway isway amiliarfay otay usway allway. 

Ethay atterlay irdthay ofway ethay eechspay asway arredmay ybay ethay esumptionray ofway ightsfay 
andway otherway ecreationsray amongway ertaincay ofway ethay adbay oysbay, andway ybay idgetingsfay 
andway isperingswhay atthay extendedway arfay andway ideway, ashingway evenway otay ethay asesbay ofway 
isolatedway andway incorruptibleway ocksray ikelay Idsay andway Arymay. Utbay ownay everyway oundsay 
easedcay uddenlysay, ithway ethay ubsidencesay ofway Mray. Altersway' oicevay, andway ethay 
onclusioncay ofway ethay eechspay asway eceivedray ithway away urstbay ofway ilentsay atitudegray. 

Away oodgay artpay ofway ethay isperingwhay adhay eenbay occasionedway ybay anway eventway ichwhay asway 
oremay orway esslay areray--the entranceway ofway isitorsvay: awyerlay Atcherthay, accompaniedway 
ybay away eryvay eeblefay andway agedway anmay; away inefay, ortlypay, iddlemay-aged entlemangay 
ithway ironway-gray airhay; andway away ignifiedday adylay owhay asway oubtlessday ethay atterlay's 
ifeway. Ethay adylay asway eadinglay away ildchay. Omtay adhay eenbay estlessray andway ullfay ofway 
afingschay andway epiningsray; onsciencecay-smitten, ootay--he ouldcay otnay eetmay Amyway 
Awrencelay's eyeway, ehay ouldcay otnay ookbray erhay ovinglay azegay. Utbay enwhay ehay awsay isthay 
allsmay ewcomernay ishay oulsay asway allway ablazeway ithway issblay inway away omentmay. Ethay extnay 
omentmay ehay asway "owingshay offway" ithway allway ishay ightmay--cuffing oysbay, ullingpay 
airhay, akingmay acesfay--in away ordway, usingway everyway artway atthay eemedsay ikelylay otay 
ascinatefay away irlgay andway inway erhay applauseway. Ishay exaltationway adhay utbay oneway 
alloyway--the emorymay ofway ishay umiliationhay inway isthay angelway's ardengay--and atthay 
ecordray inway andsay asway astfay ashingway outway, underway ethay avesway ofway appinesshay atthay 
ereway eepingsway overway itway ownay. 

Ethay isitorsvay ereway ivengay ethay ighesthay eatsay ofway onorhay, andway asway oonsay asway Mray. 
Altersway' eechspay asway inishedfay, ehay introducedway emthay otay ethay oolschay. Ethay 
iddlemay-aged anmay urnedtay outway otay ebay away odigiouspray ersonagepay--no esslay away oneway 
anthay ethay ountycay udgejay--altogether ethay ostmay augustway eationcray esethay ildrenchay 
adhay everway ookedlay uponway--and eythay onderedway atwhay indkay ofway aterialmay ehay asway ademay 
ofway--and eythay alfhay antedway otay earhay imhay oarray, andway ereway alfhay afraidway ehay ightmay, 
ootay. Ehay asway omfray Onstantinoplecay, elvetway ilesmay awayway--so ehay adhay avelledtray, 
andway eensay ethay orldway--these eryvay eyesway adhay ookedlay uponway ethay ountycay 
ourtcay-house--which asway aidsay otay avehay away intay oofray. Ethay aweway ichwhay esethay 
eflectionsray inspiredway asway attestedway ybay ethay impressiveway ilencesay andway ethay 
anksray ofway aringstay eyesway. Isthay asway ethay eatgray Udgejay Atcherthay, otherbray ofway 
eirthay ownway awyerlay. Effjay Atcherthay immediatelyway entway orwardfay, otay ebay amiliarfay 
ithway ethay eatgray anmay andway ebay enviedway ybay ethay oolschay. Itway ouldway avehay eenbay usicmay 
otay ishay oulsay otay earhay ethay isperingswhay: 

"Ooklay atway imhay, Imjay! Ehay's away oinggay upway erethay. Aysay--look! ehay's away oinggay otay 
akeshay andshay ithway imhay--he _isway_ akingshay andshay ithway imhay! Ybay ingsjay, onday't youway 
ishway youway asway Effjay?" 

Mray. Altersway ellfay otay "owingshay offway," ithway allway ortssay ofway officialway ustlingsbay 
andway activitiesway, ivinggay ordersway, eliveringday udgmentsjay, ischargingday 
irectionsday erehay, erethay, everywhereway atthay ehay ouldcay indfay away argettay. Ethay 
ibrarianlay "owedshay offway"--running itherhay andway itherthay ithway ishay armsway ullfay ofway 
ooksbay andway akingmay away ealday ofway ethay uttersplay andway ussfay atthay insectway authorityway 
elightsday inway. Ethay youngway adylay eacherstay "owedshay offway"--bending eetlysway overway 
upilspay atthay ereway atelylay eingbay oxedbay, iftinglay ettypray arningway ingersfay 
atway adbay ittlelay oysbay andway attingpay oodgay onesway ovinglylay. Ethay youngway entlemengay 
eacherstay "owedshay offway" ithway allsmay oldingsscay andway otherway ittlelay isplaysday ofway 
authorityway andway inefay attentionway otay isciplineday--and ostmay ofway ethay eacherstay, ofway 
othbay exessay, oundfay usinessbay upway atway ethay ibrarylay, ybay ethay ulpitpay; andway itway asway 
usinessbay atthay equentlyfray adhay otay ebay oneday overway againway otway orway eethray imestay 
(ithway uchmay eemingsay exationvay). Ethay ittlelay irlsgay "owedshay offway" inway ariousvay 
aysway, andway ethay ittlelay oysbay "owedshay offway" ithway uchsay iligenceday atthay ethay airway 
asway ickthay ithway aperpay adsway andway ethay urmurmay ofway ufflingsscay. Andway aboveway itway 
allway ethay eatgray anmay atsay andway eamedbay away ajesticmay udicialjay ilesmay uponway allway 
ethay ousehay, andway armedway imselfhay inway ethay unsay ofway ishay ownway andeurgray--for ehay asway 
"owingshay offway," ootay. 

Erethay asway onlyway oneway ingthay antingway otay akemay Mray. Altersway' ecstasyway ompletecay, 
andway atthay asway away ancechay otay eliverday away Iblebay-prize andway exhibitway away odigypray. 
Everalsay upilspay adhay away ewfay yellowway icketstay, utbay onenay adhay enoughway--he adhay eenbay 
aroundway amongway ethay arstay upilspay inquiringway. Ehay ouldway avehay ivengay orldsway, ownay, 
otay avehay atthay Ermangay adlay ackbay againway ithway away oundsay indmay. 

Andway ownay atway isthay omentmay, enwhay opehay asway eadday, Omtay Awyersay amecay orwardfay ithway 
inenay yellowway icketstay, inenay edray icketstay, andway entay ueblay onesway, andway emandedday 
away Iblebay. Isthay asway away underboltthay outway ofway away earclay yskay. Altersway asway otnay 
expectingway anway applicationway omfray isthay ourcesay orfay ethay extnay entay yearsway. Utbay 
erethay asway onay ettinggay aroundway itway--here ereway ethay ertifiedcay eckschay, andway eythay 
ereway oodgay orfay eirthay acefay. Omtay asway ereforethay elevatedway otay away aceplay ithway 
ethay Udgejay andway ethay otherway electway, andway ethay eatgray ewsnay asway announcedway omfray 
eadquartershay. Itway asway ethay ostmay unningstay urprisesay ofway ethay ecadeday, andway 
osay ofoundpray asway ethay ensationsay atthay itway iftedlay ethay ewnay erohay upway otay ethay 
udicialjay oneway's altitudeway, andway ethay oolschay adhay otway arvelsmay otay azegay uponway 
inway aceplay ofway oneway. Ethay oysbay ereway allway eatenway upway ithway envyway--but osethay atthay 
ufferedsay ethay itterestbay angspay ereway osethay owhay erceivedpay ootay atelay atthay eythay 
emselvesthay adhay ontributedcay otay isthay atedhay endorsplay ybay adingtray icketstay otay 
Omtay orfay ethay ealthway ehay adhay amassedway inway ellingsay itewashingwhay ivilegespray. 
Esethay espisedday emselvesthay, asway eingbay ethay upesday ofway away ilyway audfray, away 
uilefulgay akesnay inway ethay assgray. 

Ethay izepray asway eliveredday otay Omtay ithway asway uchmay effusionway asway ethay 
uperintendentsay ouldcay umppay upway underway ethay ircumstancescay; utbay itway ackedlay 
omewhatsay ofway ethay uetray ushgay, orfay ethay oorpay ellowfay's instinctway aughttay imhay 
atthay erethay asway away ysterymay erehay atthay ouldcay otnay ellway earbay ethay ightlay, 
erhapspay; itway asway implysay eposterouspray atthay isthay oybay adhay arehousedway otway 
ousandthay eavesshay ofway Ipturalscray isdomway onway ishay emisespray--a ozenday ouldway 
ainstray ishay apacitycay, ithoutway away oubtday. 

Amyway Awrencelay asway oudpray andway adglay, andway eshay iedtray otay akemay Omtay eesay itway inway 
erhay acefay--but ehay ouldnway't ooklay. Eshay onderedway; enthay eshay asway ustjay away aingray 
oubledtray; extnay away imday uspicionsay amecay andway entway--came againway; eshay atchedway; 
away urtivefay anceglay oldtay erhay orldsway--and enthay erhay earthay okebray, andway eshay asway 
ealousjay, andway angryway, andway ethay earstay amecay andway eshay atedhay everybodyway. Omtay ostmay 
ofway allway (eshay oughtthay). 

Omtay asway introducedway otay ethay Udgejay; utbay ishay onguetay asway iedtay, ishay eathbray 
ouldway ardlyhay omecay, ishay earthay uakedqay--partly ecausebay ofway ethay awfulway 
eatnessgray ofway ethay anmay, utbay ainlymay ecausebay ehay asway erhay arentpay. Ehay ouldway 
avehay ikedlay otay allfay ownday andway orshipway imhay, ifway itway ereway inway ethay arkday. Ethay 
Udgejay utpay ishay andhay onway Omtay's eadhay andway alledcay imhay away inefay ittlelay anmay, andway 
askedway imhay atwhay ishay amenay asway. Ethay oybay ammeredstay, aspedgay, andway otgay itway outway: 

"Omtay." 

"Ohway, onay, otnay Omtay--it isway--" 

"Omasthay." 

"Ahway, atthay's itway. Iway oughtthay erethay asway oremay otay itway, aybemay. Atthay's eryvay ellway. 
Utbay youway've anotherway oneway Iway aresayday, andway youway'll elltay itway otay emay, onway't youway?" 

"Elltay ethay entlemangay yourway otherway amenay, Omasthay," aidsay Altersway, "andway aysay 
irsay. Youway ustnmay't orgetfay yourway annersmay." 

"Omasthay Awyersay--sir." 

"Atthay's itway! Atthay's away oodgay oybay. Inefay oybay. Inefay, anlymay ittlelay ellowfay. Otway 
ousandthay ersesvay isway away eatgray anymay--very, eryvay eatgray anymay. Andway youway evernay ancay 
ebay orrysay orfay ethay oubletray youway ooktay otay earnlay emthay; orfay owledgeknay isway orthway 
oremay anthay anythingway erethay isway inway ethay orldway; itway's atwhay akesmay eatgray enmay 
andway oodgay enmay; youway'll ebay away eatgray anmay andway away oodgay anmay yourselfway, omesay 
ayday, Omasthay, andway enthay youway'll ooklay ackbay andway aysay, Itway's allway owingway otay ethay 
eciouspray Undaysay-school ivilegespray ofway ymay oyhoodbay--it's allway owingway otay 
ymay earday eacherstay atthay aughttay emay otay earnlay--it's allway owingway otay ethay oodgay 
uperintendentsay, owhay encouragedway emay, andway atchedway overway emay, andway avegay emay away 
eautifulbay Iblebay--a endidsplay elegantway Iblebay--to eepkay andway avehay itway allway orfay ymay 
ownway, alwaysway--it's allway owingway otay ightray ingingbray upway! Atthay isway atwhay youway illway 
aysay, Omasthay--and youway ouldnway't aketay anyway oneymay orfay osethay otway ousandthay 
ersesvay--no indeedway youway ouldnway't. Andway ownay youway ouldnway't indmay ellingtay emay andway 
isthay adylay omesay ofway ethay ingsthay youway've earnedlay--no, Iway owknay youway ouldnway't--for 
eway areway oudpray ofway ittlelay oysbay atthay earnlay. Ownay, onay oubtday youway owknay ethay amesnay 
ofway allway ethay elvetway isciplesday. Onway't youway elltay usway ethay amesnay ofway ethay irstfay 
otway atthay ereway appointedway?" 

Omtay asway uggingtay atway away uttonbay-hole andway ookinglay eepishshay. Ehay ushedblay, 
ownay, andway ishay eyesway ellfay. Mray. Altersway' earthay anksay ithinway imhay. Ehay aidsay 
otay imselfhay, itway isway otnay ossiblepay atthay ethay oybay ancay answerway ethay implestsay
