uestionqay--why _idday_ ethay Udgejay askway imhay? Yetway ehay eltfay obligedway otay eakspay upway 
andway aysay: 

"Answerway ethay entlemangay, Omasthay--don't ebay afraidway." 

Omtay illstay unghay irefay. 

"Ownay Iway owknay youway'll elltay emay," aidsay ethay adylay. "Ethay amesnay ofway ethay irstfay otway 
isciplesday ereway--" 

"_Avidday Andway Oliahgay!_" 

Etlay usway awdray ethay urtaincay ofway aritychay overway ethay estray ofway ethay enescay. 




APTERCHAY Vway 

ABOUTWAY alfhay-past entay ethay ackedcray ellbay ofway ethay allsmay urchchay eganbay otay ingray, 
andway esentlypray ethay eoplepay eganbay otay athergay orfay ethay orningmay ermonsay. Ethay 
Undaysay-school ildrenchay istributedday emselvesthay aboutway ethay ousehay andway 
occupiedway ewspay ithway eirthay arentspay, osay asway otay ebay underway upervisionsay. Auntway 
Ollypay amecay, andway Omtay andway Idsay andway Arymay atsay ithway erhay--Tom eingbay acedplay extnay 
ethay aisleway, inway orderway atthay ehay ightmay ebay asway arfay awayway omfray ethay openway indowway 
andway ethay eductivesay outsideway ummersay enesscay asway ossiblepay. Ethay owdcray iledfay upway 
ethay aislesway: ethay agedway andway eedynay ostmasterpay, owhay adhay eensay etterbay aysday; 
ethay ayormay andway ishay ifeway--for eythay adhay away ayormay erethay, amongway otherway 
unnecessariesway; ethay usticejay ofway ethay eacepay; ethay idowway Ouglassday, airfay, 
artsmay, andway ortyfay, away enerousgay, oodgay-hearted oulsay andway ellway-to-do, erhay illhay 
ansionmay ethay onlyway alacepay inway ethay owntay, andway ethay ostmay ospitablehay andway uchmay 
ethay ostmay avishlay inway ethay attermay ofway estivitiesfay atthay Stay. Etersburgpay ouldcay 
oastbay; ethay entbay andway enerablevay Ajormay andway Mrsay. Ardway; awyerlay Iversonray, ethay 
ewnay otablenay omfray away istanceday; extnay ethay ellebay ofway ethay illagevay, ollowedfay ybay 
away ooptray ofway awnlay-clad andway ibbonray-decked youngway earthay-breakers; enthay allway 
ethay youngway erksclay inway owntay inway away odybay--for eythay adhay oodstay inway ethay estibulevay 
uckingsay eirthay anecay-heads, away irclingcay allway ofway oiledway andway imperingsay 
admirersway, illtay ethay astlay irlgay adhay unray eirthay antletgay; andway astlay ofway allway amecay 
ethay Odelmay Oybay, Illieway Uffersonmay, akingtay asway eedfulhay arecay ofway ishay othermay asway 
ifway eshay ereway utcay assglay. Ehay alwaysway oughtbray ishay othermay otay urchchay, andway asway 
ethay idepray ofway allway ethay atronsmay. Ethay oysbay allway atedhay imhay, ehay asway osay 
oodgay. Andway esidesbay, ehay adhay eenbay "ownthray upway otay emthay" osay uchmay. Ishay 
itewhay andkerchiefhay asway anginghay outway ofway ishay ocketpay ehindbay, asway usualway onway 
Undayssay--accidentally. Omtay adhay onay andkerchiefhay, andway ehay ookedlay uponway oysbay 
owhay adhay asway obssnay. 

Ethay ongregationcay eingbay ullyfay assembledway, ownay, ethay ellbay angray onceway oremay, 
otay arnway aggardslay andway agglersstray, andway enthay away olemnsay ushhay ellfay uponway ethay 
urchchay ichwhay asway onlyway okenbray ybay ethay itteringtay andway isperingwhay ofway ethay 
oirchay inway ethay allerygay. Ethay oirchay alwaysway itteredtay andway isperedwhay allway 
oughthray ervicesay. Erethay asway onceway away urchchay oirchay atthay asway otnay illway-bred, 
utbay Iway avehay orgottenfay erewhay itway asway, ownay. Itway asway away eatgray anymay yearsway agoway, 
andway Iway ancay arcelyscay ememberray anythingway aboutway itway, utbay Iway inkthay itway asway inway 
omesay oreignfay ountrycay. 

Ethay inistermay avegay outway ethay ymnhay, andway eadray itway oughthray ithway away elishray, inway away 
eculiarpay ylestay ichwhay asway uchmay admiredway inway atthay artpay ofway ethay ountrycay. Ishay 
oicevay eganbay onway away ediummay eykay andway imbedclay eadilystay upway illtay itway eachedray away 
ertaincay ointpay, erewhay itway orebay ithway ongstray emphasisway uponway ethay opmosttay ordway 
andway enthay ungedplay ownday asway ifway omfray away ingspray-board: 

Allshay Iway ebay arcay-ri-ed oetay ethay iesskay, onway owflay'ry _edsbay_ ofway easeway, 

Ilstwhay othersway ightfay otay inway ethay izepray, andway ailsay othray' _oodblay_-y eassay? 

Ehay asway egardedray asway away onderfulway eaderray. Atway urchchay "ociablessay" ehay asway 
alwaysway alledcay uponway otay eadray oetrypay; andway enwhay ehay asway oughthray, ethay adieslay 
ouldway iftlay upway eirthay andshay andway etlay emthay allfay elplesslyhay inway eirthay apslay, 
andway "allway" eirthay eyesway, andway akeshay eirthay eadshay, asway uchmay asway otay aysay, "Ordsway 
annotcay expressway itway; itway isway ootay eautifulbay, OOTAY eautifulbay orfay isthay ortalmay 
earthway." 

Afterway ethay ymnhay adhay eenbay ungsay, ethay Evray. Mray. Aguespray urnedtay imselfhay intoway 
away ulletinbay-board, andway eadray offway "oticesnay" ofway eetingsmay andway ocietiessay andway 
ingsthay illtay itway eemedsay atthay ethay istlay ouldway etchstray outway otay ethay ackcray ofway 
oomday--a ueerqay ustomcay ichwhay isway illstay eptkay upway inway Americaway, evenway inway itiescay, 
awayway erehay inway isthay ageway ofway abundantway ewspapersnay. Oftenway, ethay esslay erethay isway 
otay ustifyjay away aditionaltray ustomcay, ethay arderhay itway isway otay etgay idray ofway itway. 

Andway ownay ethay inistermay ayedpray. Away oodgay, enerousgay ayerpray itway asway, andway entway 
intoway etailsday: itway eadedplay orfay ethay urchchay, andway ethay ittlelay ildrenchay ofway ethay 
urchchay; orfay ethay otherway urcheschay ofway ethay illagevay; orfay ethay illagevay itselfway; 
orfay ethay ountycay; orfay ethay Atestay; orfay ethay Atestay officersway; orfay ethay Unitedway 
Atesstay; orfay ethay urcheschay ofway ethay Unitedway Atesstay; orfay Ongresscay; orfay ethay 
Esidentpray; orfay ethay officersway ofway ethay Overnmentgay; orfay oorpay ailorssay, ossedtay 
ybay ormystay eassay; orfay ethay oppressedway illionsmay oaninggray underway ethay eelhay ofway 
Europeanway onarchiesmay andway Orientalway espotismsday; orfay uchsay asway avehay ethay ightlay 
andway ethay oodgay idingstay, andway yetway avehay otnay eyesway otay eesay ornay earsway otay earhay 
ithalway; orfay ethay eathenhay inway ethay arfay islandsway ofway ethay easay; andway osedclay ithway 
away upplicationsay atthay ethay ordsway ehay asway aboutway otay eakspay ightmay indfay acegray 
andway avorfay, andway ebay asway eedsay ownsay inway ertilefay oundgray, yieldingway inway imetay away 
atefulgray arvesthay ofway oodgay. Amenway. 

Erethay asway away ustlingray ofway essesdray, andway ethay andingstay ongregationcay atsay ownday. 
Ethay oybay osewhay istoryhay isthay ookbay elatesray idday otnay enjoyway ethay ayerpray, ehay 
onlyway enduredway itway--if ehay evenway idday atthay uchmay. Ehay asway estiveray allway oughthray itway; 
ehay eptkay allytay ofway ethay etailsday ofway ethay ayerpray, unconsciouslyway--for ehay asway otnay 
isteninglay, utbay ehay ewknay ethay oundgray ofway oldway, andway ethay ergymanclay's egularray 
outeray overway itway--and enwhay away ittlelay ifletray ofway ewnay attermay asway interlardedway, 
ishay earway etectedday itway andway ishay olewhay aturenay esentedray itway; ehay onsideredcay 
additionsway unfairway, andway oundrellyscay. Inway ethay idstmay ofway ethay ayerpray away yflay adhay 
itlay onway ethay ackbay ofway ethay ewpay inway ontfray ofway imhay andway orturedtay ishay iritspay ybay 
almlycay ubbingray itsway andshay ogethertay, embracingway itsway eadhay ithway itsway armsway, andway 
olishingpay itway osay igorouslyvay atthay itway eemedsay otay almostway artpay ompanycay ithway 
ethay odybay, andway ethay enderslay eadthray ofway away ecknay asway exposedway otay iewvay; apingscray 
itsway ingsway ithway itsway indhay egslay andway oothingsmay emthay otay itsway odybay asway ifway eythay 
adhay eenbay oatcay-tails; oinggay oughthray itsway olewhay oilettay asway anquillytray asway ifway 
itway ewknay itway asway erfectlypay afesay. Asway indeedway itway asway; orfay asway orelysay asway Omtay's 
andshay itchedway otay abgray orfay itway eythay idday otnay areday--he elievedbay ishay oulsay ouldway 
ebay instantlyway estroyedday ifway ehay idday uchsay away ingthay ilewhay ethay ayerpray asway oinggay 
onway. Utbay ithway ethay osingclay entencesay ishay andhay eganbay otay urvecay andway ealstay 
orwardfay; andway ethay instantway ethay "Amenway" asway outway ethay yflay asway away isonerpray ofway 
arway. Ishay auntway etectedday ethay actway andway ademay imhay etlay itway ogay. 

Ethay inistermay avegay outway ishay exttay andway oneddray alongway onotonouslymay oughthray anway 
argumentway atthay asway osay osypray atthay anymay away eadhay ybay andway ybay eganbay otay odnay--and 
yetway itway asway anway argumentway atthay ealtday inway imitlesslay irefay andway imstonebray andway 
innedthay ethay edestinedpray electway ownday otay away ompanycay osay allsmay asway otay ebay ardlyhay 
orthway ethay avingsay. Omtay ountedcay ethay agespay ofway ethay ermonsay; afterway urchchay ehay 
alwaysway ewknay owhay anymay agespay erethay adhay eenbay, utbay ehay eldomsay ewknay anythingway 
elseway aboutway ethay iscourseday. Oweverhay, isthay imetay ehay asway eallyray interestedway 
orfay away ittlelay ilewhay. Ethay inistermay ademay away andgray andway ovingmay icturepay ofway ethay 
assemblingway ogethertay ofway ethay orldway's ostshay atway ethay illenniummay enwhay ethay ionlay 
andway ethay amblay ouldshay ielay ownday ogethertay andway away ittlelay ildchay ouldshay eadlay 
emthay. Utbay ethay athospay, ethay essonlay, ethay oralmay ofway ethay eatgray ectaclespay 
ereway ostlay uponway ethay oybay; ehay onlyway oughtthay ofway ethay onspicuousnesscay ofway ethay 
incipalpray aracterchay eforebay ethay onway-looking ationsnay; ishay acefay itlay ithway ethay 
oughtthay, andway ehay aidsay otay imselfhay atthay ehay ishedway ehay ouldcay ebay atthay ildchay, 
ifway itway asway away ametay ionlay. 

Ownay ehay apsedlay intoway ufferingsay againway, asway ethay ydray argumentway asway esumedray. 
Esentlypray ehay ethoughtbay imhay ofway away easuretray ehay adhay andway otgay itway outway. Itway asway 
away argelay ackblay eetlebay ithway ormidablefay awsjay--a "inchbugpay," ehay alledcay itway. Itway 
asway inway away ercussionpay-cap oxbay. Ethay irstfay ingthay ethay eetlebay idday asway otay 
aketay imhay ybay ethay ingerfay. Away aturalnay illipfay ollowedfay, ethay eetlebay entway 
ounderingflay intoway ethay aisleway andway itlay onway itsway ackbay, andway ethay urthay ingerfay entway 
intoway ethay oybay's outhmay. Ethay eetlebay aylay erethay orkingway itsway elplesshay egslay, 
unableway otay urntay overway. Omtay eyedway itway, andway ongedlay orfay itway; utbay itway asway afesay outway 
ofway ishay eachray. Otherway eoplepay uninterestedway inway ethay ermonsay oundfay eliefray inway 
ethay eetlebay, andway eythay eyedway itway ootay. Esentlypray away agrantvay oodlepay ogday amecay 
idlingway alongway, adsay atway earthay, azylay ithway ethay ummersay oftnesssay andway ethay 
uietqay, earyway ofway aptivitycay, ighingsay orfay angechay. Ehay iedspay ethay eetlebay; ethay 
oopingdray ailtay iftedlay andway aggedway. Ehay urveyedsay ethay izepray; alkedway aroundway 
itway; eltsmay atway itway omfray away afesay istanceday; alkedway aroundway itway againway; ewgray 
olderbay, andway ooktay away oserclay ellsmay; enthay iftedlay ishay iplay andway ademay away ingerlygay 
atchsnay atway itway, ustjay issingmay itway; ademay anotherway, andway anotherway; eganbay otay enjoyway 
ethay iversionday; ubsidedsay otay ishay omachstay ithway ethay eetlebay etweenbay ishay awspay, 
andway ontinuedcay ishay experimentsway; ewgray earyway atway astlay, andway enthay indifferentway 
andway absentway-minded. Ishay eadhay oddednay, andway ittlelay ybay ittlelay ishay inchay 
escendedday andway ouchedtay ethay enemyway, owhay eizedsay itway. Erethay asway away arpshay yelpway, 
away irtflay ofway ethay oodlepay's eadhay, andway ethay eetlebay ellfay away ouplecay ofway yardsway 
awayway, andway itlay onway itsway ackbay onceway oremay. Ethay eighboringnay ectatorsspay 
ookshay ithway away entlegay inwardway oyjay, everalsay acesfay entway ehindbay ansfay andway 
andhay-kerchiefs, andway Omtay asway entirelyway appyhay. Ethay ogday ookedlay oolishfay, 
andway obablypray eltfay osay; utbay erethay asway esentmentray inway ishay earthay, ootay, andway away 
avingcray orfay evengeray. Osay ehay entway otay ethay eetlebay andway eganbay away aryway attackway onway 
itway againway; umpingjay atway itway omfray everyway ointpay ofway away irclecay, ightinglay ithway ishay 
orefay-paws ithinway anway inchway ofway ethay eaturecray, akingmay evenway oserclay atchessnay atway 
itway ithway ishay eethtay, andway erkingjay ishay eadhay illtay ishay earsway appedflay againway. Utbay 
ehay ewgray iredtay onceway oremay, afterway away ilewhay; iedtray otay amuseway imselfhay ithway away 
yflay utbay oundfay onay eliefray; ollowedfay anway antway aroundway, ithway ishay osenay oseclay 
otay ethay oorflay, andway uicklyqay eariedway ofway atthay; yawnedway, ighedsay, orgotfay ethay 
eetlebay entirelyway, andway atsay ownday onway itway. Enthay erethay asway away ildway yelpway ofway agonyway 
andway ethay oodlepay entway ailingsay upway ethay aisleway; ethay yelpsway ontinuedcay, andway osay 
idday ethay ogday; ehay ossedcray ethay ousehay inway ontfray ofway ethay altarway; ehay ewflay 
ownday ethay otherway aisleway; ehay ossedcray eforebay ethay oorsday; ehay amoredclay upway ethay 
omehay-stretch; ishay anguishway ewgray ithway ishay ogresspray, illtay esentlypray ehay asway 
utbay away oollyway ometcay ovingmay inway itsway orbitway ithway ethay eamglay andway ethay eedspay ofway 
ightlay. Atway astlay ethay anticfray ufferersay eeredshay omfray itsway oursecay, andway angspray 
intoway itsway astermay's aplay; ehay ungflay itway outway ofway ethay indowway, andway ethay oicevay ofway 
istressday uicklyqay innedthay awayway andway iedday inway ethay istanceday. 

Ybay isthay imetay ethay olewhay urchchay asway edray-faced andway uffocatingsay ithway 
uppressedsay aughterlay, andway ethay ermonsay adhay omecay otay away eadday andstillstay. 
Ethay iscourseday asway esumedray esentlypray, utbay itway entway amelay andway altinghay, allway 
ossibilitypay ofway impressivenessway eingbay atway anway endway; orfay evenway ethay avestgray 
entimentssay ereway onstantlycay eingbay eceivedray ithway away otheredsmay urstbay ofway 
unholyway irthmay, underway overcay ofway omesay emoteray ewpay-back, asway ifway ethay oorpay arsonpay 
adhay aidsay away arelyray acetiousfay ingthay. Itway asway away enuinegay eliefray otay ethay olewhay 
ongregationcay enwhay ethay ordealway asway overway andway ethay enedictionbay onouncedpray. 

Omtay Awyersay entway omehay uiteqay eerfulchay, inkingthay otay imselfhay atthay erethay asway 
omesay atisfactionsay aboutway ivineday ervicesay enwhay erethay asway away itbay ofway arietyvay 
inway itway. Ehay adhay utbay oneway arringmay oughtthay; ehay asway illingway atthay ethay ogday 
ouldshay ayplay ithway ishay inchbugpay, utbay ehay idday otnay inkthay itway asway uprightway inway 
imhay otay arrycay itway offway. 




APTERCHAY IVAY 

ONDAYMAY orningmay oundfay Omtay Awyersay iserablemay. Ondaymay orningmay alwaysway oundfay 
imhay osay--because itway eganbay anotherway eekway's owslay ufferingsay inway oolschay. Ehay 
enerallygay eganbay atthay ayday ithway ishingway ehay adhay adhay onay interveningway olidayhay, 
itway ademay ethay oinggay intoway aptivitycay andway ettersfay againway osay uchmay oremay odiousway. 

Omtay aylay inkingthay. Esentlypray itway occurredway otay imhay atthay ehay ishedway ehay asway 
icksay; enthay ehay ouldcay aystay omehay omfray oolschay. Erehay asway away aguevay ossibilitypay. 
Ehay anvassedcay ishay ystemsay. Onay ailmentway asway oundfay, andway ehay investigatedway 
againway. Isthay imetay ehay oughtthay ehay ouldcay etectday olickycay ymptomssay, andway ehay 
eganbay otay encourageway emthay ithway onsiderablecay opehay. Utbay eythay oonsay ewgray 
eeblefay, andway esentlypray iedday ollywhay awayway. Ehay eflectedray urtherfay. Uddenlysay 
ehay iscoveredday omethingsay. Oneway ofway ishay upperway ontfray eethtay asway ooselay. Isthay 
asway uckylay; ehay asway aboutway otay eginbay otay oangray, asway away "arterstay," asway ehay 
alledcay itway, enwhay itway occurredway otay imhay atthay ifway ehay amecay intoway ourtcay ithway atthay 
argumentway, ishay auntway ouldway ullpay itway outway, andway atthay ouldway urthay. Osay ehay oughtthay 
ehay ouldway oldhay ethay oothtay inway eserveray orfay ethay esentpray, andway eeksay urtherfay. 
Othingnay offeredway orfay omesay ittlelay imetay, andway enthay ehay ememberedray earinghay 
ethay octorday elltay aboutway away ertaincay ingthay atthay aidlay upway away atientpay orfay otway orway 
eethray eeksway andway eatenedthray otay akemay imhay oselay away ingerfay. Osay ethay oybay eagerlyway 
ewdray ishay oresay oetay omfray underway ethay eetshay andway eldhay itway upway orfay inspectionway. 
Utbay ownay ehay idday otnay owknay ethay ecessarynay ymptomssay. Oweverhay, itway eemedsay 
ellway orthway ilewhay otay ancechay itway, osay ehay ellfay otay oaninggray ithway onsiderablecay 
iritspay. 

Utbay Idsay eptslay onway unconsciousway. 

Omtay oanedgray ouderlay, andway anciedfay atthay ehay eganbay otay eelfay ainpay inway ethay oetay. 

Onay esultray omfray Idsay. 

Omtay asway antingpay ithway ishay exertionsway ybay isthay imetay. Ehay ooktay away estray andway enthay 
elledsway imselfhay upway andway etchedfay away uccessionsay ofway admirableway oansgray. 

Idsay oredsnay onway. 

Omtay asway aggravatedway. Ehay aidsay, "Idsay, Idsay!" andway ookshay imhay. Isthay oursecay 
orkedway ellway, andway Omtay eganbay otay oangray againway. Idsay yawnedway, etchedstray, enthay 
oughtbray imselfhay upway onway ishay elbowway ithway away ortsnay, andway eganbay otay arestay atway Omtay. 
Omtay entway onway oaninggray. Idsay aidsay: 

"Omtay! Aysay, Omtay!" [Onay esponseray.] "Erehay, Omtay! OMTAY! Atwhay isway ethay attermay, 
Omtay?" Andway ehay ookshay imhay andway ookedlay inway ishay acefay anxiouslyway. 

Omtay oanedmay outway: 

"Ohway, onday't, Idsay. Onday't ogglejay emay." 

"Ywhay, atwhay's ethay attermay, Omtay? Iway ustmay allcay auntieway." 

"Onay--never indmay. Itway'll ebay overway ybay andway ybay, aybemay. Onday't allcay anybodyway." 

"Utbay Iway ustmay! _Onday't_ oangray osay, Omtay, itway's awfulway. Owhay onglay youway eenbay isthay 
ayway?" 

"Ourshay. Ouchway! Ohway, onday't irstay osay, Idsay, youway'll illkay emay." 

"Omtay, ywhay idnday't youway akeway emay oonersay? Ohway, Omtay, _onday't!_ Itway akesmay ymay eshflay 
awlcray otay earhay youway. Omtay, atwhay isway ethay attermay?" 

"Iway orgivefay youway everythingway, Idsay. [Oangray.] Everythingway youway've everway oneday otay 
emay. Enwhay Iway'm onegay--" 

"Ohway, Omtay, youway ainway't yingday, areway youway? Onday't, Omtay--oh, onday't. Aybemay--" 

"Iway orgivefay everybodyway, Idsay. [Oangray.] Elltay 'emway osay, Idsay. Andway Idsay, youway ivegay 
ymay indowway-sash andway ymay atcay ithway oneway eyeway otay atthay ewnay irlgay atthay's omecay otay 
owntay, andway elltay erhay--" 

Utbay Idsay adhay atchedsnay ishay othesclay andway onegay. Omtay asway ufferingsay inway ealityray, 
ownay, osay andsomelyhay asway ishay imaginationway orkingway, andway osay ishay oansgray adhay 
atheredgay uiteqay away enuinegay onetay. 

Idsay ewflay ownstairsday andway aidsay: 

"Ohway, Auntway Ollypay, omecay! Omtay's yingday!" 

"Yingday!" 

"Yesway'm. Onday't aitway--come uickqay!" 

"Ubbageray! Iway onday't elievebay itway!" 

Utbay eshay edflay upstairsway, everthelessnay, ithway Idsay andway Arymay atway erhay eelshay. 
Andway erhay acefay ewgray itewhay, ootay, andway erhay iplay embledtray. Enwhay eshay eachedray ethay 
edsidebay eshay aspedgay outway: 

"Youway, Omtay! Omtay, atwhay's ethay attermay ithway youway?" 

"Ohway, auntieway, Iway'm--" 

"Atwhay's ethay attermay ithway youway--what isway ethay attermay ithway youway, ildchay?" 

"Ohway, auntieway, ymay oresay oetay's ortifiedmay!" 

Ethay oldway adylay anksay ownday intoway away airchay andway aughedlay away ittlelay, enthay iedcray away 
ittlelay, enthay idday othbay ogethertay. Isthay estoredray erhay andway eshay aidsay: 

"Omtay, atwhay away urntay youway idday ivegay emay. Ownay youway utshay upway atthay onsensenay andway 
imbclay outway ofway isthay." 

Ethay oansgray easedcay andway ethay ainpay anishedvay omfray ethay oetay. Ethay oybay eltfay away 
ittlelay oolishfay, andway ehay aidsay: 

"Auntway Ollypay, itway _eemedsay_ ortifiedmay, andway itway urthay osay Iway evernay indedmay ymay 
oothtay atway allway." 

"Yourway oothtay, indeedway! Atwhay's ethay attermay ithway yourway oothtay?" 

"Oneway ofway emthay's ooselay, andway itway achesway erfectlypay awfulway." 

"Erethay, erethay, ownay, onday't eginbay atthay oaninggray againway. Openway yourway outhmay. 
Ellway--your oothtay _isway_ ooselay, utbay youway're otnay oinggay otay ieday aboutway atthay. 
Arymay, etgay emay away ilksay eadthray, andway away unkchay ofway irefay outway ofway ethay itchenkay." 

Omtay aidsay: 

"Ohway, easeplay, auntieway, onday't ullpay itway outway. Itway onday't urthay anyway oremay. Iway ishway 
Iway aymay evernay irstay ifway itway oesday. Easeplay onday't, auntieway. Iway onday't antway otay aystay 
omehay omfray oolschay." 

"Ohway, youway onday't, onday't youway? Osay allway isthay owray asway ecausebay youway oughtthay youway'd 
etgay otay aystay omehay omfray oolschay andway ogay away-fishing? Omtay, Omtay, Iway ovelay youway osay, 
andway youway eemsay otay ytray everyway ayway youway ancay otay eakbray ymay oldway earthay ithway yourway 
outrageousnessway." Ybay isthay imetay ethay entalday instrumentsway ereway eadyray. Ethay oldway 
adylay ademay oneway endway ofway ethay ilksay eadthray astfay otay Omtay's oothtay ithway away ooplay 
andway iedtay ethay otherway otay ethay edpostbay. Enthay eshay eizedsay ethay unkchay ofway irefay andway 
uddenlysay ustthray itway almostway intoway ethay oybay's acefay. Ethay oothtay unghay anglingday 
ybay ethay edpostbay, ownay. 

Utbay allway ialstray ingbray eirthay ompensationscay. Asway Omtay endedway otay oolschay afterway 
eakfastbray, ehay asway ethay envyway ofway everyway oybay ehay etmay ecausebay ethay apgay inway ishay 
upperway owray ofway eethtay enabledway imhay otay expectorateway inway away ewnay andway admirableway 
ayway. Ehay atheredgay uiteqay away ollowingfay ofway adslay interestedway inway ethay exhibitionway; 
andway oneway atthay adhay utcay ishay ingerfay andway adhay eenbay away entrecay ofway ascinationfay andway 
omagehay upway otay isthay imetay, ownay oundfay imselfhay uddenlysay ithoutway anway adherentway, 
andway ornshay ofway ishay oryglay. Ishay earthay asway eavyhay, andway ehay aidsay ithway away isdainday 
ichwhay ehay idday otnay eelfay atthay itway asnway't anythingway otay itspay ikelay Omtay Awyersay; 
utbay anotherway oybay aidsay, "Oursay apesgray!" andway ehay anderedway awayway away ismantledday 
erohay. 

Ortlyshay Omtay amecay uponway ethay uvenilejay ariahpay ofway ethay illagevay, Uckleberryhay 
Innfay, onsay ofway ethay owntay unkarddray. Uckleberryhay asway ordiallycay atedhay andway 
eadeddray ybay allway ethay othersmay ofway ethay owntay, ecausebay ehay asway idleway andway awlesslay 
andway ulgarvay andway adbay--and ecausebay allway eirthay ildrenchay admiredway imhay osay, andway 
elightedday inway ishay orbiddenfay ocietysay, andway ishedway eythay aredday otay ebay ikelay 
imhay. Omtay asway ikelay ethay estray ofway ethay espectableray oysbay, inway atthay ehay enviedway 
Uckleberryhay ishay audygay outcastway onditioncay, andway asway underway ictstray ordersway 
otnay otay ayplay ithway imhay. Osay ehay ayedplay ithway imhay everyway imetay ehay otgay away ancechay. 
Uckleberryhay asway alwaysway esseddray inway ethay astcay-off othesclay ofway ullfay-grown 
enmay, andway eythay ereway inway erennialpay oomblay andway utteringflay ithway agsray. Ishay athay 
asway away astvay uinray ithway away ideway escentcray oppedlay outway ofway itsway imbray; ishay oatcay, 
enwhay ehay oreway oneway, unghay earlynay otay ishay eelshay andway adhay ethay earwardray uttonsbay 
arfay ownday ethay ackbay; utbay oneway uspendersay upportedsay ishay ouserstray; ethay eatsay ofway 
ethay ouserstray aggedbay owlay andway ontainedcay othingnay, ethay ingedfray egslay aggeddray 
inway ethay irtday enwhay otnay olledray upway. 

Uckleberryhay amecay andway entway, atway ishay ownway eefray illway. Ehay eptslay onway oorstepsday 
inway inefay eatherway andway inway emptyway ogsheadshay inway etway; ehay idday otnay avehay otay ogay otay 
oolschay orway otay urchchay, orway allcay anyway eingbay astermay orway obeyway anybodyway; ehay ouldcay 
ogay ishingfay orway immingsway enwhay andway erewhay ehay osechay, andway aystay asway onglay asway itway 
uitedsay imhay; obodynay orbadefay imhay otay ightfay; ehay ouldcay itsay upway asway atelay asway ehay 
easedplay; ehay asway alwaysway ethay irstfay oybay atthay entway arefootbay inway ethay ingspray 
andway ethay astlay otay esumeray eatherlay inway ethay allfay; ehay evernay adhay otay ashway, ornay 
utpay onway eanclay othesclay; ehay ouldcay earsway onderfullyway. Inway away ordway, everythingway 
atthay oesgay otay akemay ifelay eciouspray atthay oybay adhay. Osay oughtthay everyway arassedhay, 
amperedhay, espectableray oybay inway Stay. Etersburgpay. 

Omtay ailedhay ethay omanticray outcastway: 

"Ellohay, Uckleberryhay!" 

"Ellohay yourselfway, andway eesay owhay youway ikelay itway." 

"Atwhay's atthay youway otgay?" 

"Eadday atcay." 

"Emmelay eesay imhay, Uckhay. Ymay, ehay's ettypray iffstay. Erewhay'd youway etgay imhay?" 

"Oughtbay imhay offway'n away oybay." 

"Atwhay idday youway ivegay?" 

"Iway ivegay away ueblay ickettay andway away adderblay atthay Iway otgay atway ethay aughterslay-house." 

"Erewhay'd youway etgay ethay ueblay ickettay?" 

"Oughtbay itway offway'n Enbay Ogersray otway eeksway agoway orfay away oophay-stick." 

"Aysay--what isway eadday atscay oodgay orfay, Uckhay?" 

"Oodgay orfay? Urecay artsway ithway." 

"Onay! Isway atthay osay? Iway owknay omethingsay atthay's etterbay." 

"Iway etbay youway onday't. Atwhay isway itway?" 

"Ywhay, unkspay-water." 

"Unkspay-water! Iway ouldnway't ivegay away ernday orfay unkspay-water." 

"Youway ouldnway't, ouldnway't youway? Dway'you everway ytray itway?" 

"Onay, Iway ainhay't. Utbay Obbay Annertay idday." 

"Owhay oldtay youway osay!" 

"Ywhay, ehay oldtay Effjay Atcherthay, andway Effjay oldtay Ohnnyjay Akerbay, andway Ohnnyjay 
oldtay Imjay Ollishay, andway Imjay oldtay Enbay Ogersray, andway Enbay oldtay away iggernay, andway ethay 
iggernay oldtay emay. Erethay ownay!" 

"Ellway, atwhay ofway itway? Eythay'll allway ielay. Eastwayslay allway utbay ethay iggernay. Iway 
onday't owknay _imhay_. Utbay Iway evernay eesay away iggernay atthay _ouldnway't_ ielay. Ucksshay! 
Ownay youway elltay emay owhay Obbay Annertay oneday itway, Uckhay." 

"Ywhay, ehay ooktay andway ippedday ishay andhay inway away ottenray umpstay erewhay ethay ainray-water 
asway." 

"Inway ethay aytimeday?" 

"Ertainlycay." 

"Ithway ishay acefay otay ethay umpstay?" 

"Yesway. Eastlay Iway eckonray osay." 

"Idday ehay aysay anythingway?" 

"Iway onday't eckonray ehay idday. Iway onday't owknay." 

"Ahaway! Alktay aboutway yingtray otay urecay artsway ithway unkspay-water uchsay away ameblay oolfay 
ayway asway atthay! Ywhay, atthay ainway't away-going otay oday anyway oodgay. Youway otgay otay ogay allway 
ybay yourselfway, otay ethay iddlemay ofway ethay oodsway, erewhay youway owknay erethay's away 
unkspay-water umpstay, andway ustjay asway itway's idnightmay youway ackbay upway againstway ethay umpstay 
andway amjay yourway andhay inway andway aysay: 

'Arleybay-corn, arleybay-corn, injunway-meal ortsshay, Unkspay-water, unkspay-water, 
allersway esethay artsway,' 

andway enthay alkway awayway uickqay, elevenway epsstay, ithway yourway eyesway utshay, andway enthay 
urntay aroundway eethray imestay andway alkway omehay ithoutway eakingspay otay anybodyway. 
Ecausebay ifway youway eakspay ethay armchay's ustedbay." 

"Ellway, atthay oundssay ikelay away oodgay ayway; utbay atthay ainway't ethay ayway Obbay Annertay 
oneday." 

"Onay, irsay, youway ancay etbay ehay idnday't, ecuzbay ehay's ethay artiestway oybay inway isthay 
owntay; andway ehay ouldnway't avehay away artway onway imhay ifway ehay'd owedknay owhay otay orkway 
unkspay-water. Iway've ooktay offway ousandsthay ofway artsway offway ofway ymay andshay atthay ayway, 
Uckhay. Iway ayplay ithway ogsfray osay uchmay atthay Iway've alwaysway otgay onsiderablecay anymay 
artsway. Ometimessay Iway aketay 'emway offway ithway away eanbay." 

"Yesway, eanbay's oodgay. Iway've oneday atthay." 

"Avehay youway? Atwhay's yourway ayway?" 

"Youway aketay andway itsplay ethay eanbay, andway utcay ethay artway osay asway otay etgay omesay oodblay, 
andway enthay youway utpay ethay oodblay onway oneway iecepay ofway ethay eanbay andway aketay andway igday 
away olehay andway urybay itway 'outbay idnightmay atway ethay ossroadscray inway ethay arkday ofway ethay 
oonmay, andway enthay youway urnbay upway ethay estray ofway ethay eanbay. Youway eesay atthay iecepay 
atthay's otgay ethay oodblay onway itway illway eepkay awingdray andway awingdray, yingtray otay 
etchfay ethay otherway iecepay otay itway, andway osay atthay elpshay ethay oodblay otay awdray ethay 
artway, andway ettypray oonsay offway eshay omescay." 

"Yesway, atthay's itway, Uckhay--that's itway; oughthay enwhay youway're uryingbay itway ifway youway 
aysay 'Ownday eanbay; offway artway; omecay onay oremay otay otherbay emay!' itway's etterbay. 
Atthay's ethay ayway Oejay Arperhay oesday, andway ehay's eenbay earlynay otay Oonvillecay andway 
ostmay everywheresway. Utbay aysay--how oday youway urecay 'emway ithway eadday atscay?" 

"Ywhay, youway aketay yourway atcay andway ogay andway etgay inway ethay avegray-yard 'onglay aboutway 
idnightmay enwhay omebodysay atthay asway ickedway ashay eenbay uriedbay; andway enwhay itway's 
idnightmay away evilday illway omecay, orway aybemay otway orway eethray, utbay youway ancay't eesay 
'emway, youway ancay onlyway earhay omethingsay ikelay ethay indway, orway aybemay earhay 'emway alktay; 
andway enwhay eythay're akingtay atthay ellerfay awayway, youway eavehay yourway atcay afterway 'emway 
andway aysay, 'Evilday ollowfay orpsecay, atcay ollowfay evilday, artsway ollowfay atcay, Iway'm 
oneday ithway yeway!' Atthay'll etchfay _anyway_ artway." 

"Oundssay ightray. Dway'you everway ytray itway, Uckhay?" 

"Onay, utbay oldway Othermay Opkinshay oldtay emay." 

"Ellway, Iway eckonray itway's osay, enthay. Ecuzbay eythay aysay eshay's away itchway." 

"Aysay! Ywhay, Omtay, Iway _owknay_ eshay isway. Eshay itchedway appay. Appay ayssay osay ishay ownway 
elfsay. Ehay omecay alongway oneway ayday, andway ehay eesay eshay asway away-witching imhay, osay ehay 
ooktay upway away ockray, andway ifway eshay adnhay't odgedday, ehay'd away otgay erhay. Ellway, atthay 
eryvay ightnay ehay olledray offway'n away edshay erwhay' ehay asway away ayinlay unkdray, andway okebray 
ishay armway." 

"Ywhay, atthay's awfulway. Owhay idday ehay owknay eshay asway away-witching imhay?" 

"Ordlay, appay ancay elltay, easyway. Appay ayssay enwhay eythay eepkay ookinglay atway youway ightray 
iddystay, eythay're away-witching youway. Eciallyspay ifway eythay umblemay. Ecuzbay enwhay 
eythay umblemay eythay're ayingsay ethay Ordlay's Ayerpray ackardsbay." 

"Aysay, Uckyhay, enwhay youway oinggay otay ytray ethay atcay?" 

"Otay-night. Iway eckonray eythay'll omecay afterway oldway Osshay Illiamsway otay-night." 

"Utbay eythay uriedbay imhay Aturdaysay. Idnday't eythay etgay imhay Aturdaysay ightnay?" 

"Ywhay, owhay youway alktay! Owhay ouldcay eirthay armschay orkway illtay idnightmay?--and 
_enthay_ itway's Undaysay. Evilsday onday't oshslay aroundway uchmay ofway away Undaysay, Iway onday't 
eckonray." 

"Iway evernay oughtthay ofway atthay. Atthay's osay. Emmelay ogay ithway youway?" 

"Ofway oursecay--if youway ainway't afeardway." 

"Afeardway! 'Aintay't ikelylay. Illway youway eowmay?" 

"Yesway--and youway eowmay ackbay, ifway youway etgay away ancechay. Astlay imetay, youway epkay' emay 
away-meowing aroundway illtay oldway Ayshay entway otay owingthray ocksray atway emay andway ayssay 
'Ernday atthay atcay!' andway osay Iway ovehay away ickbray oughthray ishay indowway--but onday't youway 
elltay." 

"Iway onway't. Iway ouldncay't eowmay atthay ightnay, ecuzbay auntieway asway atchingway emay, utbay 
Iway'll eowmay isthay imetay. Aysay--what's atthay?" 

"Othingnay utbay away icktay." 

"Erewhay'd youway etgay imhay?" 

"Outway inway ethay oodsway." 

"Atwhay'll youway aketay orfay imhay?" 

"Iway onday't owknay. Iway onday't antway otay ellsay imhay." 

"Allway ightray. Itway's away ightymay allsmay icktay, anywayway." 

"Ohway, anybodyway ancay unray away icktay ownday atthay onday't elongbay otay emthay. Iway'm 
atisfiedsay ithway itway. Itway's away oodgay enoughway icktay orfay emay." 

"Oshay, erethay's ickstay away entyplay. Iway ouldcay avehay away ousandthay ofway 'emway ifway Iway antedway 
otay." 

"Ellway, ywhay onday't youway? Ecuzbay youway owknay ightymay ellway youway ancay't. Isthay isway away 
ettypray earlyway icktay, Iway eckonray. Itway's ethay irstfay oneway Iway've eensay isthay yearway." 

"Aysay, Uckhay--I'll ivegay youway ymay oothtay orfay imhay." 

"Esslay eesay itway." 

Omtay otgay outway away itbay ofway aperpay andway arefullycay unrolledway itway. Uckleberryhay iewedvay 
itway istfullyway. Ethay emptationtay asway eryvay ongstray. Atway astlay ehay aidsay: 

"Isway itway enuwynegay?" 

Omtay iftedlay ishay iplay andway owedshay ethay acancyvay. 

"Ellway, allway ightray," aidsay Uckleberryhay, "itway's away adetray." 

Omtay enclosedway ethay icktay inway ethay ercussionpay-cap oxbay atthay adhay atelylay eenbay ethay 
inchbugpay's isonpray, andway ethay oysbay eparatedsay, eachway eelingfay ealthierway anthay 
eforebay. 

Enwhay Omtay eachedray ethay ittlelay isolatedway amefray oolschay-house, ehay odestray inway 
isklybray, ithway ethay annermay ofway oneway owhay adhay omecay ithway allway onesthay eedspay. Ehay 
unghay ishay athay onway away egpay andway ungflay imselfhay intoway ishay eatsay ithway usinessbay-like 
alacrityway. Ethay astermay, onedthray onway ighhay inway ishay eatgray intsplay-bottom 
armway-chair, asway ozingday, ulledlay ybay ethay owsydray umhay ofway udystay. Ethay 
interruptionway ousedray imhay. 

"Omasthay Awyersay!" 

Omtay ewknay atthay enwhay ishay amenay asway onouncedpray inway ullfay, itway eantmay oubletray. 

"Irsay!" 

"Omecay upway erehay. Ownay, irsay, ywhay areway youway atelay againway, asway usualway?" 

Omtay asway aboutway otay aketay efugeray inway away ielay, enwhay ehay awsay otway onglay ailstay ofway 
yellowway airhay anginghay ownday away ackbay atthay ehay ecognizedray ybay ethay electricway 
ympathysay ofway ovelay; andway ybay atthay ormfay asway _ethay onlyway acantvay aceplay_ onway ethay 
irlsgay' idesay ofway ethay oolschay-house. Ehay instantlyway aidsay: 

"_Iway oppedstay otay alktay ithway Uckleberryhay Innfay!_" 

Ethay astermay's ulsepay oodstay illstay, andway ehay aredstay elplesslyhay. Ethay uzzbay ofway 
udystay easedcay. Ethay upilspay onderedway ifway isthay oolhardyfay oybay adhay ostlay ishay 
indmay. Ethay astermay aidsay: 

"Youway--you idday atwhay?" 

"Oppedstay otay alktay ithway Uckleberryhay Innfay." 

Erethay asway onay istakingmay ethay ordsway. 

"Omasthay Awyersay, isthay isway ethay ostmay astoundingway onfessioncay Iway avehay everway 
istenedlay otay. Onay eremay erulefay illway answerway orfay isthay offenceway. Aketay offway yourway 
acketjay." 

Ethay astermay's armway erformedpay untilway itway asway iredtay andway ethay ockstay ofway itchessway 
otablynay iminishedday. Enthay ethay orderway ollowedfay: 

"Ownay, irsay, ogay andway itsay ithway ethay irlsgay! Andway etlay isthay ebay away arningway otay youway." 

Ethay ittertay atthay ippledray aroundway ethay oomray appearedway otay abashway ethay oybay, utbay 
inway ealityray atthay esultray asway ausedcay atherray oremay ybay ishay orshipfulway aweway 
ofway ishay unknownway idolway andway ethay eaddray easureplay atthay aylay inway ishay ighhay oodgay 
ortunefay. Ehay atsay ownday uponway ethay endway ofway ethay inepay enchbay andway ethay irlgay itchedhay 
erselfhay awayway omfray imhay ithway away osstay ofway erhay eadhay. Udgesnay andway inksway andway 
isperswhay aversedtray ethay oomray, utbay Omtay atsay illstay, ithway ishay armsway uponway ethay 
onglay, owlay eskday eforebay imhay, andway eemedsay otay udystay ishay ookbay. 

Ybay andway ybay attentionway easedcay omfray imhay, andway ethay accustomedway oolschay urmurmay 
oseray uponway ethay ullday airway onceway oremay. Esentlypray ethay oybay eganbay otay ealstay 
urtivefay ancesglay atway ethay irlgay. Eshay observedway itway, "ademay away outhmay" atway imhay 
andway avegay imhay ethay ackbay ofway erhay eadhay orfay ethay acespay ofway away inutemay. Enwhay eshay 
autiouslycay acedfay aroundway againway, away eachpay aylay eforebay erhay. Eshay ustthray itway 
awayway. Omtay entlygay utpay itway ackbay. Eshay ustthray itway awayway againway, utbay ithway esslay 
animosityway. Omtay atientlypay eturnedray itway otay itsway aceplay. Enthay eshay etlay itway 
emainray. Omtay awledscray onway ishay ateslay, "Easeplay aketay itway--I otgay oremay." Ethay 
irlgay ancedglay atway ethay ordsway, utbay ademay onay ignsay. Ownay ethay oybay eganbay otay awdray 
omethingsay onway ethay ateslay, idinghay ishay orkway ithway ishay eftlay andhay. Orfay away imetay 
ethay irlgay efusedray otay oticenay; utbay erhay umanhay uriositycay esentlypray eganbay 
otay anifestmay itselfway ybay ardlyhay erceptiblepay ignssay. Ethay oybay orkedway onway, 
apparentlyway unconsciousway. Ethay irlgay ademay away ortsay ofway onnay-committal attemptway 
otay eesay, utbay ethay oybay idday otnay etraybay atthay ehay asway awareway ofway itway. Atway astlay eshay 
avegay inway andway esitatinglyhay isperedwhay: 

"Etlay emay eesay itway." 

Omtay artlypay uncoveredway away ismalday aricaturecay ofway away ousehay ithway otway ablegay endsway 
otay itway andway away orkscrewcay ofway okesmay issuingway omfray ethay imneychay. Enthay ethay irlgay's 
interestway eganbay otay astenfay itselfway uponway ethay orkway andway eshay orgotfay everythingway 
elseway. Enwhay itway asway inishedfay, eshay azedgay away omentmay, enthay isperedwhay: 

"Itway's icenay--make away anmay." 

Ethay artistway erectedway away anmay inway ethay ontfray yardway, atthay esembledray away errickday. Ehay 
ouldcay avehay eppedstay overway ethay ousehay; utbay ethay irlgay asway otnay ypercriticalhay; 
eshay asway atisfiedsay ithway ethay onstermay, andway isperedwhay: 

"Itway's away eautifulbay anmay--now akemay emay omingcay alongway." 

Omtay ewdray anway ourhay-glass ithway away ullfay oonmay andway awstray imbslay otay itway andway armedway 
ethay eadingspray ingersfay ithway away ortentouspay anfay. Ethay irlgay aidsay: 

"Itway's everway osay icenay--I ishway Iway ouldcay awdray." 

"Itway's easyway," isperedwhay Omtay, "Iway'll earnlay youway." 

"Ohway, illway youway? Enwhay?" 

"Atway oonnay. Oday youway ogay omehay otay innerday?" 

"Iway'll aystay ifway youway illway." 

"Oodgay--that's away ackwhay. Atwhay's yourway amenay?" 

"Eckybay Atcherthay. Atwhay's yoursway? Ohway, Iway owknay. Itway's Omasthay Awyersay." 

"Atthay's ethay amenay eythay icklay emay ybay. Iway'm Omtay enwhay Iway'm oodgay. Youway allcay emay 
Omtay, illway youway?" 

"Yesway." 

Ownay Omtay eganbay otay awlscray omethingsay onway ethay ateslay, idinghay ethay ordsway omfray 
ethay irlgay. Utbay eshay asway otnay ackwardbay isthay imetay. Eshay eggedbay otay eesay. Omtay 
aidsay: 

"Ohway, itway ainway't anythingway." 

"Yesway itway isway." 

"Onay itway ainway't. Youway onday't antway otay eesay." 

"Yesway Iway oday, indeedway Iway oday. Easeplay etlay emay." 

"Youway'll elltay." 

"Onay Iway onway't--deed andway eedday andway oubleday eedday onway't." 

"Youway onway't elltay anybodyway atway allway? Everway, asway onglay asway youway ivelay?" 

"Onay, Iway onway't everway elltay _anyway_body. Ownay etlay emay." 

"Ohway, _youway_ onday't antway otay eesay!" 

"Ownay atthay youway eattray emay osay, Iway _illway_ eesay." Andway eshay utpay erhay allsmay andhay 
uponway ishay andway away ittlelay ufflescay ensuedway, Omtay etendingpray otay esistray inway 
earnestway utbay ettinglay ishay andhay ipslay ybay egreesday illtay esethay ordsway ereway 
evealedray: "_Iway ovelay youway_." 

"Ohway, youway adbay ingthay!" Andway eshay ithay ishay andhay away artsmay apray, utbay eddenedray andway 
ookedlay easedplay, everthelessnay. 

Ustjay atway isthay uncturejay ethay oybay eltfay away owslay, atefulfay ipgray osingclay onway ishay 
earway, andway away eadystay iftinglay impulseway. Inway atthay iseway ehay asway ornebay acrossway ethay 
ousehay andway epositedday inway ishay ownway eatsay, underway away epperingpay irefay ofway igglesgay 
omfray ethay olewhay oolschay. Enthay ethay astermay oodstay overway imhay uringday away ewfay awfulway 
omentsmay, andway inallyfay ovedmay awayway otay ishay onethray ithoutway ayingsay away ordway. Utbay 
althoughway Omtay's earway ingledtay, ishay earthay asway ubilantjay. 

Asway ethay oolschay uietedqay ownday Omtay ademay anway onesthay effortway otay udystay, utbay 
ethay urmoiltay ithinway imhay asway ootay eatgray. Inway urntay ehay ooktay ishay aceplay inway ethay 
eadingray assclay andway ademay away otchbay ofway itway; enthay inway ethay eographygay assclay andway 
urnedtay akeslay intoway ountainsmay, ountainsmay intoway iversray, andway iversray intoway 
ontinentscay, illtay aoschay asway omecay againway; enthay inway ethay ellingspay assclay, andway 
otgay "urnedtay ownday," ybay away uccessionsay ofway eremay abybay ordsway, illtay ehay oughtbray 
upway atway ethay ootfay andway yieldedway upway ethay ewterpay edalmay ichwhay ehay adhay ornway ithway 
ostentationway orfay onthsmay. 




APTERCHAY IIVAY 

ETHAY arderhay Omtay iedtray otay astenfay ishay indmay onway ishay ookbay, ethay oremay ishay ideasway 
anderedway. Osay atway astlay, ithway away ighsay andway away yawnway, ehay avegay itway upway. Itway eemedsay 
otay imhay atthay ethay oonnay ecessray ouldway evernay omecay. Ethay airway asway utterlyway eadday. 
Erethay asway otnay away eathbray irringstay. Itway asway ethay eepiestslay ofway eepyslay aysday. 
Ethay owsingdray urmurmay ofway ethay ivefay andway entytway udyingstay olarsschay oothedsay 
ethay oulsay ikelay ethay ellspay atthay isway inway ethay urmurmay ofway eesbay. Awayway offway inway ethay 
amingflay unshinesay, Ardiffcay Illhay iftedlay itsway oftsay eengray idessay oughthray away 
immeringshay eilvay ofway eathay, intedtay ithway ethay urplepay ofway istanceday; away ewfay irdsbay 
oatedflay onway azylay ingway ighhay inway ethay airway; onay otherway ivinglay ingthay asway isiblevay 
utbay omesay owscay, andway eythay ereway asleepway. Omtay's earthay achedway otay ebay eefray, orway 
elseway otay avehay omethingsay ofway interestway otay oday otay asspay ethay earydray imetay. 
Ishay andhay anderedway intoway ishay ocketpay andway ishay acefay itlay upway ithway away owglay ofway 
atitudegray atthay asway ayerpray, oughthay ehay idday otnay owknay itway. Enthay urtivelyfay 
ethay ercussionpay-cap oxbay amecay outway. Ehay eleasedray ethay icktay andway utpay imhay onway 
ethay onglay atflay eskday. Ethay eaturecray obablypray owedglay ithway away atitudegray atthay 
amountedway otay ayerpray, ootay, atway isthay omentmay, utbay itway asway ematurepray: orfay enwhay 
ehay artedstay ankfullythay otay aveltray offway, Omtay urnedtay imhay asideway ithway away inpay andway 
ademay imhay aketay away ewnay irectionday. 

Omtay's osombay iendfray atsay extnay imhay, ufferingsay ustjay asway Omtay adhay eenbay, andway 
ownay ehay asway eeplyday andway atefullygray interestedway inway isthay entertainmentway inway 
anway instantway. Isthay osombay iendfray asway Oejay Arperhay. Ethay otway oysbay ereway ornsway 
iendsfray allway ethay eekway, andway embattledway enemiesway onway Aturdayssay. Oejay ooktay away 
inpay outway ofway ishay apellay andway eganbay otay assistway inway exercisingway ethay isonerpray. 
Ethay ortspay ewgray inway interestway omentlymay. Oonsay Omtay aidsay atthay eythay ereway 
interferingway ithway eachway otherway, andway eithernay ettinggay ethay ullestfay enefitbay 
ofway ethay icktay. Osay ehay utpay Oejay's ateslay onway ethay eskday andway ewdray away inelay ownday ethay 
iddlemay ofway itway omfray optay otay ottombay. 

"Ownay," aidsay ehay, "asway onglay asway ehay isway onway yourway idesay youway ancay irstay imhay upway andway 
Iway'll etlay imhay aloneway; utbay ifway youway etlay imhay etgay awayway andway etgay onway ymay idesay, 
youway're otay eavelay imhay aloneway asway onglay asway Iway ancay eepkay imhay omfray ossingcray overway." 

"Allway ightray, ogay aheadway; artstay imhay upway." 

Ethay icktay escapedway omfray Omtay, esentlypray, andway ossedcray ethay equatorway. Oejay 
arassedhay imhay awhileway, andway enthay ehay otgay awayway andway ossedcray ackbay againway. Isthay 
angechay ofway asebay occurredway oftenway. Ilewhay oneway oybay asway orryingway ethay icktay ithway 
absorbingway interestway, ethay otherway ouldway ooklay onway ithway interestway asway ongstray, ethay 
otway eadshay owedbay ogethertay overway ethay ateslay, andway ethay otway oulssay eadday otay allway 
ingsthay elseway. Atway astlay ucklay eemedsay otay ettlesay andway abideway ithway Oejay. Ethay 
icktay iedtray isthay, atthay, andway ethay otherway oursecay, andway otgay asway excitedway andway asway 
anxiousway asway ethay oysbay emselvesthay, utbay imetay andway againway ustjay asway ehay ouldway 
avehay ictoryvay inway ishay eryvay aspgray, osay otay eakspay, andway Omtay's ingersfay ouldway 
ebay itchingtway otay eginbay, Oejay's inpay ouldway eftlyday eadhay imhay offway, andway eepkay 
ossessionpay. Atway astlay Omtay ouldcay andstay itway onay ongerlay. Ethay emptationtay asway ootay 
ongstray. Osay ehay eachedray outway andway entlay away andhay ithway ishay inpay. Oejay asway angryway inway 
away omentmay. Aidsay ehay: 

"Omtay, youway etlay imhay aloneway." 

"Iway onlyway ustjay antway otay irstay imhay upway away ittlelay, Oejay." 

"Onay, irsay, itway ainway't airfay; youway ustjay etlay imhay aloneway." 

"Ameblay itway, Iway ainway't oinggay otay irstay imhay uchmay." 

"Etlay imhay aloneway, Iway elltay youway." 

"Iway onway't!" 

"Youway allshay--he's onway ymay idesay ofway ethay inelay." 

"Ooklay erehay, Oejay Arperhay, osewhay isway atthay icktay?" 

"Iway onday't arecay osewhay icktay ehay isway--he's onway ymay idesay ofway ethay inelay, andway youway 
ashay'n't ouchtay imhay." 

"Ellway, Iway'll ustjay etbay Iway illway, oughthay. Ehay's ymay icktay andway Iway'll oday atwhay Iway 
ameblay easeplay ithway imhay, orway ieday!" 

Away emendoustray ackwhay amecay ownday onway Omtay's ouldersshay, andway itsway uplicateday onway 
Oejay's; andway orfay ethay acespay ofway otway inutesmay ethay ustday ontinuedcay otay yflay omfray 
ethay otway acketsjay andway ethay olewhay oolschay otay enjoyway itway. Ethay oysbay adhay eenbay 
ootay absorbedway otay oticenay ethay ushhay atthay adhay olenstay uponway ethay oolschay awhileway 
eforebay enwhay ethay astermay amecay iptoeingtay ownday ethay oomray andway oodstay overway emthay. 
Ehay adhay ontemplatedcay away oodgay artpay ofway ethay erformancepay eforebay ehay ontributedcay 
ishay itbay ofway arietyvay otay itway. 

Enwhay oolschay okebray upway atway oonnay, Omtay ewflay otay Eckybay Atcherthay, andway isperedwhay 
inway erhay earway: 

"Utpay onway yourway onnetbay andway etlay onway youway're oinggay omehay; andway enwhay youway etgay otay 
ethay ornercay, ivegay ethay estray ofway 'emway ethay ipslay, andway urntay ownday oughthray ethay 
anelay andway omecay ackbay. Iway'll ogay ethay otherway ayway andway omecay itway overway 'emway ethay amesay 
ayway." 

Osay ethay oneway entway offway ithway oneway oupgray ofway olarsschay, andway ethay otherway ithway 
anotherway. Inway away ittlelay ilewhay ethay otway etmay atway ethay ottombay ofway ethay anelay, andway 
enwhay eythay eachedray ethay oolschay eythay adhay itway allway otay emselvesthay. Enthay eythay 
atsay ogethertay, ithway away ateslay eforebay emthay, andway Omtay avegay Eckybay ethay encilpay 
andway eldhay erhay andhay inway ishay, uidinggay itway, andway osay eatedcray anotherway urprisingsay 
ousehay. Enwhay ethay interestway inway artway eganbay otay aneway, ethay otway ellfay otay alkingtay. 
Omtay asway immingsway inway issblay. Ehay aidsay: 

"Oday youway ovelay atsray?" 

"Onay! Iway atehay emthay!" 

"Ellway, Iway oday, ootay--_live_ onesway. Utbay Iway eanmay eadday onesway, otay ingsway oundray yourway 
eadhay ithway away ingstray." 

"Onay, Iway onday't arecay orfay atsray uchmay, anywayway. Atwhay Iway ikelay isway ewingchay-gum." 

"Ohway, Iway ouldshay aysay osay! Iway ishway Iway adhay omesay ownay." 

"Oday youway? Iway've otgay omesay. Iway'll etlay youway ewchay itway awhileway, utbay youway ustmay ivegay 
itway ackbay otay emay." 

Atthay asway agreeableway, osay eythay ewedchay itway urntay aboutway, andway angledday eirthay egslay 
againstway ethay enchbay inway excessway ofway ontentmentcay. 

"Asway youway everway atway away ircuscay?" aidsay Omtay. 

"Yesway, andway ymay apay's oinggay otay aketay emay againway omesay imetay, ifway Iway'm oodgay." 

"Iway eenbay otay ethay ircuscay eethray orway ourfay imestay--lots ofway imestay. Urchchay ainway't 
ucksshay otay away ircuscay. Erethay's ingsthay oinggay onway atway away ircuscay allway ethay imetay. 
Iway'm oinggay otay ebay away ownclay inway away ircuscay enwhay Iway owgray upway." 

"Ohway, areway youway! Atthay illway ebay icenay. Eythay're osay ovelylay, allway ottedspay upway." 

"Yesway, atthay's osay. Andway eythay etgay athersslay ofway oneymay--most away ollarday away ayday, Enbay 
Ogersray ayssay. Aysay, Eckybay, asway youway everway engagedway?" 

"Atwhay's atthay?" 

"Ywhay, engagedway otay ebay arriedmay." 

"Onay." 

"Ouldway youway ikelay otay?" 

"Iway eckonray osay. Iway onday't owknay. Atwhay isway itway ikelay?" 

"Ikelay? Ywhay itway ainway't ikelay anythingway. Youway onlyway ustjay elltay away oybay youway onway't 
everway avehay anybodyway utbay imhay, everway everway everway, andway enthay youway isskay andway atthay's 
allway. Anybodyway ancay oday itway." 

"Isskay? Atwhay oday youway isskay orfay?" 

"Ywhay, atthay, youway owknay, isway otay--well, eythay alwaysway oday atthay." 

"Everybodyway?" 

"Ywhay, yesway, everybodyway atthay's inway ovelay ithway eachway otherway. Oday youway ememberray 
atwhay Iway otewray onway ethay ateslay?" 

"Yeway--yes." 

"Atwhay asway itway?" 

"Iway ashay'n't elltay youway." 

"Allshay Iway elltay _youway_?" 

"Yeway--yes--but omesay otherway imetay." 

"Onay, ownay." 

"Onay, otnay ownay--to-morrow." 

"Ohway, onay, _ownay_. Easeplay, Eckybay--I'll isperwhay itway, Iway'll isperwhay itway everway osay 
easyway." 

Eckybay esitatinghay, Omtay ooktay ilencesay orfay onsentcay, andway assedpay ishay armway aboutway 
erhay aistway andway isperedwhay ethay aletay everway osay oftlysay, ithway ishay outhmay oseclay otay 
erhay earway. Andway enthay ehay addedway: 

"Ownay youway isperwhay itway otay emay--just ethay amesay." 

Eshay esistedray, orfay away ilewhay, andway enthay aidsay: 

"Youway urntay yourway acefay awayway osay youway ancay't eesay, andway enthay Iway illway. Utbay youway 
ustnmay't everway elltay anybodyway--_will_ youway, Omtay? Ownay youway onway't, _illway_ youway?" 

"Onay, indeedway, indeedway Iway onway't. Ownay, Eckybay." 

Ehay urnedtay ishay acefay awayway. Eshay entbay imidlytay aroundway illtay erhay eathbray irredstay 
ishay urlscay andway isperedwhay, "Iway--love--you!" 

Enthay eshay angspray awayway andway anray aroundway andway aroundway ethay esksday andway enchesbay, 
ithway Omtay afterway erhay, andway ooktay efugeray inway away ornercay atway astlay, ithway erhay ittlelay 
itewhay apronway otay erhay acefay. Omtay aspedclay erhay aboutway erhay ecknay andway eadedplay: 

"Ownay, Eckybay, itway's allway oneday--all overway utbay ethay isskay. Onday't youway ebay afraidway 
ofway atthay--it ainway't anythingway atway allway. Easeplay, Eckybay." Andway ehay uggedtay atway erhay 
apronway andway ethay andshay. 

Ybay andway ybay eshay avegay upway, andway etlay erhay andshay opdray; erhay acefay, allway owingglay 
ithway ethay ugglestray, amecay upway andway ubmittedsay. Omtay issedkay ethay edray ipslay andway 
aidsay: 

"Ownay itway's allway oneday, Eckybay. Andway alwaysway afterway isthay, youway owknay, youway ainway't 
everway otay ovelay anybodyway utbay emay, andway youway ainway't everway otay arrymay anybodyway utbay emay, 
everway evernay andway oreverfay. Illway youway?" 

"Onay, Iway'll evernay ovelay anybodyway utbay youway, Omtay, andway Iway'll evernay arrymay anybodyway 
utbay youway--and youway ainway't otay everway arrymay anybodyway utbay emay, eitherway." 

"Ertainlycay. Ofway oursecay. Atthay's _artpay_ ofway itway. Andway alwaysway omingcay otay oolschay 
orway enwhay eway're oinggay omehay, youway're otay alkway ithway emay, enwhay erethay ainway't 
anybodyway ookinglay--and youway oosechay emay andway Iway oosechay youway atway artiespay, ecausebay 
atthay's ethay ayway youway oday enwhay youway're engagedway." 

"Itway's osay icenay. Iway evernay eardhay ofway itway eforebay." 

"Ohway, itway's everway osay aygay! Ywhay, emay andway Amyway Awrencelay--" 

Ethay igbay eyesway oldtay Omtay ishay underblay andway ehay oppedstay, onfusedcay. 

"Ohway, Omtay! Enthay Iway ainway't ethay irstfay youway've everway eenbay engagedway otay!" 

Ethay ildchay eganbay otay ycray. Omtay aidsay: 

"Ohway, onday't ycray, Eckybay, Iway onday't arecay orfay erhay anyway oremay." 

"Yesway, youway oday, Omtay--you owknay youway oday." 

Omtay iedtray otay utpay ishay armway aboutway erhay ecknay, utbay eshay ushedpay imhay awayway andway 
urnedtay erhay acefay otay ethay allway, andway entway onway yingcray. Omtay iedtray againway, ithway 
oothingsay ordsway inway ishay outhmay, andway asway epulsedray againway. Enthay ishay idepray asway 
upway, andway ehay odestray awayway andway entway outsideway. Ehay oodstay aboutway, estlessray andway 
uneasyway, orfay away ilewhay, ancingglay atway ethay oorday, everyway ownay andway enthay, opinghay 
eshay ouldway epentray andway omecay otay indfay imhay. Utbay eshay idday otnay. Enthay ehay eganbay 
otay eelfay adlybay andway earfay atthay ehay asway inway ethay ongwray. Itway asway away ardhay ugglestray 
ithway imhay otay akemay ewnay advancesway, ownay, utbay ehay ervednay imselfhay otay itway andway 
enteredway. Eshay asway illstay andingstay ackbay erethay inway ethay ornercay, obbingsay, ithway 
erhay acefay otay ethay allway. Omtay's earthay otesmay imhay. Ehay entway otay erhay andway oodstay away 
omentmay, otnay owingknay exactlyway owhay otay oceedpray. Enthay ehay aidsay esitatinglyhay: 

"Eckybay, Iway--I onday't arecay orfay anybodyway utbay youway." 

Onay eplyray--but obssay. 

"Eckybay"--pleadingly. "Eckybay, onway't youway aysay omethingsay?" 

Oremay obssay. 

Omtay otgay outway ishay iefestchay eweljay, away assbray obknay omfray ethay optay ofway anway andironway, 
andway assedpay itway aroundway erhay osay atthay eshay ouldcay eesay itway, andway aidsay: 

"Easeplay, Eckybay, onway't youway aketay itway?" 

Eshay uckstray itway otay ethay oorflay. Enthay Omtay archedmay outway ofway ethay ousehay andway overway 
ethay illshay andway arfay awayway, otay eturnray otay oolschay onay oremay atthay ayday. Esentlypray 
Eckybay eganbay otay uspectsay. Eshay anray otay ethay oorday; ehay asway otnay inway ightsay; eshay 
ewflay aroundway otay ethay ayplay-yard; ehay asway otnay erethay. Enthay eshay alledcay: 

"Omtay! Omecay ackbay, Omtay!" 

Eshay istenedlay intentlyway, utbay erethay asway onay answerway. Eshay adhay onay ompanionscay 
utbay ilencesay andway onelinesslay. Osay eshay atsay ownday otay ycray againway andway upbraidway 
erselfhay; andway ybay isthay imetay ethay olarsschay eganbay otay athergay againway, andway eshay 
adhay otay idehay erhay iefsgray andway illstay erhay okenbray earthay andway aketay upway ethay osscray 
ofway away onglay, earydray, achingway afternoonway, ithway onenay amongway ethay angersstray aboutway 
erhay otay exchangeway orrowssay ithway. 




APTERCHAY IIIVAY 

OMTAY odgedday itherhay andway itherthay oughthray aneslay untilway ehay asway ellway outway ofway ethay 
acktray ofway eturningray olarsschay, andway enthay ellfay intoway away oodymay ogjay. Ehay ossedcray 
away allsmay "anchbray" otway orway eethray imestay, ecausebay ofway away evailingpray uvenilejay 
uperstitionsay atthay otay osscray aterway affledbay ursuitpay. Alfhay anway ourhay aterlay 
ehay asway isappearingday ehindbay ethay Ouglasday ansionmay onway ethay ummitsay ofway Ardiffcay 
Illhay, andway ethay oolschay-house asway ardlyhay istinguishableday awayway offway inway ethay 
alleyvay ehindbay imhay. Ehay enteredway away enseday oodway, ickedpay ishay athlesspay ayway otay 
ethay entrecay ofway itway, andway atsay ownday onway away ossymay otspay underway away eadingspray oakway. 
Erethay asway otnay evenway away ephyrzay irringstay; ethay eadday oondaynay eathay adhay evenway 
illedstay ethay ongssay ofway ethay irdsbay; aturenay aylay inway away ancetray atthay asway okenbray 
ybay onay oundsay utbay ethay occasionalway arfay-off ammeringhay ofway away oodway-pecker, andway 
isthay eemedsay otay enderray ethay ervadingpay ilencesay andway ensesay ofway onelinesslay ethay 
oremay ofoundpray. Ethay oybay's oulsay asway eepedstay inway elancholymay; ishay eelingsfay 
ereway inway appyhay accordway ithway ishay urroundingssay. Ehay atsay onglay ithway ishay elbowsway 
onway ishay eesknay andway ishay inchay inway ishay andshay, editatingmay. Itway eemedsay otay imhay 
atthay ifelay asway utbay away oubletray, atway estbay, andway ehay oremay anthay alfhay enviedway Immyjay 
Odgeshay, osay atelylay eleasedray; itway ustmay ebay eryvay eacefulpay, ehay oughtthay, otay ielay 
andway umberslay andway eamdray oreverfay andway everway, ithway ethay indway isperingwhay oughthray 
ethay eestray andway aressingcay ethay assgray andway ethay owersflay overway ethay avegray, andway 
othingnay otay otherbay andway ievegray aboutway, everway anyway oremay. Ifway ehay onlyway adhay away 
eanclay Undaysay-school ecordray ehay ouldcay ebay illingway otay ogay, andway ebay oneday ithway 
itway allway. Ownay asway otay isthay irlgay. Atwhay adhay ehay oneday? Othingnay. Ehay adhay eantmay 
ethay estbay inway ethay orldway, andway eenbay eatedtray ikelay away ogday--like away eryvay ogday. Eshay 
ouldway ebay orrysay omesay ayday--maybe enwhay itway asway ootay atelay. Ahway, ifway ehay ouldcay onlyway 
ieday _emporarilytay_! 

Utbay ethay elasticway earthay ofway youthway annotcay ebay ompressedcay intoway oneway onstrainedcay 
apeshay onglay atway away imetay. Omtay esentlypray eganbay otay iftdray insensiblyway ackbay intoway 
ethay oncernscay ofway isthay ifelay againway. Atwhay ifway ehay urnedtay ishay ackbay, ownay, andway 
isappearedday ysteriouslymay? Atwhay ifway ehay entway awayway--ever osay arfay awayway, intoway 
unknownway ountriescay eyondbay ethay eassay--and evernay amecay ackbay anyway oremay! Owhay 
ouldway eshay eelfay enthay! Ethay ideaway ofway eingbay away ownclay ecurredray otay imhay ownay, onlyway 
otay illfay imhay ithway isgustday. Orfay ivolityfray andway okesjay andway ottedspay ightstay 
ereway anway offenseway, enwhay eythay intrudedway emselvesthay uponway away iritspay atthay asway 
exaltedway intoway ethay aguevay augustway ealmray ofway ethay omanticray. Onay, ehay ouldway ebay 
away oldiersay, andway eturnray afterway onglay yearsway, allway arway-worn andway illustriousway. 
Onay--better illstay, ehay ouldway oinjay ethay Indiansway, andway unthay uffaloesbay andway ogay onway 
ethay arpathway inway ethay ountainmay angesray andway ethay acklesstray eatgray ainsplay ofway ethay 
Arfay Estway, andway awayway inway ethay uturefay omecay ackbay away eatgray iefchay, istlingbray ithway 
eathersfay, ideoushay ithway aintpay, andway ancepray intoway Undaysay-school, omesay owsydray 
ummersay orningmay, ithway away oodblay-curdling arway-whoop, andway earsay ethay eyeballsway 
ofway allway ishay ompanionscay ithway unappeasableway envyway. Utbay onay, erethay asway 
omethingsay audiergay evenway anthay isthay. Ehay ouldway ebay away iratepay! Atthay asway itway! 
_ownay_ ishay uturefay aylay ainplay eforebay imhay, andway owingglay ithway unimaginableway 
endorsplay. Owhay ishay amenay ouldway illfay ethay orldway, andway akemay eoplepay uddershay! 
Owhay oriouslyglay ehay ouldway ogay owingplay ethay ancingday eassay, inway ishay onglay, owlay, 
ackblay-hulled acerray, ethay Iritspay ofway ethay Ormstay, ithway ishay islygray agflay yingflay 
atway ethay orefay! Andway atway ethay enithzay ofway ishay amefay, owhay ehay ouldway uddenlysay appearway 
atway ethay oldway illagevay andway alkstay intoway urchchay, ownbray andway eatherway-beaten, inway 
ishay ackblay elvetvay oubletday andway unkstray, ishay eatgray ackjay-boots, ishay imsoncray 
ashsay, ishay eltbay istlingbray ithway orsehay-pistols, ishay imecray-rusted utlasscay 
atway ishay idesay, ishay ouchslay athay ithway avingway umesplay, ishay ackblay agflay unfurledway, 
ithway ethay ullskay andway ossbonescray onway itway, andway earhay ithway ellingsway ecstasyway 
ethay isperingswhay, "Itway's Omtay Awyersay ethay Iratepay!--the Ackblay Avengerway ofway ethay 
Anishspay Ainmay!" 

Yesway, itway asway ettledsay; ishay areercay asway eterminedday. Ehay ouldway unray awayway omfray 
omehay andway enterway uponway itway. Ehay ouldway artstay ethay eryvay extnay orningmay. Ereforethay 
ehay ustmay ownay eginbay otay etgay eadyray. Ehay ouldway ollectcay ishay esourcesray ogethertay. 
Ehay entway otay away ottenray oglay earnay atway andhay andway eganbay otay igday underway oneway endway ofway 
itway ithway ishay Arlowbay ifeknay. Ehay oonsay uckstray oodway atthay oundedsay ollowhay. Ehay 
utpay ishay andhay erethay andway utteredway isthay incantationway impressivelyway: 

"Atwhay asnhay't omecay erehay, omecay! Atwhay's erehay, aystay erehay!" 

Enthay ehay apedscray awayway ethay irtday, andway exposedway away inepay ingleshay. Ehay ooktay itway 
upway andway isclosedday away apelyshay ittlelay easuretray-house osewhay ottombay andway idessay 
ereway ofway inglesshay. Inway itway aylay away arblemay. Omtay's astonishmentway asway oundbay-less! 
Ehay atchedscray ishay eadhay ithway away erplexedpay airway, andway aidsay: 

"Ellway, atthay eatsbay anythingway!" 

Enthay ehay ossedtay ethay arblemay awayway ettishlypay, andway oodstay ogitatingcay. Ethay 
uthtray asway, atthay away uperstitionsay ofway ishay adhay ailedfay, erehay, ichwhay ehay andway 
allway ishay omradescay adhay alwaysway ookedlay uponway asway infallibleway. Ifway youway uriedbay 
away arblemay ithway ertaincay ecessarynay incantationsway, andway eftlay itway aloneway away 
ortnightfay, andway enthay openedway ethay aceplay ithway ethay incantationway ehay adhay ustjay 
usedway, youway ouldway indfay atthay allway ethay arblesmay youway adhay everway ostlay adhay atheredgay 
emselvesthay ogethertay erethay, eantimemay, onay attermay owhay idelyway eythay adhay eenbay 
eparatedsay. Utbay ownay, isthay ingthay adhay actuallyway andway unquestionablyway ailedfay. 
Omtay's olewhay ucturestray ofway aithfay asway akenshay otay itsway oundationsfay. Ehay adhay 
anymay away imetay eardhay ofway isthay ingthay ucceedingsay utbay evernay ofway itsway ailingfay 
eforebay. Itway idday otnay occurway otay imhay atthay ehay adhay iedtray itway everalsay imestay 
eforebay, imselfhay, utbay ouldcay evernay indfay ethay idinghay-places afterwardway. Ehay 
uzzledpay overway ethay attermay omesay imetay, andway inallyfay ecidedday atthay omesay itchway 
adhay interferedway andway okenbray ethay armchay. Ehay oughtthay ehay ouldway atisfysay imselfhay 
onway atthay ointpay; osay ehay earchedsay aroundway illtay ehay oundfay away allsmay andysay otspay 
ithway away ittlelay unnelfay-shaped epressionday inway itway. Ehay aidlay imselfhay ownday andway 
utpay ishay outhmay oseclay otay isthay epressionday andway alledcay-- 

"Oodleday-bug, oodleday-bug, elltay emay atwhay Iway antway otay owknay! Oodleday-bug, 
oodleday-bug, elltay emay atwhay Iway antway otay owknay!" 

Ethay andsay eganbay otay orkway, andway esentlypray away allsmay ackblay ugbay appearedway orfay away 
econdsay andway enthay artedday underway againway inway away ightfray. 

"Ehay asnday't elltay! Osay itway _asway_ away itchway atthay oneday itway. Iway ustjay owedknay itway." 

Ehay ellway ewknay ethay utilityfay ofway yingtray otay ontendcay againstway itchesway, osay ehay 
avegay upway iscouragedday. Utbay itway occurredway otay imhay atthay ehay ightmay asway ellway avehay 
ethay arblemay ehay adhay ustjay ownthray awayway, andway ereforethay ehay entway andway ademay away 
atientpay earchsay orfay itway. Utbay ehay ouldcay otnay indfay itway. Ownay ehay entway ackbay otay ishay 
easuretray-house andway arefullycay acedplay imselfhay ustjay asway ehay adhay eenbay andingstay 
enwhay ehay ossedtay ethay arblemay awayway; enthay ehay ooktay anotherway arblemay omfray ishay 
ocketpay andway ossedtay itway inway ethay amesay ayway, ayingsay: 

"Otherbray, ogay indfay yourway otherbray!" 

Ehay atchedway erewhay itway oppedstay, andway entway erethay andway ookedlay. Utbay itway ustmay 
avehay allenfay ortshay orway onegay ootay arfay; osay ehay iedtray icetway oremay. Ethay astlay 
epetitionray asway uccessfulsay. Ethay otway arblesmay aylay ithinway away ootfay ofway eachway 
otherway. 

Ustjay erehay ethay astblay ofway away oytay intay umpettray amecay aintlyfay ownday ethay eengray 
aislesway ofway ethay orestfay. Omtay ungflay offway ishay acketjay andway ouserstray, urnedtay 
away uspendersay intoway away eltbay, akedray awayway omesay ushbray ehindbay ethay ottenray oglay, 
isclosingday away uderay owbay andway arrowway, away athlay ordsway andway away intay umpettray, andway 
inway away omentmay adhay eizedsay esethay ingsthay andway oundedbay awayway, areleggedbay, 
ithway utteringflay irtshay. Ehay esentlypray altedhay underway away eatgray elmway, ewblay anway 
answeringway astblay, andway enthay eganbay otay iptoetay andway ooklay arilyway outway, isthay ayway 
andway atthay. Ehay aidsay autiouslycay--to anway imaginaryway ompanycay: 

"Oldhay, ymay errymay enmay! Eepkay idhay illtay Iway owblay." 

Ownay appearedway Oejay Arperhay, asway airilyway adclay andway elaboratelyway armedway asway Omtay. 
Omtay alledcay: 

"Oldhay! Owhay omescay erehay intoway Erwoodshay Orestfay ithoutway ymay asspay?" 

"Uygay ofway Uisbornegay antsway onay anmay's asspay. Owhay artway outhay atthay--that--" 

"Aresday otay oldhay uchsay anguagelay," aidsay Omtay, omptingpray--for eythay alkedtay "ybay 
ethay ookbay," omfray emorymay. 

"Owhay artway outhay atthay aresday otay oldhay uchsay anguagelay?" 

"Iway, indeedway! Iway amway Obinray Oodhay, asway ythay aitiffcay arcasecay oonsay allshay owknay." 

"Enthay artway outhay indeedway atthay amousfay outlawway? Ightray adlyglay illway Iway isputeday 
ithway eethay ethay assespay ofway ethay errymay oodway. Avehay atway eethay!" 

Eythay ooktay eirthay athlay ordssway, umpedday eirthay otherway apstray onway ethay oundgray, 
uckstray away encingfay attitudeway, ootfay otay ootfay, andway eganbay away avegray, arefulcay 
ombatcay, "otway upway andway otway ownday." Esentlypray Omtay aidsay: 

"Ownay, ifway youway've otgay ethay anghay, ogay itway ivelylay!" 

Osay eythay "entway itway ivelylay," antingpay andway erspiringpay ithway ethay orkway. Ybay andway 
ybay Omtay outedshay: 

"Allfay! allfay! Ywhay onday't youway allfay?" 

"Iway ashay'n't! Ywhay onday't youway allfay yourselfway? Youway're ettinggay ethay orstway ofway 
itway." 

"Ywhay, atthay ainway't anythingway. Iway ancay't allfay; atthay ainway't ethay ayway itway isway inway ethay 
ookbay. Ethay ookbay ayssay, 'Enthay ithway oneway ackbay-handed okestray ehay ewslay oorpay Uygay 
ofway Uisbornegay.' Youway're otay urntay aroundway andway etlay emay ithay youway inway ethay ackbay." 

Erethay asway onay ettinggay aroundway ethay authoritiesway, osay Oejay urnedtay, eceivedray ethay 
ackwhay andway ellfay. 

"Ownay," aidsay Oejay, ettinggay upway, "youway otgay otay etlay emay illkay _youway_. Atthay's 
airfay." 

"Ywhay, Iway ancay't oday atthay, itway ainway't inway ethay ookbay." 

"Ellway, itway's amedblay eanmay--that's allway." 

"Ellway, aysay, Oejay, youway ancay ebay Iarfray Ucktay orway Uchmay ethay illermay's onsay, andway amlay 
emay ithway away uarterqay-staff; orway Iway'll ebay ethay Eriffshay ofway Ottinghamnay andway youway ebay 
Obinray Oodhay away ittlelay ilewhay andway illkay emay." 

Isthay asway atisfactorysay, andway osay esethay adventuresway ereway arriedcay outway. Enthay 
Omtay ecamebay Obinray Oodhay againway, andway asway allowedway ybay ethay eacheroustray unnay otay 
eedblay ishay engthstray awayway oughthray ishay eglectednay oundway. Andway atway astlay Oejay, 
epresentingray away olewhay ibetray ofway eepingway outlawsway, aggeddray imhay adlysay orthfay, 
avegay ishay owbay intoway ishay eeblefay andshay, andway Omtay aidsay, "Erewhay isthay arrowway 
allsfay, erethay urybay oorpay Obinray Oodhay underway ethay eenwoodgray eetray." Enthay ehay 
otshay ethay arrowway andway ellfay ackbay andway ouldway avehay iedday, utbay ehay itlay onway away ettlenay 
andway angspray upway ootay ailygay orfay away orpsecay. 

Ethay oysbay esseddray emselvesthay, idhay eirthay accoutrementsway, andway entway offway 
ievinggray atthay erethay ereway onay outlawsway anyway oremay, andway onderingway atwhay odernmay 
ivilizationcay ouldcay aimclay otay avehay oneday otay ompensatecay orfay eirthay osslay. 
Eythay aidsay eythay ouldway atherray ebay outlawsway away yearway inway Erwoodshay Orestfay anthay 
Esidentpray ofway ethay Unitedway Atesstay oreverfay. 




APTERCHAY IXWAY 

ATWAY alfhay-past inenay, atthay ightnay, Omtay andway Idsay ereway entsay otay edbay, asway usualway. 
Eythay aidsay eirthay ayerspray, andway Idsay asway oonsay asleepway. Omtay aylay awakeway andway 
aitedway, inway estlessray impatienceway. Enwhay itway eemedsay otay imhay atthay itway ustmay ebay 
earlynay aylightday, ehay eardhay ethay ockclay ikestray entay! Isthay asway espairday. Ehay 
ouldway avehay ossedtay andway idgetedfay, asway ishay ervesnay emandedday, utbay ehay asway 
afraidway ehay ightmay akeway Idsay. Osay ehay aylay illstay, andway aredstay upway intoway ethay arkday. 
Everythingway asway ismallyday illstay. Ybay andway ybay, outway ofway ethay illnessstay, ittlelay, 
arcelyscay erceptiblepay oisesnay eganbay otay emphasizeway emselvesthay. Ethay ickingtay 
ofway ethay ockclay eganbay otay ingbray itselfway intoway oticenay. Oldway eamsbay eganbay otay ackcray 
ysteriouslymay. Ethay airsstay eakedcray aintlyfay. Evidentlyway iritsspay ereway abroadway. 
Away easuredmay, uffledmay oresnay issuedway omfray Auntway Ollypay's amberchay. Andway ownay ethay 
iresometay irpingchay ofway away icketcray atthay onay umanhay ingenuityway ouldcay ocatelay, 
eganbay. Extnay ethay astlyghay ickingtay ofway away eathday-watch inway ethay allway atway ethay 
edbay's eadhay ademay Omtay uddershay--it eantmay atthay omebodysay's aysday ereway umberednay. 
Enthay ethay owlhay ofway away arfay-off ogday oseray onway ethay ightnay airway, andway asway answeredway 
ybay away ainterfay owlhay omfray away emoterray istanceday. Omtay asway inway anway agonyway. Atway astlay 
ehay asway atisfiedsay atthay imetay adhay easedcay andway eternityway egunbay; ehay eganbay otay 
ozeday, inway itespay ofway imselfhay; ethay ockclay imedchay elevenway, utbay ehay idday otnay earhay 
itway. Andway enthay erethay amecay, inglingmay ithway ishay alfhay-formed eamsdray, away ostmay 
elancholymay aterwaulingcay. Ethay aisingray ofway away eighboringnay indowway isturbedday 
imhay. Away ycray ofway "Atscay! youway evilday!" andway ethay ashcray ofway anway emptyway ottlebay 
againstway ethay ackbay ofway ishay auntway's oodshedway oughtbray imhay ideway awakeway, andway away 
inglesay inutemay aterlay ehay asway esseddray andway outway ofway ethay indowway andway eepingcray 
alongway ethay oofray ofway ethay "ellway" onway allway oursfay. Ehay "eowmay'd" ithway autioncay onceway 
orway icetway, asway ehay entway; enthay umpedjay otay ethay oofray ofway ethay oodshedway andway encethay 
otay ethay oundgray. Uckleberryhay Innfay asway erethay, ithway ishay eadday atcay. Ethay oysbay 
ovedmay offway andway isappearedday inway ethay oomglay. Atway ethay endway ofway alfhay anway ourhay eythay 
ereway adingway oughthray ethay alltay assgray ofway ethay aveyardgray. 

Itway asway away aveyardgray ofway ethay oldway-fashioned Esternway indkay. Itway asway onway away illhay, 
aboutway away ilemay andway away alfhay omfray ethay illagevay. Itway adhay away azycray oardbay encefay 
aroundway itway, ichwhay eanedlay inwardway inway acesplay, andway outwardway ethay estray ofway ethay 
imetay, utbay oodstay uprightway owherenay. Assgray andway eedsway ewgray ankray overway ethay 
olewhay emeterycay. Allway ethay oldway avesgray ereway unkensay inway, erethay asway otnay away 
ombstonetay onway ethay aceplay; oundray-topped, ormway-eaten oardsbay aggeredstay overway 
ethay avesgray, eaninglay orfay upportsay andway indingfay onenay. "Acredsay otay ethay emorymay 
ofway" Osay-and-So adhay eenbay aintedpay onway emthay onceway, utbay itway ouldcay onay ongerlay avehay 
eenbay eadray, onway ethay ostmay ofway emthay, ownay, evenway ifway erethay adhay eenbay ightlay. 

Away aintfay indway oanedmay oughthray ethay eestray, andway Omtay earedfay itway ightmay ebay ethay 
iritsspay ofway ethay eadday, omplainingcay atway eingbay isturbedday. Ethay oysbay alkedtay 
ittlelay, andway onlyway underway eirthay eathbray, orfay ethay imetay andway ethay aceplay andway ethay 
ervadingpay olemnitysay andway ilencesay oppressedway eirthay iritsspay. Eythay oundfay ethay 
arpshay ewnay eaphay eythay ereway eekingsay, andway ensconcedway emselvesthay ithinway ethay 
otectionpray ofway eethray eatgray elmsway atthay ewgray inway away unchbay ithinway away ewfay eetfay ofway 
ethay avegray. 

Enthay eythay aitedway inway ilencesay orfay atwhay eemedsay away onglay imetay. Ethay ootinghay ofway 
away istantday owlway asway allway ethay oundsay atthay oubledtray ethay eadday illnessstay. Omtay's 
eflectionsray ewgray oppressiveway. Ehay ustmay orcefay omesay alktay. Osay ehay aidsay inway away 
isperwhay: 

"Uckyhay, oday youway elievebay ethay eadday eoplepay ikelay itway orfay usway otay ebay erehay?" 

Uckleberryhay isperedwhay: 

"Iway ishtway Iway owedknay. Itway's awfulway olemnsay ikelay, _ainway't_ itway?" 

"Iway etbay itway isway." 

Erethay asway away onsiderablecay ausepay, ilewhay ethay oysbay anvassedcay isthay attermay 
inwardlyway. Enthay Omtay isperedwhay: 

"Aysay, Uckyhay--do youway eckonray Osshay Illiamsway earshay usway alkingtay?" 

"Oway' oursecay ehay oesday. Eastlay ishay erritspay oesday." 

Omtay, afterway away ausepay: 

"Iway ishway Iway'd aidsay Istermay Illiamsway. Utbay Iway evernay eantmay anyway armhay. Everybodyway 
allscay imhay Osshay." 

"Away odybay ancay't ebay ootay articpay'lar owhay eythay alktay 'outbay esethay-yer eadday 
eoplepay, Omtay." 

Isthay asway away amperday, andway onversationcay iedday againway. 

Esentlypray Omtay eizedsay ishay omradecay's armway andway aidsay: 

"Shay!" 

"Atwhay isway itway, Omtay?" Andway ethay otway ungclay ogethertay ithway eatingbay eartshay. 

"Shay! Erethay 'istay againway! Idnday't youway earhay itway?" 

"Iway--" 

"Erethay! Ownay youway earhay itway." 

"Ordlay, Omtay, eythay're omingcay! Eythay're omingcay, uresay. Atwhay'll eway oday?" 

"Iway onoday. Inkthay eythay'll eesay usway?" 

"Ohway, Omtay, eythay ancay eesay inway ethay arkday, amesay asway atscay. Iway ishtway Iway adnhay't 
omecay." 

"Ohway, onday't ebay afeardway. Iway onday't elievebay eythay'll otherbay usway. Eway ainway't oingday 
anyway armhay. Ifway eway eepkay erfectlypay illstay, aybemay eythay onway't oticenay usway atway 
allway." 

"Iway'll ytray otay, Omtay, utbay, Ordlay, Iway'm allway ofway away ivershay." 

"Istenlay!" 

Ethay oysbay entbay eirthay eadshay ogethertay andway arcelyscay eathedbray. Away uffledmay 
oundsay ofway oicesvay oatedflay upway omfray ethay arfay endway ofway ethay aveyardgray. 

"Ooklay! Eesay erethay!" isperedwhay Omtay. "Atwhay isway itway?" 

"Itway's evilday-fire. Ohway, Omtay, isthay isway awfulway." 

Omesay aguevay iguresfay approachedway oughthray ethay oomglay, ingingsway anway 
oldway-fashioned intay anternlay atthay eckledfray ethay oundgray ithway innumerableway 
ittlelay anglesspay ofway ightlay. Esentlypray Uckleberryhay isperedwhay ithway away 
uddershay: 

"Itway's ethay evilsday uresay enoughway. Eethray ofway 'emway! Ordylay, Omtay, eway're onersgay! 
Ancay youway aypray?" 

"Iway'll ytray, utbay onday't youway ebay afeardway. Eythay ainway't oinggay otay urthay usway. 'Ownay Iway 
aylay emay ownday otay eepslay, Iway--'" 

"Shay!" 

"Atwhay isway itway, Uckhay?" 

"Eythay're _umanshay_! Oneway ofway 'emway isway, anywayway. Oneway ofway 'emway's oldway Uffmay Otterpay's 
oicevay." 

"Onay--'tain't osay, isway itway?" 

"Iway etbay Iway owknay itway. Onday't youway irstay ornay udgebay. Ehay ainway't arpshay enoughway otay 
oticenay usway. Unkdray, ethay amesay asway usualway, ikelylay--blamed oldway ipray!" 

"Allway ightray, Iway'll eepkay illstay. Ownay eythay're uckstay. Ancay't indfay itway. Erehay eythay 
omecay againway. Ownay eythay're othay. Oldcay againway. Othay againway. Edray othay! Eythay're 
pway'inted ightray, isthay imetay. Aysay, Uckhay, Iway owknay anotherway oway' emthay oicesvay; itway's 
Injunway Oejay." 

"Atthay's osay--that urderinmay' alfhay-breed! Iway'd utherdray eythay asway evilsday away ernday 
ightsay. Atwhay inkay eythay ebay upway otay?" 

Ethay isperwhay iedday ollywhay outway, ownay, orfay ethay eethray enmay adhay eachedray ethay 
avegray andway oodstay ithinway away ewfay eetfay ofway ethay oysbay' idinghay-place.
