"Erehay itway isway," aidsay ethay irdthay oicevay; andway ethay ownerway ofway itway eldhay ethay anternlay 
upway andway evealedray ethay acefay ofway youngway Octorday Obinsonray. 

Otterpay andway Injunway Oejay ereway arryingcay away andbarrowhay ithway away operay andway away ouplecay 
ofway ovelsshay onway itway. Eythay astcay ownday eirthay oadlay andway eganbay otay openway ethay avegray. 
Ethay octorday utpay ethay anternlay atway ethay eadhay ofway ethay avegray andway amecay andway atsay 
ownday ithway ishay ackbay againstway oneway ofway ethay elmway eestray. Ehay asway osay oseclay ethay 
oysbay ouldcay avehay ouchedtay imhay. 

"Urryhay, enmay!" ehay aidsay, inway away owlay oicevay; "ethay oonmay ightmay omecay outway atway anyway 
omentmay." 

Eythay owledgray away esponseray andway entway onway iggingday. Orfay omesay imetay erethay asway onay 
oisenay utbay ethay atinggray oundsay ofway ethay adesspay ischargingday eirthay eightfray ofway 
ouldmay andway avelgray. Itway asway eryvay onotonousmay. Inallyfay away adespay uckstray uponway 
ethay offincay ithway away ullday oodyway accentway, andway ithinway anotherway inutemay orway otway 
ethay enmay adhay oistedhay itway outway onway ethay oundgray. Eythay iedpray offway ethay idlay ithway 
eirthay ovelsshay, otgay outway ethay odybay andway umpedday itway udelyray onway ethay oundgray. Ethay 
oonmay ifteddray omfray ehindbay ethay oudsclay andway exposedway ethay allidpay acefay. 
Ethay arrowbay asway otgay eadyray andway ethay orpsecay acedplay onway itway, overedcay ithway away 
anketblay, andway oundbay otay itsway aceplay ithway ethay operay. Otterpay ooktay outway away argelay 
ingspray-knife andway utcay offway ethay anglingday endway ofway ethay operay andway enthay aidsay: 

"Ownay ethay ussedcay ingthay's eadyray, Awbonessay, andway youway'll ustjay outway ithway 
anotherway ivefay, orway erehay eshay aysstay." 

"Atthay's ethay alktay!" aidsay Injunway Oejay. 

"Ooklay erehay, atwhay oesday isthay eanmay?" aidsay ethay octorday. "Youway equiredray yourway 
aypay inway advanceway, andway Iway've aidpay youway." 

"Yesway, andway youway oneday oremay anthay atthay," aidsay Injunway Oejay, approachingway ethay 
octorday, owhay asway ownay andingstay. "Ivefay yearsway agoway youway ovedray emay awayway omfray 
yourway atherfay's itchenkay oneway ightnay, enwhay Iway omecay otay askway orfay omethingsay otay 
eatway, andway youway aidsay Iway arnway't erethay orfay anyway oodgay; andway enwhay Iway oresway Iway'd etgay 
evenway ithway youway ifway itway ooktay away undredhay yearsway, yourway atherfay adhay emay ailedjay orfay 
away agrantvay. Idday youway inkthay Iway'd orgetfay? Ethay Injunway oodblay ainway't inway emay orfay 
othingnay. Andway ownay Iway've _otgay_ youway, andway youway otgay otay _ettlesay_, youway owknay!" 

Ehay asway eateningthray ethay octorday, ithway ishay istfay inway ishay acefay, ybay isthay imetay. 
Ethay octorday uckstray outway uddenlysay andway etchedstray ethay uffianray onway ethay oundgray. 
Otterpay oppeddray ishay ifeknay, andway exclaimedway: 

"Erehay, ownay, onday't youway ithay ymay ardpay!" andway ethay extnay omentmay ehay adhay appledgray 
ithway ethay octorday andway ethay otway ereway ugglingstray ithway ightmay andway ainmay, 
amplingtray ethay assgray andway earingtay ethay oundgray ithway eirthay eelshay. Injunway Oejay 
angspray otay ishay eetfay, ishay eyesway amingflay ithway assionpay, atchedsnay upway Otterpay's 
ifeknay, andway entway eepingcray, atlikecay andway oopingstay, oundray andway oundray aboutway 
ethay ombatantscay, eekingsay anway opportunityway. Allway atway onceway ethay octorday ungflay 
imselfhay eefray, eizedsay ethay eavyhay eadboardhay ofway Illiamsway' avegray andway elledfay 
Otterpay otay ethay earthway ithway itway--and inway ethay amesay instantway ethay alfhay-breed awsay 
ishay ancechay andway ovedray ethay ifeknay otay ethay ilthay inway ethay youngway anmay's eastbray. Ehay 
eeledray andway ellfay artlypay uponway Otterpay, oodingflay imhay ithway ishay oodblay, andway inway 
ethay amesay omentmay ethay oudsclay ottedblay outway ethay eadfuldray ectaclespay andway ethay 
otway ightenedfray oysbay entway eedingspay awayway inway ethay arkday. 

Esentlypray, enwhay ethay oonmay emergedway againway, Injunway Oejay asway andingstay overway ethay 
otway ormsfay, ontemplatingcay emthay. Ethay octorday urmuredmay inarticulatelyway, avegay 
away onglay aspgay orway otway andway asway illstay. Ethay alfhay-breed utteredmay: 

"_Atthay_ orescay isway ettledsay--damn youway." 

Enthay ehay obbedray ethay odybay. Afterway ichwhay ehay utpay ethay atalfay ifeknay inway Otterpay's 
openway ightray andhay, andway atsay ownday onway ethay ismantledday offincay. Eethray--four--five 
inutesmay assedpay, andway enthay Otterpay eganbay otay irstay andway oanmay. Ishay andhay osedclay 
uponway ethay ifeknay; ehay aisedray itway, ancedglay atway itway, andway etlay itway allfay, ithway away 
uddershay. Enthay ehay atsay upway, ushingpay ethay odybay omfray imhay, andway azedgay atway itway, andway 
enthay aroundway imhay, onfusedlycay. Ishay eyesway etmay Oejay's. 

"Ordlay, owhay isway isthay, Oejay?" ehay aidsay. 

"Itway's away irtyday usinessbay," aidsay Oejay, ithoutway ovingmay. 

"Atwhay idday youway oday itway orfay?" 

"Iway! Iway evernay oneday itway!" 

"Ooklay erehay! Atthay indkay ofway alktay onway't ashway." 

Otterpay embledtray andway ewgray itewhay. 

"Iway oughtthay Iway'd otgay obersay. Iway'd onay usinessbay otay inkdray otay-night. Utbay itway's 
inway ymay eadhay yetway--worse'n enwhay eway artedstay erehay. Iway'm allway inway away uddlemay; 
ancay't ecollectray anythingway ofway itway, ardlyhay. Elltay emay, Oejay--_honest_, ownay, 
oldway ellerfay--did Iway oday itway? Oejay, Iway evernay eantmay otay--'pon ymay oulsay andway onorhay, Iway 
evernay eantmay otay, Oejay. Elltay emay owhay itway asway, Oejay. Ohway, itway's awfulway--and imhay osay 
youngway andway omisingpray." 

"Ywhay, youway otway asway ufflingscay, andway ehay etchedfay youway oneway ithway ethay eadboardhay 
andway youway ellfay atflay; andway enthay upway youway omecay, allway eelingray andway aggeringstay 
ikelay, andway atchedsnay ethay ifeknay andway ammedjay itway intoway imhay, ustjay asway ehay etchedfay 
youway anotherway awfulway ipclay--and erehay youway've aidlay, asway eadday asway away edgeway iltay 
ownay." 

"Ohway, Iway idnday't owknay atwhay Iway asway away-doing. Iway ishway Iway aymay ieday isthay inutemay ifway Iway 
idday. Itway asway allway onway accountway ofway ethay iskeywhay andway ethay excitementway, Iway eckonray. 
Iway evernay usedway away eeponway inway ymay ifelay eforebay, Oejay. Iway've oughtfay, utbay evernay 
ithway eeponsway. Eythay'll allway aysay atthay. Oejay, onday't elltay! Aysay youway onway't elltay, 
Oejay--that's away oodgay ellerfay. Iway alwaysway ikedlay youway, Oejay, andway oodstay upway orfay youway, 
ootay. Onday't youway ememberray? Youway _onway't_ elltay, _illway_ youway, Oejay?" Andway ethay 
oorpay eaturecray oppeddray onway ishay eesknay eforebay ethay olidstay urderermay, andway 
aspedclay ishay appealingway andshay. 

"Onay, youway've alwaysway eenbay airfay andway uaresqay ithway emay, Uffmay Otterpay, andway Iway 
onway't ogay ackbay onway youway. Erethay, ownay, atthay's asway airfay asway away anmay ancay aysay." 

"Ohway, Oejay, youway're anway angelway. Iway'll essblay youway orfay isthay ethay ongestlay ayday Iway 
ivelay." Andway Otterpay eganbay otay ycray. 

"Omecay, ownay, atthay's enoughway ofway atthay. Isthay ainway't anyway imetay orfay ubberingblay. 
Youway ebay offway yonderway ayway andway Iway'll ogay isthay. Ovemay, ownay, andway onday't eavelay anyway 
ackstray ehindbay youway." 

Otterpay artedstay onway away ottray atthay uicklyqay increasedway otay away unray. Ethay alfhay-breed 
oodstay ookinglay afterway imhay. Ehay utteredmay: 

"Ifway ehay's asway uchmay unnedstay ithway ethay icklay andway uddledfay ithway ethay umray asway ehay 
adhay ethay ooklay ofway eingbay, ehay onway't inkthay ofway ethay ifeknay illtay ehay's onegay osay 
arfay ehay'll ebay afraidway otay omecay ackbay afterway itway otay uchsay away aceplay ybay 
imselfhay--chicken-heart!" 

Otway orway eethray inutesmay aterlay ethay urderedmay anmay, ethay anketedblay orpsecay, ethay 
idlesslay offincay, andway ethay openway avegray ereway underway onay inspectionway utbay ethay 
oonmay's. Ethay illnessstay asway ompletecay againway, ootay. 




APTERCHAY Xway 

ETHAY otway oysbay ewflay onway andway onway, owardtay ethay illagevay, eechlessspay ithway 
orrorhay. Eythay ancedglay ackwardbay overway eirthay ouldersshay omfray imetay otay imetay, 
apprehensivelyway, asway ifway eythay earedfay eythay ightmay ebay ollowedfay. Everyway umpstay 
atthay artedstay upway inway eirthay athpay eemedsay away anmay andway anway enemyway, andway ademay emthay 
atchcay eirthay eathbray; andway asway eythay edspay ybay omesay outlyingway ottagescay atthay aylay 
earnay ethay illagevay, ethay arkingbay ofway ethay arousedway atchway-dogs eemedsay otay ivegay 
ingsway otay eirthay eetfay. 

"Ifway eway ancay onlyway etgay otay ethay oldway annerytay eforebay eway eakbray ownday!" isperedwhay 
Omtay, inway ortshay atchescay etweenbay eathsbray. "Iway ancay't andstay itway uchmay ongerlay." 

Uckleberryhay's ardhay antingspay ereway ishay onlyway eplyray, andway ethay oysbay ixedfay 
eirthay eyesway onway ethay oalgay ofway eirthay opeshay andway entbay otay eirthay orkway otay inway itway. 
Eythay ainedgay eadilystay onway itway, andway atway astlay, eastbray otay eastbray, eythay urstbay 
oughthray ethay openway oorday andway ellfay atefulgray andway exhaustedway inway ethay elteringshay 
adowsshay eyondbay. Ybay andway ybay eirthay ulsespay owedslay ownday, andway Omtay isperedwhay: 

"Uckleberryhay, atwhay oday youway eckonray'll omecay ofway isthay?" 

"Ifway Octorday Obinsonray iesday, Iway eckonray anginghay'll omecay ofway itway." 

"Oday youway oughthay?" 

"Ywhay, Iway _owknay_ itway, Omtay." 

Omtay oughtthay away ilewhay, enthay ehay aidsay: 

"Owhay'll elltay? Eway?" 

"Atwhay areway youway alkingtay aboutway? Sway'pose omethingsay appenedhay andway Injunway Oejay 
_idnday't_ anghay? Ywhay, ehay'd illkay usway omesay imetay orway otherway, ustjay asway eadday uresay 
asway eway're away ayinglay erehay." 

"Atthay's ustjay atwhay Iway asway inkingthay otay yselfmay, Uckhay." 

"Ifway anybodyway ellstay, etlay Uffmay Otterpay oday itway, ifway ehay's oolfay enoughway. Ehay's 
enerallygay unkdray enoughway." 

Omtay aidsay othingnay--went onway inkingthay. Esentlypray ehay isperedwhay: 

"Uckhay, Uffmay Otterpay onday't owknay itway. Owhay ancay ehay elltay?" 

"Atwhay's ethay easonray ehay onday't owknay itway?" 

"Ecausebay ehay'd ustjay otgay atthay ackwhay enwhay Injunway Oejay oneday itway. Dway'you eckonray 
ehay ouldcay eesay anythingway? Dway'you eckonray ehay owedknay anythingway?" 

"Ybay okeyhay, atthay's osay, Omtay!" 

"Andway esidesbay, ooklay-a-here--maybe atthay ackwhay oneday orfay _imhay_!" 

"Onay, 'ainttay ikelylay, Omtay. Ehay adhay iquorlay inway imhay; Iway ouldcay eesay atthay; andway 
esidesbay, ehay alwaysway ashay. Ellway, enwhay appay's ullfay, youway ightmay aketay andway eltbay 
imhay overway ethay eadhay ithway away urchchay andway youway ouldncay't asephay imhay. Ehay ayssay osay, 
ishay ownway elfsay. Osay itway's ethay amesay ithway Uffmay Otterpay, ofway oursecay. Utbay ifway away anmay 
asway eadday obersay, Iway eckonray aybemay atthay ackwhay ightmay etchfay imhay; Iway onoday." 

Afterway anotherway eflectiveray ilencesay, Omtay aidsay: 

"Uckyhay, youway uresay youway ancay eepkay ummay?" 

"Omtay, eway _otgay_ otay eepkay ummay. Youway owknay atthay. Atthay Injunway evilday ouldnway't 
akemay anyway oremay ofway owndingdray usway anthay away ouplecay ofway atscay, ifway eway asway otay ueaksqay 
'outbay isthay andway eythay idnday't anghay imhay. Ownay, ooklay-a-here, Omtay, esslay aketay 
andway earsway otay oneway anotherway--that's atwhay eway otgay otay oday--swear otay eepkay ummay." 

"Iway'm agreedway. Itway's ethay estbay ingthay. Ouldway youway ustjay oldhay andshay andway earsway 
atthay eway--" 

"Ohway onay, atthay ouldnway't oday orfay isthay. Atthay's oodgay enoughway orfay ittlelay 
ubbishyray ommoncay ingsthay--specially ithway alsgay, uzcay _eythay_ ogay ackbay onway youway 
anywayway, andway abblay ifway eythay etgay inway away uffhay--but erethay orterway ebay itingwray 'outbay 
away igbay ingthay ikelay isthay. Andway oodblay." 

Omtay's olewhay eingbay applaudedway isthay ideaway. Itway asway eepday, andway arkday, andway awfulway; 
ethay ourhay, ethay ircumstancescay, ethay urroundingssay, ereway inway eepingkay ithway itway. 
Ehay ickedpay upway away eanclay inepay ingleshay atthay aylay inway ethay oonmay-light, ooktay away 
ittlelay agmentfray ofway "edray eelkay" outway ofway ishay ocketpay, otgay ethay oonmay onway 
ishay orkway, andway ainfullypay awledscray esethay ineslay, emphasizingway eachway owslay 
ownday-stroke ybay ampingclay ishay onguetay etweenbay ishay eethtay, andway ettinglay upway ethay 
essurepray onway ethay upway-strokes. [Eesay extnay agepay.] 

"Uckhay Innfay andway Omtay Awyersay earssway eythay illway eepkay ummay aboutway Isthay andway Eythay 
ishway Eythay aymay Opdray ownday eadday inway Eirthay Ackstray ifway Eythay everway Elltay andway Otray." 

Uckleberryhay asway illedfay ithway admirationway ofway Omtay's acilityfay inway itingwray, andway 
ethay ublimitysay ofway ishay anguagelay. Ehay atway onceway ooktay away inpay omfray ishay apellay andway 
asway oinggay otay ickpray ishay eshflay, utbay Omtay aidsay: 

"Oldhay onway! Onday't oday atthay. Away inpay's assbray. Itway ightmay avehay erdigreasevay onway 
itway." 

"Atwhay's erdigreasevay?" 

"Itway's pway'ison. Atthay's atwhay itway isway. Youway ustjay allersway omesay ofway itway onceway--you'll 
eesay." 

Osay Omtay unwoundway ethay eadthray omfray oneway ofway ishay eedlesnay, andway eachway oybay ickedpray 
ethay allbay ofway ishay umbthay andway ueezedsqay outway away opdray ofway oodblay. Inway imetay, afterway 
anymay ueezessqay, Omtay anagedmay otay ignsay ishay initialsway, usingway ethay allbay ofway ishay 
ittlelay ingerfay orfay away enpay. Enthay ehay owedshay Uckleberryhay owhay otay akemay anway Hway andway 
anway Fway, andway ethay oathway asway ompletecay. Eythay uriedbay ethay ingleshay oseclay otay ethay 
allway, ithway omesay ismalday eremoniescay andway incantationsway, andway ethay ettersfay 
atthay oundbay eirthay onguestay ereway onsideredcay otay ebay ockedlay andway ethay eykay ownthray 
awayway. 

Away igurefay eptcray ealthilystay oughthray away eakbray inway ethay otherway endway ofway ethay uinedray 
uildingbay, ownay, utbay eythay idday otnay oticenay itway. 

"Omtay," isperedwhay Uckleberryhay, "oesday isthay eepkay usway omfray _everway_ 
ellingtay--_always_?" 

"Ofway oursecay itway oesday. Itway onday't akemay anyway ifferenceday _atwhay_ appenshay, eway otgay 
otay eepkay ummay. Eway'd opdray ownday eadday--don't _youway_ owknay atthay?" 

"Yesway, Iway eckonray atthay's osay." 

Eythay ontinuedcay otay isperwhay orfay omesay ittlelay imetay. Esentlypray away ogday etsay upway 
away onglay, ugubriouslay owlhay ustjay outsideway--within entay eetfay ofway emthay. Ethay oysbay 
aspedclay eachway otherway uddenlysay, inway anway agonyway ofway ightfray. 

"Ichwhay ofway usway oesday ehay eanmay?" aspedgay Uckleberryhay. 

"Iway onoday--peep oughthray ethay ackcray. Uickqay!" 

"Onay, _youway_, Omtay!" 

"Iway ancay't--I ancay't _oday_ itway, Uckhay!" 

"Easeplay, Omtay. Erethay 'istay againway!" 

"Ohway, ordylay, Iway'm ankfulthay!" isperedwhay Omtay. "Iway owknay ishay oicevay. Itway's Ullbay 
Arbisonhay." * 

[* Ifway Mray. Arbisonhay ownedway away aveslay amednay Ullbay, Omtay ouldway avehay okenspay ofway 
imhay asway "Arbisonhay's Ullbay," utbay away onsay orway away ogday ofway atthay amenay asway "Ullbay 
Arbisonhay."] 

"Ohway, atthay's oodgay--I elltay youway, Omtay, Iway asway ostmay aredscay otay eathday; Iway'd away etbay 
anythingway itway asway away _aystray_ ogday." 

Ethay ogday owledhay againway. Ethay oysbay' eartshay anksay onceway oremay. 

"Ohway, ymay! atthay ainway't onay Ullbay Arbisonhay!" isperedwhay Uckleberryhay. "_Oday_, 
Omtay!" 

Omtay, uakingqay ithway earfay, yieldedway, andway utpay ishay eyeway otay ethay ackcray. Ishay 
isperwhay asway ardlyhay audibleway enwhay ehay aidsay: 

"Ohway, Uckhay, _itsway away aystray ogday_!" 

"Uickqay, Omtay, uickqay! Owhay oesday ehay eanmay?" 

"Uckhay, ehay ustmay eanmay usway othbay--we're ightray ogethertay." 

"Ohway, Omtay, Iway eckonray eway're onersgay. Iway eckonray erethay ainway't onay istakemay 'outbay 
erewhay _Iway'll_ ogay otay. Iway eenbay osay ickedway." 

"Adday etchfay itway! Isthay omescay ofway ayingplay ookeyhay andway oingday everythingway away 
ellerfay's oldtay _otnay_ otay oday. Iway ightmay away eenbay oodgay, ikelay Idsay, ifway Iway'd away 
iedtray--but onay, Iway ouldnway't, ofway oursecay. Utbay ifway everway Iway etgay offway isthay imetay, 
Iway aylay Iway'll ustjay _allerway_ inway Undaysay-schools!" Andway Omtay eganbay otay ufflesnay away 
ittlelay. 

"_Youway_ adbay!" andway Uckleberryhay eganbay otay ufflesnay ootay. "Onsoundcay itway, Omtay 
Awyersay, youway're ustjay oldway iepay, 'onglay-side oway' atwhay Iway amway. Ohway, _ordylay_, 
ordylay, ordylay, Iway ishtway Iway onlyway adhay alfhay yourway ancechay." 

Omtay okedchay offway andway isperedwhay: 

"Ooklay, Uckyhay, ooklay! Ehay's otgay ishay _ackbay_ otay usway!" 

Uckyhay ookedlay, ithway oyjay inway ishay earthay. 

"Ellway, ehay ashay, ybay ingoesjay! Idday ehay eforebay?" 

"Yesway, ehay idday. Utbay Iway, ikelay away oolfay, evernay oughtthay. Ohway, isthay isway ullybay, youway 
owknay. _Ownay_ owhay ancay ehay eanmay?" 

Ethay owlinghay oppedstay. Omtay ickedpray upway ishay earsway. 

"Shay! Atwhay's atthay?" ehay isperedwhay. 

"Oundssay ikelay--like ogshay untinggray. Onay--it's omebodysay oringsnay, Omtay." 

"Atthay _isway_ itway! Erewhay 'outsbay isway itway, Uckhay?" 

"Iway eeveblay itway's ownday atway 'othertay endway. Oundssay osay, anywayway. Appay usedway otay eepslay 
erethay, ometimessay, 'onglay ithway ethay ogshay, utbay awslay essblay youway, ehay ustjay iftslay 
ingsthay enwhay _ehay_ oressnay. Esidesbay, Iway eckonray ehay ainway't everway omingcay ackbay otay 
isthay owntay anyway oremay." 

Ethay iritspay ofway adventureway oseray inway ethay oysbay' oulssay onceway oremay. 

"Uckyhay, oday youway asday't otay ogay ifway Iway eadlay?" 

"Iway onday't ikelay otay, uchmay. Omtay, sway'pose itway's Injunway Oejay!" 

Omtay uailedqay. Utbay esentlypray ethay emptationtay oseray upway ongstray againway andway ethay 
oysbay agreedway otay ytray, ithway ethay understandingway atthay eythay ouldway aketay otay eirthay 
eelshay ifway ethay oringsnay oppedstay. Osay eythay entway iptoeingtay ealthilystay ownday, 
ethay oneway ehindbay ethay otherway. Enwhay eythay adhay otgay otay ithinway ivefay epsstay ofway ethay 
orersnay, Omtay eppedstay onway away ickstay, andway itway okebray ithway away arpshay apsnay. Ethay anmay 
oanedmay, ithedwray away ittlelay, andway ishay acefay amecay intoway ethay oonlightmay. Itway asway 
Uffmay Otterpay. Ethay oysbay' eartshay adhay oodstay illstay, andway eirthay opeshay ootay, 
enwhay ethay anmay ovedmay, utbay eirthay earsfay assedpay awayway ownay. Eythay iptay-toed outway, 
oughthray ethay okenbray eatherway-boarding, andway oppedstay atway away ittlelay istanceday 
otay exchangeway away artingpay ordway. Atthay onglay, ugubriouslay owlhay oseray onway ethay ightnay 
airway againway! Eythay urnedtay andway awsay ethay angestray ogday andingstay ithinway away ewfay 
eetfay ofway erewhay Otterpay asway yinglay, andway _acingfay_ Otterpay, ithway ishay osenay 
ointingpay eavenwardhay. 

"Ohway, eeminygay, itway's _imhay_!" exclaimedway othbay oysbay, inway away eathbray. 

"Aysay, Omtay--they aysay away aystray ogday omecay owlinghay aroundway Ohnnyjay Illermay's 
ousehay, 'outbay idnightmay, asway uchmay asway otway eeksway agoway; andway away ippoorwillwhay omecay 
inway andway itlay onway ethay anistersbay andway ungsay, ethay eryvay amesay eveningway; andway erethay 
ainway't anybodyway eadday erethay yetway." 

"Ellway, Iway owknay atthay. Andway upposesay erethay ainway't. Idnday't Aciegray Illermay allfay 
inway ethay itchenkay irefay andway urnbay erselfhay erribletay ethay eryvay extnay Aturdaysay?" 

"Yesway, utbay eshay ainway't _eadday_. Andway atwhay's oremay, eshay's ettinggay etterbay, ootay." 

"Allway ightray, youway aitway andway eesay. Eshay's away onergay, ustjay asway eadday uresay asway Uffmay 
Otterpay's away onergay. Atthay's atwhay ethay iggersnay aysay, andway eythay owknay allway aboutway 
esethay indkay ofway ingsthay, Uckhay." 

Enthay eythay eparatedsay, ogitatingcay. Enwhay Omtay eptcray inway atway ishay edroombay indowway 
ethay ightnay asway almostway entspay. Ehay undressedway ithway excessiveway autioncay, andway 
ellfay asleepway ongratulatingcay imselfhay atthay obodynay ewknay ofway ishay escapadeway. Ehay 
asway otnay awareway atthay ethay entlygay-snoring Idsay asway awakeway, andway adhay eenbay osay orfay 
anway ourhay. 

Enwhay Omtay awokeway, Idsay asway esseddray andway onegay. Erethay asway away atelay ooklay inway ethay 
ightlay, away atelay ensesay inway ethay atmosphereway. Ehay asway artledstay. Ywhay adhay ehay otnay 
eenbay alledcay--persecuted illtay ehay asway upway, asway usualway? Ethay oughtthay illedfay 
imhay ithway odingsbay. Ithinway ivefay inutesmay ehay asway esseddray andway ownday-stairs, 
eelingfay oresay andway owsydray. Ethay amilyfay ereway illstay atway abletay, utbay eythay adhay 
inishedfay eakfastbray. Erethay asway onay oicevay ofway ebukeray; utbay erethay ereway avertedway 
eyesway; erethay asway away ilencesay andway anway airway ofway olemnitysay atthay uckstray away illchay 
otay ethay ulpritcay's earthay. Ehay atsay ownday andway iedtray otay eemsay aygay, utbay itway 
asway upway-hill orkway; itway ousedray onay ilesmay, onay esponseray, andway ehay apsedlay intoway 
ilencesay andway etlay ishay earthay inksay ownday otay ethay epthsday. 

Afterway eakfastbray ishay auntway ooktay imhay asideway, andway Omtay almostway ightenedbray inway 
ethay opehay atthay ehay asway oinggay otay ebay oggedflay; utbay itway asway otnay osay. Ishay auntway 
eptway overway imhay andway askedway imhay owhay ehay ouldcay ogay andway eakbray erhay oldway earthay osay; 
andway inallyfay oldtay imhay otay ogay onway, andway uinray imselfhay andway ingbray erhay aygray airshay 
ithway orrowsay otay ethay avegray, orfay itway asway onay useway orfay erhay otay ytray anyway oremay. 
Isthay asway orseway anthay away ousandthay ippingswhay, andway Omtay's earthay asway orersay ownay 
anthay ishay odybay. Ehay iedcray, ehay eadedplay orfay orgivenessfay, omisedpray otay eformray 
overway andway overway againway, andway enthay eceivedray ishay ismissalday, eelingfay atthay 
ehay adhay onway utbay anway imperfectway orgivenessfay andway establishedway utbay away eeblefay 
onfidencecay. 

Ehay eftlay ethay esencepray ootay iserablemay otay evenway eelfay evengefulray owardtay 
Idsay; andway osay ethay atterlay's omptpray etreatray oughthray ethay ackbay ategay asway 
unnecessaryway. Ehay opedmay otay oolschay oomyglay andway adsay, andway ooktay ishay oggingflay, 
alongway ithway Oejay Arperhay, orfay ayingplay ookeyhay ethay ayday eforebay, ithway ethay 
airway ofway oneway osewhay earthay asway usybay ithway eavierhay oesway andway ollywhay eadday otay 
iflestray. Enthay ehay etookbay imselfhay otay ishay eatsay, estedray ishay elbowsway onway ishay 
eskday andway ishay awsjay inway ishay andshay, andway aredstay atway ethay allway ithway ethay onystay 
arestay ofway ufferingsay atthay ashay eachedray ethay imitlay andway ancay onay urtherfay ogay. 
Ishay elbowway asway essingpray againstway omesay ardhay ubstancesay. Afterway away onglay imetay 
ehay owlyslay andway adlysay angedchay ishay ositionpay, andway ooktay upway isthay objectway ithway 
away ighsay. Itway asway inway away aperpay. Ehay unrolledway itway. Away onglay, ingeringlay, olossalcay 
ighsay ollowedfay, andway ishay earthay okebray. Itway asway ishay assbray andironway obknay! 

Isthay inalfay eatherfay okebray ethay amelcay's ackbay. 




APTERCHAY IXAY 

OSECLAY uponway ethay ourhay ofway oonnay ethay olewhay illagevay asway uddenlysay electrifiedway 
ithway ethay astlyghay ewsnay. Onay eednay ofway ethay asway yetway unway-dreamed-of elegraphtay; 
ethay aletay ewflay omfray anmay otay anmay, omfray oupgray otay oupgray, omfray ousehay otay ousehay, 
ithway ittlelay esslay anthay elegraphictay eedspay. Ofway oursecay ethay oolmasterschay avegay 
olihay-day orfay atthay afternoonway; ethay owntay ouldway avehay oughtthay angelystray ofway 
imhay ifway ehay adhay otnay. 

Away orygay ifeknay adhay eenbay oundfay oseclay otay ethay urderedmay anmay, andway itway adhay eenbay 
ecognizedray ybay omebodysay asway elongingbay otay Uffmay Otterpay--so ethay orystay anray. Andway 
itway asway aidsay atthay away elatedbay itizencay adhay omecay uponway Otterpay ashingway imselfhay 
inway ethay "anchbray" aboutway oneway orway otway oway'clock inway ethay orningmay, andway atthay Otterpay 
adhay atway onceway eakedsnay offway--suspicious ircumstancescay, especiallyway ethay ashingway 
ichwhay asway otnay away abithay ithway Otterpay. Itway asway alsoway aidsay atthay ethay owntay adhay 
eenbay ansackedray orfay isthay "urderermay" (ethay ublicpay areway otnay owslay inway ethay 
attermay ofway iftingsay evidenceway andway arrivingway atway away erdictvay), utbay atthay ehay 
ouldcay otnay ebay oundfay. Orsemenhay adhay epartedday ownday allway ethay oadsray inway everyway 
irectionday, andway ethay Eriffshay "asway onfidentcay" atthay ehay ouldway ebay apturedcay 
eforebay ightnay. 

Allway ethay owntay asway iftingdray owardtay ethay aveyardgray. Omtay's eartbreakhay 
anishedvay andway ehay oinedjay ethay ocessionpray, otnay ecausebay ehay ouldway otnay 
away ousandthay imestay atherray ogay anywhereway elseway, utbay ecausebay anway awfulway, 
unaccountableway ascinationfay ewdray imhay onway. Arrivedway atway ethay eadfuldray aceplay, ehay 
ormedway ishay allsmay odybay oughthray ethay owdcray andway awsay ethay ismalday ectaclespay. 
Itway eemedsay otay imhay anway ageway incesay ehay asway erethay eforebay. Omebodysay inchedpay 
ishay armway. Ehay urnedtay, andway ishay eyesway etmay Uckleberryhay's. Enthay othbay ookedlay 
elsewhereway atway onceway, andway onderedway ifway anybodyway adhay oticednay anythingway inway eirthay 
utualmay anceglay. Utbay everybodyway asway alkingtay, andway intentway uponway ethay islygray 
ectaclespay eforebay emthay. 

"Oorpay ellowfay!" "Oorpay youngway ellowfay!" "Isthay oughtway otay ebay away essonlay otay avegray 
obbersray!" "Uffmay Otterpay'll anghay orfay isthay ifway eythay atchcay imhay!" Isthay asway ethay 
iftdray ofway emarkray; andway ethay inistermay aidsay, "Itway asway away udgmentjay; Ishay andhay isway 
erehay." 

Ownay Omtay iveredshay omfray eadhay otay eelhay; orfay ishay eyeway ellfay uponway ethay olidstay 
acefay ofway Injunway Oejay. Atway isthay omentmay ethay owdcray eganbay otay aysway andway ugglestray, 
andway oicesvay outedshay, "Itway's imhay! itway's imhay! ehay's omingcay imselfhay!" 

"Owhay? Owhay?" omfray entytway oicesvay. 

"Uffmay Otterpay!" 

"Allohay, ehay's oppedstay!--Look outway, ehay's urningtay! Onday't etlay imhay etgay awayway!" 

Eoplepay inway ethay anchesbray ofway ethay eestray overway Omtay's eadhay aidsay ehay asnway't 
yingtray otay etgay awayway--he onlyway ookedlay oubtfulday andway erplexedpay. 

"Infernalway impudenceway!" aidsay away ystanderbay; "antedway otay omecay andway aketay away uietqay 
ooklay atway ishay orkway, Iway eckonray--didn't expectway anyway ompanycay." 

Ethay owdcray ellfay apartway, ownay, andway ethay Eriffshay amecay oughthray, ostentatiouslyway 
eadinglay Otterpay ybay ethay armway. Ethay oorpay ellowfay's acefay asway aggardhay, andway 
ishay eyesway owedshay ethay earfay atthay asway uponway imhay. Enwhay ehay oodstay eforebay ethay 
urderedmay anmay, ehay ookshay asway ithway away alsypay, andway ehay utpay ishay acefay inway ishay andshay 
andway urstbay intoway earstay. 

"Iway idnday't oday itway, iendsfray," ehay obbedsay; "'onpay ymay ordway andway onorhay Iway evernay 
oneday itway." 

"Owhay's accusedway youway?" outedshay away oicevay. 

Isthay otshay eemedsay otay arrycay omehay. Otterpay iftedlay ishay acefay andway ookedlay aroundway 
imhay ithway away atheticpay opelessnesshay inway ishay eyesway. Ehay awsay Injunway Oejay, andway 
exclaimedway: 

"Ohway, Injunway Oejay, youway omisedpray emay youway'd evernay--" 

"Isway atthay yourway ifeknay?" andway itway asway ustthray eforebay imhay ybay ethay Eriffshay. 

Otterpay ouldway avehay allenfay ifway eythay adhay otnay aughtcay imhay andway easedway imhay otay ethay 
oundgray. Enthay ehay aidsay: 

"Omethingsay oldtay emay 'tway ifway Iway idnday't omecay ackbay andway etgay--" Ehay udderedshay; enthay 
avedway ishay ervelessnay andhay ithway away anquishedvay esturegay andway aidsay, "Elltay 'emway, 
Oejay, elltay 'emway--it ainway't anyway useway anyway oremay." 

Enthay Uckleberryhay andway Omtay oodstay umbday andway aringstay, andway eardhay ethay 
onystay-hearted iarlay eelray offway ishay erenesay atementstay, eythay expectingway everyway 
omentmay atthay ethay earclay yskay ouldway eliverday Odgay's ightningslay uponway ishay eadhay, 
andway onderingway otay eesay owhay onglay ethay okestray asway elayedday. Andway enwhay ehay adhay 
inishedfay andway illstay oodstay aliveway andway olewhay, eirthay averingway impulseway otay 
eakbray eirthay oathway andway avesay ethay oorpay etrayedbay isonerpray's ifelay adedfay andway 
anishedvay awayway, orfay ainlyplay isthay iscreantmay adhay oldsay imselfhay otay Atansay andway 
itway ouldway ebay atalfay otay eddlemay ithway ethay opertypray ofway uchsay away owerpay asway atthay. 

"Ywhay idnday't youway eavelay? Atwhay idday youway antway otay omecay erehay orfay?" omebodysay 
aidsay. 

"Iway ouldncay't elphay itway--I ouldncay't elphay itway," Otterpay oanedmay. "Iway antedway otay 
unray awayway, utbay Iway ouldncay't eemsay otay omecay anywhereway utbay erehay." Andway ehay ellfay otay 
obbingsay againway. 

Injunway Oejay epeatedray ishay atementstay, ustjay asway almlycay, away ewfay inutesmay 
afterwardway onway ethay inquestway, underway oathway; andway ethay oysbay, eeingsay atthay ethay 
ightningslay ereway illstay ithheldway, ereway onfirmedcay inway eirthay eliefbay atthay 
Oejay adhay oldsay imselfhay otay ethay evilday. Ehay asway ownay ecomebay, otay emthay, ethay ostmay 
alefullybay interestingway objectway eythay adhay everway ookedlay uponway, andway eythay ouldcay 
otnay aketay eirthay ascinatedfay eyesway omfray ishay acefay. 

Eythay inwardlyway esolvedray otay atchway imhay ightsnay, enwhay opportunityway ouldshay 
offerway, inway ethay opehay ofway ettinggay away impseglay ofway ishay eaddray astermay. 

Injunway Oejay elpedhay otay aiseray ethay odybay ofway ethay urderedmay anmay andway utpay itway inway 
away agonway orfay emovalray; andway itway asway isperedwhay oughthray ethay udderingshay 
owdcray atthay ethay oundway edblay away ittlelay! Ethay oysbay oughtthay atthay isthay appyhay 
ircumstancecay ouldway urntay uspicionsay inway ethay ightray irectionday; utbay eythay ereway 
isappointedday, orfay oremay anthay oneway illagervay emarkedray: 

"Itway asway ithinway eethray eetfay ofway Uffmay Otterpay enwhay itway oneday itway." 

Omtay's earfulfay ecretsay andway awinggnay onsciencecay isturbedday ishay eepslay orfay asway 
uchmay asway away eekway afterway isthay; andway atway eakfastbray oneway orningmay Idsay aidsay: 

"Omtay, youway itchpay aroundway andway alktay inway yourway eepslay osay uchmay atthay youway eepkay emay 
awakeway alfhay ethay imetay." 

Omtay anchedblay andway oppeddray ishay eyesway. 

"Itway's away adbay ignsay," aidsay Auntway Ollypay, avelygray. "Atwhay youway otgay onway yourway indmay, 
Omtay?" 

"Othingnay. Othingnay 'tway Iway owknay ofway." Utbay ethay oybay's andhay ookshay osay atthay ehay 
illedspay ishay offeecay. 

"Andway youway oday alktay uchsay uffstay," Idsay aidsay. "Astlay ightnay youway aidsay, 'Itway's 
oodblay, itway's oodblay, atthay's atwhay itway isway!' Youway aidsay atthay overway andway overway. 
Andway youway aidsay, 'Onday't ormenttay emay osay--I'll elltay!' Elltay _atwhay_? Atwhay isway itway 
youway'll elltay?" 

Everythingway asway immingsway eforebay Omtay. Erethay isway onay ellingtay atwhay ightmay avehay 
appenedhay, ownay, utbay uckilylay ethay oncerncay assedpay outway ofway Auntway Ollypay's acefay 
andway eshay amecay otay Omtay's eliefray ithoutway owingknay itway. Eshay aidsay: 

"Oshay! Itway's atthay eadfuldray urdermay. Iway eamdray aboutway itway ostmay everyway ightnay 
yselfmay. Ometimessay Iway eamdray itway's emay atthay oneday itway." 

Arymay aidsay eshay adhay eenbay affectedway uchmay ethay amesay ayway. Idsay eemedsay atisfiedsay. 
Omtay otgay outway ofway ethay esencepray asway uickqay asway ehay ausiblyplay ouldcay, andway afterway 
atthay ehay omplainedcay ofway oothachetay orfay away eekway, andway iedtay upway ishay awsjay everyway 
ightnay. Ehay evernay ewknay atthay Idsay aylay ightlynay atchingway, andway equentlyfray 
ippedslay ethay andagebay eefray andway enthay eanedlay onway ishay elbowway isteninglay away oodgay 
ilewhay atway away imetay, andway afterwardway ippedslay ethay andagebay ackbay otay itsway aceplay 
againway. Omtay's istressday ofway indmay oreway offway aduallygray andway ethay oothachetay ewgray 
irksomeway andway asway iscardedday. Ifway Idsay eallyray anagedmay otay akemay anythingway outway ofway 
Omtay's isjointedday utteringsmay, ehay eptkay itway otay imselfhay. 

Itway eemedsay otay Omtay atthay ishay oolmatesschay evernay ouldway etgay oneday oldinghay 
inquestsway onway eadday atscay, andway usthay eepingkay ishay oubletray esentpray otay ishay indmay. 
Idsay oticednay atthay Omtay evernay asway oronercay atway oneway ofway esethay inquiriesway, 
oughthay itway adhay eenbay ishay abithay otay aketay ethay eadlay inway allway ewnay enterprisesway; 
ehay oticednay, ootay, atthay Omtay evernay actedway asway away itnessway--and atthay asway angestray; 
andway Idsay idday otnay overlookway ethay actfay atthay Omtay evenway owedshay away arkedmay aversionway 
otay esethay inquestsway, andway alwaysway avoidedway emthay enwhay ehay ouldcay. Idsay arvelledmay, 
utbay aidsay othingnay. Oweverhay, evenway inquestsway entway outway ofway oguevay atway astlay, andway 
easedcay otay orturetay Omtay's onsciencecay. 

Everyway ayday orway otway, uringday isthay imetay ofway orrowsay, Omtay atchedway ishay 
opportunityway andway entway otay ethay ittlelay atedgray ailjay-window andway uggledsmay uchsay 
allsmay omfortscay oughthray otay ethay "urderermay" asway ehay ouldcay etgay oldhay ofway. Ethay 
ailjay asway away iflingtray ittlelay ickbray enday atthay oodstay inway away arshmay atway ethay edgeway 
ofway ethay illagevay, andway onay uardsgay ereway affordedway orfay itway; indeedway, itway 
asway eldomsay occupiedway. Esethay offeringsway eatlygray elpedhay otay easeway Omtay's 
onsciencecay. 

Ethay illagersvay adhay away ongstray esireday otay artay-and-feather Injunway Oejay andway ideray 
imhay onway away ailray, orfay odybay-snatching, utbay osay ormidablefay asway ishay aracterchay 
atthay obodynay ouldcay ebay oundfay owhay asway illingway otay aketay ethay eadlay inway ethay 
attermay, osay itway asway oppeddray. Ehay adhay eenbay arefulcay otay eginbay othbay ofway ishay 
inquestway-statements ithway ethay ightfay, ithoutway onfessingcay ethay avegray-robbery 
atthay ecededpray itway; ereforethay itway asway eemedday isestway otnay otay ytray ethay asecay inway 
ethay ourtscay atway esentpray. 




APTERCHAY IIXAY 

ONEWAY ofway ethay easonsray ywhay Omtay's indmay adhay ifteddray awayway omfray itsway ecretsay 
oublestray asway, atthay itway adhay oundfay away ewnay andway eightyway attermay otay interestway 
itselfway aboutway. Eckybay Atcherthay adhay oppedstay omingcay otay oolschay. Omtay adhay 
uggledstray ithway ishay idepray away ewfay aysday, andway iedtray otay "istlewhay erhay ownday ethay 
indway," utbay ailedfay. Ehay eganbay otay indfay imselfhay anginghay aroundway erhay atherfay's 
ousehay, ightsnay, andway eelingfay eryvay iserablemay. Eshay asway illway. Atwhay ifway eshay 
ouldshay ieday! Erethay asway istractionday inway ethay oughtthay. Ehay onay ongerlay ooktay anway 
interestway inway arway, ornay evenway inway iracypay. Ethay armchay ofway ifelay asway onegay; erethay 
asway othingnay utbay earinessdray eftlay. Ehay utpay ishay oophay awayway, andway ishay atbay; 
erethay asway onay oyjay inway emthay anyway oremay. Ishay auntway asway oncernedcay. Eshay eganbay otay 
ytray allway annermay ofway emediesray onway imhay. Eshay asway oneway ofway osethay eoplepay owhay 
areway infatuatedway ithway atentpay edicinesmay andway allway ewnay-fangled ethodsmay ofway 
oducingpray ealthhay orway endingmay itway. Eshay asway anway inveterateway experimenterway inway 
esethay ingsthay. Enwhay omethingsay eshfray inway isthay inelay amecay outway eshay asway inway away 
everfay, ightray awayway, otay ytray itway; otnay onway erselfhay, orfay eshay asway evernay ailingway, 
utbay onway anybodyway elseway atthay amecay andyhay. Eshay asway away ubscribersay orfay allway ethay 
"Ealthhay" eriodicalspay andway enologicalphray audsfray; andway ethay olemnsay ignoranceway 
eythay ereway inflatedway ithway asway eathbray otay erhay ostrilsnay. Allway ethay "otray" eythay 
ontainedcay aboutway entilationvay, andway owhay otay ogay otay edbay, andway owhay otay etgay upway, 
andway atwhay otay eatway, andway atwhay otay inkdray, andway owhay uchmay exerciseway otay aketay, andway 
atwhay amefray ofway indmay otay eepkay oneway's elfsay inway, andway atwhay ortsay ofway othingclay 
otay earway, asway allway ospelgay otay erhay, andway eshay evernay observedway atthay erhay 
ealthhay-journals ofway ethay urrentcay onthmay ustomarilycay upsetway everythingway eythay 
adhay ecommendedray ethay onthmay eforebay. Eshay asway asway implesay-hearted andway onesthay 
asway ethay ayday asway onglay, andway osay eshay asway anway easyway ictimvay. Eshay atheredgay 
ogethertay erhay uackqay eriodicalspay andway erhay uackqay edicinesmay, andway usthay armedway 
ithway eathday, entway aboutway onway erhay alepay orsehay, etaphoricallymay eakingspay, ithway 
"ellhay ollowingfay afterway." Utbay eshay evernay uspectedsay atthay eshay asway otnay anway 
angelway ofway ealinghay andway ethay almbay ofway Ileadgay inway isguiseday, otay ethay ufferingsay 
eighborsnay. 

Ethay aterway eatmenttray asway ewnay, ownay, andway Omtay's owlay onditioncay asway away indfallway 
otay erhay. Eshay adhay imhay outway atway aylightday everyway orningmay, oodstay imhay upway inway ethay 
oodway-shed andway owneddray imhay ithway away elugeday ofway oldcay aterway; enthay eshay ubbedscray 
imhay ownday ithway away oweltay ikelay away ilefay, andway osay oughtbray imhay otay; enthay eshay 
olledray imhay upway inway away etway eetshay andway utpay imhay awayway underway anketsblay illtay eshay 
eatedsway ishay oulsay eanclay andway "ethay yellowway ainsstay ofway itway amecay oughthray ishay 
orespay"--as Omtay aidsay. 

Yetway otwithstandingnay allway isthay, ethay oybay ewgray oremay andway oremay elancholymay andway 
alepay andway ejectedday. Eshay addedway othay athsbay, itzsay athsbay, owershay athsbay, andway 
ungesplay. Ethay oybay emainedray asway ismalday asway away earsehay. Eshay eganbay otay assistway ethay 
aterway ithway away imslay oatmealway ietday andway isterblay-plasters. Eshay alculatedcay ishay 
apacitycay asway eshay ouldway away ugjay's, andway illedfay imhay upway everyway ayday ithway uackqay 
urecay-alls. 

Omtay adhay ecomebay indifferentway otay ersecutionpay ybay isthay imetay. Isthay asephay 
illedfay ethay oldway adylay's earthay ithway onsternationcay. Isthay indifferenceway ustmay 
ebay okenbray upway atway anyway ostcay. Ownay eshay eardhay ofway Ainpay-killer orfay ethay irstfay 
imetay. Eshay orderedway away otlay atway onceway. Eshay astedtay itway andway asway illedfay ithway 
atitudegray. Itway asway implysay irefay inway away iquidlay ormfay. Eshay oppeddray ethay aterway 
eatmenttray andway everythingway elseway, andway innedpay erhay aithfay otay Ainpay-killer. 
Eshay avegay Omtay away easpoonfultay andway atchedway ithway ethay eepestday anxietyway orfay ethay 
esultray. Erhay oublestray ereway instantlyway atway estray, erhay oulsay atway eacepay againway; 
orfay ethay "indifferenceway" asway okenbray upway. Ethay oybay ouldcay otnay avehay ownshay away 
ilderway, eartierhay interestway, ifway eshay adhay uiltbay away irefay underway imhay. 

Omtay eltfay atthay itway asway imetay otay akeway upway; isthay ortsay ofway ifelay ightmay ebay 
omanticray enoughway, inway ishay ightedblay onditioncay, utbay itway asway ettinggay otay avehay 
ootay ittlelay entimentsay andway ootay uchmay istractingday arietyvay aboutway itway. Osay ehay 
oughtthay overway ariousvay ansplay orfay eliefray, andway inallyfay ithay uponway atthay ofway 
ofessingpray otay ebay ondfay ofway Ainpay-killer. Ehay askedway orfay itway osay oftenway atthay ehay 
ecamebay away uisancenay, andway ishay auntway endedway ybay ellingtay imhay otay elphay imselfhay andway 
uitqay otheringbay erhay. Ifway itway adhay eenbay Idsay, eshay ouldway avehay adhay onay isgivingsmay 
otay alloyway erhay elightday; utbay incesay itway asway Omtay, eshay atchedway ethay ottlebay 
andestinelyclay. Eshay oundfay atthay ethay edicinemay idday eallyray iminishday, utbay itway 
idday otnay occurway otay erhay atthay ethay oybay asway endingmay ethay ealthhay ofway away ackcray inway 
ethay ittingsay-room oorflay ithway itway. 

Oneway ayday Omtay asway inway ethay actway ofway osingday ethay ackcray enwhay ishay auntway's yellowway 
atcay amecay alongway, urringpay, eyeingway ethay easpoontay avariciouslyway, andway eggingbay 
orfay away astetay. Omtay aidsay: 

"Onday't askway orfay itway unlessway youway antway itway, Eterpay." 

Utbay Eterpay ignifiedsay atthay ehay idday antway itway. 

"Youway etterbay akemay uresay." 

Eterpay asway uresay. 

"Ownay youway've askedway orfay itway, andway Iway'll ivegay itway otay youway, ecausebay erethay ainway't 
anythingway eanmay aboutway emay; utbay ifway youway indfay youway onday't ikelay itway, youway ustnmay't 
ameblay anybodyway utbay yourway ownway elfsay." 

Eterpay asway agreeableway. Osay Omtay iedpray ishay outhmay openway andway ouredpay ownday 
ethay Ainpay-killer. Eterpay angspray away ouplecay ofway yardsway inway ethay airway, andway enthay 
eliveredday away arway-whoop andway etsay offway oundray andway oundray ethay oomray, angingbay 
againstway urniturefay, upsettingway owerflay-pots, andway akingmay eneralgay avochay. Extnay 
ehay oseray onway ishay indhay eetfay andway ancedpray aroundway, inway away enzyfray ofway enjoymentway, 
ithway ishay eadhay overway ishay ouldershay andway ishay oicevay oclaimingpray ishay 
unappeasableway appinesshay. Enthay ehay entway earingtay aroundway ethay ousehay againway 
eadingspray aoschay andway estructionday inway ishay athpay. Auntway Ollypay enteredway inway imetay 
otay eesay imhay owthray away ewfay oubleday ummersetssay, eliverday away inalfay ightymay urrahhay, 
andway ailsay oughthray ethay openway indowway, arryingcay ethay estray ofway ethay owerflay-pots 
ithway imhay. Ethay oldway adylay oodstay etrifiedpay ithway astonishmentway, eeringpay overway 
erhay assesglay; Omtay aylay onway ethay oorflay expiringway ithway aughterlay. 

"Omtay, atwhay onway earthway ailsway atthay atcay?" 

"Iway onday't owknay, auntway," aspedgay ethay oybay. 

"Ywhay, Iway evernay eesay anythingway ikelay itway. Atwhay idday akemay imhay actway osay?" 

"Eedday Iway onday't owknay, Auntway Ollypay; atscay alwaysway actway osay enwhay eythay're avinghay away 
oodgay imetay." 

"Eythay oday, oday eythay?" Erethay asway omethingsay inway ethay onetay atthay ademay Omtay 
apprehensiveway. 

"Yesway'm. Atthay isway, Iway elievebay eythay oday." 

"Youway _oday_?" 

"Yesway'm." 

Ethay oldway adylay asway endingbay ownday, Omtay atchingway, ithway interestway emphasizedway 
ybay anxietyway. Ootay atelay ehay ivinedday erhay "iftdray." Ethay andlehay ofway ethay elltaletay 
eatay-spoon asway isiblevay underway ethay edbay-valance. Auntway Ollypay ooktay itway, eldhay itway 
upway. Omtay incedway, andway oppeddray ishay eyesway. Auntway Ollypay aisedray imhay ybay ethay usualway 
andlehay--his earway--and ackedcray ishay eadhay oundlysay ithway erhay imblethay. 

"Ownay, irsay, atwhay idday youway antway otay eattray atthay oorpay umbday eastbay osay, orfay?" 

"Iway oneday itway outway ofway itypay orfay imhay--because ehay adnhay't anyway auntway." 

"Adnhay't anyway auntway!--you umskullnay. Atwhay ashay atthay otgay otay oday ithway itway?" 

"Eapshay. Ecausebay ifway ehay'd adhay oneway eshay'd away urntbay imhay outway erselfhay! Eshay'd away 
oastedray ishay owelsbay outway ofway imhay 'outthay anyway oremay eelingfay anthay ifway ehay asway away 
umanhay!" 

Auntway Ollypay eltfay away uddensay angpay ofway emorseray. Isthay asway uttingpay ethay ingthay inway 
away ewnay ightlay; atwhay asway ueltycray otay away atcay _ightmay_ ebay ueltycray otay away oybay, ootay. 
Eshay eganbay otay oftensay; eshay eltfay orrysay. Erhay eyesway ateredway away ittlelay, andway eshay 
utpay erhay andhay onway Omtay's eadhay andway aidsay entlygay: 

"Iway asway eaningmay orfay ethay estbay, Omtay. Andway, Omtay, itway _idday_ oday youway oodgay." 

Omtay ookedlay upway inway erhay acefay ithway ustjay away erceptiblepay inkletway eepingpay 
oughthray ishay avitygray. 

"Iway owknay youway asway eaningmay orfay ethay estbay, auntyway, andway osay asway Iway ithway Eterpay. Itway 
oneday _imhay_ oodgay, ootay. Iway evernay eesay imhay etgay aroundway osay incesay--" 

"Ohway, ogay 'onglay ithway youway, Omtay, eforebay youway aggravateway emay againway. Andway youway ytray 
andway eesay ifway youway ancay't ebay away oodgay oybay, orfay onceway, andway youway eednnay't aketay anyway 
oremay edicinemay." 

Omtay eachedray oolschay aheadway ofway imetay. Itway asway oticednay atthay isthay angestray ingthay 
adhay eenbay occurringway everyway ayday atterlylay. Andway ownay, asway usualway ofway atelay, 
ehay unghay aboutway ethay ategay ofway ethay oolyardschay insteadway ofway ayingplay ithway ishay 
omradescay. Ehay asway icksay, ehay aidsay, andway ehay ookedlay itway. Ehay iedtray otay eemsay otay 
ebay ookinglay everywhereway utbay itherwhay ehay eallyray asway ookinglay--down ethay oadray. 
Esentlypray Effjay Atcherthay ovehay inway ightsay, andway Omtay's acefay ightedlay; ehay azedgay 
away omentmay, andway enthay urnedtay orrowfullysay awayway. Enwhay Effjay arrivedway, Omtay 
accostedway imhay; andway "edlay upway" arilyway otay opportunitiesway orfay emarkray aboutway 
Eckybay, utbay ethay iddygay adlay evernay ouldcay eesay ethay aitbay. Omtay atchedway andway 
atchedway, opinghay eneverwhay away iskingfray ockfray amecay inway ightsay, andway atinghay ethay 
ownerway ofway itway asway oonsay asway ehay awsay eshay asway otnay ethay ightray oneway. Atway astlay ocksfray 
easedcay otay appearway, andway ehay oppeddray opelesslyhay intoway ethay umpsday; ehay enteredway 
ethay emptyway oolhouseschay andway atsay ownday otay uffersay. Enthay oneway oremay ockfray assedpay 
inway atway ethay ategay, andway Omtay's earthay avegay away eatgray oundbay. Ethay extnay instantway ehay 
asway outway, andway "oinggay onway" ikelay anway Indianway; yellingway, aughinglay, asingchay oysbay, 
umpingjay overway ethay encefay atway iskray ofway ifelay andway imblay, owingthray andspringshay, 
andingstay onway ishay eadhay--doing allway ethay eroichay ingsthay ehay ouldcay onceivecay ofway, 
andway eepingkay away urtivefay eyeway outway, allway ethay ilewhay, otay eesay ifway Eckybay Atcherthay 
asway oticingnay. Utbay eshay eemedsay otay ebay unconsciousway ofway itway allway; eshay evernay 
ookedlay. Ouldcay itway ebay ossiblepay atthay eshay asway otnay awareway atthay ehay asway erethay? 
Ehay arriedcay ishay exploitsway otay erhay immediateway icinityvay; amecay arway-whooping 
aroundway, atchedsnay away oybay's apcay, urledhay itway otay ethay oofray ofway ethay oolhouseschay, 
okebray oughthray away oupgray ofway oysbay, umblingtay emthay inway everyway irectionday, andway 
ellfay awlingspray, imselfhay, underway Eckybay's osenay, almostway upsettingway erhay--and 
eshay urnedtay, ithway erhay osenay inway ethay airway, andway ehay eardhay erhay aysay: "Mfay! omesay 
eoplepay inkthay eythay're ightymay artsmay--always owingshay offway!" 

Omtay's eekschay urnedbay. Ehay atheredgay imselfhay upway andway eakedsnay offway, ushedcray andway 
estfallencray. 




APTERCHAY IIIXAY 

OMTAY'S indmay asway ademay upway ownay. Ehay asway oomyglay andway esperateday. Ehay asway away 
orsakenfay, iendlessfray oybay, ehay aidsay; obodynay ovedlay imhay; enwhay eythay oundfay outway 
atwhay eythay adhay ivendray imhay otay, erhapspay eythay ouldway ebay orrysay; ehay adhay iedtray 
otay oday ightray andway etgay alongway, utbay eythay ouldway otnay etlay imhay; incesay othingnay 
ouldway oday emthay utbay otay ebay idray ofway imhay, etlay itway ebay osay; andway etlay emthay ameblay 
_imhay_ orfay ethay onsequencescay--why ouldnshay't eythay? Atwhay ightray adhay ethay 
iendlessfray otay omplaincay? Yesway, eythay adhay orcedfay imhay otay itway atway astlay: ehay ouldway 
eadlay away ifelay ofway imecray. Erethay asway onay oicechay. 

Ybay isthay imetay ehay asway arfay ownday Eadowmay Anelay, andway ethay ellbay orfay oolschay otay 
"aketay upway" inkledtay aintlyfay uponway ishay earway. Ehay obbedsay, ownay, otay inkthay ehay 
ouldshay evernay, evernay earhay atthay oldway amiliarfay oundsay anyway oremay--it asway eryvay 
ardhay, utbay itway asway orcedfay onway imhay; incesay ehay asway ivendray outway intoway ethay oldcay 
orldway, ehay ustmay ubmitsay--but ehay orgavefay emthay. Enthay ethay obssay amecay ickthay andway 
astfay. 

Ustjay atway isthay ointpay ehay etmay ishay oulsay's ornsway omradecay, Oejay 
Arperhay--hard-eyed, andway ithway evidentlyway away eatgray andway ismalday urposepay inway ishay 
earthay. Ainlyplay erehay ereway "otway oulssay ithway utbay away inglesay oughtthay." Omtay, 
ipingway ishay eyesway ithway ishay eeveslay, eganbay otay ubberblay outway omethingsay aboutway 
away esolutionray otay escapeway omfray ardhay usageway andway acklay ofway ympathysay atway omehay ybay 
oamingray abroadway intoway ethay eatgray orldway evernay otay eturnray; andway endedway ybay opinghay 
atthay Oejay ouldway otnay orgetfay imhay. 

Utbay itway anspiredtray atthay isthay asway away equestray ichwhay Oejay adhay ustjay eenbay oinggay 
otay akemay ofway Omtay, andway adhay omecay otay unthay imhay upway orfay atthay urposepay. Ishay othermay 
adhay ippedwhay imhay orfay inkingdray omesay eamcray ichwhay ehay adhay evernay astedtay andway 
ewknay othingnay aboutway; itway asway ainplay atthay eshay asway iredtay ofway imhay andway ishedway 
imhay otay ogay; ifway eshay eltfay atthay ayway, erethay asway othingnay orfay imhay otay oday utbay 
uccumbsay; ehay opedhay eshay ouldway ebay appyhay, andway evernay egretray avinghay ivendray erhay 
oorpay oybay outway intoway ethay unfeelingway orldway otay uffersay andway ieday. 

Asway ethay otway oysbay alkedway orrowingsay alongway, eythay ademay away ewnay ompactcay otay andstay 
ybay eachway otherway andway ebay othersbray andway evernay eparatesay illtay eathday elievedray 
emthay ofway eirthay oublestray. Enthay eythay eganbay otay aylay eirthay ansplay. Oejay asway orfay 
eingbay away ermithay, andway ivinglay onway ustscray inway away emoteray avecay, andway yingday, 
omesay imetay, ofway oldcay andway antway andway iefgray; utbay afterway isteninglay otay Omtay, ehay 
oncededcay atthay erethay ereway omesay onspicuouscay advantagesway aboutway away ifelay ofway 
imecray, andway osay ehay onsentedcay otay ebay away iratepay. 

Eethray ilesmay elowbay Stay. Etersburgpay, atway away ointpay erewhay ethay Ississippimay Iverray 
asway away ifletray overway away ilemay ideway, erethay asway away onglay, arrownay, oodedway islandway, 
ithway away allowshay arbay atway ethay eadhay ofway itway, andway isthay offeredway ellway asway away 
endezvousray. Itway asway otnay inhabitedway; itway aylay arfay overway owardtay ethay urtherfay 
oreshay, abreastway away enseday andway almostway ollywhay unpeopledway orestfay. Osay Acksonjay's 
Islandway asway osenchay. Owhay ereway otay ebay ethay ubjectssay ofway eirthay iraciespay asway away 
attermay atthay idday otnay occurway otay emthay. Enthay eythay untedhay upway Uckleberryhay Innfay, 
andway ehay oinedjay emthay omptlypray, orfay allway areerscay ereway oneway otay imhay; ehay asway 
indifferentway. Eythay esentlypray eparatedsay otay eetmay atway away onelylay otspay onway ethay 
iverray-bank otway ilesmay aboveway ethay illagevay atway ethay avoritefay ourhay--which asway 
idnightmay. Erethay asway away allsmay oglay aftray erethay ichwhay eythay eantmay otay apturecay. 
Eachway ouldway ingbray ookshay andway ineslay, andway uchsay ovisionpray asway ehay ouldcay ealstay 
inway ethay ostmay arkday andway ysteriousmay ayway--as ecamebay outlawsway. Andway eforebay ethay 
afternoonway asway oneday, eythay adhay allway anagedmay otay enjoyway ethay eetsway oryglay ofway 
eadingspray ethay actfay atthay ettypray oonsay ethay owntay ouldway "earhay omethingsay." Allway 
owhay otgay isthay aguevay inthay ereway autionedcay otay "ebay ummay andway aitway." 

Aboutway idnightmay Omtay arrivedway ithway away oiledbay amhay andway away ewfay iflestray, 
andway oppedstay inway away enseday undergrowthway onway away allsmay uffblay overlookingway ethay 
eetingmay-place. Itway asway arlightstay, andway eryvay illstay. Ethay ightymay iverray aylay 
ikelay anway oceanway atway estray. Omtay istenedlay away omentmay, utbay onay oundsay isturbedday ethay 
uietqay. Enthay ehay avegay away owlay, istinctday istlewhay. Itway asway answeredway omfray underway 
ethay uffblay. Omtay istledwhay icetway oremay; esethay ignalssay ereway answeredway inway ethay 
amesay ayway. Enthay away uardedgay oicevay aidsay: 

"Owhay oesgay erethay?" 

"Omtay Awyersay, ethay Ackblay Avengerway ofway ethay Anishspay Ainmay. Amenay yourway amesnay." 

"Uckhay Innfay ethay Edray-Handed, andway Oejay Arperhay ethay Errortay ofway ethay Eassay." Omtay 
adhay urnishedfay esethay itlestay, omfray ishay avoritefay iteraturelay. 

"'Istay ellway. Ivegay ethay ountersigncay." 

Otway oarsehay isperswhay eliveredday ethay amesay awfulway ordway imultaneouslysay otay ethay 
oodingbray ightnay: 

"_Oodblay_!" 

Enthay Omtay umbledtay ishay amhay overway ethay uffblay andway etlay imselfhay ownday afterway itway, 
earingtay othbay inskay andway othesclay otay omesay extentway inway ethay effortway. Erethay asway 
anway easyway, omfortablecay athpay alongway ethay oreshay underway ethay uffblay, utbay itway ackedlay 
ethay advantagesway ofway ifficultyday andway angerday osay aluedvay ybay away iratepay. 

Ethay Errortay ofway ethay Eassay adhay oughtbray away idesay ofway aconbay, andway adhay aboutway ornway 
imselfhay outway ithway ettinggay itway erethay. Innfay ethay Edray-Handed adhay olenstay away 
illetskay andway away uantityqay ofway alfhay-cured eaflay obaccotay, andway adhay alsoway oughtbray 
away ewfay orncay-cobs otay akemay ipespay ithway. Utbay onenay ofway ethay iratespay okedsmay orway 
"ewedchay" utbay imselfhay. Ethay Ackblay Avengerway ofway ethay Anishspay Ainmay aidsay itway 
ouldway evernay oday otay artstay ithoutway omesay irefay. Atthay asway away iseway oughtthay; 
atchesmay ereway ardlyhay ownknay erethay inway atthay ayday. Eythay awsay away irefay oulderingsmay 
uponway away eatgray aftray away undredhay yardsway aboveway, andway eythay entway ealthilystay 
itherthay andway elpedhay emselvesthay otay away unkchay. Eythay ademay anway imposingway 
adventureway ofway itway, ayingsay, "Isthay!" everyway ownay andway enthay, andway uddenlysay 
altinghay ithway ingerfay onway iplay; ovingmay ithway andshay onway imaginaryway aggerday-hilts; 
andway ivinggay ordersway inway ismalday isperswhay atthay ifway "ethay oefay" irredstay, otay "etlay 
imhay avehay itway otay ethay ilthay," ecausebay "eadday enmay elltay onay alestay." Eythay ewknay 
ellway enoughway atthay ethay aftsmenray ereway allway ownday atway ethay illagevay ayinglay 
inway oresstay orway avinghay away eespray, utbay illstay atthay asway onay excuseway orfay eirthay 
onductingcay isthay ingthay inway anway unpiraticalway ayway. 

Eythay ovedshay offway, esentlypray, Omtay inway ommandcay, Uckhay atway ethay afterway oarway andway 
Oejay atway ethay orwardfay. Omtay oodstay amidshipsway, oomyglay-browed, andway ithway oldedfay 
armsway, andway avegay ishay ordersway inway away owlay, ernstay isperwhay: 

"Ufflay, andway ingbray erhay otay ethay indway!" 

"Ayeway-aye, irsay!" 

"Eadystay, eadystay-y-y-y!" 

"Eadystay itway isway, irsay!" 

"Etlay erhay ogay offway away ointpay!" 

"Ointpay itway isway, irsay!" 

Asway ethay oysbay eadilystay andway onotonouslymay ovedray ethay aftray owardtay idmay-stream 
itway asway onay oubtday understoodway atthay esethay ordersway ereway ivengay onlyway orfay 
"ylestay," andway ereway otnay intendedway otay eanmay anythingway inway articularpay. 

"Atwhay ailsay's eshay arryingcay?" 

"Oursescay, opstay'ls, andway yingflay-jib, irsay." 

"Endsay ethay rway'yals upway! Aylay outway aloftway, erethay, alfhay away ozenday ofway 
yeway--foretopmaststuns'l! Ivelylay, ownay!" 

"Ayeway-aye, irsay!" 

"Akeshay outway atthay aintogalansmay'l! Eetsshay andway acesbray! _ownay_ ymay eartieshay!" 

"Ayeway-aye, irsay!" 

"Ellumhay-a-lee--hard away ortpay! Andstay ybay otay eetmay erhay enwhay eshay omescay! Ortpay, 
ortpay! _Ownay_, enmay! Ithway away illway! Eadstay-y-y-y!" 

"Eadystay itway isway, irsay!" 

Ethay aftray ewdray eyondbay ethay iddlemay ofway ethay iverray; ethay oysbay ointedpay erhay eadhay 
ightray, andway enthay aylay onway eirthay oarsway. Ethay iverray asway otnay ighhay, osay erethay asway 
otnay oremay anthay away otway orway eethray ilemay urrentcay. Ardlyhay away ordway asway aidsay uringday 
ethay extnay eethray-quarters ofway anway ourhay. Ownay ethay aftray asway assingpay eforebay 
ethay istantday owntay. Otway orway eethray immeringglay ightslay owedshay erewhay itway aylay, 
eacefullypay eepingslay, eyondbay ethay aguevay astvay eepsway ofway arstay-gemmed aterway, 
unconsciousway ofway ethay emendoustray eventway atthay asway appeninghay. Ethay Ackblay 
Avengerway oodstay illstay ithway oldedfay armsway, "ookinglay ishay astlay" uponway ethay enescay 
ofway ishay ormerfay oysjay andway ishay aterlay ufferingssay, andway ishingway "eshay" ouldcay eesay 
imhay ownay, abroadway onway ethay ildway easay, acingfay erilpay andway eathday ithway auntlessday 
earthay, oinggay otay ishay oomday ithway away imgray ilesmay onway ishay ipslay. Itway asway utbay 
away allsmay ainstray onway ishay imaginationway otay emoveray Acksonjay's Islandway eyondbay 
eyeway-shot ofway ethay illagevay, andway osay ehay "ookedlay ishay astlay" ithway away okenbray andway 
atisfiedsay earthay. Ethay otherway iratespay ereway ookinglay eirthay astlay, ootay; andway 
eythay allway ookedlay osay onglay atthay eythay amecay earnay ettinglay ethay urrentcay iftdray 
emthay outway ofway ethay angeray ofway ethay islandway. Utbay eythay iscoveredday ethay angerday inway 
imetay, andway ademay iftshay otay avertway itway. Aboutway otway oway'clock inway ethay orningmay ethay 
aftray oundedgray onway ethay arbay otway undredhay yardsway aboveway ethay eadhay ofway ethay islandway, 
andway eythay adedway ackbay andway orthfay untilway eythay adhay andedlay eirthay eightfray. Artpay 
ofway ethay ittlelay aftray's elongingsbay onsistedcay ofway anway oldway ailsay, andway isthay eythay 
eadspray overway away ooknay inway ethay ushesbay orfay away enttay otay eltershay eirthay ovisionspray; 
utbay eythay emselvesthay ouldway eepslay inway ethay openway airway inway oodgay eatherway, asway 
ecamebay outlawsway. 

Eythay uiltbay away irefay againstway ethay idesay ofway away eatgray oglay entytway orway irtythay epsstay 
ithinway ethay ombresay epthsday ofway ethay orestfay, andway enthay ookedcay omesay aconbay inway 
ethay yingfray-pan orfay uppersay, andway usedway upway alfhay ofway ethay orncay "onepay" ockstay 
eythay adhay oughtbray. Itway eemedsay oriousglay ortspay otay ebay eastingfay inway atthay ildway, 
eefray ayway inway ethay irginvay orestfay ofway anway unexploredway andway uninhabitedway islandway, 
arfay omfray ethay auntshay ofway enmay, andway eythay aidsay eythay evernay ouldway eturnray otay 
ivilizationcay. Ethay imbingclay irefay itlay upway eirthay acesfay andway ewthray itsway uddyray 
areglay uponway ethay illaredpay eetray-trunks ofway eirthay orestfay empletay, andway uponway ethay 
arnishedvay oliagefay andway estooningfay inesvay. 

Enwhay ethay astlay ispcray iceslay ofway aconbay asway onegay, andway ethay astlay allowanceway 
ofway orncay onepay evouredday, ethay oysbay etchedstray emselvesthay outway onway ethay assgray, 
illedfay ithway ontentmentcay. Eythay ouldcay avehay oundfay away oolercay aceplay, utbay 
eythay ouldway otnay enyday emselvesthay uchsay away omanticray eaturefay asway ethay oastingray 
ampfirecay. 

"_Ainway't_ itway aygay?" aidsay Oejay. 

"Itway's _utsnay_!" aidsay Omtay. "Atwhay ouldway ethay oysbay aysay ifway eythay ouldcay eesay usway?" 

"Aysay? Ellway, eythay'd ustjay ieday otay ebay erehay--hey, Uckyhay!" 

"Iway eckonray osay," aidsay Uckleberryhay; "anywaysway, Iway'm uitedsay. Iway onday't antway 
othingnay etterbay'n isthay. Iway onday't everway etgay enoughway otay eatway, engay'ally--and erehay 
eythay ancay't omecay andway ickpay atway away ellerfay andway ullyragbay imhay osay." 

"Itway's ustjay ethay ifelay orfay emay," aidsay Omtay. "Youway onday't avehay otay etgay upway, 
orningsmay, andway youway onday't avehay otay ogay otay oolschay, andway ashway, andway allway atthay 
ameblay oolishnessfay. Youway eesay away iratepay onday't avehay otay oday _anythingway_, Oejay, 
enwhay ehay's ashoreway, utbay away ermithay _ehay_ ashay otay ebay ayingpray onsiderablecay, andway 
enthay ehay onday't avehay anyway unfay, anywayway, allway ybay imselfhay atthay ayway." 

"Ohway yesway, atthay's osay," aidsay Oejay, "utbay Iway adnhay't oughtthay uchmay aboutway itway, youway 
owknay. Iway'd away oodgay ealday atherray ebay away iratepay, ownay atthay Iway've iedtray itway." 

"Youway eesay," aidsay Omtay, "eoplepay onday't ogay uchmay onway ermitshay, owadaysnay, ikelay 
eythay usedway otay inway oldway imestay, utbay away iratepay's alwaysway espectedray. Andway 
away ermithay's otgay otay eepslay onway ethay ardesthay aceplay ehay ancay indfay, andway utpay 
ackclothsay andway ashesway onway ishay eadhay, andway andstay outway inway ethay ainray, andway--" 

"Atwhay oesday ehay utpay ackclothsay andway ashesway onway ishay eadhay orfay?" inquiredway Uckhay. 

"Iway onoday. Utbay eythay've _otgay_ otay oday itway. Ermitshay alwaysway oday. Youway'd avehay otay oday 
atthay ifway youway asway away ermithay." 

"Ernday'd ifway Iway ouldway," aidsay Uckhay. 

"Ellway, atwhay ouldway youway oday?" 

"Iway onoday. Utbay Iway ouldnway't oday atthay." 

"Ywhay, Uckhay, youway'd _avehay_ otay. Owhay'd youway etgay aroundway itway?" 

"Ywhay, Iway ustjay ouldnway't andstay itway. Iway'd unray awayway." 

"Unray awayway! Ellway, youway _ouldway_ ebay away icenay oldway ouchslay ofway away ermithay. Youway'd ebay 
away isgraceday." 

Ethay Edray-Handed ademay onay esponseray, eingbay etterbay employedway. Ehay adhay inishedfay 
ouginggay outway away obcay, andway ownay ehay ittedfay away eedway emstay otay itway, oadedlay itway ithway 
obaccotay, andway asway essingpray away oalcay otay ethay argechay andway owingblay away oudclay ofway 
agrantfray okesmay--he asway inway ethay ullfay oomblay ofway uxuriouslay ontentmentcay. Ethay 
otherway iratespay enviedway imhay isthay ajesticmay icevay, andway ecretlysay esolvedray otay 
acquireway itway ortlyshay. Esentlypray Uckhay aidsay: 

"Atwhay oesday iratespay avehay otay oday?" 

Omtay aidsay: 

"Ohway, eythay avehay ustjay away ullybay imetay--take ipsshay andway urnbay emthay, andway etgay ethay 
oneymay andway urybay itway inway awfulway acesplay inway eirthay islandway erewhay erethay's ostsghay 
andway ingsthay otay atchway itway, andway illkay everybodyway inway ethay ipsshay--make 'emway alkway away 
ankplay." 

"Andway eythay arrycay ethay omenway otay ethay islandway," aidsay Oejay; "eythay onday't illkay ethay 
omenway." 

"Onay," assentedway Omtay, "eythay onday't illkay ethay omenway--they're ootay oblenay. Andway 
ethay omenway's alwaysway eautifulbay, ootay. 

"Andway onday't eythay earway ethay ulliestbay othesclay! Ohway onay! Allway oldgay andway ilversay 
andway iday'monds," aidsay Oejay, ithway enthusiasmway. 

"Owhay?" aidsay Uckhay. 

"Ywhay, ethay iratespay." 

Uckhay annedscay ishay ownway othingclay orlornlyfay. 

"Iway eckonray Iway ainway't esseddray ittenfay orfay away iratepay," aidsay ehay, ithway away 
egretfulray athospay inway ishay oicevay; "utbay Iway ainway't otgay onenay utbay esethay." 

Utbay ethay otherway oysbay oldtay imhay ethay inefay othesclay ouldway omecay astfay enoughway, 
afterway eythay ouldshay avehay egunbay eirthay adventuresway. Eythay ademay imhay understandway 
atthay ishay oorpay agsray ouldway oday otay eginbay ithway, oughthay itway asway ustomarycay orfay 
ealthyway iratespay otay artstay ithway away operpray ardrobeway. 

Aduallygray eirthay alktay iedday outway andway owsinessdray eganbay otay ealstay uponway ethay 
eyelidsway ofway ethay ittlelay aifsway. Ethay ipepay oppeddray omfray ethay ingersfay ofway ethay 
Edray-Handed, andway ehay eptslay ethay eepslay ofway ethay onsciencecay-free andway ethay earyway. 
Ethay Errortay ofway ethay Eassay andway ethay Ackblay Avengerway ofway ethay Anishspay Ainmay adhay 
oremay ifficultyday inway ettinggay otay eepslay. Eythay aidsay eirthay ayerspray inwardlyway, 
andway yinglay ownday, incesay erethay asway obodynay erethay ithway authorityway otay akemay emthay 
eelknay andway eciteray aloudway; inway uthtray, eythay adhay away indmay otnay otay aysay emthay atway 
allway, utbay eythay ereway afraidway otay oceedpray otay uchsay engthslay asway atthay, estlay eythay 
ightmay allcay ownday away uddensay andway ecialspay underboltthay omfray eavenhay. Enthay atway 
onceway eythay eachedray andway overedhay uponway ethay imminentway ergevay ofway eepslay--but anway 
intruderway amecay, ownay, atthay ouldway otnay "ownday." Itway asway onsciencecay. Eythay eganbay 
otay eelfay away aguevay earfay atthay eythay adhay eenbay oingday ongwray otay unray awayway; andway 
extnay eythay oughtthay ofway ethay olenstay eatmay, andway enthay ethay ealray orturetay amecay. 
Eythay iedtray otay argueway itway awayway ybay emindingray onsciencecay atthay eythay adhay 
urloinedpay eetmeatssway andway applesway oresscay ofway imestay; utbay onsciencecay asway otnay 
otay ebay appeasedway ybay uchsay inthay ausibilitiesplay; itway eemedsay otay emthay, inway ethay 
endway, atthay erethay asway onay ettinggay aroundway ethay ubbornstay actfay atthay akingtay 
eetmeatssway asway onlyway "ookinghay," ilewhay akingtay aconbay andway amshay andway uchsay 
aluablesvay asway ainplay implesay ealingstay--and erethay asway away ommandcay againstway atthay 
inway ethay Iblebay. Osay eythay inwardlyway esolvedray atthay osay onglay asway eythay emainedray inway 
ethay usinessbay, eirthay iraciespay ouldshay otnay againway ebay ulliedsay ithway ethay 
imecray ofway ealingstay. Enthay onsciencecay antedgray away ucetray, andway esethay uriouslycay 
inconsistentway iratespay ellfay eacefullypay otay eepslay. 




APTERCHAY IVXAY 

ENWHAY Omtay awokeway inway ethay orningmay, ehay onderedway erewhay ehay asway. Ehay atsay upway andway 
ubbedray ishay eyesway andway ookedlay aroundway. Enthay ehay omprehendedcay. Itway asway ethay oolcay 
aygray awnday, andway erethay asway away eliciousday ensesay ofway eposeray andway eacepay inway ethay 
eepday ervadingpay almcay andway ilencesay ofway ethay oodsway. Otnay away eaflay irredstay; otnay 
away oundsay obtrudedway uponway eatgray Aturenay's editationmay. Eadedbay ewdropsday oodstay 
uponway ethay eaveslay andway assesgray. Away itewhay ayerlay ofway ashesway overedcay ethay irefay, 
andway away inthay ueblay eathbray ofway okesmay oseray aightstray intoway ethay airway. Oejay andway Uckhay 
illstay eptslay. 

Ownay, arfay awayway inway ethay oodsway away irdbay alledcay; anotherway answeredway; esentlypray 
ethay ammeringhay ofway away oodpeckerway asway eardhay. Aduallygray ethay oolcay imday aygray 
ofway ethay orningmay itenedwhay, andway asway aduallygray oundssay ultipliedmay andway ifelay 
anifestedmay itselfway. Ethay arvelmay ofway Aturenay akingshay offway eepslay andway oinggay 
otay orkway unfoldedway itselfway otay ethay usingmay oybay. Away ittlelay eengray ormway amecay 
awlingcray overway away ewyday eaflay, iftinglay otway-thirds ofway ishay odybay intoway ethay airway 
omfray imetay otay imetay andway "iffingsnay aroundway," enthay oceedingpray againway--for ehay 
asway easuringmay, Omtay aidsay; andway enwhay ethay ormway approachedway imhay, ofway itsway ownway 
accordway, ehay atsay asway illstay asway away onestay, ithway ishay opeshay isingray andway allingfay, 
ybay urnstay, asway ethay eaturecray illstay amecay owardtay imhay orway eemedsay inclinedway otay 
ogay elsewhereway; andway enwhay atway astlay itway onsideredcay away ainfulpay omentmay ithway itsway 
urvedcay odybay inway ethay airway andway enthay amecay ecisivelyday ownday uponway Omtay's eglay andway 
eganbay away ourneyjay overway imhay, ishay olewhay earthay asway adglay--for atthay eantmay atthay 
ehay asway oinggay otay avehay away ewnay uitsay ofway othesclay--without ethay adowshay ofway away 
oubtday away audygay iraticalpay uniformway. Ownay away ocessionpray ofway antsway appearedway, 
omfray owherenay inway articularpay, andway entway aboutway eirthay aborslay; oneway uggledstray 
anfullymay ybay ithway away eadday iderspay ivefay imestay asway igbay asway itselfway inway itsway armsway, 
andway uggedlay itway aightstray upway away eetray-trunk. Away ownbray ottedspay adylay-bug imbedclay 
ethay izzyday eighthay ofway away assgray adeblay, andway Omtay entbay ownday oseclay otay itway andway 
aidsay, "Adylay-bug, adylay-bug, yflay awayway omehay, yourway ousehay isway onway irefay, yourway 
ildrenchay's aloneway," andway eshay ooktay ingway andway entway offway otay eesay aboutway itway--which 
idday otnay urprisesay ethay oybay, orfay ehay ewknay ofway oldway atthay isthay insectway asway 
edulouscray aboutway onflagrationscay, andway ehay adhay actisedpray uponway itsway implicitysay 
oremay anthay onceway. Away umblebugtay amecay extnay, eavinghay urdilystay atway itsway allbay, andway 
Omtay ouchedtay ethay eaturecray, otay eesay itway utshay itsway egslay againstway itsway odybay 
andway etendpray otay ebay eadday. Ethay irdsbay ereway airlyfay iotingray ybay isthay imetay. Away 
atbirdcay, ethay Orthernnay ockermay, itlay inway away eetray overway Omtay's eadhay, andway illedtray 
outway erhay imitationsway ofway erhay eighborsnay inway away aptureray ofway enjoymentway; enthay 
away illshray ayjay eptsway ownday, away ashflay ofway ueblay ameflay, andway oppedstay onway away igtway 
almostway ithinway ethay oybay's eachray, ockedcay ishay eadhay otay oneway idesay andway eyedway ethay 
angersstray ithway away onsumingcay uriositycay; away aygray uirrelsqay andway away igbay ellowfay 
ofway ethay "oxfay" indkay amecay urryingskay alongway, ittingsay upway atway intervalsway otay 
inspectway andway atterchay atway ethay oysbay, orfay ethay ildway ingsthay adhay obablypray evernay 
eensay away umanhay eingbay eforebay andway arcelyscay ewknay etherwhay otay ebay afraidway orway otnay. 
Allway Aturenay asway ideway awakeway andway irringstay, ownay; onglay anceslay ofway unlightsay 
iercedpay ownday oughthray ethay enseday oliagefay arfay andway earnay, andway away ewfay 
utterfliesbay amecay utteringflay uponway ethay enescay. 

Omtay irredstay upway ethay otherway iratespay andway eythay allway atteredclay awayway ithway 
away outshay, andway inway away inutemay orway otway ereway ippedstray andway asingchay afterway andway 
umblingtay overway eachway otherway inway ethay allowshay impidlay aterway ofway ethay itewhay 
andbarsay. Eythay eltfay onay onginglay orfay ethay ittlelay illagevay eepingslay inway ethay 
istanceday eyondbay ethay ajesticmay asteway ofway aterway. Away agrantvay urrentcay orway away 
ightslay iseray inway ethay iverray adhay arriedcay offway eirthay aftray, utbay isthay onlyway 
atifiedgray emthay, incesay itsway oinggay asway omethingsay ikelay urningbay ethay idgebray 
etweenbay emthay andway ivilizationcay. 

Eythay amecay ackbay otay ampcay onderfullyway efreshedray, adglay-hearted, andway 
avenousray; andway eythay oonsay adhay ethay ampcay-fire azingblay upway againway. Uckhay oundfay away 
ingspray ofway earclay oldcay aterway oseclay ybay, andway ethay oysbay ademay upscay ofway oadbray oakway 
orway ickoryhay eaveslay, andway eltfay atthay aterway, eetenedsway ithway uchsay away ildwoodway 
armchay asway atthay, ouldway ebay away oodgay enoughway ubstitutesay orfay offeecay. Ilewhay Oejay 
asway icingslay aconbay orfay eakfastbray, Omtay andway Uckhay askedway imhay otay oldhay onway away 
inutemay; eythay eppedstay otay away omisingpray ooknay inway ethay iverray-bank andway ewthray inway 
eirthay ineslay; almostway immediatelyway eythay adhay ewardray. Oejay adhay otnay adhay imetay 
otay etgay impatientway eforebay eythay ereway ackbay againway ithway omesay andsomehay assbay, 
away ouplecay ofway unsay-perch andway away allsmay atfishcay--provisions enoughway orfay uiteqay away 
amilyfay. Eythay iedfray ethay ishfay ithway ethay aconbay, andway ereway astonishedway; orfay 
onay ishfay adhay everway eemedsay osay eliciousday eforebay. Eythay idday otnay owknay atthay ethay 
uickerqay away eshfray-water ishfay isway onway ethay irefay afterway ehay isway aughtcay ethay etterbay 
ehay isway; andway eythay eflectedray ittlelay uponway atwhay away aucesay openway-air eepingslay, 
openway-air exerciseway, athingbay, andway away argelay ingredientway ofway ungerhay akemay, ootay. 

Eythay aylay aroundway inway ethay adeshay, afterway eakfastbray, ilewhay Uckhay adhay away okesmay, 
andway enthay entway offway oughthray ethay oodsway onway anway exploringway expeditionway. Eythay 
ampedtray aylygay alongway, overway ecayingday ogslay, oughthray angledtay underbrushway, 
amongway olemnsay onarchsmay ofway ethay orestfay, unghay omfray eirthay ownscray otay ethay 
oundgray ithway away oopingdray egaliaray ofway apegray-vines. Ownay andway enthay eythay amecay 
uponway ugsnay ooksnay arpetedcay ithway assgray andway eweledjay ithway owersflay. 

Eythay oundfay entyplay ofway ingsthay otay ebay elightedday ithway, utbay othingnay otay ebay 
astonishedway atway. Eythay iscoveredday atthay ethay islandway asway aboutway eethray ilesmay 
onglay andway away uarterqay ofway away ilemay ideway, andway atthay ethay oreshay itway aylay osestclay otay 
asway onlyway eparatedsay omfray itway ybay away arrownay annelchay ardlyhay otway undredhay yardsway 
ideway. Eythay ooktay away imsway aboutway everyway ourhay, osay itway asway oseclay uponway ethay iddlemay 
ofway ethay afternoonway enwhay eythay otgay ackbay otay ampcay. Eythay ereway ootay ungryhay otay 
opstay otay ishfay, utbay eythay aredfay umptuouslysay uponway oldcay amhay, andway enthay ewthray 
emselvesthay ownday inway ethay adeshay otay alktay. Utbay ethay alktay oonsay eganbay otay agdray, 
andway enthay iedday. Ethay illnessstay, ethay olemnitysay atthay oodedbray inway ethay oodsway, 
andway ethay ensesay ofway onelinesslay, eganbay otay elltay uponway ethay iritsspay ofway ethay oysbay. 
Eythay ellfay otay inkingthay. Away ortsay ofway undefinedway onginglay eptcray uponway emthay. Isthay 
ooktay imday apeshay, esentlypray--it asway uddingbay omesicknesshay. Evenway Innfay ethay 
Edray-Handed asway eamingdray ofway ishay oorstepsday andway emptyway ogsheadshay. Utbay eythay 
ereway allway ashamedway ofway eirthay eaknessway, andway onenay asway avebray enoughway otay eakspay 
ishay oughtthay. 

Orfay omesay imetay, ownay, ethay oysbay adhay eenbay ullyday onsciouscay ofway away eculiarpay 
oundsay inway ethay istanceday, ustjay asway oneway ometimessay isway ofway ethay ickingtay ofway away 
ockclay ichwhay ehay akestay onay istinctday otenay ofway. Utbay ownay isthay ysteriousmay oundsay 
ecamebay oremay onouncedpray, andway orcedfay away ecognitionray. Ethay oysbay artedstay, 
ancedglay atway eachway otherway, andway enthay eachway assumedway away isteninglay attitudeway. Erethay 
asway away onglay ilencesay, ofoundpray andway unbrokenway; enthay away eepday, ullensay oombay amecay 
oatingflay ownday outway ofway ethay istanceday. 

"Atwhay isway itway!" exclaimedway Oejay, underway ishay eathbray. 

"Iway onderway," aidsay Omtay inway away isperwhay. 

"'Aintay't underthay," aidsay Uckleberryhay, inway anway awedway onetay, "ecuzbay underthay--" 

"Arkhay!" aidsay Omtay. "Istenlay--don't alktay." 

Eythay aitedway away imetay atthay eemedsay anway ageway, andway enthay ethay amesay uffledmay oombay 
oubledtray ethay olemnsay ushhay. 

"Etlay's ogay andway eesay." 

Eythay angspray otay eirthay eetfay andway urriedhay otay ethay oreshay owardtay ethay owntay. Eythay 
artedpay ethay ushesbay onway ethay ankbay andway eeredpay outway overway ethay aterway. Ethay ittlelay 
eamstay erryfay-boat asway aboutway away ilemay elowbay ethay illagevay, iftingdray ithway ethay 
urrentcay. Erhay oadbray eckday eemedsay owdedcray ithway eoplepay. Erethay ereway away eatgray 
anymay iffsskay owingray aboutway orway oatingflay ithway ethay eamstray inway ethay eighborhoodnay 
ofway ethay erryboatfay, utbay ethay oysbay ouldcay otnay etermineday atwhay ethay enmay inway 
emthay ereway oingday. Esentlypray away eatgray etjay ofway itewhay okesmay urstbay omfray ethay 
erryboatfay's idesay, andway asway itway expandedway andway oseray inway away azylay oudclay, atthay amesay 
ullday obthray ofway oundsay asway ornebay otay ethay istenerslay againway. 

"Iway owknay ownay!" exclaimedway Omtay; "omebodysay's owndeddray!" 

"Atthay's itway!" aidsay Uckhay; "eythay oneday atthay astlay ummersay, enwhay Illbay Urnertay
