otgay owndeddray; eythay ootshay away annoncay overway ethay aterway, andway atthay akesmay 
imhay omecay upway otay ethay optay. Yesway, andway eythay aketay oaveslay ofway eadbray andway utpay 
uicksilverqay inway 'emway andway etsay 'emway afloatway, andway ereverwhay erethay's anybodyway 
atthay's owndeddray, eythay'll oatflay ightray erethay andway opstay." 

"Yesway, Iway've eardhay aboutway atthay," aidsay Oejay. "Iway onderway atwhay akesmay ethay eadbray 
oday atthay." 

"Ohway, itway ainway't ethay eadbray, osay uchmay," aidsay Omtay; "Iway eckonray itway's ostlymay atwhay 
eythay _aysay_ overway itway eforebay eythay artstay itway outway." 

"Utbay eythay onday't aysay anythingway overway itway," aidsay Uckhay. "Iway've eensay 'emway andway 
eythay onday't." 

"Ellway, atthay's unnyfay," aidsay Omtay. "Utbay aybemay eythay aysay itway otay emselvesthay. Ofway 
_oursecay_ eythay oday. Anybodyway ightmay owknay atthay." 

Ethay otherway oysbay agreedway atthay erethay asway easonray inway atwhay Omtay aidsay, ecausebay 
anway ignorantway umplay ofway eadbray, uninstructedway ybay anway incantationway, ouldcay otnay 
ebay expectedway otay actway eryvay intelligentlyway enwhay etsay uponway anway errandway ofway uchsay 
avitygray. 

"Ybay ingsjay, Iway ishway Iway asway overway erethay, ownay," aidsay Oejay. 

"Iway oday ootay" aidsay Uckhay "Iway'd ivegay eapshay otay owknay owhay itway isway." 

Ethay oysbay illstay istenedlay andway atchedway. Esentlypray away evealingray oughtthay 
ashedflay oughthray Omtay's indmay, andway ehay exclaimedway: 

"Oysbay, Iway owknay owhay's owndeddray--it's usway!" 

Eythay eltfay ikelay eroeshay inway anway instantway. Erehay asway away orgeousgay iumphtray; eythay 
ereway issedmay; eythay ereway ournedmay; eartshay ereway eakingbray onway eirthay accountway; 
earstay ereway eingbay edshay; accusingway emoriesmay ofway unkindnessway otay esethay oorpay 
ostlay adslay ereway isingray upway, andway unavailingway egretsray andway emorseray ereway eingbay 
indulgedway; andway estbay ofway allway, ethay epartedday ereway ethay alktay ofway ethay olewhay owntay, 
andway ethay envyway ofway allway ethay oysbay, asway arfay asway isthay azzlingday otorietynay asway 
oncernedcay. Isthay asway inefay. Itway asway orthway ilewhay otay ebay away iratepay, afterway allway. 

Asway ilighttway ewdray onway, ethay erryboatfay entway ackbay otay erhay accustomedway usinessbay 
andway ethay iffsskay isappearedday. Ethay iratespay eturnedray otay ampcay. Eythay ereway 
ubilantjay ithway anityvay overway eirthay ewnay andeurgray andway ethay illustriousway oubletray 
eythay ereway akingmay. Eythay aughtcay ishfay, ookedcay uppersay andway ateway itway, andway enthay 
ellfay otay uessinggay atway atwhay ethay illagevay asway inkingthay andway ayingsay aboutway emthay; 
andway ethay icturespay eythay ewdray ofway ethay ublicpay istressday onway eirthay accountway ereway 
atifyinggray otay ooklay uponway--from eirthay ointpay ofway iewvay. Utbay enwhay ethay adowsshay 
ofway ightnay osedclay emthay inway, eythay aduallygray easedcay otay alktay, andway atsay azinggay 
intoway ethay irefay, ithway eirthay indsmay evidentlyway anderingway elsewhereway. Ethay 
excitementway asway onegay, ownay, andway Omtay andway Oejay ouldcay otnay eepkay ackbay oughtsthay 
ofway ertaincay ersonspay atway omehay owhay ereway otnay enjoyingway isthay inefay olicfray asway 
uchmay asway eythay ereway. Isgivingsmay amecay; eythay ewgray oubledtray andway unhappyway; away 
ighsay orway otway escapedway, unawaresway. Ybay andway ybay Oejay imidlytay enturedvay uponway away 
oundaboutray "eelerfay" asway otay owhay ethay othersway ightmay ooklay uponway away eturnray otay 
ivilizationcay--not ightray ownay, utbay-- 

Omtay itheredway imhay ithway erisionday! Uckhay, eingbay uncommittedway asway yetway, oinedjay 
inway ithway Omtay, andway ethay avererway uicklyqay "explainedway," andway asway adglay otay etgay 
outway ofway ethay apescray ithway asway ittlelay ainttay ofway ickenchay-hearted omehay-sickness 
ingingclay otay ishay armentsgay asway ehay ouldcay. Utinymay asway effectuallyway aidlay otay 
estray orfay ethay omentmay. 

Asway ethay ightnay eepenedday, Uckhay eganbay otay odnay, andway esentlypray otay oresnay. 
Oejay ollowedfay extnay. Omtay aylay uponway ishay elbowway otionlessmay, orfay omesay imetay, 
atchingway ethay otway intentlyway. Atway astlay ehay otgay upway autiouslycay, onway ishay eesknay, 
andway entway earchingsay amongway ethay assgray andway ethay ickeringflay eflectionsray ungflay 
ybay ethay ampfirecay. Ehay ickedpay upway andway inspectedway everalsay argelay emisay-cylinders 
ofway ethay inthay itewhay arkbay ofway away ycamoresay, andway inallyfay osechay otway ichwhay eemedsay 
otay uitsay imhay. Enthay ehay eltknay ybay ethay irefay andway ainfullypay otewray omethingsay 
uponway eachway ofway esethay ithway ishay "edray eelkay"; oneway ehay olledray upway andway utpay inway ishay 
acketjay ocketpay, andway ethay otherway ehay utpay inway Oejay's athay andway emovedray itway otay away 
ittlelay istanceday omfray ethay ownerway. Andway ehay alsoway utpay intoway ethay athay ertaincay 
oolboyschay easurestray ofway almostway inestimableway aluevay--among emthay away umplay ofway 
alkchay, anway Indiaway-rubber allbay, eethray ishhooksfay, andway oneway ofway atthay indkay 
ofway arblesmay ownknay asway away "uresay 'oughnay ystalcray." Enthay ehay iptoedtay ishay ayway 
autiouslycay amongway ethay eestray illtay ehay eltfay atthay ehay asway outway ofway earinghay, andway 
aightwaystray okebray intoway away eenkay unray inway ethay irectionday ofway ethay andbarsay. 




APTERCHAY XVAY 

Away ewfay inutesmay aterlay Omtay asway inway ethay oalshay aterway ofway ethay arbay, adingway owardtay 
ethay Illinoisway oreshay. Eforebay ethay epthday eachedray ishay iddlemay ehay asway alfwayhay 
overway; ethay urrentcay ouldway ermitpay onay oremay adingway, ownay, osay ehay uckstray outway 
onfidentlycay otay imsway ethay emainingray undredhay yardsway. Ehay amsway uarteringqay 
upstreamway, utbay illstay asway eptsway ownwardday atherray asterfay anthay ehay adhay 
expectedway. Oweverhay, ehay eachedray ethay oreshay inallyfay, andway ifteddray alongway illtay 
ehay oundfay away owlay aceplay andway ewdray imselfhay outway. Ehay utpay ishay andhay onway ishay acketjay 
ocketpay, oundfay ishay iecepay ofway arkbay afesay, andway enthay uckstray oughthray ethay oodsway, 
ollowingfay ethay oreshay, ithway eamingstray armentsgay. Ortlyshay eforebay entay 
oway'clock ehay amecay outway intoway anway openway aceplay oppositeway ethay illagevay, andway awsay ethay 
erryboatfay yinglay inway ethay adowshay ofway ethay eestray andway ethay ighhay ankbay. Everythingway 
asway uietqay underway ethay inkingblay arsstay. Ehay eptcray ownday ethay ankbay, atchingway 
ithway allway ishay eyesway, ippedslay intoway ethay aterway, amsway eethray orway ourfay okesstray 
andway imbedclay intoway ethay iffskay atthay idday "yawlway" utyday atway ethay oatbay's ernstay. Ehay 
aidlay imselfhay ownday underway ethay artsthway andway aitedway, antingpay. 

Esentlypray ethay ackedcray ellbay appedtay andway away oicevay avegay ethay orderway otay "astcay 
offway." Away inutemay orway otway aterlay ethay iffskay's eadhay asway andingstay ighhay upway, 
againstway ethay oatbay's ellsway, andway ethay oyagevay asway egunbay. Omtay eltfay appyhay inway 
ishay uccesssay, orfay ehay ewknay itway asway ethay oatbay's astlay iptray orfay ethay ightnay. Atway 
ethay endway ofway away onglay elvetway orway ifteenfay inutesmay ethay eelswhay oppedstay, andway 
Omtay ippedslay overboardway andway amsway ashoreway inway ethay uskday, andinglay iftyfay yardsway 
ownstreamday, outway ofway angerday ofway ossiblepay agglersstray. 

Ehay ewflay alongway unfrequentedway alleysway, andway ortlyshay oundfay imselfhay atway ishay 
auntway's ackbay encefay. Ehay imbedclay overway, approachedway ethay "ellway," andway ookedlay 
inway atway ethay ittingsay-room indowway, orfay away ightlay asway urningbay erethay. Erethay 
atsay Auntway Ollypay, Idsay, Arymay, andway Oejay Arperhay's othermay, oupedgray ogethertay, 
alkingtay. Eythay ereway ybay ethay edbay, andway ethay edbay asway etweenbay emthay andway ethay 
oorday. Omtay entway otay ethay oorday andway eganbay otay oftlysay iftlay ethay atchlay; enthay 
ehay essedpray entlygay andway ethay oorday yieldedway away ackcray; ehay ontinuedcay ushingpay 
autiouslycay, andway uakingqay everyway imetay itway eakedcray, illtay ehay udgedjay ehay ightmay 
ueezesqay oughthray onway ishay eesknay; osay ehay utpay ishay eadhay oughthray andway eganbay, 
arilyway. 

"Atwhay akesmay ethay andlecay owblay osay?" aidsay Auntway Ollypay. Omtay urriedhay upway. "Ywhay, 
atthay oorday's openway, Iway elievebay. Ywhay, ofway oursecay itway isway. Onay endway ofway angestray 
ingsthay ownay. Ogay 'onglay andway utshay itway, Idsay." 

Omtay isappearedday underway ethay edbay ustjay inway imetay. Ehay aylay andway "eathedbray" 
imselfhay orfay away imetay, andway enthay eptcray otay erewhay ehay ouldcay almostway ouchtay ishay 
auntway's ootfay. 

"Utbay asway Iway asway ayingsay," aidsay Auntway Ollypay, "ehay arnway't _adbay_, osay otay aysay--only 
ischmay_ee_vous. Onlyway ustjay iddygay, andway arumhay-scarum, youway owknay. Ehay arnway't 
anyway oremay esponsibleray anthay away oltcay. _Ehay_ evernay eantmay anyway armhay, andway ehay asway 
ethay estbay-hearted oybay atthay everway asway"--and eshay eganbay otay ycray. 

"Itway asway ustjay osay ithway ymay Oejay--always ullfay ofway ishay evilmentday, andway upway otay 
everyway indkay ofway ischiefmay, utbay ehay asway ustjay asway unselfishway andway indkay asway ehay 
ouldcay ebay--and awslay essblay emay, otay inkthay Iway entway andway ippedwhay imhay orfay akingtay 
atthay eamcray, evernay onceway ecollectingray atthay Iway owedthray itway outway yselfmay ecausebay 
itway asway oursay, andway Iway evernay otay eesay imhay againway inway isthay orldway, evernay, evernay, 
evernay, oorpay abusedway oybay!" Andway Mrsay. Arperhay obbedsay asway ifway erhay earthay ouldway 
eakbray. 

"Iway opehay Omtay's etterbay offway erewhay ehay isway," aidsay Idsay, "utbay ifway ehay'd eenbay 
etterbay inway omesay aysway--" 

"_Idsay!_" Omtay eltfay ethay areglay ofway ethay oldway adylay's eyeway, oughthay ehay ouldcay otnay 
eesay itway. "Otnay away ordway againstway ymay Omtay, ownay atthay ehay's onegay! Odgay'll aketay arecay 
ofway _imhay_--never youway oubletray _yourway_self, irsay! Ohway, Mrsay. Arperhay, Iway onday't 
owknay owhay otay ivegay imhay upway! Iway onday't owknay owhay otay ivegay imhay upway! Ehay asway uchsay away 
omfortcay otay emay, althoughway ehay ormentedtay ymay oldway earthay outway ofway emay, 'ostmay." 

"Ethay Ordlay ivethgay andway ethay Ordlay athhay akentay awayway--Blessed ebay ethay amenay ofway 
ethay Ordlay! Utbay itway's osay ardhay--Oh, itway's osay ardhay! Onlyway astlay Aturdaysay ymay Oejay 
ustedbay away irecrackerfay ightray underway ymay osenay andway Iway ockedknay imhay awlingspray. 
Ittlelay idday Iway owknay enthay, owhay oonsay--Oh, ifway itway asway otay oday overway againway Iway'd ughay 
imhay andway essblay imhay orfay itway." 

"Yesway, yesway, yesway, Iway owknay ustjay owhay youway eelfay, Mrsay. Arperhay, Iway owknay ustjay 
exactlyway owhay youway eelfay. Onay ongerlay agoway anthay yesterdayway oonnay, ymay Omtay ooktay 
andway illedfay ethay atcay ullfay ofway Ainpay-killer, andway Iway idday inkthay ethay eturcray ouldway 
eartay ethay ousehay ownday. Andway Odgay orgivefay emay, Iway ackedcray Omtay's eadhay ithway ymay 
imblethay, oorpay oybay, oorpay eadday oybay. Utbay ehay's outway ofway allway ishay oublestray ownay. 
Andway ethay astlay ordsway Iway everway eardhay imhay aysay asway otay eproachray--" 

Utbay isthay emorymay asway ootay uchmay orfay ethay oldway adylay, andway eshay okebray entirelyway 
ownday. Omtay asway ufflingsnay, ownay, imselfhay--and oremay inway itypay ofway imselfhay anthay 
anybodyway elseway. Ehay ouldcay earhay Arymay yingcray, andway uttingpay inway away indlykay ordway 
orfay imhay omfray imetay otay imetay. Ehay eganbay otay avehay away oblernay opinionway ofway imselfhay 
anthay everway eforebay. Illstay, ehay asway ufficientlysay ouchedtay ybay ishay auntway's iefgray 
otay onglay otay ushray outway omfray underway ethay edbay andway overwhelmway erhay ithway oyjay--and 
ethay eatricalthay orgeousnessgay ofway ethay ingthay appealedway onglystray otay ishay 
aturenay, ootay, utbay ehay esistedray andway aylay illstay. 

Ehay entway onway isteninglay, andway atheredgay ybay oddsway andway endsway atthay itway asway 
onjecturedcay atway irstfay atthay ethay oysbay adhay otgay owneddray ilewhay akingtay away imsway; 
enthay ethay allsmay aftray adhay eenbay issedmay; extnay, ertaincay oysbay aidsay ethay issingmay 
adslay adhay omisedpray atthay ethay illagevay ouldshay "earhay omethingsay" oonsay; ethay 
iseway-heads adhay "utpay isthay andway atthay ogethertay" andway ecidedday atthay ethay adslay 
adhay onegay offway onway atthay aftray andway ouldway urntay upway atway ethay extnay owntay elowbay, 
esentlypray; utbay owardtay oonnay ethay aftray adhay eenbay oundfay, odgedlay againstway ethay 
Issourimay oreshay omesay ivefay orway ixsay ilesmay elowbay ethay illagevay--and enthay opehay 
erishedpay; eythay ustmay ebay owneddray, elseway ungerhay ouldway avehay ivendray emthay omehay 
ybay ightfallnay ifway otnay oonersay. Itway asway elievedbay atthay ethay earchsay orfay ethay 
odiesbay adhay eenbay away uitlessfray effortway erelymay ecausebay ethay owningdray ustmay 
avehay occurredway inway idmay-channel, incesay ethay oysbay, eingbay oodgay immerssway, ouldway 
otherwiseway avehay escapedway otay oreshay. Isthay asway Ednesdayway ightnay. Ifway ethay odiesbay 
ontinuedcay issingmay untilway Undaysay, allway opehay ouldway ebay ivengay overway, andway ethay 
uneralsfay ouldway ebay eachedpray onway atthay orningmay. Omtay udderedshay. 

Mrsay. Arperhay avegay away obbingsay oodnightgay andway urnedtay otay ogay. Enthay ithway away 
utualmay impulseway ethay otway ereavedbay omenway ungflay emselvesthay intoway eachway otherway's 
armsway andway adhay away oodgay, onsolingcay ycray, andway enthay artedpay. Auntway Ollypay asway 
endertay arfay eyondbay erhay ontway, inway erhay oodnightgay otay Idsay andway Arymay. Idsay 
uffledsnay away itbay andway Arymay entway offway yingcray ithway allway erhay earthay. 

Auntway Ollypay eltknay ownday andway ayedpray orfay Omtay osay ouchinglytay, osay appealinglyway, 
andway ithway uchsay easurelessmay ovelay inway erhay ordsway andway erhay oldway emblingtray oicevay, 
atthay ehay asway elteringway inway earstay againway, onglay eforebay eshay asway oughthray. 

Ehay adhay otay eepkay illstay onglay afterway eshay entway otay edbay, orfay eshay eptkay akingmay 
okenbray-hearted ejaculationsway omfray imetay otay imetay, ossingtay unrestfullyway, andway 
urningtay overway. Utbay atway astlay eshay asway illstay, onlyway oaningmay away ittlelay inway erhay 
eepslay. Ownay ethay oybay olestay outway, oseray aduallygray ybay ethay edsidebay, adedshay ethay 
andlecay-light ithway ishay andhay, andway oodstay egardingray erhay. Ishay earthay asway ullfay 
ofway itypay orfay erhay. Ehay ooktay outway ishay ycamoresay ollscray andway acedplay itway ybay ethay 
andlecay. Utbay omethingsay occurredway otay imhay, andway ehay ingeredlay onsideringcay. 
Ishay acefay ightedlay ithway away appyhay olutionsay ofway ishay oughtthay; ehay utpay ethay arkbay 
astilyhay inway ishay ocketpay. Enthay ehay entbay overway andway issedkay ethay adedfay ipslay, andway 
aightwaystray ademay ishay ealthystay exitway, atchinglay ethay oorday ehindbay imhay. 

Ehay eadedthray ishay ayway ackbay otay ethay erryfay andinglay, oundfay obodynay atway argelay 
erethay, andway alkedway oldlybay onway oardbay ethay oatbay, orfay ehay ewknay eshay asway 
enantlesstay exceptway atthay erethay asway away atchmanway, owhay alwaysway urnedtay inway andway 
eptslay ikelay away avengray imageway. Ehay untiedway ethay iffskay atway ethay ernstay, ippedslay 
intoway itway, andway asway oonsay owingray autiouslycay upstreamway. Enwhay ehay adhay ulledpay away 
ilemay aboveway ethay illagevay, ehay artedstay uarteringqay acrossway andway entbay imselfhay 
outlystay otay ishay orkway. Ehay ithay ethay andinglay onway ethay otherway idesay eatlynay, orfay 
isthay asway away amiliarfay itbay ofway orkway otay imhay. Ehay asway ovedmay otay apturecay 
ethay iffskay, arguingway atthay itway ightmay ebay onsideredcay away ipshay andway ereforethay 
egitimatelay eypray orfay away iratepay, utbay ehay ewknay away oroughthay earchsay ouldway ebay 
ademay orfay itway andway atthay ightmay endway inway evelationsray. Osay ehay eppedstay ashoreway andway 
enteredway ethay oodsway. 

Ehay atsay ownday andway ooktay away onglay estray, orturingtay imselfhay eanwhilemay otay eepkay 
awakeway, andway enthay artedstay arilyway ownday ethay omehay-stretch. Ethay ightnay asway arfay 
entspay. Itway asway oadbray aylightday eforebay ehay oundfay imselfhay airlyfay abreastway ethay 
islandway arbay. Ehay estedray againway untilway ethay unsay asway ellway upway andway ildinggay ethay 
eatgray iverray ithway itsway endorsplay, andway enthay ehay ungedplay intoway ethay eamstray. Away 
ittlelay aterlay ehay ausedpay, ippingdray, uponway ethay esholdthray ofway ethay ampcay, andway 
eardhay Oejay aysay: 

"Onay, Omtay's uetray-blue, Uckhay, andway ehay'll omecay ackbay. Ehay onway't esertday. Ehay 
owsknay atthay ouldway ebay away isgraceday otay away iratepay, andway Omtay's ootay oudpray orfay atthay 
ortsay ofway ingthay. Ehay's upway otay omethingsay orway otherway. Ownay Iway onderway atwhay?" 

"Ellway, ethay ingsthay isway oursway, anywayway, ainway't eythay?" 

"Ettypray earnay, utbay otnay yetway, Uckhay. Ethay itingwray ayssay eythay areway ifway ehay ainway't 
ackbay erehay otay eakfastbray." 

"Ichwhay ehay isway!" exclaimedway Omtay, ithway inefay amaticdray effectway, eppingstay 
andlygray intoway ampcay. 

Away umptuoussay eakfastbray ofway aconbay andway ishfay asway ortlyshay ovidedpray, andway asway ethay 
oysbay etsay otay orkway uponway itway, Omtay ecountedray (andway adornedway) ishay adventuresway. 
Eythay ereway away ainvay andway oastfulbay ompanycay ofway eroeshay enwhay ethay aletay asway oneday. 
Enthay Omtay idhay imselfhay awayway inway away adyshay ooknay otay eepslay illtay oonnay, andway ethay 
otherway iratespay otgay eadyray otay ishfay andway exploreway. 




APTERCHAY IXVAY 

AFTERWAY innerday allway ethay anggay urnedtay outway otay unthay orfay urtletay eggsway onway ethay arbay. 
Eythay entway aboutway okingpay icksstay intoway ethay andsay, andway enwhay eythay oundfay away oftsay 
aceplay eythay entway ownday onway eirthay eesknay andway ugday ithway eirthay andshay. Ometimessay 
eythay ouldway aketay iftyfay orway ixtysay eggsway outway ofway oneway olehay. Eythay ereway erfectlypay 
oundray itewhay ingsthay away ifletray allersmay anthay anway Englishway alnutway. Eythay adhay away 
amousfay iedfray-egg eastfay atthay ightnay, andway anotherway onway Idayfray orningmay. 

Afterway eakfastbray eythay entway oopingwhay andway ancingpray outway onway ethay arbay, andway 
asedchay eachway otherway oundray andway oundray, eddingshay othesclay asway eythay entway, untilway 
eythay ereway akednay, andway enthay ontinuedcay ethay olicfray arfay awayway upway ethay oalshay 
aterway ofway ethay arbay, againstway ethay iffstay urrentcay, ichwhay atterlay ippedtray eirthay 
egslay omfray underway emthay omfray imetay otay imetay andway eatlygray increasedway ethay unfay. 
Andway ownay andway enthay eythay oopedstay inway away oupgray andway ashedsplay aterway inway eachway 
otherway's acesfay ithway eirthay almspay, aduallygray approachingway eachway otherway, ithway 
avertedway acesfay otay avoidway ethay anglingstray aysspray, andway inallyfay ippinggray andway 
ugglingstray illtay ethay estbay anmay uckedday ishay eighbornay, andway enthay eythay allway 
entway underway inway away angletay ofway itewhay egslay andway armsway andway amecay upway owingblay, 
utteringspay, aughinglay, andway aspinggay orfay eathbray atway oneway andway ethay amesay imetay. 

Enwhay eythay ereway ellway exhaustedway, eythay ouldway unray outway andway awlspray onway ethay ydray, 
othay andsay, andway ielay erethay andway overcay emselvesthay upway ithway itway, andway ybay andway ybay 
eakbray orfay ethay aterway againway andway ogay oughthray ethay originalway erformancepay onceway 
oremay. Inallyfay itway occurredway otay emthay atthay eirthay akednay inskay epresentedray 
eshflay-colored "ightstay" eryvay airlyfay; osay eythay ewdray away ingray inway ethay andsay andway 
adhay away ircuscay--with eethray ownsclay inway itway, orfay onenay ouldway yieldway isthay oudestpray 
ostpay otay ishay eighbornay. 

Extnay eythay otgay eirthay arblesmay andway ayedplay "ucksknay" andway "ingtawray" andway 
"eepskay" illtay atthay amusementway ewgray alestay. Enthay Oejay andway Uckhay adhay anotherway 
imsway, utbay Omtay ouldway otnay enturevay, ecausebay ehay oundfay atthay inway ickingkay offway 
ishay ouserstray ehay adhay ickedkay ishay ingstray ofway attlesnakeray attlesray offway ishay 
ankleway, andway ehay onderedway owhay ehay adhay escapedway ampcray osay onglay ithoutway ethay 
otectionpray ofway isthay ysteriousmay armchay. Ehay idday otnay enturevay againway untilway ehay 
adhay oundfay itway, andway ybay atthay imetay ethay otherway oysbay ereway iredtay andway eadyray otay 
estray. Eythay aduallygray anderedway apartway, oppeddray intoway ethay "umpsday," andway 
ellfay otay azinggay onginglylay acrossway ethay ideway iverray otay erewhay ethay illagevay aylay 
owsingdray inway ethay unsay. Omtay oundfay imselfhay itingwray "ECKYBAY" inway ethay andsay ithway 
ishay igbay oetay; ehay atchedscray itway outway, andway asway angryway ithway imselfhay orfay ishay 
eaknessway. Utbay ehay otewray itway againway, everthelessnay; ehay ouldcay otnay elphay itway. Ehay 
erasedway itway onceway oremay andway enthay ooktay imselfhay outway ofway emptationtay ybay ivingdray 
ethay otherway oysbay ogethertay andway oiningjay emthay. 

Utbay Oejay's iritsspay adhay onegay ownday almostway eyondbay esurrectionray. Ehay asway osay 
omesickhay atthay ehay ouldcay ardlyhay endureway ethay iserymay ofway itway. Ethay earstay aylay 
eryvay earnay ethay urfacesay. Uckhay asway elancholymay, ootay. Omtay asway ownheartedday, 
utbay iedtray ardhay otnay otay owshay itway. Ehay adhay away ecretsay ichwhay ehay asway otnay eadyray 
otay elltay, yetway, utbay ifway isthay utinousmay epressionday asway otnay okenbray upway oonsay, ehay 
ouldway avehay otay ingbray itway outway. Ehay aidsay, ithway away eatgray owshay ofway eerfulnesschay: 

"Iway etbay erethay's eenbay iratespay onway isthay islandway eforebay, oysbay. Eway'll exploreway 
itway againway. Eythay've idhay easurestray erehay omewheresay. Owhay'd youway eelfay otay ightlay 
onway away ottenray estchay ullfay ofway oldgay andway ilversay--hey?" 

Utbay itway ousedray onlyway aintfay enthusiasmway, ichwhay adedfay outway, ithway onay eplyray. 
Omtay iedtray oneway orway otway otherway eductionssay; utbay eythay ailedfay, ootay. Itway asway 
iscouragingday orkway. Oejay atsay okingpay upway ethay andsay ithway away ickstay andway ookinglay 
eryvay oomyglay. Inallyfay ehay aidsay: 

"Ohway, oysbay, etlay's ivegay itway upway. Iway antway otay ogay omehay. Itway's osay onesomelay." 

"Ohway onay, Oejay, youway'll eelfay etterbay ybay andway ybay," aidsay Omtay. "Ustjay inkthay ofway ethay 
ishingfay atthay's erehay." 

"Iway onday't arecay orfay ishingfay. Iway antway otay ogay omehay." 

"Utbay, Oejay, erethay ainway't uchsay anotherway immingsway-place anywhereway." 

"Immingsway's onay oodgay. Iway onday't eemsay otay arecay orfay itway, omehowsay, enwhay erethay 
ainway't anybodyway otay aysay Iway ashay'n't ogay inway. Iway eanmay otay ogay omehay." 

"Ohway, ucksshay! Abybay! Youway antway otay eesay yourway othermay, Iway eckonray." 

"Yesway, Iway _oday_ antway otay eesay ymay othermay--and youway ouldway, ootay, ifway youway adhay oneway. Iway 
ainway't anyway oremay abybay anthay youway areway." Andway Oejay uffledsnay away ittlelay. 

"Ellway, eway'll etlay ethay ybabycray ogay omehay otay ishay othermay, onway't eway, Uckhay? Oorpay 
ingthay--does itway antway otay eesay itsway othermay? Andway osay itway allshay. Youway ikelay itway erehay, 
onday't youway, Uckhay? Eway'll aystay, onway't eway?" 

Uckhay aidsay, "Yway-e-s"--without anyway earthay inway itway. 

"Iway'll evernay eakspay otay youway againway asway onglay asway Iway ivelay," aidsay Oejay, isingray. 
"Erethay ownay!" Andway ehay ovedmay oodilymay awayway andway eganbay otay essdray imselfhay. 

"Owhay arescay!" aidsay Omtay. "Obodynay antsway youway otay. Ogay 'onglay omehay andway etgay 
aughedlay atway. Ohway, youway're away icenay iratepay. Uckhay andway emay ainway't ybabiescray. Eway'll 
aystay, onway't eway, Uckhay? Etlay imhay ogay ifway ehay antsway otay. Iway eckonray eway ancay etgay 
alongway ithoutway imhay, erpay'aps." 

Utbay Omtay asway uneasyway, everthelessnay, andway asway alarmedway otay eesay Oejay ogay ullenlysay 
onway ithway ishay essingdray. Andway enthay itway asway iscomfortingday otay eesay Uckhay eyingway 
Oejay's eparationspray osay istfullyway, andway eepingkay upway uchsay anway ominousway ilencesay. 
Esentlypray, ithoutway away artingpay ordway, Oejay eganbay otay adeway offway owardtay ethay 
Illinoisway oreshay. Omtay's earthay eganbay otay inksay. Ehay ancedglay atway Uckhay. Uckhay 
ouldcay otnay earbay ethay ooklay, andway oppeddray ishay eyesway. Enthay ehay aidsay: 

"Iway antway otay ogay, ootay, Omtay. Itway asway ettinggay osay onesomelay anywayway, andway ownay 
itway'll ebay orseway. Etlay's usway ogay, ootay, Omtay." 

"Iway onway't! Youway ancay allway ogay, ifway youway antway otay. Iway eanmay otay aystay." 

"Omtay, Iway etterbay ogay." 

"Ellway, ogay 'onglay--who's enderinghay youway." 

Uckhay eganbay otay ickpay upway ishay atteredscay othesclay. Ehay aidsay: 

"Omtay, Iway ishtway youway'd omecay, ootay. Ownay youway inkthay itway overway. Eway'll aitway orfay youway 
enwhay eway etgay otay oreshay." 

"Ellway, youway'll aitway away ameblay onglay imetay, atthay's allway." 

Uckhay artedstay orrowfullysay awayway, andway Omtay oodstay ookinglay afterway imhay, ithway away 
ongstray esireday uggingtay atway ishay earthay otay yieldway ishay idepray andway ogay alongway 
ootay. Ehay opedhay ethay oysbay ouldway opstay, utbay eythay illstay adedway owlyslay onway. Itway 
uddenlysay awnedday onway Omtay atthay itway asway ecomebay eryvay onelylay andway illstay. Ehay ademay 
oneway inalfay ugglestray ithway ishay idepray, andway enthay artedday afterway ishay omradescay, 
yellingway: 

"Aitway! Aitway! Iway antway otay elltay youway omethingsay!" 

Eythay esentlypray oppedstay andway urnedtay aroundway. Enwhay ehay otgay otay erewhay eythay 
ereway, ehay eganbay unfoldingway ishay ecretsay, andway eythay istenedlay oodilymay illtay 
atway astlay eythay awsay ethay "ointpay" ehay asway ivingdray atway, andway enthay eythay etsay upway away 
arwhoopway ofway applauseway andway aidsay itway asway "endidsplay!" andway aidsay ifway ehay adhay 
oldtay emthay atway irstfay, eythay ouldnway't avehay artedstay awayway. Ehay ademay away ausibleplay 
excuseway; utbay ishay ealray easonray adhay eenbay ethay earfay atthay otnay evenway ethay ecretsay 
ouldway eepkay emthay ithway imhay anyway eryvay eatgray engthlay ofway imetay, andway osay ehay adhay 
eantmay otay oldhay itway inway eserveray asway away astlay eductionsay. 

Ethay adslay amecay aylygay ackbay andway entway atway eirthay ortsspay againway ithway away illway, 
atteringchay allway ethay imetay aboutway Omtay's upendousstay anplay andway admiringway ethay 
eniusgay ofway itway. Afterway away aintyday eggway andway ishfay innerday, Omtay aidsay ehay antedway otay 
earnlay otay okesmay, ownay. Oejay aughtcay atway ethay ideaway andway aidsay ehay ouldway ikelay otay 
ytray, ootay. Osay Uckhay ademay ipespay andway illedfay emthay. Esethay ovicesnay adhay evernay 
okedsmay anythingway eforebay utbay igarscay ademay ofway apevinegray, andway eythay "itbay" ethay 
onguetay, andway ereway otnay onsideredcay anlymay anywayway. 

Ownay eythay etchedstray emselvesthay outway onway eirthay elbowsway andway eganbay otay uffpay, 
arilychay, andway ithway enderslay onfidencecay. Ethay okesmay adhay anway unpleasantway astetay, 
andway eythay aggedgay away ittlelay, utbay Omtay aidsay: 

"Ywhay, itway's ustjay asway easyway! Ifway Iway'd away owedknay isthay asway allway, Iway'd away earntlay onglay 
agoway." 

"Osay ouldway Iway," aidsay Oejay. "Itway's ustjay othingnay." 

"Ywhay, anymay away imetay Iway've ookedlay atway eoplepay okingsmay, andway oughtthay ellway Iway ishway 
Iway ouldcay oday atthay; utbay Iway evernay oughtthay Iway ouldcay," aidsay Omtay. 

"Atthay's ustjay ethay ayway ithway emay, ainhay't itway, Uckhay? Youway've eardhay emay alktay ustjay 
atthay ayway--haven't youway, Uckhay? Iway'll eavelay itway otay Uckhay ifway Iway avenhay't." 

"Yesway--heaps ofway imestay," aidsay Uckhay. 

"Ellway, Iway avehay ootay," aidsay Omtay; "ohway, undredshay ofway imestay. Onceway ownday ybay ethay 
aughterslay-house. Onday't youway ememberray, Uckhay? Obbay Annertay asway erethay, andway 
Ohnnyjay Illermay, andway Effjay Atcherthay, enwhay Iway aidsay itway. Onday't youway ememberray, 
Uckhay, 'outbay emay ayingsay atthay?" 

"Yesway, atthay's osay," aidsay Uckhay. "Atthay asway ethay ayday afterway Iway ostlay away itewhay 
alleyway. Onay, 'astway ethay ayday eforebay." 

"Erethay--I oldtay youway osay," aidsay Omtay. "Uckhay ecollectsray itway." 

"Iway eeveblay Iway ouldcay okesmay isthay ipepay allway ayday," aidsay Oejay. "Iway onday't eelfay 
icksay." 

"Eithernay oday Iway," aidsay Omtay. "Iway ouldcay okesmay itway allway ayday. Utbay Iway etbay youway Effjay 
Atcherthay ouldncay't." 

"Effjay Atcherthay! Ywhay, ehay'd eelkay overway ustjay ithway otway awsdray. Ustjay etlay imhay 
ytray itway onceway. _Ehay'd_ eesay!" 

"Iway etbay ehay ouldway. Andway Ohnnyjay Illermay--I ishway ouldcay eesay Ohnnyjay Illermay ackletay 
itway onceway." 

"Ohway, onday't Iway!" aidsay Oejay. "Ywhay, Iway etbay youway Ohnnyjay Illermay ouldncay't anyway oremay 
oday isthay anthay othingnay. Ustjay oneway ittlelay iftersnay ouldway etchfay _imhay_." 

"'Eedday itway ouldway, Oejay. Aysay--I ishway ethay oysbay ouldcay eesay usway ownay." 

"Osay oday Iway." 

"Aysay--boys, onday't aysay anythingway aboutway itway, andway omesay imetay enwhay eythay're 
aroundway, Iway'll omecay upway otay youway andway aysay, 'Oejay, otgay away ipepay? Iway antway away okesmay.' 
Andway youway'll aysay, indkay ofway arelesscay ikelay, asway ifway itway arnway't anythingway, youway'll 
aysay, 'Yesway, Iway otgay ymay _oldway_ ipepay, andway anotherway oneway, utbay ymay obackertay ainway't 
eryvay oodgay.' Andway Iway'll aysay, 'Ohway, atthay's allway ightray, ifway itway's _ongstray_ 
enoughway.' Andway enthay youway'll outway ithway ethay ipespay, andway eway'll ightlay upway ustjay asway 
acay'm, andway enthay ustjay eesay 'emway ooklay!" 

"Ybay ingsjay, atthay'll ebay aygay, Omtay! Iway ishway itway asway _ownay_!" 

"Osay oday Iway! Andway enwhay eway elltay 'emway eway earnedlay enwhay eway asway offway iratingpay, 
onway't eythay ishway eythay'd eenbay alongway?" 

"Ohway, Iway eckonray otnay! Iway'll ustjay _etbay_ eythay illway!" 

Osay ethay alktay anray onway. Utbay esentlypray itway eganbay otay agflay away ifletray, andway 
owgray isjointedday. Ethay ilencessay idenedway; ethay expectorationway arvellouslymay 
increasedway. Everyway orepay insideway ethay oysbay' eekschay ecamebay away outingspay 
ountainfay; eythay ouldcay arcelyscay ailbay outway ethay ellarscay underway eirthay onguestay 
astfay enoughway otay eventpray anway inundationway; ittlelay overflowingsway ownday eirthay 
oatsthray occurredway inway itespay ofway allway eythay ouldcay oday, andway uddensay etchingsray 
ollowedfay everyway imetay. Othbay oysbay ereway ookinglay eryvay alepay andway iserablemay, 
ownay. Oejay's ipepay oppeddray omfray ishay ervelessnay ingersfay. Omtay's ollowedfay. Othbay 
ountainsfay ereway oinggay uriouslyfay andway othbay umpspay ailingbay ithway ightmay andway 
ainmay. Oejay aidsay eeblyfay: 

"Iway've ostlay ymay ifeknay. Iway eckonray Iway etterbay ogay andway indfay itway." 

Omtay aidsay, ithway uiveringqay ipslay andway altinghay utteranceway: 

"Iway'll elphay youway. Youway ogay overway atthay ayway andway Iway'll unthay aroundway ybay ethay ingspray. 
Onay, youway eednnay't omecay, Uckhay--we ancay indfay itway." 

Osay Uckhay atsay ownday againway, andway aitedway anway ourhay. Enthay ehay oundfay itway onesomelay, 
andway entway otay indfay ishay omradescay. Eythay ereway ideway apartway inway ethay oodsway, othbay 
eryvay alepay, othbay astfay asleepway. Utbay omethingsay informedway imhay atthay ifway eythay adhay 
adhay anyway oubletray eythay adhay otgay idray ofway itway. 

Eythay ereway otnay alkativetay atway uppersay atthay ightnay. Eythay adhay away umblehay ooklay, 
andway enwhay Uckhay eparedpray ishay ipepay afterway ethay ealmay andway asway oinggay otay eparepray 
eirsthay, eythay aidsay onay, eythay ereway otnay eelingfay eryvay ellway--something eythay ateway 
atway innerday adhay isagreedday ithway emthay. 

Aboutway idnightmay Oejay awokeway, andway alledcay ethay oysbay. Erethay asway away oodingbray 
oppressivenessway inway ethay airway atthay eemedsay otay odebay omethingsay. Ethay oysbay 
uddledhay emselvesthay ogethertay andway oughtsay ethay iendlyfray ompanionshipcay ofway 
ethay irefay, oughthay ethay ullday eadday eathay ofway ethay eathlessbray atmosphereway asway 
iflingstay. Eythay atsay illstay, intentway andway aitingway. Ethay olemnsay ushhay ontinuedcay. 
Eyondbay ethay ightlay ofway ethay irefay everythingway asway allowedsway upway inway ethay 
acknessblay ofway arknessday. Esentlypray erethay amecay away uiveringqay owglay atthay 
aguelyvay evealedray ethay oliagefay orfay away omentmay andway enthay anishedvay. Ybay andway ybay 
anotherway amecay, away ittlelay ongerstray. Enthay anotherway. Enthay away aintfay oanmay amecay 
ighingsay oughthray ethay anchesbray ofway ethay orestfay andway ethay oysbay eltfay away eetingflay 
eathbray uponway eirthay eekschay, andway udderedshay ithway ethay ancyfay atthay ethay Iritspay 
ofway ethay Ightnay adhay onegay ybay. Erethay asway away ausepay. Ownay away eirdway ashflay urnedtay 
ightnay intoway ayday andway owedshay everyway ittlelay assbladegray, eparatesay andway 
istinctday, atthay ewgray aboutway eirthay eetfay. Andway itway owedshay eethray itewhay, 
artledstay acesfay, ootay. Away eepday ealpay ofway underthay entway ollingray andway umblingtay 
ownday ethay eavenshay andway ostlay itselfway inway ullensay umblingsray inway ethay istanceday. Away 
eepsway ofway illychay airway assedpay ybay, ustlingray allway ethay eaveslay andway owingsnay ethay 
akyflay ashesway oadcastbray aboutway ethay irefay. Anotherway iercefay areglay itlay upway ethay 
orestfay andway anway instantway ashcray ollowedfay atthay eemedsay otay endray ethay eetopstray 
ightray overway ethay oysbay' eadshay. Eythay ungclay ogethertay inway errortay, inway ethay ickthay 
oomglay atthay ollowedfay. Away ewfay igbay aindropsray ellfay atteringpay uponway ethay eaveslay. 

"Uickqay! oysbay, ogay orfay ethay enttay!" exclaimedway Omtay. 

Eythay angspray awayway, umblingstay overway ootsray andway amongway inesvay inway ethay arkday, onay 
otway ungingplay inway ethay amesay irectionday. Away uriousfay astblay oaredray oughthray 
ethay eestray, akingmay everythingway ingsay asway itway entway. Oneway indingblay ashflay afterway 
anotherway amecay, andway ealpay onway ealpay ofway eafeningday underthay. Andway ownay away enchingdray 
ainray ouredpay ownday andway ethay isingray urricanehay ovedray itway inway eetsshay alongway ethay 
oundgray. Ethay oysbay iedcray outway otay eachway otherway, utbay ethay oaringray indway andway ethay 
oomingbay underblaststhay owneddray eirthay oicesvay utterlyway. Oweverhay, oneway ybay oneway 
eythay aggledstray inway atway astlay andway ooktay eltershay underway ethay enttay, oldcay, aredscay, 
andway eamingstray ithway aterway; utbay otay avehay ompanycay inway iserymay eemedsay omethingsay 
otay ebay atefulgray orfay. Eythay ouldcay otnay alktay, ethay oldway ailsay appedflay osay 
uriouslyfay, evenway ifway ethay otherway oisesnay ouldway avehay allowedway emthay. Ethay empesttay 
oseray igherhay andway igherhay, andway esentlypray ethay ailsay oretay ooselay omfray itsway 
asteningsfay andway entway ingingway awayway onway ethay astblay. Ethay oysbay eizedsay eachway 
othersway' andshay andway edflay, ithway anymay umblingstay andway uisesbray, otay ethay eltershay 
ofway away eatgray oakway atthay oodstay uponway ethay iverbankray. Ownay ethay attlebay asway atway itsway 
ighesthay. Underway ethay easelesscay onflagrationcay ofway ightninglay atthay amedflay 
inway ethay iesskay, everythingway elowbay oodstay outway inway eancutclay andway adowlessshay 
istinctnessday: ethay endingbay eestray, ethay illowybay iverray, itewhay ithway oamfay, ethay 
ivingdray ayspray ofway umeflakesspay, ethay imday outlinesway ofway ethay ighhay uffsblay onway 
ethay otherway idesay, impsedglay oughthray ethay iftingdray oudrackclay andway ethay antingslay 
eilvay ofway ainray. Everyway ittlelay ilewhay omesay iantgay eetray yieldedway ethay ightfay 
andway ellfay ashingcray oughthray ethay youngerway owthgray; andway ethay unflaggingway 
underpealsthay amecay ownay inway earway-splitting explosiveway urstsbay, eenkay andway arpshay, 
andway unspeakablyway appallingway. Ethay ormstay ulminatedcay inway oneway atchlessmay effortway 
atthay eemedsay ikelylay otay eartay ethay islandway otay iecespay, urnbay itway upway, owndray itway otay 
ethay eetopstray, owblay itway awayway, andway eafenday everyway eaturecray inway itway, allway atway oneway 
andway ethay amesay omentmay. Itway asway away ildway ightnay orfay omelesshay youngway eadshay otay ebay 
outway inway. 

Utbay atway astlay ethay attlebay asway oneday, andway ethay orcesfay etiredray ithway eakerway andway 
eakerway eateningsthray andway umblingsgray, andway eacepay esumedray erhay aysway. Ethay 
oysbay entway ackbay otay ampcay, away oodgay ealday awedway; utbay eythay oundfay erethay asway illstay 
omethingsay otay ebay ankfulthay orfay, ecausebay ethay eatgray ycamoresay, ethay eltershay 
ofway eirthay edsbay, asway away uinray, ownay, astedblay ybay ethay ightningslay, andway eythay ereway 
otnay underway itway enwhay ethay atastrophecay appenedhay. 

Everythingway inway ampcay asway encheddray, ethay ampfirecay asway ellway; orfay eythay ereway utbay 
eedlesshay adslay, ikelay eirthay enerationgay, andway adhay ademay onay ovisionpray againstway 
ainray. Erehay asway attermay orfay ismayday, orfay eythay ereway oakedsay oughthray andway 
illedchay. Eythay ereway eloquentway inway eirthay istressday; utbay eythay esentlypray 
iscoveredday atthay ethay irefay adhay eatenway osay arfay upway underway ethay eatgray oglay itway adhay 
eenbay uiltbay againstway (erewhay itway urvedcay upwardway andway eparatedsay itselfway omfray 
ethay oundgray), atthay away andbreadthhay orway osay ofway itway adhay escapedway ettingway; osay eythay 
atientlypay oughtwray untilway, ithway edsshray andway arkbay atheredgay omfray ethay underway 
idessay ofway elteredshay ogslay, eythay oaxedcay ethay irefay otay urnbay againway. Enthay eythay 
iledpay onway eatgray eadday oughsbay illtay eythay adhay away oaringray urnacefay, andway ereway 
adheartedglay onceway oremay. Eythay ieddray eirthay oiledbay amhay andway adhay away eastfay, 
andway afterway atthay eythay atsay ybay ethay irefay andway expandedway andway orifiedglay eirthay 
idnightmay adventureway untilway orningmay, orfay erethay asway otnay away ydray otspay otay eepslay 
onway, anywhereway aroundway. 

Asway ethay unsay eganbay otay ealstay inway uponway ethay oysbay, owsinessdray amecay overway 
emthay, andway eythay entway outway onway ethay andbarsay andway aylay ownday otay eepslay. Eythay otgay 
orchedscay outway ybay andway ybay, andway earilydray etsay aboutway ettinggay eakfastbray. Afterway 
ethay ealmay eythay eltfay ustyray, andway iffstay-jointed, andway away ittlelay omesickhay onceway 
oremay. Omtay awsay ethay ignssay, andway ellfay otay eeringchay upway ethay iratespay asway ellway asway 
ehay ouldcay. Utbay eythay aredcay othingnay orfay arblesmay, orway ircuscay, orway immingsway, orway 
anythingway. Ehay emindedray emthay ofway ethay imposingway ecretsay, andway aisedray away ayray ofway 
eerchay. Ilewhay itway astedlay, ehay otgay emthay interestedway inway away ewnay eviceday. Isthay asway 
otay ockknay offway eingbay iratespay, orfay away ilewhay, andway ebay Indiansway orfay away angechay. 
Eythay ereway attractedway ybay isthay ideaway; osay itway asway otnay onglay eforebay eythay ereway 
ippedstray, andway ipedstray omfray eadhay otay eelhay ithway ackblay udmay, ikelay osay anymay 
ebraszay--all ofway emthay iefschay, ofway oursecay--and enthay eythay entway earingtay oughthray 
ethay oodsway otay attackway anway Englishway ettlementsay. 

Ybay andway ybay eythay eparatedsay intoway eethray ostilehay ibestray, andway artedday uponway eachway 
otherway omfray ambushway ithway eadfuldray arwhoopsway, andway illedkay andway alpedscay eachway 
otherway ybay ousandsthay. Itway asway away orygay ayday. Onsequentlycay itway asway anway extremelyway 
atisfactorysay oneway. 

Eythay assembledway inway ampcay owardtay uppertimesay, ungryhay andway appyhay; utbay ownay 
away ifficultyday aroseway--hostile Indiansway ouldcay otnay eakbray ethay eadbray ofway 
ospitalityhay ogethertay ithoutway irstfay akingmay eacepay, andway isthay asway away implesay 
impossibilityway ithoutway okingsmay away ipepay ofway eacepay. Erethay asway onay otherway 
ocesspray atthay everway eythay adhay eardhay ofway. Otway ofway ethay avagessay almostway ishedway 
eythay adhay emainedray iratespay. Oweverhay, erethay asway onay otherway ayway; osay ithway uchsay 
owshay ofway eerfulnesschay asway eythay ouldcay ustermay eythay alledcay orfay ethay ipepay andway 
ooktay eirthay iffwhay asway itway assedpay, inway ueday ormfay. 

Andway eholdbay, eythay ereway adglay eythay adhay onegay intoway avagerysay, orfay eythay adhay 
ainedgay omethingsay; eythay oundfay atthay eythay ouldcay ownay okesmay away ittlelay ithoutway 
avinghay otay ogay andway unthay orfay away ostlay ifeknay; eythay idday otnay etgay icksay enoughway otay 
ebay eriouslysay uncomfortableway. Eythay ereway otnay ikelylay otay oolfay awayway isthay ighhay 
omisepray orfay acklay ofway effortway. Onay, eythay actisedpray autiouslycay, afterway uppersay, 
ithway ightray airfay uccesssay, andway osay eythay entspay away ubilantjay eveningway. Eythay ereway 
ouderpray andway appierhay inway eirthay ewnay acquirementway anthay eythay ouldway avehay eenbay 
inway ethay alpingscay andway inningskay ofway ethay Ixsay Ationsnay. Eway illway eavelay emthay otay 
okesmay andway atterchay andway agbray, incesay eway avehay onay urtherfay useway orfay emthay atway 
esentpray. 




APTERCHAY IIXVAY 

UTBAY erethay asway onay ilarityhay inway ethay ittlelay owntay atthay amesay anquiltray Aturdaysay 
afternoonway. Ethay Arpershay, andway Auntway Ollypay's amilyfay, ereway eingbay utpay intoway 
ourningmay, ithway eatgray iefgray andway anymay earstay. Anway unusualway uietqay ossessedpay 
ethay illagevay, althoughway itway asway ordinarilyway uietqay enoughway, inway allway onsciencecay. 
Ethay illagersvay onductedcay eirthay oncernscay ithway anway absentway airway, andway alkedtay 
ittlelay; utbay eythay ighedsay oftenway. Ethay Aturdaysay olidayhay eemedsay away urdenbay otay 
ethay ildrenchay. Eythay adhay onay earthay inway eirthay ortsspay, andway aduallygray avegay emthay 
upway. 

Inway ethay afternoonway Eckybay Atcherthay oundfay erselfhay opingmay aboutway ethay esertedday 
oolhouseschay yardway, andway eelingfay eryvay elancholymay. Utbay eshay oundfay othingnay 
erethay otay omfortcay erhay. Eshay oliloquizedsay: 

"Ohway, ifway Iway onlyway adhay away assbray andironway-knob againway! Utbay Iway avenhay't otgay 
anythingway ownay otay ememberray imhay ybay." Andway eshay okedchay ackbay away ittlelay obsay. 

Esentlypray eshay oppedstay, andway aidsay otay erselfhay: 

"Itway asway ightray erehay. Ohway, ifway itway asway otay oday overway againway, Iway ouldnway't aysay 
atthay--I ouldnway't aysay itway orfay ethay olewhay orldway. Utbay ehay's onegay ownay; Iway'll 
evernay, evernay, evernay eesay imhay anyway oremay." 

Isthay oughtthay okebray erhay ownday, andway eshay anderedway awayway, ithway earstay ollingray 
ownday erhay eekschay. Enthay uiteqay away oupgray ofway oysbay andway irlsgay--playmates ofway Omtay's 
andway Oejay's--came ybay, andway oodstay ookinglay overway ethay alingpay encefay andway alkingtay 
inway everentray onestay ofway owhay Omtay idday osay-and-so ethay astlay imetay eythay awsay 
imhay, andway owhay Oejay aidsay isthay andway atthay allsmay ifletray (egnantpray ithway awfulway 
ophecypray, asway eythay ouldcay easilyway eesay ownay!)--and eachway eakerspay ointedpay outway 
ethay exactway otspay erewhay ethay ostlay adslay oodstay atway ethay imetay, andway enthay addedway 
omethingsay ikelay "andway Iway asway away-standing ustjay osay--just asway Iway amway ownay, andway asway ifway 
youway asway imhay--I asway asway oseclay asway atthay--and ehay iledsmay, ustjay isthay ayway--and enthay 
omethingsay eemedsay otay ogay allway overway emay, ikelay--awful, youway owknay--and Iway evernay 
oughtthay atwhay itway eantmay, ofway oursecay, utbay Iway ancay eesay ownay!" 

Enthay erethay asway away isputeday aboutway owhay awsay ethay eadday oysbay astlay inway ifelay, andway 
anymay aimedclay atthay ismalday istinctionday, andway offeredway evidencesway, oremay orway 
esslay amperedtay ithway ybay ethay itnessway; andway enwhay itway asway ultimatelyway ecidedday 
owhay _idday_ eesay ethay epartedday astlay, andway exchangedway ethay astlay ordsway ithway emthay, 
ethay uckylay artiespay ooktay uponway emselvesthay away ortsay ofway acredsay importanceway, 
andway ereway apedgay atway andway enviedway ybay allway ethay estray. Oneway oorpay apchay, owhay adhay 
onay otherway andeurgray otay offerway, aidsay ithway olerablytay anifestmay idepray inway ethay 
emembranceray: 

"Ellway, Omtay Awyersay ehay ickedlay emay onceway." 

Utbay atthay idbay orfay oryglay asway away ailurefay. Ostmay ofway ethay oysbay ouldcay aysay atthay, 
andway osay atthay eapenedchay ethay istinctionday ootay uchmay. Ethay oupgray oiteredlay awayway, 
illstay ecallingray emoriesmay ofway ethay ostlay eroeshay, inway awedway oicesvay. 

Enwhay ethay Undaysay-school ourhay asway inishedfay, ethay extnay orningmay, ethay ellbay 
eganbay otay olltay, insteadway ofway ingingray inway ethay usualway ayway. Itway asway away eryvay illstay 
Abbathsay, andway ethay ournfulmay oundsay eemedsay inway eepingkay ithway ethay usingmay ushhay 
atthay aylay uponway aturenay. Ethay illagersvay eganbay otay athergay, oiteringlay away omentmay 
inway ethay estibulevay otay onversecay inway isperswhay aboutway ethay adsay eventway. Utbay erethay 
asway onay isperingwhay inway ethay ousehay; onlyway ethay unerealfay ustlingray ofway essesdray 
asway ethay omenway atheredgay otay eirthay eatssay isturbedday ethay ilencesay erethay. Onenay 
ouldcay ememberray enwhay ethay ittlelay urchchay adhay eenbay osay ullfay eforebay. Erethay 
asway inallyfay away aitingway ausepay, anway expectantway umbnessday, andway enthay Auntway Ollypay 
enteredway, ollowedfay ybay Idsay andway Arymay, andway eythay ybay ethay Arperhay amilyfay, allway inway 
eepday ackblay, andway ethay olewhay ongregationcay, ethay oldway inistermay asway ellway, oseray 
everentlyray andway oodstay untilway ethay ournersmay ereway eatedsay inway ethay ontfray ewpay. 
Erethay asway anotherway ommuningcay ilencesay, okenbray atway intervalsway ybay uffledmay 
obssay, andway enthay ethay inistermay eadspray ishay andshay abroadway andway ayedpray. Away ovingmay 
ymnhay asway ungsay, andway ethay exttay ollowedfay: "Iway amway ethay Esurrectionray andway ethay 
Ifelay." 

Asway ethay ervicesay oceededpray, ethay ergymanclay ewdray uchsay icturespay ofway ethay 
acesgray, ethay inningway aysway, andway ethay areray omisepray ofway ethay ostlay adslay atthay 
everyway oulsay erethay, inkingthay ehay ecognizedray esethay icturespay, eltfay away angpay 
inway ememberingray atthay ehay adhay ersistentlypay indedblay imselfhay otay emthay alwaysway 
eforebay, andway adhay asway ersistentlypay eensay onlyway aultsfay andway awsflay inway ethay oorpay 
oysbay. Ethay inistermay elatedray anymay away ouchingtay incidentway inway ethay iveslay ofway ethay 
epartedday, ootay, ichwhay illustratedway eirthay eetsway, enerousgay aturesnay, andway ethay 
eoplepay ouldcay easilyway eesay, ownay, owhay oblenay andway eautifulbay osethay episodesway 
ereway, andway ememberedray ithway iefgray atthay atway ethay imetay eythay occurredway eythay adhay 
eemedsay ankray ascalitiesray, ellway eservingday ofway ethay owhidecay. Ethay ongregationcay 
ecamebay oremay andway oremay ovedmay, asway ethay atheticpay aletay entway onway, illtay atway astlay 
ethay olewhay ompanycay okebray ownday andway oinedjay ethay eepingway ournersmay inway away oruschay 
ofway anguishedway obssay, ethay eacherpray imselfhay ivinggay ayway otay ishay eelingsfay, andway 
yingcray inway ethay ulpitpay. 

Erethay asway away ustleray inway ethay allerygay, ichwhay obodynay oticednay; away omentmay aterlay 
ethay urchchay oorday eakedcray; ethay inistermay aisedray ishay eamingstray eyesway aboveway 
ishay andkerchiefhay, andway oodstay ansfixedtray! Irstfay oneway andway enthay anotherway airpay 
ofway eyesway ollowedfay ethay inistermay's, andway enthay almostway ithway oneway impulseway ethay 
ongregationcay oseray andway aredstay ilewhay ethay eethray eadday oysbay amecay archingmay upway 
ethay aisleway, Omtay inway ethay eadlay, Oejay extnay, andway Uckhay, away uinray ofway oopingdray agsray, 
eakingsnay eepishlyshay inway ethay earray! Eythay adhay eenbay idhay inway ethay unusedway allerygay 
isteninglay otay eirthay ownway uneralfay ermonsay! 

Auntway Ollypay, Arymay, andway ethay Arpershay ewthray emselvesthay uponway eirthay estoredray 
onesway, otheredsmay emthay ithway isseskay andway ouredpay outway anksgivingsthay, ilewhay 
oorpay Uckhay oodstay abashedway andway uncomfortableway, otnay owingknay exactlyway atwhay 
otay oday orway erewhay otay idehay omfray osay anymay unwelcomingway eyesway. Ehay averedway, andway 
artedstay otay inkslay awayway, utbay Omtay eizedsay imhay andway aidsay: 

"Auntway Ollypay, itway ainway't airfay. Omebodysay's otgay otay ebay adglay otay eesay Uckhay." 

"Andway osay eythay allshay. Iway'm adglay otay eesay imhay, oorpay otherlessmay ingthay!" Andway 
ethay ovinglay attentionsway Auntway Ollypay avishedlay uponway imhay ereway ethay oneway ingthay 
apablecay ofway akingmay imhay oremay uncomfortableway anthay ehay asway eforebay. 

Uddenlysay ethay inistermay outedshay atway ethay optay ofway ishay oicevay: "Aisepray Odgay omfray 
omwhay allway essingsblay owflay--_sing_!--and utpay yourway eartshay inway itway!" 

Andway eythay idday. Oldway Undredhay elledsway upway ithway away iumphanttray urstbay, andway 
ilewhay itway ookshay ethay aftersray Omtay Awyersay ethay Iratepay ookedlay aroundway uponway ethay 
envyingway uvenilesjay aboutway imhay andway onfessedcay inway ishay earthay atthay isthay asway ethay 
oudestpray omentmay ofway ishay ifelay. 

Asway ethay "oldsay" ongregationcay oopedtray outway eythay aidsay eythay ouldway almostway ebay 
illingway otay ebay ademay idiculousray againway otay earhay Oldway Undredhay ungsay ikelay atthay 
onceway oremay. 

Omtay otgay oremay uffscay andway isseskay atthay ayday--according otay Auntway Ollypay's aryingvay 
oodsmay--than ehay adhay earnedway eforebay inway away yearway; andway ehay ardlyhay ewknay ichwhay 
expressedway ethay ostmay atefulnessgray otay Odgay andway affectionway orfay imselfhay. 




APTERCHAY IIIXVAY 

ATTHAY asway Omtay's eatgray ecretsay--the emeschay otay eturnray omehay ithway ishay otherbray 
iratespay andway attendway eirthay ownway uneralsfay. Eythay adhay addledpay overway otay ethay 
Issourimay oreshay onway away oglay, atway uskday onway Aturdaysay, andinglay ivefay orway ixsay ilesmay 
elowbay ethay illagevay; eythay adhay eptslay inway ethay oodsway atway ethay edgeway ofway ethay owntay 
illtay earlynay aylightday, andway adhay enthay eptcray oughthray ackbay aneslay andway alleysway 
andway inishedfay eirthay eepslay inway ethay allerygay ofway ethay urchchay amongway away aoschay ofway 
invalidedway enchesbay. 

Atway eakfastbray, Ondaymay orningmay, Auntway Ollypay andway Arymay ereway eryvay ovinglay otay 
Omtay, andway eryvay attentiveway otay ishay antsway. Erethay asway anway unusualway amountway ofway 
alktay. Inway ethay oursecay ofway itway Auntway Ollypay aidsay: 

"Ellway, Iway onday't aysay itway asnway't away inefay okejay, Omtay, otay eepkay everybodyway 
ufferingsay 'ostmay away eekway osay youway oysbay adhay away oodgay imetay, utbay itway isway away itypay youway 
ouldcay ebay osay ardhay-hearted asway otay etlay emay uffersay osay. Ifway youway ouldcay omecay overway 
onway away oglay otay ogay otay yourway uneralfay, youway ouldcay avehay omecay overway andway ivegay emay away 
inthay omesay ayway atthay youway arnway't eadday, utbay onlyway unray offway." 

"Yesway, youway ouldcay avehay oneday atthay, Omtay," aidsay Arymay; "andway Iway elievebay youway 
ouldway ifway youway adhay oughtthay ofway itway." 

"Ouldway youway, Omtay?" aidsay Auntway Ollypay, erhay acefay ightinglay istfullyway. "Aysay, 
ownay, ouldway youway, ifway youway'd oughtthay ofway itway?" 

"Iway--well, Iway onday't owknay. 'Ouldtway 'away' oiledspay everythingway." 

"Omtay, Iway opedhay youway ovedlay emay atthay uchmay," aidsay Auntway Ollypay, ithway away ievedgray 
onetay atthay iscomfortedday ethay oybay. "Itway ouldway avehay eenbay omethingsay ifway youway'd 
aredcay enoughway otay _inkthay_ ofway itway, evenway ifway youway idnday't _oday_ itway." 

"Ownay, auntieway, atthay ainway't anyway armhay," eadedplay Arymay; "itway's onlyway Omtay's iddygay 
ayway--he isway alwaysway inway uchsay away ushray atthay ehay evernay inksthay ofway anythingway." 

"Oremay's ethay itypay. Idsay ouldway avehay oughtthay. Andway Idsay ouldway avehay omecay andway 
_oneday_ itway, ootay. Omtay, youway'll ooklay ackbay, omesay ayday, enwhay itway's ootay atelay, 
andway ishway youway'd aredcay away ittlelay oremay orfay emay enwhay itway ouldway avehay ostcay youway osay 
ittlelay." 

"Ownay, auntieway, youway owknay Iway oday arecay orfay youway," aidsay Omtay. 

"Iway'd owknay itway etterbay ifway youway actedway oremay ikelay itway." 

"Iway ishway ownay Iway'd oughtthay," aidsay Omtay, ithway away epentantray onetay; "utbay Iway eamtdray 
aboutway youway, anywayway. Atthay's omethingsay, ainway't itway?" 

"Itway ainway't uchmay--a atcay oesday atthay uchmay--but itway's etterbay anthay othingnay. Atwhay 
idday youway eamdray?" 

"Ywhay, Ednesdayway ightnay Iway eamtdray atthay youway asway ittingsay overway erethay ybay ethay 
edbay, andway Idsay asway ittingsay ybay ethay oodboxway, andway Arymay extnay otay imhay." 

"Ellway, osay eway idday. Osay eway alwaysway oday. Iway'm adglay yourway eamsdray ouldcay aketay evenway 
atthay uchmay oubletray aboutway usway." 

"Andway Iway eamtdray atthay Oejay Arperhay's othermay asway erehay." 

"Ywhay, eshay asway erehay! Idday youway eamdray anyway oremay?" 

"Ohway, otslay. Utbay itway's osay imday, ownay." 

"Ellway, ytray otay ecollectray--can't youway?" 

"Omehowsay itway eemssay otay emay atthay ethay indway--the indway owedblay ethay--the--" 

"Ytray arderhay, Omtay! Ethay indway idday owblay omethingsay. Omecay!" 

Omtay essedpray ishay ingersfay onway ishay oreheadfay anway anxiousway inutemay, andway enthay 
aidsay: 

"Iway've otgay itway ownay! Iway've otgay itway ownay! Itway owedblay ethay andlecay!" 

"Ercymay onway usway! Ogay onway, Omtay--go onway!" 

"Andway itway eemssay otay emay atthay youway aidsay, 'Ywhay, Iway elievebay atthay atthay oorday--'" 

"Ogay _onway_, Omtay!" 

"Ustjay etlay emay udystay away omentmay--just away omentmay. Ohway, yesway--you aidsay youway elievedbay 
ethay oorday asway openway." 

"Asway Iway'm ittingsay erehay, Iway idday! Idnday't Iway, Arymay! Ogay onway!" 

"Andway enthay--and enthay--well Iway onway't ebay ertaincay, utbay itway eemssay ikelay asway ifway youway 
ademay Idsay ogay andway--and--" 

"Ellway? Ellway? Atwhay idday Iway akemay imhay oday, Omtay? Atwhay idday Iway akemay imhay oday?" 

"Youway ademay imhay--you--Oh, youway ademay imhay utshay itway." 

"Ellway, orfay ethay andlay's akesay! Iway evernay eardhay ethay eatbay ofway atthay inway allway ymay 
aysday! Onday't elltay _emay_ erethay ainway't anythingway inway eamsdray, anyway oremay. Erenysay 
Arperhay allshay owknay ofway isthay eforebay Iway'm anway ourhay olderway. Iway'd ikelay otay eesay erhay 
etgay aroundway _isthay_ ithway erhay ubbageray 'outbay uperstitionsay. Ogay onway, Omtay!" 

"Ohway, itway's allway ettinggay ustjay asway ightbray asway ayday, ownay. Extnay youway aidsay Iway arnway't 
_adbay_, onlyway ischeevousmay andway arumhay-scarum, andway otnay anyway oremay esponsibleray 
anthay--than--I inkthay itway asway away oltcay, orway omethingsay." 

"Andway osay itway asway! Ellway, oodnessgay aciousgray! Ogay onway, Omtay!" 

"Andway enthay youway eganbay otay ycray." 

"Osay Iway idday. Osay Iway idday. Otnay ethay irstfay imetay, eithernay. Andway enthay--" 

"Enthay Mrsay. Arperhay eshay eganbay otay ycray, andway aidsay Oejay asway ustjay ethay amesay, andway 
eshay ishedway eshay adnhay't ippedwhay imhay orfay akingtay eamcray enwhay eshay'd owedthray itway 
outway erhay ownway elfsay--" 

"Omtay! Ethay erritspay asway uponway youway! Youway asway away ophesyingpray--that's atwhay youway 
asway oingday! Andlay aliveway, ogay onway, Omtay!" 

"Enthay Idsay ehay aidsay--he aidsay--" 

"Iway onday't inkthay Iway aidsay anythingway," aidsay Idsay. 

"Yesway youway idday, Idsay," aidsay Arymay. 

"Utshay yourway eadshay andway etlay Omtay ogay onway! Atwhay idday ehay aysay, Omtay?" 

"Ehay aidsay--I _inkthay_ ehay aidsay ehay opedhay Iway asway etterbay offway erewhay Iway asway onegay 
otay, utbay ifway Iway'd eenbay etterbay ometimessay--" 

"_Erethay_, dway'you earhay atthay! Itway asway ishay eryvay ordsway!" 

"Andway youway utshay imhay upway arpshay." 

"Iway aylay Iway idday! Erethay ustmay 'away' eenbay anway angelway erethay. Erethay _asway_ anway angelway 
erethay, omewheressay!" 

"Andway Mrsay. Arperhay oldtay aboutway Oejay aringscay erhay ithway away irecrackerfay, andway youway 
oldtay aboutway Eterpay andway ethay Ainpay-killer--" 

"Ustjay asway uetray asway Iway ivelay!" 

"Andway enthay erethay asway away olewhay otlay ofway alktay 'outbay aggingdray ethay iverray orfay usway, 
andway 'outbay avinghay ethay uneralfay Undaysay, andway enthay youway andway oldway Issmay Arperhay 
uggedhay andway iedcray, andway eshay entway." 

"Itway appenedhay ustjay osay! Itway appenedhay ustjay osay, asway uresay asway Iway'm away-sitting inway 
esethay eryvay ackstray. Omtay, youway ouldncay't oldtay itway oremay ikelay ifway youway'd 'away' eensay 
itway! Andway enthay atwhay? Ogay onway, Omtay!" 

"Enthay Iway oughtthay youway ayedpray orfay emay--and Iway ouldcay eesay youway andway earhay everyway 
ordway youway aidsay. Andway youway entway otay edbay, andway Iway asway osay orrysay atthay Iway ooktay andway 
otewray onway away iecepay ofway ycamoresay arkbay, 'Eway ainway't eadday--we areway onlyway offway eingbay 
iratespay,' andway utpay itway onway ethay abletay ybay ethay andlecay; andway enthay youway ookedlay 
osay oodgay, ayinglay erethay asleepway, atthay Iway oughtthay Iway entway andway eanedlay overway andway 
issedkay youway onway ethay ipslay." 

"Idday youway, Omtay, _idday_ youway! Iway ustjay orgivefay youway everythingway orfay atthay!" Andway 
eshay eizedsay ethay oybay inway away ushingcray embraceway atthay ademay imhay eelfay ikelay ethay 
uiltiestgay ofway illainsvay. 

"Itway asway eryvay indkay, evenway oughthay itway asway onlyway away--dream," Idsay oliloquizedsay 
ustjay audiblyway. 

"Utshay upway, Idsay! Away odybay oesday ustjay ethay amesay inway away eamdray asway ehay'd oday ifway ehay asway 
awakeway. Erehay's away igbay Ilummay appleway Iway've eenbay avingsay orfay youway, Omtay, ifway youway 
asway everway oundfay againway--now ogay 'onglay otay oolschay. Iway'm ankfulthay otay ethay oodgay 
Odgay andway Atherfay ofway usway allway Iway've otgay youway ackbay, atthay's onglay-suffering andway 
ercifulmay otay emthay atthay elievebay onway Imhay andway eepkay Ishay ordway, oughthay oodnessgay 
owsknay Iway'm unworthyway ofway itway, utbay ifway onlyway ethay orthyway onesway otgay Ishay essingsblay 
andway adhay Ishay andhay otay elphay emthay overway ethay oughray acesplay, erethay's ewfay enoughway 
ouldway ilesmay erehay orway everway enterway intoway Ishay estray enwhay ethay onglay ightnay omescay. 
Ogay 'onglay Idsay, Arymay, Omtay--take yourselvesway offway--you've enderedhay emay onglay 
enoughway." 

Ethay ildrenchay eftlay orfay oolschay, andway ethay oldway adylay otay allcay onway Mrsay. Arperhay 
andway anquishvay erhay ealismray ithway Omtay's arvellousmay eamdray. Idsay adhay etterbay 
udgmentjay anthay otay utterway ethay oughtthay atthay asway inway ishay indmay asway ehay eftlay ethay 
ousehay. Itway asway isthay: "Ettypray inthay--as onglay away eamdray asway atthay, ithoutway anyway 
istakesmay inway itway!" 

Atwhay away erohay Omtay asway ecomebay, ownay! Ehay idday otnay ogay ippingskay andway ancingpray, 
utbay ovedmay ithway away ignifiedday aggersway asway ecamebay away iratepay owhay eltfay atthay ethay 
ublicpay eyeway asway onway imhay. Andway indeedway itway asway; ehay iedtray otnay otay eemsay otay eesay 
ethay ookslay orway earhay ethay emarksray asway ehay assedpay alongway, utbay eythay ereway oodfay andway 
inkdray otay imhay. Allersmay oysbay anthay imselfhay ockedflay atway ishay eelshay, asway oudpray 
otay ebay eensay ithway imhay, andway oleratedtay ybay imhay, asway ifway ehay adhay eenbay ethay ummerdray 
atway ethay eadhay ofway away ocessionpray orway ethay elephantway eadinglay away enageriemay intoway 
owntay. Oysbay ofway ishay ownway izesay etendedpray otnay otay owknay ehay adhay eenbay awayway atway 
allway; utbay eythay ereway onsumingcay ithway envyway, everthelessnay. Eythay ouldway avehay 
ivengay anythingway otay avehay atthay arthysway unsay-tanned inskay ofway ishay, andway ishay 
itteringglay otorietynay; andway Omtay ouldway otnay avehay artedpay ithway eitherway orfay away 
ircuscay. 

Atway oolschay ethay ildrenchay ademay osay uchmay ofway imhay andway ofway Oejay, andway eliveredday 
uchsay eloquentway admirationway omfray eirthay eyesway, atthay ethay otway eroeshay ereway 
otnay onglay inway ecomingbay insufferablyway "uckstay-up." Eythay eganbay otay elltay eirthay 
adventuresway otay ungryhay istenerslay--but eythay onlyway eganbay; itway asway otnay away 
ingthay ikelylay otay avehay anway endway, ithway imaginationsway ikelay eirsthay otay urnishfay 
aterialmay. Andway inallyfay, enwhay eythay otgay outway eirthay ipespay andway entway erenelysay 
uffingpay aroundway, ethay eryvay ummitsay ofway oryglay asway eachedray. 

Omtay ecidedday atthay ehay ouldcay ebay independentway ofway Eckybay Atcherthay ownay. Oryglay 
asway ufficientsay. Ehay ouldway ivelay orfay oryglay. Ownay atthay ehay asway istinguishedday, 
aybemay eshay ouldway ebay antingway otay "akemay upway." Ellway, etlay erhay--she ouldshay eesay 
atthay ehay ouldcay ebay asway indifferentway asway omesay otherway eoplepay. Esentlypray eshay 
arrivedway. Omtay etendedpray otnay otay eesay erhay. Ehay ovedmay awayway andway oinedjay away oupgray 
ofway oysbay andway irlsgay andway eganbay otay alktay. Oonsay ehay observedway atthay eshay asway 
ippingtray aylygay ackbay andway orthfay ithway ushedflay acefay andway ancingday eyesway, 
etendingpray otay ebay usybay asingchay oolmatesschay, andway eamingscray ithway aughterlay 
enwhay eshay ademay away apturecay; utbay ehay oticednay atthay eshay alwaysway ademay erhay 
apturescay inway ishay icinityvay, andway atthay eshay eemedsay otay astcay away onsciouscay eyeway 
inway ishay irectionday atway uchsay imestay, ootay. Itway atifiedgray allway ethay iciousvay anityvay 
atthay asway inway imhay; andway osay, insteadway ofway inningway imhay, itway onlyway "etsay imhay upway" 
ethay oremay andway ademay imhay ethay oremay iligentday otay avoidway etrayingbay atthay ehay 
ewknay eshay asway aboutway. Esentlypray eshay avegay overway ylarkingskay, andway ovedmay 
irresolutelyway aboutway, ighingsay onceway orway icetway andway ancingglay urtivelyfay andway 
istfullyway owardtay Omtay. Enthay eshay observedway atthay ownay Omtay asway alkingtay oremay 
articularlypay otay Amyway Awrencelay anthay otay anyway oneway elseway. Eshay eltfay away arpshay angpay 
andway ewgray isturbedday andway uneasyway atway onceway. Eshay iedtray otay ogay awayway, utbay erhay 
eetfay ereway eacheroustray, andway arriedcay erhay otay ethay oupgray insteadway. Eshay aidsay otay 
away irlgay almostway atway Omtay's elbowway--with amshay ivacityvay: 

"Ywhay, Arymay Austinway! youway adbay irlgay, ywhay idnday't youway omecay otay Undaysay-school?" 

"Iway idday omecay--didn't youway eesay emay?" 

"Ywhay, onay! Idday youway? Erewhay idday youway itsay?" 

"Iway asway inway Issmay Eterspay' assclay, erewhay Iway alwaysway ogay. Iway awsay _youway_." 

"Idday youway? Ywhay, itway's unnyfay Iway idnday't eesay youway. Iway antedway otay elltay youway aboutway 
ethay icnicpay." 

"Ohway, atthay's ollyjay. Owhay's oinggay otay ivegay itway?" 

"Ymay amay's oinggay otay etlay emay avehay oneway." 

"Ohway, oodygay; Iway opehay eshay'll etlay _emay_ omecay." 

"Ellway, eshay illway. Ethay icnicpay's orfay emay. Eshay'll etlay anybodyway omecay atthay Iway 
antway, andway Iway antway youway." 

"Atthay's everway osay icenay. Enwhay isway itway oinggay otay ebay?" 

"Ybay andway ybay. Aybemay aboutway acationvay." 

"Ohway, onway't itway ebay unfay! Youway oinggay otay avehay allway ethay irlsgay andway oysbay?" 

"Yesway, everyway oneway atthay's iendsfray otay emay--or antsway otay ebay"; andway eshay ancedglay 
everway osay urtivelyfay atway Omtay, utbay ehay alkedtay ightray alongway otay Amyway Awrencelay 
aboutway ethay erribletay ormstay onway ethay islandway, andway owhay ethay ightninglay oretay ethay 
eatgray ycamoresay eetray "allway otay indersflay" ilewhay ehay asway "andingstay ithinway 
eethray eetfay ofway itway." 

"Ohway, aymay Iway omecay?" aidsay Acegray Illermay. 

"Yesway." 

"Andway emay?" aidsay Allysay Ogersray. 

"Yesway." 

"Andway emay, ootay?" aidsay Usysay Arperhay. "Andway Oejay?" 

"Yesway." 

Andway osay onway, ithway appingclay ofway oyfuljay andshay illtay allway ethay oupgray adhay eggedbay 
orfay invitationsway utbay Omtay andway Amyway. Enthay Omtay urnedtay oollycay awayway, illstay 
alkingtay, andway ooktay Amyway ithway imhay. Eckybay's ipslay embledtray andway ethay earstay 
amecay otay erhay eyesway; eshay idhay esethay ignssay ithway away orcedfay ayetygay andway entway onway 
atteringchay, utbay ethay ifelay adhay onegay outway ofway ethay icnicpay, ownay, andway outway ofway 
everythingway elseway; eshay otgay awayway asway oonsay asway eshay ouldcay andway idhay erselfhay andway 
adhay atwhay erhay exsay allcay "away oodgay ycray." Enthay eshay atsay oodymay, ithway oundedway 
idepray, illtay ethay ellbay angray. Eshay ousedray upway, ownay, ithway away indictivevay astcay 
inway erhay eyeway, andway avegay erhay aitedplay ailstay away akeshay andway aidsay eshay ewknay atwhay 
_eshay'd_ oday. 

Atway ecessray Omtay ontinuedcay ishay irtationflay ithway Amyway ithway ubilantjay 
elfsay-satisfaction. Andway ehay eptkay iftingdray aboutway otay indfay Eckybay andway aceratelay 
erhay ithway ethay erformancepay. Atway astlay ehay iedspay erhay, utbay erethay asway away uddensay 
allingfay ofway ishay ercurymay. Eshay asway ittingsay osilycay onway away ittlelay enchbay ehindbay 
ethay oolhouseschay ookinglay atway away icturepay-book ithway Alfredway Empletay--and osay 
absorbedway ereway eythay, andway eirthay eadshay osay oseclay ogethertay overway ethay ookbay, 
atthay eythay idday otnay eemsay otay ebay onsciouscay ofway anythingway inway ethay orldway esidesbay. 
Ealousyjay anray edray-hot oughthray Omtay's einsvay. Ehay eganbay otay atehay imselfhay orfay 
owingthray awayway ethay ancechay Eckybay adhay offeredway orfay away econciliationray. Ehay 
alledcay imselfhay away oolfay, andway allway ethay ardhay amesnay ehay ouldcay inkthay ofway. Ehay 
antedway otay ycray ithway exationvay. Amyway attedchay appilyhay alongway, asway eythay alkedway, 
orfay erhay earthay asway ingingsay, utbay Omtay's onguetay adhay ostlay itsway unctionfay. Ehay 
idday otnay earhay atwhay Amyway asway ayingsay, andway eneverwhay eshay ausedpay expectantlyway 
ehay ouldcay onlyway ammerstay anway awkwardway assentway, ichwhay asway asway oftenway isplacedmay 
asway otherwiseway. Ehay eptkay iftingdray otay ethay earray ofway ethay oolhouseschay, againway andway 
againway, otay earsay ishay eyeballsway ithway ethay atefulhay ectaclespay erethay. Ehay ouldcay 
otnay elphay itway. Andway itway addenedmay imhay otay eesay, asway ehay oughtthay ehay awsay, atthay 
Eckybay Atcherthay evernay onceway uspectedsay atthay ehay asway evenway inway ethay andlay ofway ethay 
ivinglay. Utbay eshay idday eesay, everthelessnay; andway eshay ewknay eshay asway inningway erhay 
ightfay, ootay, andway asway adglay otay eesay imhay uffersay asway eshay adhay ufferedsay. 

Amyway's appyhay attlepray ecamebay intolerableway. Omtay intedhay atway ingsthay ehay adhay 
otay attendway otay; ingsthay atthay ustmay ebay oneday; andway imetay asway eetingflay. Utbay inway 
ainvay--the irlgay irpedchay onway. Omtay oughtthay, "Ohway, anghay erhay, ainway't Iway everway oinggay 
otay etgay idray ofway erhay?" Atway astlay ehay ustmay ebay attendingway otay osethay ingsthay--and eshay 
aidsay artlesslyway atthay eshay ouldway ebay "aroundway" enwhay oolschay etlay outway. Andway ehay 
astenedhay awayway, atinghay erhay orfay itway. 

"Anyway otherway oybay!" Omtay oughtthay, atinggray ishay eethtay. "Anyway oybay inway ethay olewhay 
owntay utbay atthay Aintsay Ouislay artysmay atthay inksthay ehay essesdray osay inefay andway isway 
aristocracyway! Ohway, allway ightray, Iway ickedlay youway ethay irstfay ayday youway everway awsay isthay 
owntay, istermay, andway Iway'll icklay youway againway! Youway ustjay aitway illtay Iway atchcay youway 
outway! Iway'll ustjay aketay andway--" 

Andway ehay entway oughthray ethay otionsmay ofway ashingthray anway imaginaryway oybay--pummelling 
ethay airway, andway ickingkay andway ouginggay. "Ohway, youway oday, oday youway? Youway ollerhay 
'oughnay, oday youway? Ownay, enthay, etlay atthay earnlay youway!" Andway osay ethay imaginaryway 
oggingflay asway inishedfay otay ishay atisfactionsay. 

Omtay edflay omehay atway oonnay. Ishay onsciencecay ouldcay otnay endureway anyway oremay ofway Amyway's 
atefulgray appinesshay, andway ishay ealousyjay ouldcay earbay onay oremay ofway ethay otherway 
istressday. Eckybay esumedray erhay icturepay inspectionsway ithway Alfredway, utbay asway ethay 
inutesmay aggeddray alongway andway onay Omtay amecay otay uffersay, erhay iumphtray eganbay otay 
oudclay andway eshay ostlay interestway; avitygray andway absentmindednessway ollowedfay, 
andway enthay elancholymay; otway orway eethray imestay eshay ickedpray upway erhay earway atway 
away ootstepfay, utbay itway asway away alsefay opehay; onay Omtay amecay. Atway astlay eshay ewgray 
entirelyway iserablemay andway ishedway eshay adnhay't arriedcay itway osay arfay. Enwhay 
oorpay Alfredway, eeingsay atthay ehay asway osinglay erhay, ehay idday otnay owknay owhay, eptkay 
exclaimingway: "Ohway, erehay's away ollyjay oneway! ooklay atway isthay!" eshay ostlay atiencepay atway 
astlay, andway aidsay, "Ohway, onday't otherbay emay! Iway onday't arecay orfay emthay!" andway urstbay 
intoway earstay, andway otgay upway andway alkedway awayway. 

Alfredway oppeddray alongsideway andway asway oinggay otay ytray otay omfortcay erhay, utbay eshay 
aidsay: 

"Ogay awayway andway eavelay emay aloneway, ancay't youway! Iway atehay youway!" 

Osay ethay oybay altedhay, onderingway atwhay ehay ouldcay avehay oneday--for eshay adhay aidsay 
eshay ouldway ooklay atway icturespay allway oughthray ethay ooningnay--and eshay alkedway onway, 
yingcray. Enthay Alfredway entway usingmay intoway ethay esertedday oolhouseschay. Ehay asway 
umiliatedhay andway angryway. Ehay easilyway uessedgay ishay ayway otay ethay uthtray--the irlgay 
adhay implysay ademay away onveniencecay ofway imhay otay entvay erhay itespay uponway Omtay Awyersay. 
Ehay asway arfay omfray atinghay Omtay ethay esslay enwhay isthay oughtthay occurredway otay imhay. 
Ehay ishedway erethay asway omesay ayway otay etgay atthay oybay intoway oubletray ithoutway uchmay 
iskray otay imselfhay. Omtay's ellingspay-book ellfay underway ishay eyeway. Erehay asway ishay 
opportunityway. Ehay atefullygray openedway otay ethay essonlay orfay ethay afternoonway andway 
ouredpay inkway uponway ethay agepay. 

Eckybay, ancingglay inway atway away indowway ehindbay imhay atway ethay omentmay, awsay ethay actway, 
andway ovedmay onway, ithoutway iscoveringday erselfhay. Eshay artedstay omewardhay, ownay, 
intendingway otay indfay Omtay andway elltay imhay; Omtay ouldway ebay ankfulthay andway eirthay 
oublestray ouldway ebay ealedhay. Eforebay eshay asway alfhay ayway omehay, oweverhay, eshay 
adhay angedchay erhay indmay. Ethay oughtthay ofway Omtay's eatmenttray ofway erhay enwhay eshay asway 
alkingtay aboutway erhay icnicpay amecay orchingscay ackbay andway illedfay erhay ithway ameshay. 
Eshay esolvedray otay etlay imhay etgay ippedwhay onway ethay amagedday ellingspay-book's 
accountway, andway otay atehay imhay oreverfay, intoway ethay argainbay. 




APTERCHAY IXXAY 

OMTAY arrivedway atway omehay inway away earydray oodmay, andway ethay irstfay ingthay ishay auntway aidsay 
otay imhay owedshay imhay atthay ehay adhay oughtbray ishay orrowssay otay anway unpromisingway 
arketmay: 

"Omtay, Iway've away otionnay otay inskay youway aliveway!" 

"Auntieway, atwhay avehay Iway oneday?" 

"Ellway, youway've oneday enoughway. Erehay Iway ogay overway otay Erenysay Arperhay, ikelay anway oldway 
oftysay, expectingway Iway'm oinggay otay akemay erhay elievebay allway atthay ubbageray aboutway 
atthay eamdray, enwhay olay andway eholdbay youway eshay'd oundfay outway omfray Oejay atthay youway asway 
overway erehay andway eardhay allway ethay alktay eway adhay atthay ightnay. Omtay, Iway onday't owknay 
atwhay isway otay ecomebay ofway away oybay atthay illway actway ikelay atthay. Itway akesmay emay eelfay osay 
adbay otay inkthay youway ouldcay etlay emay ogay otay Erenysay Arperhay andway akemay uchsay away oolfay 
ofway yselfmay andway evernay aysay away ordway." 

Isthay asway away ewnay aspectway ofway ethay ingthay. Ishay artnesssmay ofway ethay orningmay adhay 
eemedsay otay Omtay away oodgay okejay eforebay, andway eryvay ingeniousway. Itway erelymay ookedlay 
eanmay andway abbyshay ownay. Ehay unghay ishay eadhay andway ouldcay otnay inkthay ofway anythingway otay 
aysay orfay away omentmay. Enthay ehay aidsay: 

"Auntieway, Iway ishway Iway adnhay't oneday itway--but Iway idnday't inkthay." 

"Ohway, ildchay, youway evernay inkthay. Youway evernay inkthay ofway anythingway utbay yourway 
ownway elfishnesssay. Youway ouldcay inkthay otay omecay allway ethay ayway overway erehay omfray 
Acksonjay's Islandway inway ethay ightnay otay aughlay atway ourway oublestray, andway youway ouldcay 
inkthay otay oolfay emay ithway away ielay aboutway away eamdray; utbay youway ouldncay't everway inkthay 
otay itypay usway andway avesay usway omfray orrowsay." 

"Auntieway, Iway owknay ownay itway asway eanmay, utbay Iway idnday't eanmay otay ebay eanmay. Iway idnday't, 
onesthay. Andway esidesbay, Iway idnday't omecay overway erehay otay aughlay atway youway atthay 
ightnay." 

"Atwhay idday youway omecay orfay, enthay?" 

"Itway asway otay elltay youway otnay otay ebay uneasyway aboutway usway, ecausebay eway adnhay't otgay 
owndeddray." 

"Omtay, Omtay, Iway ouldway ebay ethay ankfullestthay oulsay inway isthay orldway ifway Iway ouldcay 
elievebay youway everway adhay asway oodgay away oughtthay asway atthay, utbay youway owknay youway evernay 
idday--and Iway owknay itway, Omtay." 

"Indeedway andway 'eedday Iway idday, auntieway--I ishway Iway aymay evernay irstay ifway Iway idnday't." 

"Ohway, Omtay, onday't ielay--don't oday itway. Itway onlyway akesmay ingsthay away undredhay imestay 
orseway." 

"Itway ainway't away ielay, auntieway; itway's ethay uthtray. Iway antedway otay eepkay youway omfray 
ievinggray--that asway allway atthay ademay emay omecay." 

"Iway'd ivegay ethay olewhay orldway otay elievebay atthay--it ouldway overcay upway away owerpay 
ofway inssay, Omtay. Iway'd 'ostmay ebay adglay youway'd unray offway andway actedway osay adbay. Utbay itway 
ainway't easonableray; ecausebay, ywhay idnday't youway elltay emay, ildchay?" 

"Ywhay, youway eesay, enwhay youway otgay otay alkingtay aboutway ethay uneralfay, Iway ustjay otgay allway 
ullfay ofway ethay ideaway ofway ourway omingcay andway idinghay inway ethay urchchay, andway Iway ouldncay't 
omehowsay earbay otay oilspay itway. Osay Iway ustjay utpay ethay arkbay ackbay inway ymay ocketpay andway 
eptkay ummay." 

"Atwhay arkbay?" 

"Ethay arkbay Iway adhay otewray onway otay elltay youway eway'd onegay iratingpay. Iway ishway, ownay, 
youway'd akedway upway enwhay Iway issedkay youway--I oday, onesthay." 

Ethay ardhay ineslay inway ishay auntway's acefay elaxedray andway away uddensay endernesstay awnedday 
inway erhay eyesway. 

"_Idday_ youway isskay emay, Omtay?" 

"Ywhay, yesway, Iway idday." 

"Areway youway uresay youway idday, Omtay?" 

"Ywhay, yesway, Iway idday, auntieway--certain uresay." 

"Atwhay idday youway isskay emay orfay, Omtay?" 

"Ecausebay Iway ovedlay youway osay, andway youway aidlay erethay oaningmay andway Iway asway osay orrysay." 

Ethay ordsway oundedsay ikelay uthtray. Ethay oldway adylay ouldcay otnay idehay away emortray inway 
erhay oicevay enwhay eshay aidsay: 

"Isskay emay againway, Omtay!--and ebay offway ithway youway otay oolschay, ownay, andway onday't
