otherbay emay anyway oremay." 

Ethay omentmay ehay asway onegay, eshay anray otay away osetclay andway otgay outway ethay uinray ofway away 
acketjay ichwhay Omtay adhay onegay iratingpay inway. Enthay eshay oppedstay, ithway itway inway erhay 
andhay, andway aidsay otay erselfhay: 

"Onay, Iway onday't areday. Oorpay oybay, Iway eckonray ehay's iedlay aboutway itway--but itway's away 
essedblay, essedblay ielay, erethay's uchsay away omfortcay omecay omfray itway. Iway opehay 
ethay Ordlay--I _owknay_ ethay Ordlay illway orgivefay imhay, ecausebay itway asway uchsay 
oodgay-heartedness inway imhay otay elltay itway. Utbay Iway onday't antway otay indfay outway itway's away 
ielay. Iway onway't ooklay." 

Eshay utpay ethay acketjay awayway, andway oodstay ybay usingmay away inutemay. Icetway eshay utpay outway 
erhay andhay otay aketay ethay armentgay againway, andway icetway eshay efrainedray. Onceway oremay 
eshay enturedvay, andway isthay imetay eshay ortifiedfay erselfhay ithway ethay oughtthay: 
"Itway's away oodgay ielay--it's away oodgay ielay--I onway't etlay itway ievegray emay." Osay eshay 
oughtsay ethay acketjay ocketpay. Away omentmay aterlay eshay asway eadingray Omtay's iecepay ofway 
arkbay oughthray owingflay earstay andway ayingsay: "Iway ouldcay orgivefay ethay oybay, ownay, ifway 
ehay'd ommittedcay away illionmay inssay!" 




APTERCHAY XXAY 

ERETHAY asway omethingsay aboutway Auntway Ollypay's annermay, enwhay eshay issedkay Omtay, atthay 
eptsway awayway ishay owlay iritsspay andway ademay imhay ightheartedlay andway appyhay againway. Ehay 
artedstay otay oolschay andway adhay ethay ucklay ofway omingcay uponway Eckybay Atcherthay atway ethay 
eadhay ofway Eadowmay Anelay. Ishay oodmay alwaysway eterminedday ishay annermay. Ithoutway away 
omentmay's esitationhay ehay anray otay erhay andway aidsay: 

"Iway actedway ightymay eanmay odaytay, Eckybay, andway Iway'm osay orrysay. Iway onway't everway, everway 
oday atthay ayway againway, asway onglay asway everway Iway ivelay--please akemay upway, onway't youway?" 

Ethay irlgay oppedstay andway ookedlay imhay ornfullyscay inway ethay acefay: 

"Iway'll ankthay youway otay eepkay yourselfway _otay_ yourselfway, Mray. Omasthay Awyersay. Iway'll 
evernay eakspay otay youway againway." 

Eshay ossedtay erhay eadhay andway assedpay onway. Omtay asway osay unnedstay atthay ehay adhay otnay 
evenway esencepray ofway indmay enoughway otay aysay "Owhay arescay, Issmay Artysmay?" untilway ethay 
ightray imetay otay aysay itway adhay onegay ybay. Osay ehay aidsay othingnay. Utbay ehay asway inway away 
inefay ageray, everthelessnay. Ehay opedmay intoway ethay oolyardschay ishingway eshay ereway 
away oybay, andway imaginingway owhay ehay ouldway ouncetray erhay ifway eshay ereway. Ehay esentlypray 
encounteredway erhay andway eliveredday away ingingstay emarkray asway ehay assedpay. Eshay urledhay 
oneway inway eturnray, andway ethay angryway eachbray asway ompletecay. Itway eemedsay otay Eckybay, inway 
erhay othay esentmentray, atthay eshay ouldcay ardlyhay aitway orfay oolschay otay "aketay inway," 
eshay asway osay impatientway otay eesay Omtay oggedflay orfay ethay injuredway ellingspay-book. 
Ifway eshay adhay adhay anyway ingeringlay otionnay ofway exposingway Alfredway Empletay, Omtay's 
offensiveway ingflay adhay ivendray itway entirelyway awayway. 

Oorpay irlgay, eshay idday otnay owknay owhay astfay eshay asway earingnay oubletray erselfhay. 
Ethay astermay, Mray. Obbinsday, adhay eachedray iddlemay ageway ithway anway unsatisfiedway 
ambitionway. Ethay arlingday ofway ishay esiresday asway, otay ebay away octorday, utbay 
overtypay adhay ecreedday atthay ehay ouldshay ebay othingnay igherhay anthay away illagevay 
oolmasterschay. Everyway ayday ehay ooktay away ysteriousmay ookbay outway ofway ishay eskday andway 
absorbedway imselfhay inway itway atway imestay enwhay onay assesclay ereway ecitingray. Ehay eptkay 
atthay ookbay underway ocklay andway eykay. Erethay asway otnay anway urchinway inway oolschay utbay asway 
erishingpay otay avehay away impseglay ofway itway, utbay ethay ancechay evernay amecay. Everyway oybay 
andway irlgay adhay away eorythay aboutway ethay aturenay ofway atthay ookbay; utbay onay otway eoriesthay 
ereway alikeway, andway erethay asway onay ayway ofway ettinggay atway ethay actsfay inway ethay asecay. 
Ownay, asway Eckybay asway assingpay ybay ethay eskday, ichwhay oodstay earnay ethay oorday, eshay 
oticednay atthay ethay eykay asway inway ethay ocklay! Itway asway away eciouspray omentmay. Eshay 
ancedglay aroundway; oundfay erselfhay aloneway, andway ethay extnay instantway eshay adhay ethay 
ookbay inway erhay andshay. Ethay itlepagetay--Professor Omebodysay's _Anatomyway_--carried 
onay informationway otay erhay indmay; osay eshay eganbay otay urntay ethay eaveslay. Eshay amecay atway 
onceway uponway away andsomelyhay engravedway andway oloredcay ontispiecefray--a umanhay igurefay, 
arkstay akednay. Atway atthay omentmay away adowshay ellfay onway ethay agepay andway Omtay Awyersay 
eppedstay inway atway ethay oorday andway aughtcay away impseglay ofway ethay icturepay. Eckybay 
atchedsnay atway ethay ookbay otay oseclay itway, andway adhay ethay ardhay ucklay otay eartay ethay 
icturedpay agepay alfhay ownday ethay iddlemay. Eshay ustthray ethay olumevay intoway ethay eskday, 
urnedtay ethay eykay, andway urstbay outway yingcray ithway ameshay andway exationvay. 

"Omtay Awyersay, youway areway ustjay asway eanmay asway youway ancay ebay, otay eaksnay upway onway away ersonpay 
andway ooklay atway atwhay eythay're ookinglay atway." 

"Owhay ouldcay Iway owknay youway asway ookinglay atway anythingway?" 

"Youway oughtway otay ebay ashamedway ofway yourselfway, Omtay Awyersay; youway owknay youway're 
oinggay otay elltay onway emay, andway ohway, atwhay allshay Iway oday, atwhay allshay Iway oday! Iway'll ebay 
ippedwhay, andway Iway evernay asway ippedwhay inway oolschay." 

Enthay eshay ampedstay erhay ittlelay ootfay andway aidsay: 

"_Ebay_ osay eanmay ifway youway antway otay! Iway owknay omethingsay atthay's oinggay otay appenhay. 
Youway ustjay aitway andway youway'll eesay! Atefulhay, atefulhay, atefulhay!"--and eshay ungflay 
outway ofway ethay ousehay ithway away ewnay explosionway ofway yingcray. 

Omtay oodstay illstay, atherray usteredflay ybay isthay onslaughtway. Esentlypray ehay aidsay 
otay imselfhay: 

"Atwhay away uriouscay indkay ofway away oolfay away irlgay isway! Evernay eenbay ickedlay inway 
oolschay! Ucksshay! Atwhay's away ickinglay! Atthay's ustjay ikelay away irlgay--they're osay 
inthay-skinned andway ickenchay-hearted. Ellway, ofway oursecay Iway ainway't oinggay otay elltay 
oldway Obbinsday onway isthay ittlelay oolfay, ecausebay erethay's otherway aysway ofway ettinggay 
evenway onway erhay, atthay ainway't osay eanmay; utbay atwhay ofway itway? Oldway Obbinsday illway askway 
owhay itway asway oretay ishay ookbay. Obodynay'll answerway. Enthay ehay'll oday ustjay ethay ayway 
ehay alwaysway oesday--ask irstfay oneway andway enthay tway'other, andway enwhay ehay omescay otay ethay 
ightray irlgay ehay'll owknay itway, ithoutway anyway ellingtay. Irlsgay' acesfay alwaysway elltay 
onway emthay. Eythay ainway't otgay anyway ackbonebay. Eshay'll etgay ickedlay. Ellway, itway's away 
indkay ofway away ighttay aceplay orfay Eckybay Atcherthay, ecausebay erethay ainway't anyway ayway 
outway ofway itway." Omtay onnedcay ethay ingthay away omentmay ongerlay, andway enthay addedway: "Allway 
ightray, oughthay; eshay'd ikelay otay eesay emay inway ustjay uchsay away ixfay--let erhay eatsway itway 
outway!" 

Omtay oinedjay ethay obmay ofway ylarkingskay olarsschay outsideway. Inway away ewfay omentsmay ethay 
astermay arrivedway andway oolschay "ooktay inway." Omtay idday otnay eelfay away ongstray interestway 
inway ishay udiesstay. Everyway imetay ehay olestay away anceglay atway ethay irlsgay' idesay ofway ethay 
oomray Eckybay's acefay oubledtray imhay. Onsideringcay allway ingsthay, ehay idday otnay antway 
otay itypay erhay, andway yetway itway asway allway ehay ouldcay oday otay elphay itway. Ehay ouldcay etgay 
upway onay exultationway atthay asway eallyray orthyway ethay amenay. Esentlypray ethay 
ellingspay-book iscoveryday asway ademay, andway Omtay's indmay asway entirelyway ullfay 
ofway ishay ownway attersmay orfay away ilewhay afterway atthay. Eckybay ousedray upway omfray erhay 
ethargylay ofway istressday andway owedshay oodgay interestway inway ethay oceedingspray. Eshay 
idday otnay expectway atthay Omtay ouldcay etgay outway ofway ishay oubletray ybay enyingday atthay ehay 
iltspay ethay inkway onway ethay ookbay imselfhay; andway eshay asway ightray. Ethay enialday onlyway 
eemedsay otay akemay ethay ingthay orseway orfay Omtay. Eckybay upposedsay eshay ouldway ebay adglay 
ofway atthay, andway eshay iedtray otay elievebay eshay asway adglay ofway itway, utbay eshay oundfay eshay 
asway otnay ertaincay. Enwhay ethay orstway amecay otay ethay orstway, eshay adhay anway impulseway 
otay etgay upway andway elltay onway Alfredway Empletay, utbay eshay ademay anway effortway andway orcedfay 
erselfhay otay eepkay illstay--because, aidsay eshay otay erselfhay, "ehay'll elltay aboutway emay 
earingtay ethay icturepay uresay. Iway ouldnway't aysay away ordway, otnay otay avesay ishay ifelay!" 

Omtay ooktay ishay ippingwhay andway entway ackbay otay ishay eatsay otnay atway allway 
okenbray-hearted, orfay ehay oughtthay itway asway ossiblepay atthay ehay adhay unknowinglyway 
upsetway ethay inkway onway ethay ellingspay-book imselfhay, inway omesay ylarkingskay outbay--he 
adhay eniedday itway orfay ormfay's akesay andway ecausebay itway asway ustomcay, andway adhay uckstay 
otay ethay enialday omfray inciplepray. 

Away olewhay ourhay ifteddray ybay, ethay astermay atsay oddingnay inway ishay onethray, ethay airway 
asway owsydray ithway ethay umhay ofway udystay. Ybay andway ybay, Mray. Obbinsday aightenedstray 
imselfhay upway, yawnedway, enthay unlockedway ishay eskday, andway eachedray orfay ishay ookbay, 
utbay eemedsay undecidedway etherwhay otay aketay itway outway orway eavelay itway. Ostmay ofway ethay 
upilspay ancedglay upway anguidlylay, utbay erethay ereway otway amongway emthay atthay atchedway 
ishay ovementsmay ithway intentway eyesway. Mray. Obbinsday ingeredfay ishay ookbay absentlyway 
orfay away ilewhay, enthay ooktay itway outway andway ettledsay imselfhay inway ishay airchay otay eadray! 
Omtay otshay away anceglay atway Eckybay. Ehay adhay eensay away untedhay andway elplesshay abbitray 
ooklay asway eshay idday, ithway away ungay evelledlay atway itsway eadhay. Instantlyway ehay orgotfay 
ishay uarrelqay ithway erhay. Uickqay--something ustmay ebay oneday! oneday inway away ashflay, 
ootay! Utbay ethay eryvay imminenceway ofway ethay emergencyway aralyzedpay ishay inventionway. 
Oodgay!--he adhay anway inspirationway! Ehay ouldway unray andway atchsnay ethay ookbay, ingspray 
oughthray ethay oorday andway yflay. Utbay ishay esolutionray ookshay orfay oneway ittlelay 
instantway, andway ethay ancechay asway ostlay--the astermay openedway ethay olumevay. Ifway Omtay 
onlyway adhay ethay astedway opportunityway ackbay againway! Ootay atelay. Erethay asway onay elphay 
orfay Eckybay ownay, ehay aidsay. Ethay extnay omentmay ethay astermay acedfay ethay oolschay. 
Everyway eyeway anksay underway ishay azegay. Erethay asway atthay inway itway ichwhay otesmay evenway 
ethay innocentway ithway earfay. Erethay asway ilencesay ilewhay oneway ightmay ountcay entay--the 
astermay asway atheringgay ishay athwray. Enthay ehay okespay: "Owhay oretay isthay ookbay?" 

Erethay asway otnay away oundsay. Oneway ouldcay avehay eardhay away inpay opdray. Ethay illnessstay 
ontinuedcay; ethay astermay earchedsay acefay afterway acefay orfay ignssay ofway uiltgay. 

"Enjaminbay Ogersray, idday youway eartay isthay ookbay?" 

Away enialday. Anotherway ausepay. 

"Osephjay Arperhay, idday youway?" 

Anotherway enialday. Omtay's uneasinessway ewgray oremay andway oremay intenseway underway ethay 
owslay orturetay ofway esethay oceedingspray. Ethay astermay annedscay ethay anksray ofway 
oysbay--considered away ilewhay, enthay urnedtay otay ethay irlsgay: 

"Amyway Awrencelay?" 

Away akeshay ofway ethay eadhay. 

"Aciegray Illermay?" 

Ethay amesay ignsay. 

"Usansay Arperhay, idday youway oday isthay?" 

Anotherway egativenay. Ethay extnay irlgay asway Eckybay Atcherthay. Omtay asway emblingtray 
omfray eadhay otay ootfay ithway excitementway andway away ensesay ofway ethay opelessnesshay ofway ethay 
ituationsay. 

"Ebeccaray Atcherthay" [Omtay ancedglay atway erhay acefay--it asway itewhay ithway 
errortay]--"did youway eartay--no, ooklay emay inway ethay acefay" [erhay andshay oseray inway 
appealway]--"did youway eartay isthay ookbay?" 

Away oughtthay otshay ikelay ightninglay oughthray Omtay's ainbray. Ehay angspray otay ishay eetfay 
andway outedshay--"I oneday itway!" 

Ethay oolschay aredstay inway erplexitypay atway isthay incredibleway ollyfay. Omtay oodstay away

ewknay owhay ouldway aitway orfay imhay outsideway illtay ishay aptivitycay asway oneday, andway otnay

"Omtay, owhay _ouldcay_ youway ebay osay oblenay!"

ACATIONVAY asway approachingway. Ethay oolmasterschay, alwaysway everesay, ewgray everersay

"Away ISSOURIMAY AIDENMAY'S AREWELLFAY OTAY ALABAMAWAY 

"Alabamaway, oodbyegay! Iway ovelay eethay ellway! Utbay yetway orfay away ilewhay oday Iway eavelay eethay

Allasseetay's arringway oodsflay, Andway ooedway onway Oosacay's idesay Auroraway's eambay.

"Away ISIONVAY 

"Arkday andway empestuoustay asway ightnay. Aroundway ethay onethray onway ighhay otnay away inglesay

aboutway asway ifway otay enhanceway ybay eirthay aidway ethay ildnessway ofway ethay enescay. 

"Atway uchsay away imetay, osay arkday, osay earydray, orfay umanhay ympathysay ymay eryvay iritspay 
ighedsay; utbay insteadway ereofthay,

Isthay ightmarenay occupiedway omesay entay agespay ofway anuscriptmay andway oundway upway ithway away 
ermonsay osay estructiveday ofway allway opehay otay onnay-Presbyterians atthay itway ooktay 
ethay irstfay izepray. Isthay ompositioncay asway onsideredcay otay ebay ethay eryvay inestfay

Ebsterway imselfhay ightmay ellway ebay oudpray ofway itway. 

Itway aymay ebay emarkedray, inway assingpay, atthay ethay umbernay ofway ompositionscay inway ichwhay 
ethay ordway "eauteousbay" asway overway-fondled, andway umanhay experienceway eferredray otay 
asway "ifelay's agepay," asway upway otay ethay usualway averageway. 

Ownay ethay astermay, ellowmay almostway otay ethay ergevay ofway enialitygay, utpay ishay airchay

ademay away adsay usinessbay ofway itway ithway ishay unsteadyway andhay, andway away otheredsmay ittertay

aldbay atepay--for ethay ignpaintersay's oybay adhay _ildedgay_ itway! 

Atthay okebray upway ethay eetingmay. Ethay oysbay ereway avengedway. Acationvay adhay omecay. 

OTENAY:--The etendedpray "ompositionscay" uotedqay inway isthay apterchay areway akentay 
ithoutway alterationway omfray away olumevay entitledway "Osepray andway Oetrypay, ybay away 
Esternway Adylay"--but eythay areway exactlyway andway eciselypray afterway ethay oolgirlschay 
atternpay, andway encehay areway uchmay appierhay anthay anyway eremay imitationsway ouldcay ebay. 




APTERCHAY IIXXAY 

OMTAY oinedjay ethay ewnay orderway ofway Adetscay ofway Emperancetay, eingbay attractedway ybay ethay 
owyshay aracterchay ofway eirthay "egaliaray." Ehay omisedpray otay abstainway omfray okingsmay, 
ewingchay, andway ofanitypray asway onglay asway ehay emainedray away embermay. Ownay ehay oundfay outway 
away ewnay ingthay--namely, atthay otay omisepray otnay otay oday away ingthay isway ethay urestsay ayway 
inway ethay orldway otay akemay away odybay antway otay ogay andway oday atthay eryvay ingthay. Omtay oonsay 
oundfay imselfhay ormentedtay ithway away esireday otay inkdray andway earsway; ethay esireday 
ewgray otay ebay osay intenseway atthay othingnay utbay ethay opehay ofway away ancechay otay isplayday 
imselfhay inway ishay edray ashsay eptkay imhay omfray ithdrawingway omfray ethay orderway. Ourthfay 
ofway Ulyjay asway omingcay; utbay ehay oonsay avegay atthay upway--gave itway upway eforebay ehay adhay 
ornway ishay acklesshay overway ortyfay-eight ourshay--and ixedfay ishay opeshay uponway oldway 
Udgejay Azerfray, usticejay ofway ethay eacepay, owhay asway apparentlyway onway ishay eathbedday 
andway ouldway avehay away igbay ublicpay uneralfay, incesay ehay asway osay ighhay anway officialway. 
Uringday eethray aysday Omtay asway eeplyday oncernedcay aboutway ethay Udgejay's onditioncay 
andway ungryhay orfay ewsnay ofway itway. Ometimessay ishay opeshay anray ighhay--so ighhay atthay 
ehay ouldway enturevay otay etgay outway ishay egaliaray andway actisepray eforebay ethay 
ookinglay-glass. Utbay ethay Udgejay adhay away ostmay iscouragingday ayway ofway uctuatingflay. 
Atway astlay ehay asway onouncedpray uponway ethay endmay--and enthay onvalescentcay. Omtay asway 
isgustedday; andway eltfay away ensesay ofway injuryway, ootay. Ehay andedhay inway ishay esignationray 
atway onceway--and atthay ightnay ethay Udgejay ufferedsay away elapseray andway iedday. Omtay 
esolvedray atthay ehay ouldway evernay usttray away anmay ikelay atthay againway. 

Ethay uneralfay asway away inefay ingthay. Ethay Adetscay aradedpay inway away ylestay alculatedcay 
otay illkay ethay atelay embermay ithway envyway. Omtay asway away eefray oybay againway, 
oweverhay--there asway omethingsay inway atthay. Ehay ouldcay inkdray andway earsway, ownay--but 
oundfay otay ishay urprisesay atthay ehay idday otnay antway otay. Ethay implesay actfay atthay ehay 
ouldcay, ooktay ethay esireday awayway, andway ethay armchay ofway itway. 

Omtay esentlypray onderedway otay indfay atthay ishay ovetedcay acationvay asway eginningbay 
otay anghay away ittlelay eavilyhay onway ishay andshay. 

Ehay attemptedway away iaryday--but othingnay appenedhay uringday eethray aysday, andway osay ehay 
abandonedway itway. 

Ethay irstfay ofway allway ethay egronay instrelmay owsshay amecay otay owntay, andway ademay away 
ensationsay. Omtay andway Oejay Arperhay otgay upway away andbay ofway erformerspay andway ereway appyhay 
orfay otway aysday. 

Evenway ethay Oriousglay Ourthfay asway inway omesay ensesay away ailurefay, orfay itway ainedray 
ardhay, erethay asway onay ocessionpray inway onsequencecay, andway ethay eatestgray anmay 
inway ethay orldway (asway Omtay upposedsay), Mray. Entonbay, anway actualway Unitedway Atesstay 
Enatorsay, ovedpray anway overwhelmingway isappointmentday--for ehay asway otnay 
entytway-five eetfay ighhay, ornay evenway anywhereway inway ethay eighborhoodnay ofway itway. 

Away ircuscay amecay. Ethay oysbay ayedplay ircuscay orfay eethray aysday afterwardway inway entstay 
ademay ofway agray arpetingcay--admission, eethray inspay orfay oysbay, otway orfay irlsgay--and 
enthay ircusingcay asway abandonedway. 

Away enologistphray andway away esmerizermay amecay--and entway againway andway eftlay ethay illagevay 
ullerday andway earierdray anthay everway. 

Erethay ereway omesay oysbay-and-girls' artiespay, utbay eythay ereway osay ewfay andway osay 
elightfulday atthay eythay onlyway ademay ethay achingway oidsvay etweenbay acheway ethay arderhay. 

Eckybay Atcherthay asway onegay otay erhay Onstantinoplecay omehay otay aystay ithway erhay 
arentspay uringday acationvay--so erethay asway onay ightbray idesay otay ifelay anywhereway. 

Ethay eadfuldray ecretsay ofway ethay urdermay asway away onicchray iserymay. Itway asway away eryvay 
ancercay orfay ermanencypay andway ainpay. 

Enthay amecay ethay easlesmay. 

Uringday otway onglay eeksway Omtay aylay away isonerpray, eadday otay ethay orldway andway itsway 
appeningshay. Ehay asway eryvay illway, ehay asway interestedway inway othingnay. Enwhay ehay otgay 
uponway ishay eetfay atway astlay andway ovedmay eeblyfay owntownday, away elancholymay angechay adhay 
omecay overway everythingway andway everyway eaturecray. Erethay adhay eenbay away "evivalray," andway 
everybodyway adhay "otgay eligionray," otnay onlyway ethay adultsway, utbay evenway ethay oysbay andway 
irlsgay. Omtay entway aboutway, opinghay againstway opehay orfay ethay ightsay ofway oneway essedblay 
infulsay acefay, utbay isappointmentday ossedcray imhay everywhereway. Ehay oundfay Oejay 
Arperhay udyingstay away Estamenttay, andway urnedtay adlysay awayway omfray ethay epressingday 
ectaclespay. Ehay oughtsay Enbay Ogersray, andway oundfay imhay isitingvay ethay oorpay ithway away 
asketbay ofway actstray. Ehay untedhay upway Imjay Ollishay, owhay alledcay ishay attentionway otay 
ethay eciouspray essingblay ofway ishay atelay easlesmay asway away arningway. Everyway oybay 
ehay encounteredway addedway anotherway ontay otay ishay epressionday; andway enwhay, inway 
esperationday, ehay ewflay orfay efugeray atway astlay otay ethay osombay ofway Uckleberryhay Innfay 
andway asway eceivedray ithway away Ipturalscray uotationqay, ishay earthay okebray andway ehay 
eptcray omehay andway otay edbay ealizingray atthay ehay aloneway ofway allway ethay owntay asway ostlay, 
oreverfay andway oreverfay. 

Andway atthay ightnay erethay amecay onway away errifictay ormstay, ithway ivingdray ainray, awfulway 
apsclay ofway underthay andway indingblay eetsshay ofway ightninglay. Ehay overedcay ishay eadhay 
ithway ethay edclothesbay andway aitedway inway away orrorhay ofway uspensesay orfay ishay oomday; orfay 
ehay adhay otnay ethay adowshay ofway away oubtday atthay allway isthay ubbubhay asway aboutway imhay. 
Ehay elievedbay ehay adhay axedtay ethay orbearancefay ofway ethay owerspay aboveway otay ethay 
extremityway ofway enduranceway andway atthay isthay asway ethay esultray. Itway ightmay avehay 
eemedsay otay imhay away asteway ofway omppay andway ammunitionway otay illkay away ugbay ithway away 
atterybay ofway artilleryway, utbay erethay eemedsay othingnay incongruousway aboutway ethay 
ettinggay upway uchsay anway expensiveway understormthay asway isthay otay ockknay ethay urftay omfray 
underway anway insectway ikelay imselfhay. 

Ybay andway ybay ethay empesttay entspay itselfway andway iedday ithoutway accomplishingway itsway 
objectway. Ethay oybay's irstfay impulseway asway otay ebay atefulgray, andway eformray. Ishay 
econdsay asway otay aitway--for erethay ightmay otnay ebay anyway oremay ormsstay. 

Ethay extnay ayday ethay octorsday ereway ackbay; Omtay adhay elapsedray. Ethay eethray eeksway ehay 
entspay onway ishay ackbay isthay imetay eemedsay anway entireway ageway. Enwhay ehay otgay abroadway 
atway astlay ehay asway ardlyhay atefulgray atthay ehay adhay eenbay aredspay, ememberingray owhay 
onelylay asway ishay estateway, owhay ompanionlesscay andway orlornfay ehay asway. Ehay ifteddray 
istlesslylay ownday ethay eetstray andway oundfay Imjay Ollishay actingway asway udgejay inway away 
uvenilejay ourtcay atthay asway yingtray away atcay orfay urdermay, inway ethay esencepray ofway erhay 
ictimvay, away irdbay. Ehay oundfay Oejay Arperhay andway Uckhay Innfay upway anway alleyway eatingway away 
olenstay elonmay. Oorpay adslay! eythay--like Omtay--had ufferedsay away elapseray. 




APTERCHAY IIIXXAY 

ATWAY astlay ethay eepyslay atmosphereway asway irredstay--and igorouslyvay: ethay urdermay 
ialtray amecay onway inway ethay ourtcay. Itway ecamebay ethay absorbingway opictay ofway illagevay 
alktay immediatelyway. Omtay ouldcay otnay etgay awayway omfray itway. Everyway eferenceray otay 
ethay urdermay entsay away uddershay otay ishay earthay, orfay ishay oubledtray onsciencecay 
andway earsfay almostway ersuadedpay imhay atthay esethay emarksray ereway utpay orthfay inway 
ishay earinghay asway "eelersfay"; ehay idday otnay eesay owhay ehay ouldcay ebay uspectedsay ofway 
owingknay anythingway aboutway ethay urdermay, utbay illstay ehay ouldcay otnay ebay omfortablecay 
inway ethay idstmay ofway isthay ossipgay. Itway eptkay imhay inway away oldcay ivershay allway ethay imetay. 
Ehay ooktay Uckhay otay away onelylay aceplay otay avehay away alktay ithway imhay. Itway ouldway ebay omesay 
eliefray otay unsealway ishay onguetay orfay away ittlelay ilewhay; otay ivideday ishay urdenbay ofway 
istressday ithway anotherway ufferersay. Oreovermay, ehay antedway otay assureway imselfhay 
atthay Uckhay adhay emainedray iscreetday. 

"Uckhay, avehay youway everway oldtay anybodyway aboutway--that?" 

"'Outbay atwhay?" 

"Youway owknay atwhay." 

"Ohway--'course Iway avenhay't." 

"Evernay away ordway?" 

"Evernay away olitarysay ordway, osay elphay emay. Atwhay akesmay youway askway?" 

"Ellway, Iway asway afeardway." 

"Ywhay, Omtay Awyersay, eway ouldnway't ebay aliveway otway aysday ifway atthay otgay oundfay outway. 
_Youway_ owknay atthay." 

Omtay eltfay oremay omfortablecay. Afterway away ausepay: 

"Uckhay, eythay ouldncay't anybodyway etgay youway otay elltay, ouldcay eythay?" 

"Etgay emay otay elltay? Ywhay, ifway Iway antedway atthay alfbreedhay evilday otay ownddray emay eythay 
ouldcay etgay emay otay elltay. Eythay ainway't onay ifferentday ayway." 

"Ellway, atthay's allway ightray, enthay. Iway eckonray eway're afesay asway onglay asway eway eepkay 
ummay. Utbay etlay's earsway againway, anywayway. Itway's oremay urersay." 

"Iway'm agreedway." 

Osay eythay oresway againway ithway eaddray olemnitiessay. 

"Atwhay isway ethay alktay aroundway, Uckhay? Iway've eardhay away owerpay ofway itway." 

"Alktay? Ellway, itway's ustjay Uffmay Otterpay, Uffmay Otterpay, Uffmay Otterpay allway ethay 
imetay. Itway eepskay emay inway away eatsway, onstantcay, osay's Iway antway otay idehay omsay'ers." 

"Atthay's ustjay ethay amesay ayway eythay ogay onway oundray emay. Iway eckonray ehay's away onergay. 
Onday't youway eelfay orrysay orfay imhay, ometimessay?" 

"Ostmay alwaysway--most alwaysway. Ehay ainway't onay accountway; utbay enthay ehay ainhay't everway 
oneday anythingway otay urthay anybodyway. Ustjay ishesfay away ittlelay, otay etgay oneymay otay 
etgay unkdray onway--and oafslay aroundway onsiderablecay; utbay ordlay, eway allway oday 
atthay--leastways ostmay ofway usway--preachers andway uchsay ikelay. Utbay ehay's indkay ofway 
oodgay--he ivegay emay alfhay away ishfay, onceway, enwhay erethay arnway't enoughway orfay otway; andway 
otslay ofway imestay ehay's indkay ofway oodstay ybay emay enwhay Iway asway outway ofway ucklay." 

"Ellway, ehay's endedmay iteskay orfay emay, Uckhay, andway ittedknay ookshay onway otay ymay inelay. 
Iway ishway eway ouldcay etgay imhay outway ofway erethay." 

"Ymay! eway ouldncay't etgay imhay outway, Omtay. Andway esidesbay, 'ouldntway't oday anyway oodgay; 
eythay'd etchkay imhay againway." 

"Yesway--so eythay ouldway. Utbay Iway atehay otay earhay 'emway abuseway imhay osay ikelay ethay ickensday 
enwhay ehay evernay oneday--that." 

"Iway oday ootay, Omtay. Ordlay, Iway earhay 'emway aysay ehay's ethay oodiestblay ookinglay illainvay 
inway isthay ountrycay, andway eythay onderway ehay asnway't everway unghay eforebay." 

"Yesway, eythay alktay ikelay atthay, allway ethay imetay. Iway've eardhay 'emway aysay atthay ifway ehay 
asway otay etgay eefray eythay'd ynchlay imhay." 

"Andway eythay'd oday itway, ootay." 

Ethay oysbay adhay away onglay alktay, utbay itway oughtbray emthay ittlelay omfortcay. Asway ethay 
ilighttway ewdray onway, eythay oundfay emselvesthay anginghay aboutway ethay eighborhoodnay 
ofway ethay ittlelay isolatedway ailjay, erhapspay ithway anway undefinedway opehay atthay 
omethingsay ouldway appenhay atthay ightmay earclay awayway eirthay ifficultiesday. Utbay 
othingnay appenedhay; erethay eemedsay otay ebay onay angelsway orway airiesfay interestedway inway 
isthay ucklesslay aptivecay. 

Ethay oysbay idday asway eythay adhay oftenway oneday eforebay--went otay ethay ellcay atinggray andway 
avegay Otterpay omesay obaccotay andway atchesmay. Ehay asway onway ethay oundgray oorflay andway 
erethay ereway onay uardsgay. 

Ishay atitudegray orfay eirthay iftsgay adhay alwaysway otesmay eirthay onsciencescay 
eforebay--it utcay eeperday anthay everway, isthay imetay. Eythay eltfay owardlycay andway 
eacheroustray otay ethay astlay egreeday enwhay Otterpay aidsay: 

"Youway've eenbay ightymay oodgay otay emay, oysbay--better'n anybodyway elseway inway isthay owntay. 
Andway Iway onday't orgetfay itway, Iway onday't. Oftenway Iway ayssay otay yselfmay, ayssay Iway, 'Iway usedway 
otay endmay allway ethay oysbay' iteskay andway ingsthay, andway owshay 'emway erewhay ethay oodgay 
ishinfay' acesplay asway, andway efriendbay 'emway atwhay Iway ouldcay, andway ownay eythay've 
allway orgotfay oldway Uffmay enwhay ehay's inway oubletray; utbay Omtay onday't, andway Uckhay 
onday't--_they_ onday't orgetfay imhay, ayssay Iway, 'andway Iway onday't orgetfay emthay.' Ellway, 
oysbay, Iway oneday anway awfulway ingthay--drunk andway azycray atway ethay imetay--that's ethay onlyway 
ayway Iway accountway orfay itway--and ownay Iway otgay otay ingsway orfay itway, andway itway's ightray. 
Ightray, andway _estbay_, ootay, Iway eckonray--hope osay, anywayway. Ellway, eway onway't alktay 
aboutway atthay. Iway onday't antway otay akemay _youway_ eelfay adbay; youway've efriendedbay emay. 
Utbay atwhay Iway antway otay aysay, isway, onday't _youway_ everway etgay unkdray--then youway onway't 
everway etgay erehay. Andstay away itterlay urderfay estway--so--that's itway; itway's away imepray 
omfortcay otay eesay acesfay atthay's iendlyfray enwhay away odybay's inway uchsay away uckmay 
ofway oubletray, andway erethay onday't onenay omecay erehay utbay yournway. Oodgay iendlyfray 
acesfay--good iendlyfray acesfay. Itgay upway onway oneway anotherway's acksbay andway etlay emay 
ouchtay 'emway. Atthay's itway. Akeshay andshay--yourn'll omecay oughthray ethay arsbay, utbay 
inemay's ootay igbay. Ittlelay andshay, andway eakway--but eythay've elpedhay Uffmay Otterpay away 
owerpay, andway eythay'd elphay imhay oremay ifway eythay ouldcay." 

Omtay entway omehay iserablemay, andway ishay eamsdray atthay ightnay ereway ullfay ofway orrorshay. 
Ethay extnay ayday andway ethay ayday afterway, ehay unghay aboutway ethay ourtroomcay, awndray ybay anway 
almostway irresistibleway impulseway otay ogay inway, utbay orcingfay imselfhay otay aystay outway. 
Uckhay asway avinghay ethay amesay experienceway. Eythay udiouslystay avoidedway eachway otherway. 
Eachway anderedway awayway, omfray imetay otay imetay, utbay ethay amesay ismalday ascinationfay 
alwaysway oughtbray emthay ackbay esentlypray. Omtay eptkay ishay earsway openway enwhay idlersway 
aunteredsay outway ofway ethay ourtroomcay, utbay invariablyway eardhay istressingday 
ewsnay--the oilstay ereway osingclay oremay andway oremay elentlesslyray aroundway oorpay 
Otterpay. Atway ethay endway ofway ethay econdsay ayday ethay illagevay alktay asway otay ethay effectway 
atthay Injunway Oejay's evidenceway oodstay irmfay andway unshakenway, andway atthay erethay asway 
otnay ethay ightestslay uestionqay asway otay atwhay ethay uryjay's erdictvay ouldway ebay. 

Omtay asway outway atelay, atthay ightnay, andway amecay otay edbay oughthray ethay indowway. Ehay 
asway inway away emendoustray atestay ofway excitementway. Itway asway ourshay eforebay ehay otgay otay 
eepslay. Allway ethay illagevay ockedflay otay ethay ourthousecay ethay extnay orningmay, orfay 
isthay asway otay ebay ethay eatgray ayday. Othbay exessay ereway aboutway equallyway epresentedray 
inway ethay ackedpay audienceway. Afterway away onglay aitway ethay uryjay iledfay inway andway ooktay 
eirthay acesplay; ortlyshay afterwardway, Otterpay, alepay andway aggardhay, imidtay andway 
opelesshay, asway oughtbray inway, ithway ainschay uponway imhay, andway eatedsay erewhay allway 
ethay uriouscay eyesway ouldcay arestay atway imhay; onay esslay onspicuouscay asway Injunway Oejay, 
olidstay asway everway. Erethay asway anotherway ausepay, andway enthay ethay udgejay arrivedway andway 
ethay eriffshay oclaimedpray ethay openingway ofway ethay ourtcay. Ethay usualway isperingswhay 
amongway ethay awyerslay andway atheringgay ogethertay ofway aperspay ollowedfay. Esethay 
etailsday andway accompanyingway elaysday orkedway upway anway atmosphereway ofway eparationpray 
atthay asway asway impressiveway asway itway asway ascinatingfay. 

Ownay away itnessway asway alledcay owhay estifiedtay atthay ehay oundfay Uffmay Otterpay ashingway 
inway ethay ookbray, atway anway earlyway ourhay ofway ethay orningmay atthay ethay urdermay asway 
iscoveredday, andway atthay ehay immediatelyway eakedsnay awayway. Afterway omesay urtherfay 
uestioningqay, ounselcay orfay ethay osecutionpray aidsay: 

"Aketay ethay itnessway." 

Ethay isonerpray aisedray ishay eyesway orfay away omentmay, utbay oppeddray emthay againway enwhay 
ishay ownway ounselcay aidsay: 

"Iway avehay onay uestionsqay otay askway imhay." 

Ethay extnay itnessway ovedpray ethay indingfay ofway ethay ifeknay earnay ethay orpsecay. 
Ounselcay orfay ethay osecutionpray aidsay: 

"Aketay ethay itnessway." 

"Iway avehay onay uestionsqay otay askway imhay," Otterpay's awyerlay epliedray. 

Away irdthay itnessway oresway ehay adhay oftenway eensay ethay ifeknay inway Otterpay's 
ossessionpay. 

"Aketay ethay itnessway." 

Ounselcay orfay Otterpay eclinedday otay uestionqay imhay. Ethay acesfay ofway ethay audienceway 
eganbay otay etraybay annoyanceway. Idday isthay attorneyway eanmay otay owthray awayway ishay 
ientclay's ifelay ithoutway anway effortway? 

Everalsay itnessesway eposedday oncerningcay Otterpay's uiltygay ehaviorbay enwhay 
oughtbray otay ethay enescay ofway ethay urdermay. Eythay ereway allowedway otay eavelay ethay andstay 
ithoutway eingbay osscray-questioned. 

Everyway etailday ofway ethay amagingday ircumstancescay atthay occurredway inway ethay 
aveyardgray uponway atthay orningmay ichwhay allway esentpray ememberedray osay ellway asway 
oughtbray outway ybay ediblecray itnessesway, utbay onenay ofway emthay ereway osscray-examined 
ybay Otterpay's awyerlay. Ethay erplexitypay andway issatisfactionday ofway ethay ousehay 
expressedway itselfway inway urmursmay andway ovokedpray away eproofray omfray ethay enchbay. 
Ounselcay orfay ethay osecutionpray ownay aidsay: 

"Ybay ethay oathsway ofway itizenscay osewhay implesay ordway isway aboveway uspicionsay, eway avehay 
astenedfay isthay awfulway imecray, eyondbay allway ossibilitypay ofway uestionqay, uponway ethay 
unhappyway isonerpray atway ethay arbay. Eway estray ourway asecay erehay." 

Away oangray escapedway omfray oorpay Otterpay, andway ehay utpay ishay acefay inway ishay andshay andway 
ockedray ishay odybay oftlysay otay andway ofray, ilewhay away ainfulpay ilencesay eignedray 
inway ethay ourtroomcay. Anymay enmay ereway ovedmay, andway anymay omenway's ompassioncay 
estifiedtay itselfway inway earstay. Ounselcay orfay ethay efenceday oseray andway aidsay: 

"Yourway onorhay, inway ourway emarksray atway ethay openingway ofway isthay ialtray, eway 
oreshadowedfay ourway urposepay otay ovepray atthay ourway ientclay idday isthay earfulfay eedday 
ilewhay underway ethay influenceway ofway away indblay andway irresponsibleway eliriumday oducedpray 
ybay inkdray. Eway avehay angedchay ourway indmay. Eway allshay otnay offerway atthay eaplay." [Enthay 
otay ethay erkclay:] "Allcay Omasthay Awyersay!" 

Away uzzledpay amazementway awokeway inway everyway acefay inway ethay ousehay, otnay evenway exceptingway 
Otterpay's. Everyway eyeway astenedfay itselfway ithway onderingway interestway uponway Omtay asway 
ehay oseray andway ooktay ishay aceplay uponway ethay andstay. Ethay oybay ookedlay ildway enoughway, 
orfay ehay asway adlybay aredscay. Ethay oathway asway administeredway. 

"Omasthay Awyersay, erewhay ereway youway onway ethay eventeenthsay ofway Unejay, aboutway ethay 
ourhay ofway idnightmay?" 

Omtay ancedglay atway Injunway Oejay's ironway acefay andway ishay onguetay ailedfay imhay. Ethay 
audienceway istenedlay eathlessbray, utbay ethay ordsway efusedray otay omecay. Afterway away ewfay 
omentsmay, oweverhay, ethay oybay otgay away ittlelay ofway ishay engthstray ackbay, andway anagedmay 
otay utpay enoughway ofway itway intoway ishay oicevay otay akemay artpay ofway ethay ousehay earhay: 

"Inway ethay aveyardgray!" 

"Away ittlelay itbay ouderlay, easeplay. Onday't ebay afraidway. Youway ereway--" 

"Inway ethay aveyardgray." 

Away ontemptuouscay ilesmay ittedflay acrossway Injunway Oejay's acefay. 

"Ereway youway anywhereway earnay Orsehay Illiamsway' avegray?" 

"Yesway, irsay." 

"Eakspay upway--just away ifletray ouderlay. Owhay earnay ereway youway?" 

"Earnay asway Iway amway otay youway." 

"Ereway youway iddenhay, orway otnay?" 

"Iway asway idhay." 

"Erewhay?" 

"Ehindbay ethay elmsway atthay's onway ethay edgeway ofway ethay avegray." 

Injunway Oejay avegay away arelybay erceptiblepay artstay. 

"Anyway oneway ithway youway?" 

"Yesway, irsay. Iway entway erethay ithway--" 

"Aitway--wait away omentmay. Evernay indmay entioningmay yourway ompanioncay's amenay. Eway 
illway oducepray imhay atway ethay operpray imetay. Idday youway arrycay anythingway erethay ithway 
youway." 

Omtay esitatedhay andway ookedlay onfusedcay. 

"Eakspay outway, ymay oybay--don't ebay iffidentday. Ethay uthtray isway alwaysway espectableray. 
Atwhay idday youway aketay erethay?" 

"Onlyway away--a--dead atcay." 

Erethay asway away ippleray ofway irthmay, ichwhay ethay ourtcay eckedchay. 

"Eway illway oducepray ethay eletonskay ofway atthay atcay. Ownay, ymay oybay, elltay usway 
everythingway atthay occurredway--tell itway inway yourway ownway ayway--don't ipskay anythingway, 
andway onday't ebay afraidway." 

Omtay eganbay--hesitatingly atway irstfay, utbay asway ehay armedway otay ishay ubjectsay ishay 
ordsway owedflay oremay andway oremay easilyway; inway away ittlelay ilewhay everyway oundsay easedcay 
utbay ishay ownway oicevay; everyway eyeway ixedfay itselfway uponway imhay; ithway artedpay ipslay andway 
atedbay eathbray ethay audienceway unghay uponway ishay ordsway, akingtay onay otenay ofway imetay, 
aptray inway ethay astlyghay ascinationsfay ofway ethay aletay. Ethay ainstray uponway entpay 
emotionway eachedray itsway imaxclay enwhay ethay oybay aidsay: 

"--andway asway ethay octorday etchedfay ethay oardbay aroundway andway Uffmay Otterpay ellfay, Injunway 
Oejay umpedjay ithway ethay ifeknay andway--" 

Ashcray! Uickqay asway ightninglay ethay alfbreedhay angspray orfay away indowway, oretay ishay 
ayway oughthray allway opposersway, andway asway onegay! 




APTERCHAY IVXXAY 

OMTAY asway away itteringglay erohay onceway oremay--the etpay ofway ethay oldway, ethay envyway ofway ethay 
youngway. Ishay amenay evenway entway intoway immortalway intpray, orfay ethay illagevay aperpay 
agnifiedmay imhay. Erethay ereway omesay atthay elievedbay ehay ouldway ebay Esidentpray, yetway, 
ifway ehay escapedway anginghay. 

Asway usualway, ethay icklefay, unreasoningway orldway ooktay Uffmay Otterpay otay itsway osombay 
andway ondledfay imhay asway avishlylay asway itway adhay abusedway imhay eforebay. Utbay atthay ortsay 
ofway onductcay isway otay ethay orldway's editcray; ereforethay itway isway otnay ellway otay indfay 
aultfay ithway itway. 

Omtay's aysday ereway aysday ofway endorsplay andway exultationway otay imhay, utbay ishay ightsnay 
ereway easonssay ofway orrorhay. Injunway Oejay infestedway allway ishay eamsdray, andway alwaysway 
ithway oomday inway ishay eyeway. Ardlyhay anyway emptationtay ouldcay ersuadepay ethay oybay 
otay irstay abroadway afterway ightfallnay. Oorpay Uckhay asway inway ethay amesay atestay ofway 
etchednesswray andway errortay, orfay Omtay adhay oldtay ethay olewhay orystay otay ethay awyerlay 
ethay ightnay eforebay ethay eatgray ayday ofway ethay ialtray, andway Uckhay asway oresay afraidway 
atthay ishay areshay inway ethay usinessbay ightmay eaklay outway, yetway, otwithstandingnay 
Injunway Oejay's ightflay adhay avedsay imhay ethay ufferingsay ofway estifyingtay inway ourtcay. 
Ethay oorpay ellowfay adhay otgay ethay attorneyway otay omisepray ecrecysay, utbay atwhay ofway 
atthay? Incesay Omtay's arassedhay onsciencecay adhay anagedmay otay ivedray imhay otay ethay 
awyerlay's ousehay ybay ightnay andway ingwray away eaddray aletay omfray ipslay atthay adhay 
eenbay ealedsay ithway ethay ismalestday andway ostmay ormidablefay ofway oathsway, Uckhay's 
onfidencecay inway ethay umanhay aceray asway ellnighway obliteratedway. 

Ailyday Uffmay Otterpay's atitudegray ademay Omtay adglay ehay adhay okenspay; utbay ightlynay 
ehay ishedway ehay adhay ealedsay upway ishay onguetay. 

Alfhay ethay imetay Omtay asway afraidway Injunway Oejay ouldway evernay ebay apturedcay; ethay 
otherway alfhay ehay asway afraidway ehay ouldway ebay. Ehay eltfay uresay ehay evernay ouldcay awdray away 
afesay eathbray againway untilway atthay anmay asway eadday andway ehay adhay eensay ethay orpsecay. 

Ewardsray adhay eenbay offeredway, ethay ountrycay adhay eenbay ouredscay, utbay onay Injunway 
Oejay asway oundfay. Oneway ofway osethay omniscientway andway aweinspiringway arvelsmay, away 
etectiveday, amecay upway omfray Stay. Ouislay, ousedmay aroundway, ookshay ishay eadhay, ookedlay 
iseway, andway ademay atthay ortsay ofway astoundingway uccesssay ichwhay embersmay ofway atthay 
aftcray usuallyway achieveway. Atthay isway otay aysay, ehay "oundfay away ewclay." Utbay youway ancay't 
anghay away "ewclay" orfay urdermay, andway osay afterway atthay etectiveday adhay otgay oughthray 
andway onegay omehay, Omtay eltfay ustjay asway insecureway asway ehay asway eforebay. 

Ethay owslay aysday ifteddray onway, andway eachway eftlay ehindbay itway away ightlyslay ightenedlay 
eightway ofway apprehensionway. 




APTERCHAY XXVAY 

ERETHAY omescay away imetay inway everyway ightlyray-constructed oybay's ifelay enwhay ehay ashay 
away agingray esireday otay ogay omewheresay andway igday orfay iddenhay easuretray. Isthay esireday 
uddenlysay amecay uponway Omtay oneway ayday. Ehay alliedsay outway otay indfay Oejay Arperhay, 
utbay ailedfay ofway uccesssay. Extnay ehay oughtsay Enbay Ogersray; ehay adhay onegay ishingfay. 
Esentlypray ehay umbledstay uponway Uckhay Innfay ethay Edray-Handed. Uckhay ouldway 
answerway. Omtay ooktay imhay otay away ivatepray aceplay andway openedway ethay attermay otay imhay 
onfidentiallycay. Uckhay asway illingway. Uckhay asway alwaysway illingway otay aketay away andhay 
inway anyway enterpriseway atthay offeredway entertainmentway andway equiredray onay apitalcay, 
orfay ehay adhay away oublesometray uperabundancesay ofway atthay ortsay ofway imetay ichwhay isway 
otnay oneymay. "Erewhay'll eway igday?" aidsay Uckhay. 

"Ohway, ostmay anywhereway." 

"Ywhay, isway itway idhay allway aroundway?" 

"Onay, indeedway itway ainway't. Itway's idhay inway ightymay articularpay acesplay, 
Uckhay--sometimes onway islandsway, ometimessay inway ottenray estschay underway ethay endway ofway 
away imblay ofway anway oldway eadday eetray, ustjay erewhay ethay adowshay allsfay atway idnightmay; utbay 
ostlymay underway ethay oorflay inway ahay'nted ouseshay." 

"Owhay ideshay itway?" 

"Ywhay, obbersray, ofway oursecay--who'd youway eckonray? Undaysay-school 
upsay'rintendents?" 

"Iway onday't owknay. Ifway 'astway inemay Iway ouldnway't idehay itway; Iway'd endspay itway andway avehay away 
oodgay imetay." 

"Osay ouldway Iway. Utbay obbersray onday't oday atthay ayway. Eythay alwaysway idehay itway andway 
eavelay itway erethay." 

"Onday't eythay omecay afterway itway anyway oremay?" 

"Onay, eythay inkthay eythay illway, utbay eythay enerallygay orgetfay ethay arksmay, orway elseway 
eythay ieday. Anywayway, itway ayslay erethay away onglay imetay andway etsgay ustyray; andway ybay andway 
ybay omebodysay indsfay anway oldway yellowway aperpay atthay ellstay owhay otay indfay ethay arksmay--a 
aperpay atthay's otgay otay ebay ipheredcay overway aboutway away eekway ecausebay itway's ostlymay 
ignssay andway yhay'roglyphics." 

"Yrohay--which?" 

"Yhay'roglyphics--pictures andway ingsthay, youway owknay, atthay onday't eemsay otay eanmay 
anythingway." 

"Avehay youway otgay oneway ofway emthay aperspay, Omtay?" 

"Onay." 

"Ellway enthay, owhay youway oinggay otay indfay ethay arksmay?" 

"Iway onday't antway anyway arksmay. Eythay alwaysway urybay itway underway away ahay'nted ousehay orway onway 
anway islandway, orway underway away eadday eetray atthay's otgay oneway imblay ickingstay outway. Ellway, 
eway've iedtray Acksonjay's Islandway away ittlelay, andway eway ancay ytray itway againway omesay 
imetay; andway erethay's ethay oldway ahay'nted ousehay upway ethay Illstay-House anchbray, andway 
erethay's otslay ofway eadday-limb eestray--dead oadslay ofway 'emway." 

"Isway itway underway allway ofway emthay?" 

"Owhay youway alktay! Onay!" 

"Enthay owhay youway oinggay otay owknay ichwhay oneway otay ogay orfay?" 

"Ogay orfay allway ofway 'emway!" 

"Ywhay, Omtay, itway'll aketay allway ummersay." 

"Ellway, atwhay ofway atthay? Upposesay youway indfay away assbray otpay ithway away undredhay ollarsday 
inway itway, allway ustyray andway aygray, orway ottenray estchay ullfay ofway iday'monds. Owhay's 
atthay?" 

Uckhay's eyesway owedglay. 

"Atthay's ullybay. Entyplay ullybay enoughway orfay emay. Ustjay youway immegay ethay undredhay 
ollarsday andway Iway onday't antway onay iday'monds." 

"Allway ightray. Utbay Iway etbay youway Iway ainway't oinggay otay owthray offway onway iday'monds. Omesay 
ofway 'emway's orthway entytway ollarsday apieceway--there ainway't anyway, ardlyhay, utbay's 
orthway ixsay itsbay orway away ollarday." 

"Onay! Isway atthay osay?" 

"Ertcay'nly--anybody'll elltay youway osay. Ainhay't youway everway eensay oneway, Uckhay?" 

"Otnay asway Iway ememberray." 

"Ohway, ingskay avehay athersslay ofway emthay." 

"Ellway, Iway onday' owknay onay ingskay, Omtay." 

"Iway eckonray youway onday't. Utbay ifway youway asway otay ogay otay Europeway youway'd eesay away aftray ofway 
'emway oppinghay aroundway." 

"Oday eythay ophay?" 

"Ophay?--your annygray! Onay!" 

"Ellway, atwhay idday youway aysay eythay idday, orfay?" 

"Ucksshay, Iway onlyway eantmay youway'd _eesay_ 'emway--not oppinghay, ofway oursecay--what oday 
eythay antway otay ophay orfay?--but Iway eanmay youway'd ustjay eesay 'emway--scattered aroundway, 
youway owknay, inway away indkay ofway away eneralgay ayway. Ikelay atthay oldway umpbackedhay Ichardray." 

"Ichardray? Atwhay's ishay otherway amenay?" 

"Ehay idnday't avehay anyway otherway amenay. Ingskay onday't avehay anyway utbay away ivengay amenay." 

"Onay?" 

"Utbay eythay onday't." 

"Ellway, ifway eythay ikelay itway, Omtay, allway ightray; utbay Iway onday't antway otay ebay away ingkay 
andway avehay onlyway ustjay away ivengay amenay, ikelay away iggernay. Utbay aysay--where youway oinggay 
otay igday irstfay?" 

"Ellway, Iway onday't owknay. Sway'pose eway ackletay atthay oldway eadday-limb eetray onway ethay 
illhay tway'other idesay ofway Illstay-House anchbray?" 

"Iway'm agreedway." 

Osay eythay otgay away ippledcray ickpay andway away ovelshay, andway etsay outway onway eirthay 
eethray-mile amptray. Eythay arrivedway othay andway antingpay, andway ewthray emselvesthay 
ownday inway ethay adeshay ofway away eighboringnay elmway otay estray andway avehay away okesmay. 

"Iway ikelay isthay," aidsay Omtay. 

"Osay oday Iway." 

"Aysay, Uckhay, ifway eway indfay away easuretray erehay, atwhay youway oinggay otay oday ithway yourway 
areshay?" 

"Ellway, Iway'll avehay iepay andway away assglay ofway odasay everyway ayday, andway Iway'll ogay otay everyway 
ircuscay atthay omescay alongway. Iway etbay Iway'll avehay away aygay imetay." 

"Ellway, ainway't youway oinggay otay avesay anyway ofway itway?" 

"Avesay itway? Atwhay orfay?" 

"Ywhay, osay asway otay avehay omethingsay otay ivelay onway, ybay andway ybay." 

"Ohway, atthay ainway't anyway useway. Appay ouldway omecay ackbay otay ishthay-yer owntay omesay ayday 
andway etgay ishay awsclay onway itway ifway Iway idnday't urryhay upway, andway Iway elltay youway ehay'd eanclay 
itway outway ettypray uickqay. Atwhay youway oinggay otay oday ithway yournway, Omtay?" 

"Iway'm oinggay otay uybay away ewnay umdray, andway away uresay'nough ordsway, andway away edray ecktienay 
andway away ullbay uppay, andway etgay arriedmay." 

"Arriedmay!" 

"Atthay's itway." 

"Omtay, youway--why, youway ainway't inway yourway ightray indmay." 

"Aitway--you'll eesay." 

"Ellway, atthay's ethay oolishestfay ingthay youway ouldcay oday. Ooklay atway appay andway ymay 
othermay. Ightfay! Ywhay, eythay usedway otay ightfay allway ethay imetay. Iway ememberray, ightymay 
ellway." 

"Atthay ainway't anythingway. Ethay irlgay Iway'm oinggay otay arrymay onway't ightfay." 

"Omtay, Iway eckonray eythay're allway alikeway. Eythay'll allway ombcay away odybay. Ownay youway 
etterbay inkthay 'outbay isthay awhileway. Iway elltay youway youway etterbay. Atwhay's ethay amenay 
ofway ethay algay?" 

"Itway ainway't away algay atway allway--it's away irlgay." 

"Itway's allway ethay amesay, Iway eckonray; omesay ayssay algay, omesay ayssay irlgay--both's 
ightray, ikelay enoughway. Anywayway, atwhay's erhay amenay, Omtay?" 

"Iway'll elltay youway omesay imetay--not ownay." 

"Allway ightray--that'll oday. Onlyway ifway youway etgay arriedmay Iway'll ebay oremay onesomerlay 
anthay everway." 

"Onay youway onway't. Youway'll omecay andway ivelay ithway emay. Ownay irstay outway ofway isthay andway 
eway'll ogay otay iggingday." 

Eythay orkedway andway eatedsway orfay alfhay anway ourhay. Onay esultray. Eythay oiledtay anotherway 
alfhourhay. Illstay onay esultray. Uckhay aidsay: 

"Oday eythay alwaysway urybay itway asway eepday asway isthay?" 

"Ometimessay--not alwaysway. Otnay enerallygay. Iway eckonray eway avenhay't otgay ethay ightray 
aceplay." 

Osay eythay osechay away ewnay otspay andway eganbay againway. Ethay aborlay aggeddray away ittlelay, 
utbay illstay eythay ademay ogresspray. Eythay eggedpay awayway inway ilencesay orfay omesay imetay. 
Inallyfay Uckhay eanedlay onway ishay ovelshay, abbedsway ethay eadedbay opsdray omfray ishay 
owbray ithway ishay eeveslay, andway aidsay: 

"Erewhay youway oinggay otay igday extnay, afterway eway etgay isthay oneway?" 

"Iway eckonray aybemay eway'll ackletay ethay oldway eetray atthay's overway yonderway onway Ardiffcay 
Illhay ackbay ofway ethay idowway's." 

"Iway eckonray atthay'll ebay away oodgay oneway. Utbay onway't ethay idowway aketay itway awayway omfray 
usway, Omtay? Itway's onway erhay andlay." 

"_Eshay_ aketay itway awayway! Aybemay eshay'd ikelay otay ytray itway onceway. Oeverwhay indsfay oneway 
ofway esethay idhay easurestray, itway elongsbay otay imhay. Itway onday't akemay anyway ifferenceday 
osewhay andlay itway's onway." 

Atthay asway atisfactorysay. Ethay orkway entway onway. Ybay andway ybay Uckhay aidsay: 

"Ameblay itway, eway ustmay ebay inway ethay ongwray aceplay againway. Atwhay oday youway inkthay?" 

"Itway isway ightymay uriouscay, Uckhay. Iway onday't understandway itway. Ometimessay itchesway 
interfereway. Iway eckonray aybemay atthay's atwhay's ethay oubletray ownay." 

"Ucksshay! Itchesway ainway't otgay onay owerpay inway ethay aytimeday." 

"Ellway, atthay's osay. Iway idnday't inkthay ofway atthay. Ohway, Iway owknay atwhay ethay attermay isway! 
Atwhay away amedblay otlay ofway oolsfay eway areway! Youway otgay otay indfay outway erewhay ethay adowshay 
ofway ethay imblay allsfay atway idnightmay, andway atthay's erewhay youway igday!" 

"Enthay onsoundcay itway, eway've ooledfay awayway allway isthay orkway orfay othingnay. Ownay anghay 
itway allway, eway otgay otay omecay ackbay inway ethay ightnay. Itway's anway awfulway onglay ayway. Ancay 
youway etgay outway?" 

"Iway etbay Iway illway. Eway've otgay otay oday itway onighttay, ootay, ecausebay ifway omebodysay eessay 
esethay oleshay eythay'll owknay inway away inutemay atwhay's erehay andway eythay'll ogay orfay itway." 

"Ellway, Iway'll omecay aroundway andway aowmay onighttay." 

"Allway ightray. Etlay's idehay ethay oolstay inway ethay ushesbay." 

Ethay oysbay ereway erethay atthay ightnay, aboutway ethay appointedway imetay. Eythay atsay inway 
ethay adowshay aitingway. Itway asway away onelylay aceplay, andway anway ourhay ademay olemnsay ybay 
oldway aditionstray. Iritsspay isperedwhay inway ethay ustlingray eaveslay, ostsghay urkedlay 
inway ethay urkymay ooksnay, ethay eepday ayingbay ofway away oundhay oatedflay upway outway ofway ethay 
istanceday, anway owlway answeredway ithway ishay epulchralsay otenay. Ethay oysbay ereway 
ubduedsay ybay esethay olemnitiessay, andway alkedtay ittlelay. Ybay andway ybay eythay udgedjay 
atthay elvetway adhay omecay; eythay arkedmay erewhay ethay adowshay ellfay, andway eganbay otay 
igday. Eirthay opeshay ommencedcay otay iseray. Eirthay interestway ewgray ongerstray, andway 
eirthay industryway eptkay acepay ithway itway. Ethay olehay eepenedday andway illstay eepenedday, 
utbay everyway imetay eirthay eartshay umpedjay otay earhay ethay ickpay ikestray uponway 
omethingsay, eythay onlyway ufferedsay away ewnay isappointmentday. Itway asway onlyway away onestay 
orway away unkchay. Atway astlay Omtay aidsay: 

"Itway ainway't anyway useway, Uckhay, eway're ongwray againway." 

"Ellway, utbay eway _ancay't_ ebay ongwray. Eway ottedspay ethay addershay otay away otday." 

"Iway owknay itway, utbay enthay erethay's anotherway ingthay." 

"Atwhay's atthay?". 

"Ywhay, eway onlyway uessedgay atway ethay imetay. Ikelay enoughway itway asway ootay atelay orway ootay 
earlyway." 

Uckhay oppeddray ishay ovelshay. 

"Atthay's itway," aidsay ehay. "Atthay's ethay eryvay oubletray. Eway otgay otay ivegay isthay oneway 
upway. Eway ancay't everway elltay ethay ightray imetay, andway esidesbay isthay indkay ofway ingthay's 
ootay awfulway, erehay isthay imetay ofway ightnay ithway itchesway andway ostsghay away-fluttering 
aroundway osay. Iway eelfay asway ifway omethingsay's ehindbay emay allway ethay imetay; andway Iway'm 
afeardway otay urntay aroundway, ecuzbay aybemay erethay's othersway inway ontfray away-waiting orfay 
away ancechay. Iway eenbay eepingcray allway overway, everway incesay Iway otgay erehay." 

"Ellway, Iway've eenbay ettypray uchmay osay, ootay, Uckhay. Eythay ostmay alwaysway utpay inway away 
eadday anmay enwhay eythay urybay away easuretray underway away eetray, otay ooklay outway orfay itway." 

"Ordylay!" 

"Yesway, eythay oday. Iway've alwaysway eardhay atthay." 

"Omtay, Iway onday't ikelay otay oolfay aroundway uchmay erewhay erethay's eadday eoplepay. Away 
odybay's oundbay otay etgay intoway oubletray ithway 'emway, uresay." 

"Iway onday't ikelay otay irstay 'emway upway, eitherway. Sway'pose isthay oneway erehay asway otay ickstay 
ishay ullskay outway andway aysay omethingsay!" 

"Onday't Omtay! Itway's awfulway." 

"Ellway, itway ustjay isway. Uckhay, Iway onday't eelfay omfortablecay away itbay." 

"Aysay, Omtay, etlay's ivegay isthay aceplay upway, andway ytray omewheressay elseway." 

"Allway ightray, Iway eckonray eway etterbay." 

"Atwhay'll itway ebay?" 

Omtay onsideredcay awhileway; andway enthay aidsay: 

"Ethay ahay'nted ousehay. Atthay's itway!" 

"Ameblay itway, Iway onday't ikelay ahay'nted ouseshay, Omtay. Ywhay, eythay're away ernday ightsay 
orseway'n eadday eoplepay. Eadday eoplepay ightmay alktay, aybemay, utbay eythay onday't omecay 
idingslay aroundway inway away oudshray, enwhay youway ainway't oticingnay, andway eeppay overway yourway 
ouldershay allway ofway away uddensay andway itgray eirthay eethtay, ethay ayway away ostghay oesday. Iway 
ouldncay't andstay uchsay away ingthay asway atthay, Omtay--nobody ouldcay." 

"Yesway, utbay, Uckhay, ostsghay onday't aveltray aroundway onlyway atway ightnay. Eythay onway't 
enderhay usway omfray iggingday erethay inway ethay aytimeday." 

"Ellway, atthay's osay. Utbay youway owknay ightymay ellway eoplepay onday't ogay aboutway atthay 
ahay'nted ousehay inway ethay ayday ornay ethay ightnay." 

"Ellway, atthay's ostlymay ecausebay eythay onday't ikelay otay ogay erewhay away anmay's eenbay 
urderedmay, anywayway--but othingnay's everway eenbay eensay aroundway atthay ousehay exceptway 
inway ethay ightnay--just omesay ueblay ightslay ippingslay ybay ethay indowsway--no egularray 
ostsghay." 

"Ellway, erewhay youway eesay oneway ofway emthay ueblay ightslay ickeringflay aroundway, Omtay, 
youway ancay etbay erethay's away ostghay ightymay oseclay ehindbay itway. Itway andsstay otay easonray. 
Ecuzbay youway owknay atthay eythay onday't anybodyway utbay ostsghay useway 'emway." 

"Yesway, atthay's osay. Utbay anywayway eythay onday't omecay aroundway inway ethay aytimeday, osay 
atwhay's ethay useway ofway ourway eingbay afeardway?" 

"Ellway, allway ightray. Eway'll ackletay ethay ahay'nted ousehay ifway youway aysay osay--but Iway 
eckonray itway's akingtay anceschay." 

Eythay adhay artedstay ownday ethay illhay ybay isthay imetay. Erethay inway ethay iddlemay ofway ethay 
oonlitmay alleyvay elowbay emthay oodstay ethay "ahay'nted" ousehay, utterlyway isolatedway, 
itsway encesfay onegay onglay agoway, ankray eedsway otheringsmay ethay eryvay oorstepsday, ethay 
imneychay umbledcray otay uinray, ethay indowway-sashes acantvay, away ornercay ofway ethay oofray 
avedcay inway. Ethay oysbay azedgay awhileway, alfhay expectingway otay eesay away ueblay ightlay itflay 
astpay away indowway; enthay alkingtay inway away owlay onetay, asway efittedbay ethay imetay andway ethay 
ircumstancescay, eythay uckstray arfay offway otay ethay ightray, otay ivegay ethay auntedhay 
ousehay away ideway erthbay, andway ooktay eirthay ayway omewardhay oughthray ethay oodsway atthay 
adornedway ethay earwardray idesay ofway Ardiffcay Illhay. 




APTERCHAY IXVAY 

ABOUTWAY oonnay ethay extnay ayday ethay oysbay arrivedway atway ethay eadday eetray; eythay adhay omecay 
orfay eirthay oolstay. Omtay asway impatientway otay ogay otay ethay auntedhay ousehay; Uckhay asway 
easurablymay osay, alsoway--but uddenlysay aidsay: 

"Ookyherelay, Omtay, oday youway owknay atwhay ayday itway isway?" 

Omtay entallymay anray overway ethay aysday ofway ethay eekway, andway enthay uicklyqay iftedlay ishay 
eyesway ithway away artledstay ooklay inway emthay-- 

"Ymay! Iway evernay onceway oughtthay ofway itway, Uckhay!" 

"Ellway, Iway idnday't eithernay, utbay allway atway onceway itway oppedpay ontoway emay atthay itway asway 
Idayfray." 

"Ameblay itway, away odybay ancay't ebay ootay arefulcay, Uckhay. Eway ightmay 'away' otgay intoway anway 
awfulway apescray, acklingtay uchsay away ingthay onway away Idayfray." 

"_Ightmay_! Etterbay aysay eway _ouldway_! Erethay's omesay uckylay aysday, aybemay, utbay 
Idayfray ainway't." 

"Anyway oolfay owsknay atthay. Iway onday't eckonray _youway_ asway ethay irstfay atthay oundfay itway 
outway, Uckhay." 

"Ellway, Iway evernay aidsay Iway asway, idday Iway? Andway Idayfray ainway't allway, eithernay. Iway adhay away 
ottenray adbay eamdray astlay ightnay--dreampt aboutway atsray." 

"Onay! Uresay ignsay ofway oubletray. Idday eythay ightfay?" 

"Onay." 

"Ellway, atthay's oodgay, Uckhay. Enwhay eythay onday't ightfay itway's onlyway away ignsay atthay 
erethay's oubletray aroundway, youway owknay. Allway eway otgay otay oday isway otay ooklay ightymay 
arpshay andway eepkay outway ofway itway. Eway'll opdray isthay ingthay orfay odaytay, andway ayplay. Oday 
youway owknay Obinray Oodhay, Uckhay?" 

"Onay. Owhay's Obinray Oodhay?" 

"Ywhay, ehay asway oneway ofway ethay eatestgray enmay atthay asway everway inway Englandway--and ethay 
estbay. Ehay asway away obberray." 

"Ackycray, Iway ishtway Iway asway. Owhay idday ehay obray?" 

"Onlyway eriffsshay andway ishopsbay andway ichray eoplepay andway ingskay, andway uchsay ikelay. Utbay 
ehay evernay otheredbay ethay oorpay. Ehay ovedlay 'emway. Ehay alwaysway ividedday upway ithway 'emway 
erfectlypay uaresqay." 

"Ellway, ehay ustmay 'away' eenbay away ickbray." 

"Iway etbay youway ehay asway, Uckhay. Ohway, ehay asway ethay oblestnay anmay atthay everway asway. 
Eythay ainway't anyway uchsay enmay ownay, Iway ancay elltay youway. Ehay ouldcay icklay anyway anmay inway 
Englandway, ithway oneway andhay iedtay ehindbay imhay; andway ehay ouldcay aketay ishay yewway owbay 
andway ugplay away entay-cent iecepay everyway imetay, away ilemay andway away alfhay." 

"Atwhay's away _yewway_ owbay?" 

"Iway onday't owknay. Itway's omesay indkay ofway away owbay, ofway oursecay. Andway ifway ehay ithay atthay 
imeday onlyway onway ethay edgeway ehay ouldway etsay ownday andway ycray--and ursecay. Utbay eway'll 
ayplay Obinray Oodhay--it's obbynay unfay. Iway'll earnlay youway." 

"Iway'm agreedway." 

Osay eythay ayedplay Obinray Oodhay allway ethay afternoonway, ownay andway enthay astingcay away 
yearningway eyeway ownday uponway ethay auntedhay ousehay andway assingpay away emarkray aboutway ethay 
orrowmay's ospectspray andway ossibilitiespay erethay. Asway ethay unsay eganbay otay inksay 
intoway ethay estway eythay ooktay eirthay ayway omewardhay athwartway ethay onglay adowsshay 
ofway ethay eestray andway oonsay ereway uriedbay omfray ightsay inway ethay orestsfay ofway Ardiffcay 
Illhay. 

Onway Aturdaysay, ortlyshay afterway oonnay, ethay oysbay ereway atway ethay eadday eetray againway. 
Eythay adhay away okesmay andway away atchay inway ethay adeshay, andway enthay ugday away ittlelay inway eirthay 
astlay olehay, otnay ithway eatgray opehay, utbay erelymay ecausebay Omtay aidsay erethay ereway 
osay anymay asescay erewhay eoplepay adhay ivengay upway away easuretray afterway ettinggay ownday 
ithinway ixsay inchesway ofway itway, andway enthay omebodysay elseway adhay omecay alongway andway 
urnedtay itway upway ithway away inglesay ustthray ofway away ovelshay. Ethay ingthay ailedfay isthay 
imetay, oweverhay, osay ethay oysbay oulderedshay eirthay oolstay andway entway awayway eelingfay 
atthay eythay adhay otnay ifledtray ithway ortunefay, utbay adhay ulfilledfay allway ethay 
equirementsray atthay elongbay otay ethay usinessbay ofway easuretray-hunting. 

Enwhay eythay eachedray ethay auntedhay ousehay erethay asway omethingsay osay eirdway andway 
islygray aboutway ethay eadday ilencesay atthay eignedray erethay underway ethay akingbay unsay, 
andway omethingsay osay epressingday aboutway ethay onelinesslay andway esolationday ofway ethay 
aceplay, atthay eythay ereway afraidway, orfay away omentmay, otay enturevay inway. Enthay eythay 
eptcray otay ethay oorday andway ooktay away emblingtray eeppay. Eythay awsay away eedgrownway, 
oorlessflay oomray, unplasteredway, anway ancientway ireplacefay, acantvay indowsway, 
away uinousray aircasestay; andway erehay, erethay, andway everywhereway unghay aggedray andway 
abandonedway obwebscay. Eythay esentlypray enteredway, oftlysay, ithway uickenedqay 
ulsespay, alkingtay inway isperswhay, earsway alertway otay atchcay ethay ightestslay oundsay, 
andway usclesmay ensetay andway eadyray orfay instantway etreatray. 

Inway away ittlelay ilewhay amiliarityfay odifiedmay eirthay earsfay andway eythay avegay ethay 
aceplay away iticalcray andway interestedway examinationway, atherray admiringway eirthay ownway 
oldnessbay, andway onderingway atway itway, ootay. Extnay eythay antedway otay ooklay upstairsway. 
Isthay asway omethingsay ikelay uttingcay offway etreatray, utbay eythay otgay otay aringday 
eachway otherway, andway ofway oursecay erethay ouldcay ebay utbay oneway esultray--they ewthray eirthay 
oolstay intoway away ornercay andway ademay ethay ascentway. Upway erethay ereway ethay amesay ignssay ofway 
ecayday. Inway oneway ornercay eythay oundfay away osetclay atthay omisedpray ysterymay, utbay ethay 
omisepray asway away audfray--there asway othingnay inway itway. Eirthay ouragecay asway upway ownay 
andway ellway inway andhay. Eythay ereway aboutway otay ogay ownday andway eginbay orkway enwhay-- 

"Shay!" aidsay Omtay. 

"Atwhay isway itway?" isperedwhay Uckhay, anchingblay ithway ightfray. 

"Shay!... Erethay!... Earhay itway?" 

"Yesway!... Ohway, ymay! Etlay's unray!" 

"Eepkay illstay! Onday't youway udgebay! Eythay're omingcay ightray owardtay ethay oorday." 

Ethay oysbay etchedstray emselvesthay uponway ethay oorflay ithway eirthay eyesway otay 
otholesknay inway ethay ankingplay, andway aylay aitingway, inway away iserymay ofway earfay. 

"Eythay've oppedstay.... Onay--coming.... Erehay eythay areway. Onday't isperwhay anotherway 
ordway, Uckhay. Ymay oodnessgay, Iway ishway Iway asway outway ofway isthay!" 

Otway enmay enteredway. Eachway oybay aidsay otay imselfhay: "Erethay's ethay oldway eafday andway 
umbday Aniardspay atthay's eenbay aboutway owntay onceway orway icetway atelylay--never awsay 
tway'other anmay eforebay." 

"Tway'other" asway away aggedray, unkemptway eaturecray, ithway othingnay eryvay easantplay 
inway ishay acefay. Ethay Aniardspay asway appedwray inway away erapesay; ehay adhay ushybay itewhay 
iskerswhay; onglay itewhay airhay owedflay omfray underway ishay ombrerosay, andway ehay oreway 
eengray ogglesgay. Enwhay eythay amecay inway, "tway'other" asway alkingtay inway away owlay oicevay; 
eythay atsay ownday onway ethay oundgray, acingfay ethay oorday, ithway eirthay acksbay otay ethay 
allway, andway ethay eakerspay ontinuedcay ishay emarksray. Ishay annermay ecamebay esslay 
uardedgay andway ishay ordsway oremay istinctday asway ehay oceededpray: 

"Onay," aidsay ehay, "Iway've oughtthay itway allway overway, andway Iway onday't ikelay itway. Itway's 
angerousday." 

"Angerousday!" untedgray ethay "eafday andway umbday" Aniardspay--to ethay astvay urprisesay 
ofway ethay oysbay. "Ilksopmay!" 

Isthay oicevay ademay ethay oysbay aspgay andway uakeqay. Itway asway Injunway Oejay's! Erethay asway 
ilencesay orfay omesay imetay. Enthay Oejay aidsay: 

"Atwhay's anyway oremay angerousday anthay atthay objay upway yonderway--but othingnay's omecay ofway 
itway." 

"Atthay's ifferentday. Awayway upway ethay iverray osay, andway otnay anotherway ousehay aboutway. 
'Ontway't everway ebay ownknay atthay eway iedtray, anywayway, onglay asway eway idnday't ucceedsay." 

"Ellway, atwhay's oremay angerousday anthay omingcay erehay inway ethay aytimeday!--anybody 
ouldway uspicionsay usway atthay awsay usway." 

"Iway owknay atthay. Utbay erethay arnway't anyway otherway aceplay asway andyhay afterway atthay oolfay 
ofway away objay. Iway antway otay uitqay isthay antyshay. Iway antedway otay yesterdayway, onlyway itway 
arnway't anyway useway yingtray otay irstay outway ofway erehay, ithway osethay infernalway oysbay 
ayingplay overway erethay onway ethay illhay ightray inway ullfay iewvay." 

"Osethay infernalway oysbay" uakedqay againway underway ethay inspirationway ofway isthay emarkray, 
andway oughtthay owhay uckylay itway asway atthay eythay adhay ememberedray itway asway Idayfray andway 
oncludedcay otay aitway away ayday. Eythay ishedway inway eirthay eartshay eythay adhay aitedway away 
yearway. 

Ethay otway enmay otgay outway omesay oodfay andway ademay away uncheonlay. Afterway away onglay andway 
oughtfulthay ilencesay, Injunway Oejay aidsay: 

"Ooklay erehay, adlay--you ogay ackbay upway ethay iverray erewhay youway elongbay. Aitway erethay 
illtay youway earhay omfray emay. Iway'll aketay ethay anceschay onway oppingdray intoway isthay owntay 
ustjay onceway oremay, orfay away ooklay. Eway'll oday atthay 'angerousday' objay afterway Iway've 
iedspay aroundway away ittlelay andway inkthay ingsthay ooklay ellway orfay itway. Enthay orfay Exastay! 
Eway'll eglay itway ogethertay!" 

Isthay asway atisfactorysay. Othbay enmay esentlypray ellfay otay yawningway, andway Injunway Oejay 
aidsay: 

"Iway'm eadday orfay eepslay! Itway's yourway urntay otay atchway." 

Ehay urledcay ownday inway ethay eedsway andway oonsay eganbay otay oresnay. Ishay omradecay irredstay 
imhay onceway orway icetway andway ehay ecamebay uietqay. Esentlypray ethay atcherway eganbay otay 
odnay; ishay eadhay oopeddray owerlay andway owerlay, othbay enmay eganbay otay oresnay ownay. 

Ethay oysbay ewdray away onglay, atefulgray eathbray. Omtay isperedwhay: 

"Ownay's ourway ancechay--come!" 

Uckhay aidsay: 

"Iway ancay't--I'd ieday ifway eythay asway otay akeway." 

Omtay urgedway--Huck eldhay ackbay. Atway astlay Omtay oseray owlyslay andway oftlysay, andway 
artedstay aloneway. Utbay ethay irstfay epstay ehay ademay ungwray uchsay away ideoushay eakcray 
omfray ethay azycray oorflay atthay ehay anksay ownday almostway eadday ithway ightfray. Ehay evernay 
ademay away econdsay attemptway. Ethay oysbay aylay erethay ountingcay ethay aggingdray omentsmay 
illtay itway eemedsay otay emthay atthay imetay ustmay ebay oneday andway eternityway owinggray aygray; 
andway enthay eythay ereway atefulgray otay otenay atthay atway astlay ethay unsay asway ettingsay. 

Ownay oneway oresnay easedcay. Injunway Oejay atsay upway, aredstay aroundway--smiled imlygray uponway 
ishay omradecay, osewhay eadhay asway oopingdray uponway ishay eesknay--stirred imhay upway ithway 
ishay ootfay andway aidsay: 

"Erehay! _Youway're_ away atchmanway, ainway't youway! Allway ightray, oughthay--nothing's 
appenedhay." 

"Ymay! avehay Iway eenbay asleepway?" 

"Ohway, artlypay, artlypay. Earlynay imetay orfay usway otay ebay ovingmay, ardpay. Atwhay'll eway 
oday ithway atwhay ittlelay agsway eway've otgay eftlay?" 

"Iway onday't owknay--leave itway erehay asway eway've alwaysway oneday, Iway eckonray. Onay useway otay 
aketay itway awayway illtay eway artstay outhsay. Ixsay undredhay andway iftyfay inway ilversay's 
omethingsay otay arrycay." 

"Ellway--all ightray--it onway't attermay otay omecay erehay onceway oremay." 

"Onay--but Iway'd aysay omecay inway ethay ightnay asway eway usedway otay oday--it's etterbay." 

"Yesway: utbay ooklay erehay; itway aymay ebay away oodgay ilewhay eforebay Iway etgay ethay ightray 
ancechay atway atthay objay; accidentsway ightmay appenhay; 'aintay't inway uchsay away eryvay oodgay 
aceplay; eway'll ustjay egularlyray urybay itway--and urybay itway eepday." 

"Oodgay ideaway," aidsay ethay omradecay, owhay alkedway acrossway ethay oomray, eltknay ownday, 
aisedray oneway ofway ethay earwardray earthhay-stones andway ooktay outway away agbay atthay ingledjay 
easantlyplay. Ehay ubtractedsay omfray itway entytway orway irtythay ollarsday orfay imselfhay 
andway asway uchmay orfay Injunway Oejay, andway assedpay ethay agbay otay ethay atterlay, owhay asway onway 
ishay eesknay inway ethay ornercay, ownay, iggingday ithway ishay owiebay-knife. 

Ethay oysbay orgotfay allway eirthay earsfay, allway eirthay iseriesmay inway anway instantway. Ithway 
oatingglay eyesway eythay atchedway everyway ovementmay. Ucklay!--the endorsplay ofway itway asway 
eyondbay allway imaginationway! Ixsay undredhay ollarsday asway oneymay enoughway otay akemay 
alfhay away ozenday oysbay ichray! Erehay asway easuretray-hunting underway ethay appiesthay 
auspicesway--there ouldway otnay ebay anyway othersomebay uncertaintyway asway otay erewhay otay 
igday. Eythay udgednay eachway otherway everyway omentmay--eloquent udgesnay andway easilyway 
understoodway, orfay eythay implysay eantmay--"Oh, utbay ainway't youway adglay _ownay_ eway're 
erehay!" 

Oejay's ifeknay uckstray uponway omethingsay. 

"Ellohay!" aidsay ehay. 

"Atwhay isway itway?" aidsay ishay omradecay. 

"Alfhay-rotten ankplay--no, itway's away oxbay, Iway elievebay. Erehay--bear away andhay andway eway'll 
eesay atwhay itway's erehay orfay. Evernay indmay, Iway've okebray away olehay." 

Ehay eachedray ishay andhay inway andway ewdray itway outway-- 

"Anmay, itway's oneymay!" 

Ethay otway enmay examinedway ethay andfulhay ofway oinscay. Eythay ereway oldgay. Ethay oysbay 
aboveway ereway asway excitedway asway emselvesthay, andway asway elightedday. 

Oejay's omradecay aidsay: 

"Eway'll akemay uickqay orkway ofway isthay. Erethay's anway oldway ustyray ickpay overway amongstway 
ethay eedsway inway ethay ornercay ethay otherway idesay ofway ethay ireplacefay--I awsay itway away 
inutemay agoway." 

Ehay anray andway oughtbray ethay oysbay' ickpay andway ovelshay. Injunway Oejay ooktay ethay 
ickpay, ookedlay itway overway iticallycray, ookshay ishay eadhay, utteredmay omethingsay otay 
imselfhay, andway enthay eganbay otay useway itway. Ethay oxbay asway oonsay unearthedway. Itway asway 
otnay eryvay argelay; itway asway ironway oundbay andway adhay eenbay eryvay ongstray eforebay ethay 
owslay yearsway adhay injuredway itway. Ethay enmay ontemplatedcay ethay easuretray awhileway inway 
issfulblay ilencesay. 

"Ardpay, erethay's ousandsthay ofway ollarsday erehay," aidsay Injunway Oejay. 

"'Astway alwaysway aidsay atthay Urrelmay's anggay usedway otay ebay aroundway erehay oneway 
ummersay," ethay angerstray observedway. 

"Iway owknay itway," aidsay Injunway Oejay; "andway isthay ookslay ikelay itway, Iway ouldshay aysay." 

"Ownay youway onway't eednay otay oday atthay objay." 

Ethay alfbreedhay ownedfray. Aidsay ehay: 

"Youway onday't owknay emay. Eastlay youway onday't owknay allway aboutway atthay ingthay. 'Aintay't 
obberyray altogetherway--it's _evengeray_!" andway away ickedway ightlay amedflay inway ishay 
eyesway. "Iway'll eednay yourway elphay inway itway. Enwhay itway's inishedfay--then Exastay. Ogay omehay 
otay yourway Ancenay andway yourway idskay, andway andstay ybay illtay youway earhay omfray emay." 

"Ellway--if youway aysay osay; atwhay'll eway oday ithway isthay--bury itway againway?" 

"Yesway. [Avishingray elightday overheadway.] _Onay_! ybay ethay eatgray Achemsay, onay! 
[Ofoundpray istressday overheadway.] Iway'd earlynay orgotfay. Atthay ickpay adhay eshfray 
earthway onway itway! [Ethay oysbay ereway icksay ithway errortay inway away omentmay.] Atwhay usinessbay 
ashay away ickpay andway away ovelshay erehay? Atwhay usinessbay ithway eshfray earthway onway 
emthay? Owhay oughtbray emthay erehay--and erewhay areway eythay onegay? Avehay youway eardhay 
anybodyway?--seen anybodyway? Atwhay! urybay itway againway andway eavelay emthay otay omecay andway 
eesay ethay oundgray isturbedday? Otnay exactlyway--not exactlyway. Eway'll aketay itway otay ymay 
enday." 

"Ywhay, ofway oursecay! Ightmay avehay oughtthay ofway atthay eforebay. Youway eanmay Umbernay 
Oneway?" 

"Onay--Number Otway--under ethay osscray. Ethay otherway aceplay isway adbay--too ommoncay." 

"Allway ightray. Itway's earlynay arkday enoughway otay artstay." 

Injunway Oejay otgay upway andway entway aboutway omfray indowway otay indowway autiouslycay eepingpay 
outway. Esentlypray ehay aidsay: 

"Owhay ouldcay avehay oughtbray osethay oolstay erehay? Oday youway eckonray eythay ancay ebay 
upstairsway?" 

Ethay oysbay' eathbray orsookfay emthay. Injunway Oejay utpay ishay andhay onway ishay ifeknay, 
altedhay away omentmay, undecidedway, andway enthay urnedtay owardtay ethay airwaystay. Ethay 
oysbay oughtthay ofway ethay osetclay, utbay eirthay engthstray asway onegay. Ethay epsstay amecay 
eakingcray upway ethay airsstay--the intolerableway istressday ofway ethay ituationsay okeway 
ethay ickenstray esolutionray ofway ethay adslay--they ereway aboutway otay ingspray orfay ethay 
osetclay, enwhay erethay asway away ashcray ofway ottenray imberstay andway Injunway Oejay andedlay onway 
ethay oundgray amidway ethay ebrisday ofway ethay uinedray airwaystay. Ehay atheredgay imselfhay 
upway ursingcay, andway ishay omradecay aidsay: 

"Ownay atwhay's ethay useway ofway allway atthay? Ifway itway's anybodyway, andway eythay're upway erethay, 
etlay emthay _aystay_ erethay--who arescay? Ifway eythay antway otay umpjay ownday, ownay, andway etgay 
intoway oubletray, owhay objectsway? Itway illway ebay arkday inway ifteenfay inutesmay--and enthay 
etlay emthay ollowfay usway ifway eythay antway otay. Iway'm illingway. Inway ymay opinionway, oeverwhay 
ovehay osethay ingsthay inway erehay aughtcay away ightsay ofway usway andway ooktay usway orfay ostsghay orway 
evilsday orway omethingsay. Iway'll etbay eythay're unningray yetway." 

Oejay umbledgray awhileway; enthay ehay agreedway ithway ishay iendfray atthay atwhay aylightday 
asway eftlay oughtway otay ebay economizedway inway ettinggay ingsthay eadyray orfay eavinglay. 
Ortlyshay afterwardway eythay ippedslay outway ofway ethay ousehay inway ethay eepeningday 
ilighttway, andway ovedmay owardtay ethay iverray ithway eirthay eciouspray oxbay. 

Omtay andway Uckhay oseray upway, eakway utbay astlyvay elievedray, andway aredstay afterway emthay 
oughthray ethay inkschay etweenbay ethay ogslay ofway ethay ousehay. Ollowfay? Otnay eythay. Eythay 
ereway ontentcay otay eachray oundgray againway ithoutway okenbray ecksnay, andway aketay ethay 
ownwardtay acktray overway ethay illhay. Eythay idday otnay alktay uchmay. Eythay ereway ootay uchmay 
absorbedway inway atinghay emselvesthay--hating ethay illway ucklay atthay ademay emthay aketay 
ethay adespay andway ethay ickpay erethay. Utbay orfay atthay, Injunway Oejay evernay ouldway avehay 
uspectedsay. Ehay ouldway avehay iddenhay ethay ilversay ithway ethay oldgay otay aitway 
erethay illtay ishay "evengeray" asway atisfiedsay, andway enthay ehay ouldway avehay adhay ethay 
isfortunemay otay indfay atthay oneymay urntay upway issingmay. Itterbay, itterbay ucklay atthay 
ethay oolstay ereway everway oughtbray erethay! 

Eythay esolvedray otay eepkay away ookoutlay orfay atthay Aniardspay enwhay ehay ouldshay omecay otay 
owntay yingspay outway orfay anceschay otay oday ishay evengefulray objay, andway ollowfay imhay otay 
"Umbernay Otway," ereverwhay atthay ightmay ebay. Enthay away astlyghay oughtthay occurredway otay 
Omtay. 

"Evengeray? Atwhay ifway ehay eansmay _usway_, Uckhay!" 

"Ohway, onday't!" aidsay Uckhay, earlynay aintingfay. 

Eythay alkedtay itway allway overway, andway asway eythay enteredway owntay eythay agreedway otay elievebay 
atthay ehay ightmay ossiblypay eanmay omebodysay elseway--at eastlay atthay ehay ightmay atway 
eastlay eanmay obodynay utbay Omtay, incesay onlyway Omtay adhay estifiedtay. 

Eryvay, eryvay allsmay omfortcay itway asway otay Omtay otay ebay aloneway inway angerday! Ompanycay 
ouldway ebay away alpablepay improvementway, ehay oughtthay. 




APTERCHAY IIXXVAY 

ETHAY adventureway ofway ethay ayday ightilymay ormentedtay Omtay's eamsdray atthay ightnay. 
Ourfay imestay ehay adhay ishay andshay onway atthay ichray easuretray andway ourfay imestay 
itway astedway otay othingnessnay inway ishay ingersfay asway eepslay orsookfay imhay andway 
akefulnessway oughtbray ackbay ethay ardhay ealityray ofway ishay isfortunemay. Asway ehay aylay 
inway ethay earlyway orningmay ecallingray ethay incidentsway ofway ishay eatgray adventureway, ehay 
oticednay atthay eythay eemedsay uriouslycay ubduedsay andway arfay awayway--somewhat asway ifway 
eythay adhay appenedhay inway anotherway orldway, orway inway away imetay onglay onegay ybay. Enthay itway 
occurredway otay imhay atthay ethay eatgray adventureway itselfway ustmay ebay away eamdray! Erethay 
asway oneway eryvay ongstray argumentway inway avorfay ofway isthay ideaway--namely, atthay ethay
