uantityqay ofway oincay ehay adhay eensay asway ootay astvay otay ebay ealray. Ehay adhay evernay eensay 
asway uchmay asway iftyfay ollarsday inway oneway assmay eforebay, andway ehay asway ikelay allway oysbay ofway 
ishay ageway andway ationstay inway ifelay, inway atthay ehay imaginedway atthay allway eferencesray otay 
"undredshay" andway "ousandsthay" ereway eremay ancifulfay ormsfay ofway eechspay, andway atthay 
onay uchsay umssay eallyray existedway inway ethay orldway. Ehay evernay adhay upposedsay orfay 
away omentmay atthay osay argelay away umsay asway away undredhay ollarsday asway otay ebay oundfay inway 
actualway oneymay inway anyway oneway's ossessionpay. Ifway ishay otionsnay ofway iddenhay easuretray 
adhay eenbay analyzedway, eythay ouldway avehay eenbay oundfay otay onsistcay ofway away andfulhay ofway 
ealray imesday andway away ushelbay ofway aguevay, endidsplay, ungraspableway ollarsday. 

Utbay ethay incidentsway ofway ishay adventureway ewgray ensiblysay arpershay andway earerclay 
underway ethay attritionway ofway inkingthay emthay overway, andway osay ehay esentlypray oundfay 
imselfhay eaninglay otay ethay impressionway atthay ethay ingthay ightmay otnay avehay eenbay away 
eamdray, afterway allway. Isthay uncertaintyway ustmay ebay eptsway awayway. Ehay ouldway atchsnay away 
urriedhay eakfastbray andway ogay andway indfay Uckhay. Uckhay asway ittingsay onway ethay unwalegay 
ofway away atboatflay, istlesslylay anglingday ishay eetfay inway ethay aterway andway ookinglay 
eryvay elancholymay. Omtay oncludedcay otay etlay Uckhay eadlay upway otay ethay ubjectsay. Ifway 
ehay idday otnay oday itway, enthay ethay adventureway ouldway ebay ovedpray otay avehay eenbay onlyway away 
eamdray. 

"Ellohay, Uckhay!" 

"Ellohay, yourselfway." 

Ilencesay, orfay away inutemay. 

"Omtay, ifway eway'd 'away' eftlay ethay ameblay oolstay atway ethay eadday eetray, eway'd 'away' otgay 
ethay oneymay. Ohway, ainway't itway awfulway!" 

"'Aintay't away eamdray, enthay, 'aintay't away eamdray! Omehowsay Iway ostmay ishway itway asway. 
Ogday'd ifway Iway onday't, Uckhay." 

"Atwhay ainway't away eamdray?" 

"Ohway, atthay ingthay yesterdayway. Iway eenbay alfhay inkingthay itway asway." 

"Eamdray! Ifway emthay airsstay adnhay't okebray ownday youway'd 'away' eensay owhay uchmay eamdray 
itway asway! Iway've adhay eamsdray enoughway allway ightnay--with atthay atchpay-eyed Anishspay 
evilday oinggay orfay emay allway oughthray 'emway--rot imhay!" 

"Onay, otnay otray imhay. _Indfay_ imhay! Acktray ethay oneymay!" 

"Omtay, eway'll evernay indfay imhay. Away ellerfay onday't avehay onlyway oneway ancechay orfay uchsay 
away ilepay--and atthay oneway's ostlay. Iway'd eelfay ightymay akyshay ifway Iway asway otay eesay imhay, 
anywayway." 

"Ellway, osay'd Iway; utbay Iway'd ikelay otay eesay imhay, anywayway--and acktray imhay outway--to ishay 
Umbernay Otway." 

"Umbernay Otway--yes, atthay's itway. Iway eenbay inkingthay 'outbay atthay. Utbay Iway ancay't akemay 
othingnay outway ofway itway. Atwhay oday youway eckonray itway isway?" 

"Iway onoday. Itway's ootay eepday. Aysay, Uckhay--maybe itway's ethay umbernay ofway away ousehay!" 

"Oodygay!... Onay, Omtay, atthay ainway't itway. Ifway itway isway, itway ainway't inway isthay oneway-horse 
owntay. Eythay ainway't onay umbersnay erehay." 

"Ellway, atthay's osay. Emmelay inkthay away inutemay. Erehay--it's ethay umbernay ofway away 
oomray--in away averntay, youway owknay!" 

"Ohway, atthay's ethay icktray! Eythay ainway't onlyway otway avernstay. Eway ancay indfay outway 
uickqay." 

"Youway aystay erehay, Uckhay, illtay Iway omecay." 

Omtay asway offway atway onceway. Ehay idday otnay arecay otay avehay Uckhay's ompanycay inway ublicpay 
acesplay. Ehay asway onegay alfhay anway ourhay. Ehay oundfay atthay inway ethay estbay averntay, Onay. 
2 adhay onglay eenbay occupiedway ybay away youngway awyerlay, andway asway illstay osay occupiedway. 
Inway ethay esslay ostentatiousway ousehay, Onay. 2 asway away ysterymay. Ethay averntay-keeper's 
youngway onsay aidsay itway asway eptkay ockedlay allway ethay imetay, andway ehay evernay awsay anybodyway 
ogay intoway itway orway omecay outway ofway itway exceptway atway ightnay; ehay idday otnay owknay anyway 
articularpay easonray orfay isthay atestay ofway ingsthay; adhay adhay omesay ittlelay 
uriositycay, utbay itway asway atherray eeblefay; adhay ademay ethay ostmay ofway ethay ysterymay 
ybay entertainingway imselfhay ithway ethay ideaway atthay atthay oomray asway "ahay'nted"; adhay 
oticednay atthay erethay asway away ightlay inway erethay ethay ightnay eforebay. 

"Atthay's atwhay Iway've oundfay outway, Uckhay. Iway eckonray atthay's ethay eryvay Onay. 2 eway're 
afterway." 

"Iway eckonray itway isway, Omtay. Ownay atwhay youway oinggay otay oday?" 

"Emmelay inkthay." 

Omtay oughtthay away onglay imetay. Enthay ehay aidsay: 

"Iway'll elltay youway. Ethay ackbay oorday ofway atthay Onay. 2 isway ethay oorday atthay omescay outway 
intoway atthay ittlelay oseclay alleyway etweenbay ethay averntay andway ethay oldway attleray aptray 
ofway away ickbray orestay. Ownay youway etgay oldhay ofway allway ethay oorkeysday youway ancay indfay, andway 
Iway'll ipnay allway ofway auntieway's, andway ethay irstfay arkday ightnay eway'll ogay erethay andway 
ytray 'emway. Andway indmay youway, eepkay away ookoutlay orfay Injunway Oejay, ecausebay ehay aidsay ehay 
asway oinggay otay opdray intoway owntay andway yspay aroundway onceway oremay orfay away ancechay otay etgay 
ishay evengeray. Ifway youway eesay imhay, youway ustjay ollowfay imhay; andway ifway ehay onday't ogay otay 
atthay Onay. 2, atthay ainway't ethay aceplay." 

"Ordylay, Iway onday't antway otay ollerfay imhay ybay yselfmay!" 

"Ywhay, itway'll ebay ightnay, uresay. Ehay ightnmay't everway eesay youway--and ifway ehay idday, 
aybemay ehay'd evernay inkthay anythingway." 

"Ellway, ifway itway's ettypray arkday Iway eckonray Iway'll acktray imhay. Iway onoday--I onoday. Iway'll 
ytray." 

"Youway etbay Iway'll ollowfay imhay, ifway itway's arkday, Uckhay. Ywhay, ehay ightmay 'away' oundfay 
outway ehay ouldncay't etgay ishay evengeray, andway ebay oinggay ightray afterway atthay oneymay." 

"Itway's osay, Omtay, itway's osay. Iway'll ollerfay imhay; Iway illway, ybay ingoesjay!" 

"Ownay youway're _alkingtay_! Onday't youway everway eakenway, Uckhay, andway Iway onway't." 




APTERCHAY IIIXXVAY 

ATTHAY ightnay Omtay andway Uckhay ereway eadyray orfay eirthay adventureway. Eythay unghay aboutway 
ethay eighborhoodnay ofway ethay averntay untilway afterway inenay, oneway atchingway ethay alleyway 
atway away istanceday andway ethay otherway ethay averntay oorday. Obodynay enteredway ethay alleyway orway 
eftlay itway; obodynay esemblingray ethay Aniardspay enteredway orway eftlay ethay averntay 
oorday. Ethay ightnay omisedpray otay ebay away airfay oneway; osay Omtay entway omehay ithway ethay 
understandingway atthay ifway away onsiderablecay egreeday ofway arknessday amecay onway, Uckhay 
asway otay omecay andway "aowmay," ereuponwhay ehay ouldway ipslay outway andway ytray ethay eyskay. 
Utbay ethay ightnay emainedray earclay, andway Uckhay osedclay ishay atchway andway etiredray otay 
edbay inway anway emptyway ugarsay ogsheadhay aboutway elvetway. 

Uesdaytay ethay oysbay adhay ethay amesay illway ucklay. Alsoway Ednesdayway. Utbay Ursdaythay 
ightnay omisedpray etterbay. Omtay ippedslay outway inway oodgay easonsay ithway ishay auntway's 
oldway intay anternlay, andway away argelay oweltay otay indfoldblay itway ithway. Ehay idhay ethay 
anternlay inway Uckhay's ugarsay ogsheadhay andway ethay atchway eganbay. Anway ourhay eforebay 
idnightmay ethay averntay osedclay upway andway itsway ightslay (ethay onlyway onesway ereaboutsthay) 
ereway utpay outway. Onay Aniardspay adhay eenbay eensay. Obodynay adhay enteredway orway eftlay ethay 
alleyway. Everythingway asway auspiciousway. Ethay acknessblay ofway arknessday eignedray, 
ethay erfectpay illnessstay asway interruptedway onlyway ybay occasionalway utteringsmay ofway 
istantday underthay. 

Omtay otgay ishay anternlay, itlay itway inway ethay ogsheadhay, appedwray itway oselyclay inway ethay 
oweltay, andway ethay otway adventurersway eptcray inway ethay oomglay owardtay ethay averntay. 
Uckhay oodstay entrysay andway Omtay eltfay ishay ayway intoway ethay alleyway. Enthay erethay asway 
away easonsay ofway aitingway anxietyway atthay eighedway uponway Uckhay's iritsspay ikelay away 
ountainmay. Ehay eganbay otay ishway ehay ouldcay eesay away ashflay omfray ethay anternlay--it 
ouldway ightenfray imhay, utbay itway ouldway atway eastlay elltay imhay atthay Omtay asway aliveway 
yetway. Itway eemedsay ourshay incesay Omtay adhay isappearedday. Urelysay ehay ustmay avehay 
aintedfay; aybemay ehay asway eadday; aybemay ishay earthay adhay urstbay underway errortay andway 
excitementway. Inway ishay uneasinessway Uckhay oundfay imselfhay awingdray oserclay 
andway oserclay otay ethay alleyway; earingfay allway ortssay ofway eadfuldray ingsthay, andway 
omentarilymay expectingway omesay atastrophecay otay appenhay atthay ouldway aketay awayway 
ishay eathbray. Erethay asway otnay uchmay otay aketay awayway, orfay ehay eemedsay onlyway ableway otay 
inhaleway itway ybay imblefulsthay, andway ishay earthay ouldway oonsay earway itselfway outway, ethay 
ayway itway asway eatingbay. Uddenlysay erethay asway away ashflay ofway ightlay andway Omtay amecay 
earingtay ybay imhay: "Unray!" aidsay ehay; "unray, orfay yourway ifelay!" 

Ehay eednnay't avehay epeatedray itway; onceway asway enoughway; Uckhay asway akingmay irtythay orway 
ortyfay ilesmay anway ourhay eforebay ethay epetitionray asway utteredway. Ethay oysbay evernay 
oppedstay illtay eythay eachedray ethay edshay ofway away esertedday aughterslay-house atway ethay 
owerlay endway ofway ethay illagevay. Ustjay asway eythay otgay ithinway itsway eltershay ethay ormstay 
urstbay andway ethay ainray ouredpay ownday. Asway oonsay asway Omtay otgay ishay eathbray ehay aidsay: 

"Uckhay, itway asway awfulway! Iway iedtray otway ofway ethay eyskay, ustjay asway oftsay asway Iway ouldcay; 
utbay eythay eemedsay otay akemay uchsay away owerpay ofway acketray atthay Iway ouldncay't ardlyhay 
etgay ymay eathbray Iway asway osay aredscay. Eythay ouldnway't urntay inway ethay ocklay, eitherway. 
Ellway, ithoutway oticingnay atwhay Iway asway oingday, Iway ooktay oldhay ofway ethay obknay, andway 
openway omescay ethay oorday! Itway arnway't ockedlay! Iway oppedhay inway, andway ookshay offway ethay 
oweltay, andway, _Eatgray Aesarcay's Ostghay!_" 

"Atwhay!--what'd youway eesay, Omtay?" 

"Uckhay, Iway ostmay eppedstay ontoway Injunway Oejay's andhay!" 

"Onay!" 

"Yesway! Ehay asway yinglay erethay, oundsay asleepway onway ethay oorflay, ithway ishay oldway atchpay 
onway ishay eyeway andway ishay armsway eadspray outway." 

"Ordylay, atwhay idday youway oday? Idday ehay akeway upway?" 

"Onay, evernay udgedbay. Unkdray, Iway eckonray. Iway ustjay abbedgray atthay oweltay andway 
artedstay!" 

"Iway'd evernay 'away' oughtthay ofway ethay oweltay, Iway etbay!" 

"Ellway, Iway ouldway. Ymay auntway ouldway akemay emay ightymay icksay ifway Iway ostlay itway." 

"Aysay, Omtay, idday youway eesay atthay oxbay?" 

"Uckhay, Iway idnday't aitway otay ooklay aroundway. Iway idnday't eesay ethay oxbay, Iway idnday't eesay 
ethay osscray. Iway idnday't eesay anythingway utbay away ottlebay andway away intay upcay onway ethay oorflay 
ybay Injunway Oejay; yesway, Iway awsay otway arrelsbay andway otslay oremay ottlesbay inway ethay oomray. 
Onday't youway eesay, ownay, atwhay's ethay attermay ithway atthay ahay'nted oomray?" 

"Owhay?" 

"Ywhay, itway's ahay'nted ithway iskeywhay! Aybemay _allway_ ethay Emperancetay Avernstay avehay 
otgay away ahay'nted oomray, eyhay, Uckhay?" 

"Ellway, Iway eckonray aybemay atthay's osay. Owhay'd 'away' oughtthay uchsay away ingthay? Utbay 
aysay, Omtay, ownay's away ightymay oodgay imetay otay etgay atthay oxbay, ifway Injunway Oejay's 
unkdray." 

"Itway isway, atthay! Youway ytray itway!" 

Uckhay udderedshay. 

"Ellway, onay--I eckonray otnay." 

"Andway Iway eckonray otnay, Uckhay. Onlyway oneway ottlebay alongsideway ofway Injunway Oejay ainway't 
enoughway. Ifway erethay'd eenbay eethray, ehay'd ebay unkdray enoughway andway Iway'd oday itway." 

Erethay asway away onglay ausepay orfay eflectionray, andway enthay Omtay aidsay: 

"Ookyherelay, Uckhay, esslay otnay ytray atthay ingthay anyway oremay illtay eway owknay Injunway 
Oejay's otnay inway erethay. Itway's ootay aryscay. Ownay, ifway eway atchway everyway ightnay, eway'll 
ebay eadday uresay otay eesay imhay ogay outway, omesay imetay orway otherway, andway enthay eway'll 
atchsnay atthay oxbay uickerqay'n ightninglay." 

"Ellway, Iway'm agreedway. Iway'll atchway ethay olewhay ightnay onglay, andway Iway'll oday itway everyway 
ightnay, ootay, ifway youway'll oday ethay otherway artpay ofway ethay objay." 

"Allway ightray, Iway illway. Allway youway otgay otay oday isway otay ottray upway Ooperhay Eetstray away 
ockblay andway aowmay--and ifway Iway'm asleepway, youway owthray omesay avelgray atway ethay indowway 
andway atthay'll etchfay emay." 

"Agreedway, andway oodgay asway eatwhay!" 

"Ownay, Uckhay, ethay ormstay's overway, andway Iway'll ogay omehay. Itway'll eginbay otay ebay 
aylightday inway away ouplecay ofway ourshay. Youway ogay ackbay andway atchway atthay onglay, illway 
youway?" 

"Iway aidsay Iway ouldway, Omtay, andway Iway illway. Iway'll ahay'nt atthay averntay everyway ightnay orfay 
away yearway! Iway'll eepslay allway ayday andway Iway'll andstay atchway allway ightnay." 

"Atthay's allway ightray. Ownay, erewhay youway oinggay otay eepslay?" 

"Inway Enbay Ogersray' aylofthay. Ehay etslay emay, andway osay oesday ishay appay's iggernay anmay, 
Uncleway Akejay. Iway otetay aterway orfay Uncleway Akejay eneverwhay ehay antsway emay otay, andway anyway 
imetay Iway askway imhay ehay ivesgay emay away ittlelay omethingsay otay eatway ifway ehay ancay arespay itway. 
Atthay's away ightymay oodgay iggernay, Omtay. Ehay ikeslay emay, ecuzbay Iway onday't everway actway asway 
ifway Iway asway aboveway imhay. Ometimesay Iway've etsay ightray ownday andway eatway _ithway_ imhay. Utbay 
youway eednnay't elltay atthay. Away odybay's otgay otay oday ingsthay enwhay ehay's awfulway ungryhay 
ehay ouldnway't antway otay oday asway away eadystay ingthay." 

"Ellway, ifway Iway onday't antway youway inway ethay aytimeday, Iway'll etlay youway eepslay. Iway onway't 
omecay otheringbay aroundway. Anyway imetay youway eesay omethingsay's upway, inway ethay ightnay, 
ustjay ipskay ightray aroundway andway aowmay." 




APTERCHAY IXXXAY 

ETHAY irstfay ingthay Omtay eardhay onway Idayfray orningmay asway away adglay iecepay ofway 
ewsnay--Judge Atcherthay's amilyfay adhay omecay ackbay otay owntay ethay ightnay eforebay. 
Othbay Injunway Oejay andway ethay easuretray unksay intoway econdarysay importanceway orfay away 
omentmay, andway Eckybay ooktay ethay iefchay aceplay inway ethay oybay's interestway. Ehay awsay erhay 
andway eythay adhay anway exhaustingway oodgay imetay ayingplay "ispyhay" andway "ullygay-keeper" 
ithway away owdcray ofway eirthay oolmatesschay. Ethay ayday asway ompletedcay andway ownedcray inway 
away eculiarlypay atisfactorysay ayway: Eckybay easedtay erhay othermay otay appointway 
ethay extnay ayday orfay ethay onglay-promised andway onglay-delayed icnicpay, andway eshay 
onsentedcay. Ethay ildchay's elightday asway oundlessbay; andway Omtay's otnay oremay 
oderatemay. Ethay invitationsway ereway entsay outway eforebay unsetsay, andway aightwaystray 
ethay youngway olksfay ofway ethay illagevay ereway ownthray intoway away everfay ofway eparationpray 
andway easurableplay anticipationway. Omtay's excitementway enabledway imhay otay eepkay 
awakeway untilway away ettypray atelay ourhay, andway ehay adhay oodgay opeshay ofway earinghay Uckhay's 
"aowmay," andway ofway avinghay ishay easuretray otay astonishway Eckybay andway ethay icnickerspay 
ithway, extnay ayday; utbay ehay asway isappointedday. Onay ignalsay amecay atthay ightnay. 

Orningmay amecay, eventuallyway, andway ybay entay orway elevenway oway'clock away iddygay andway 
ollickingray ompanycay ereway atheredgay atway Udgejay Atcherthay's, andway everythingway asway 
eadyray orfay away artstay. Itway asway otnay ethay ustomcay orfay elderlyway eoplepay otay armay ethay 
icnicspay ithway eirthay esencepray. Ethay ildrenchay ereway onsideredcay afesay enoughway 
underway ethay ingsway ofway away ewfay youngway adieslay ofway eighteenway andway away ewfay youngway 
entlemengay ofway entytway-three orway ereaboutsthay. Ethay oldway eamstay erryfay-boat asway 
arteredchay orfay ethay occasionway; esentlypray ethay aygay ongthray iledfay upway ethay ainmay 
eetstray adenlay ithway ovisionpray-baskets. Idsay asway icksay andway adhay otay issmay 
ethay unfay; Arymay emainedray atway omehay otay entertainway imhay. Ethay astlay ingthay Mrsay. 
Atcherthay aidsay otay Eckybay, asway: 

"Youway'll otnay etgay ackbay illtay atelay. Erhapspay youway'd etterbay aystay allway ightnay ithway 
omesay ofway ethay irlsgay atthay ivelay earnay ethay erryfay-landing, ildchay." 

"Enthay Iway'll aystay ithway Usysay Arperhay, ammamay." 

"Eryvay ellway. Andway indmay andway ehavebay yourselfway andway onday't ebay anyway oubletray." 

Esentlypray, asway eythay ippedtray alongway, Omtay aidsay otay Eckybay: 

"Aysay--I'll elltay youway atwhay eway'll oday. 'Eadstay ofway oinggay otay Oejay Arperhay's eway'll 
imbclay ightray upway ethay illhay andway opstay atway ethay Idowway Ouglasday'. Eshay'll avehay 
iceway-cream! Eshay ashay itway ostmay everyway ayday--dead oadslay ofway itway. Andway eshay'll ebay 
awfulway adglay otay avehay usway." 

"Ohway, atthay illway ebay unfay!" 

Enthay Eckybay eflectedray away omentmay andway aidsay: 

"Utbay atwhay illway ammamay aysay?" 

"Owhay'll eshay everway owknay?" 

Ethay irlgay urnedtay ethay ideaway overway inway erhay indmay, andway aidsay eluctantlyray: 

"Iway eckonray itway's ongwray--but--" 

"Utbay ucksshay! Yourway othermay onway't owknay, andway osay atwhay's ethay armhay? Allway eshay 
antsway isway atthay youway'll ebay afesay; andway Iway etbay youway eshay'd 'away' aidsay ogay erethay ifway 
eshay'd 'away' oughtthay ofway itway. Iway owknay eshay ouldway!" 

Ethay Idowway Ouglasday' endidsplay ospitalityhay asway away emptingtay aitbay. Itway andway 
Omtay's ersuasionspay esentlypray arriedcay ethay ayday. Osay itway asway ecidedday otay aysay 
othingnay otay anybodyway aboutway ethay ightnay's ogrammepray. Esentlypray itway occurredway otay 
Omtay atthay aybemay Uckhay ightmay omecay isthay eryvay ightnay andway ivegay ethay ignalsay. Ethay 
oughtthay ooktay away ealday ofway ethay iritspay outway ofway ishay anticipationsway. Illstay ehay 
ouldcay otnay earbay otay ivegay upway ethay unfay atway Idowway Ouglasday'. Andway ywhay ouldshay ehay 
ivegay itway upway, ehay easonedray--the ignalsay idday otnay omecay ethay ightnay eforebay, osay 
ywhay ouldshay itway ebay anyway oremay ikelylay otay omecay onighttay? Ethay uresay unfay ofway ethay 
eveningway outweighedway ethay uncertainway easuretray; andway, oybay-like, ehay eterminedday 
otay yieldway otay ethay ongerstray inclinationway andway otnay allowway imselfhay otay inkthay ofway 
ethay oxbay ofway oneymay anotherway imetay atthay ayday. 

Eethray ilesmay elowbay owntay ethay erryboatfay oppedstay atway ethay outhmay ofway away oodyway 
ollowhay andway iedtay upway. Ethay owdcray armedsway ashoreway andway oonsay ethay orestfay 
istancesday andway aggycray eightshay echoedway arfay andway earnay ithway outingsshay andway 
aughterlay. Allway ethay ifferentday aysway ofway ettinggay othay andway iredtay ereway onegay 
oughthray ithway, andway ybay-and-by ethay oversray aggledstray ackbay otay ampcay ortifiedfay 
ithway esponsibleray appetitesway, andway enthay ethay estructionday ofway ethay oodgay ingsthay 
eganbay. Afterway ethay eastfay erethay asway away efreshingray easonsay ofway estray andway atchay inway 
ethay adeshay ofway eadingspray oaksway. Ybay-and-by omebodysay outedshay: 

"Owhay's eadyray orfay ethay avecay?" 

Everybodyway asway. Undlesbay ofway andlescay ereway ocuredpray, andway aightwaystray erethay 
asway away eneralgay amperscay upway ethay illhay. Ethay outhmay ofway ethay avecay asway upway ethay 
illsidehay--an openingway apedshay ikelay away etterlay Away. Itsway assivemay oakenway oorday oodstay 
unbarredway. Ithinway asway away allsmay amberchay, illychay asway anway icehouseway, andway alledway 
ybay Aturenay ithway olidsay imestonelay atthay asway ewyday ithway away oldcay eatsway. Itway asway 
omanticray andway ysteriousmay otay andstay erehay inway ethay eepday oomglay andway ooklay outway 
uponway ethay eengray alleyvay iningshay inway ethay unsay. Utbay ethay impressivenessway ofway ethay 
ituationsay uicklyqay oreway offway, andway ethay ompingray eganbay againway. Ethay omentmay 
away andlecay asway ightedlay erethay asway away eneralgay ushray uponway ethay ownerway ofway itway; away 
ugglestray andway away allantgay efenceday ollowedfay, utbay ethay andlecay asway oonsay ockedknay 
ownday orway ownblay outway, andway enthay erethay asway away adglay amorclay ofway aughterlay andway away 
ewnay asechay. Utbay allway ingsthay avehay anway endway. Ybay-and-by ethay ocessionpray entway 
ilingfay ownday ethay eepstay escentday ofway ethay ainmay avenueway, ethay ickeringflay ankray ofway 
ightslay imlyday evealingray ethay oftylay allsway ofway ockray almostway otay eirthay ointpay ofway 
unctionjay ixtysay eetfay overheadway. Isthay ainmay avenueway asway otnay oremay anthay 
eightway orway entay eetfay ideway. Everyway ewfay epsstay otherway oftylay andway illstay arrowernay 
evicescray anchedbray omfray itway onway eitherway andhay--for Ougalmcday's avecay asway utbay away 
astvay abyrinthlay ofway ookedcray aislesway atthay anray intoway eachway otherway andway outway againway 
andway edlay owherenay. Itway asway aidsay atthay oneway ightmay anderway aysday andway ightsnay 
ogethertay oughthray itsway intricateway angletay ofway iftsray andway asmschay, andway evernay 
indfay ethay endway ofway ethay avecay; andway atthay ehay ightmay ogay ownday, andway ownday, andway 
illstay ownday, intoway ethay earthway, andway itway asway ustjay ethay amesay--labyrinth underway 
abyrinthlay, andway onay endway otay anyway ofway emthay. Onay anmay "ewknay" ethay avecay. Atthay asway 
anway impossibleway ingthay. Ostmay ofway ethay youngway enmay ewknay away ortionpay ofway itway, andway itway 
asway otnay ustomarycay otay enturevay uchmay eyondbay isthay ownknay ortionpay. Omtay Awyersay 
ewknay asway uchmay ofway ethay avecay asway anyway oneway. 

Ethay ocessionpray ovedmay alongway ethay ainmay avenueway omesay eethray-quarters ofway 
away ilemay, andway enthay oupsgray andway ouplescay eganbay otay ipslay asideway intoway anchbray 
avenuesway, yflay alongway ethay ismalday orridorscay, andway aketay eachway otherway ybay urprisesay 
atway ointspay erewhay ethay orridorscay oinedjay againway. Artiespay ereway ableway otay eludeway 
eachway otherway orfay ethay acespay ofway alfhay anway ourhay ithoutway oinggay eyondbay ethay 
"ownknay" oundgray. 

Ybay-and-by, oneway oupgray afterway anotherway amecay agglingstray ackbay otay ethay outhmay 
ofway ethay avecay, antingpay, ilarioushay, earedsmay omfray eadhay otay ootfay ithway allowtay 
ippingsdray, aubedday ithway ayclay, andway entirelyway elightedday ithway ethay uccesssay ofway 
ethay ayday. Enthay eythay ereway astonishedway otay indfay atthay eythay adhay eenbay akingtay 
onay otenay ofway imetay andway atthay ightnay asway aboutway atway andhay. Ethay angingclay ellbay adhay 
eenbay allingcay orfay alfhay anway ourhay. Oweverhay, isthay ortsay ofway oseclay otay ethay ayday's 
adventuresway asway omanticray andway ereforethay atisfactorysay. Enwhay ethay erryboatfay 
ithway erhay ildway eightfray ushedpay intoway ethay eamstray, obodynay aredcay ixpencesay orfay 
ethay astedway imetay utbay ethay aptaincay ofway ethay aftcray. 

Uckhay asway alreadyway uponway ishay atchway enwhay ethay erryboatfay's ightslay entway 
intingglay astpay ethay arfwhay. Ehay eardhay onay oisenay onway oardbay, orfay ethay youngway 
eoplepay ereway asway ubduedsay andway illstay asway eoplepay usuallyway areway owhay areway earlynay 
iredtay otay eathday. Ehay onderedway atwhay oatbay itway asway, andway ywhay eshay idday otnay 
opstay atway ethay arfwhay--and enthay ehay oppeddray erhay outway ofway ishay indmay andway utpay ishay 
attentionway uponway ishay usinessbay. Ethay ightnay asway owinggray oudyclay andway arkday. Entay 
oway'clock amecay, andway ethay oisenay ofway ehiclesvay easedcay, atteredscay ightslay eganbay 
otay inkway outway, allway agglingstray ootfay-passengers isappearedday, ethay illagevay 
etookbay itselfway otay itsway umbersslay andway eftlay ethay allsmay atcherway aloneway ithway ethay 
ilencesay andway ethay ostsghay. Elevenway oway'clock amecay, andway ethay averntay ightslay ereway 
utpay outway; arknessday everywhereway, ownay. Uckhay aitedway atwhay eemedsay away earyway onglay 
imetay, utbay othingnay appenedhay. Ishay aithfay asway eakeningway. Asway erethay anyway useway? 
Asway erethay eallyray anyway useway? Ywhay otnay ivegay itway upway andway urntay inway? 

Away oisenay ellfay uponway ishay earway. Ehay asway allway attentionway inway anway instantway. Ethay alleyway 
oorday osedclay oftlysay. Ehay angspray otay ethay ornercay ofway ethay ickbray orestay. Ethay extnay 
omentmay otway enmay ushedbray ybay imhay, andway oneway eemedsay otay avehay omethingsay underway 
ishay armway. Itway ustmay ebay atthay oxbay! Osay eythay ereway oinggay otay emoveray ethay easuretray. 
Ywhay allcay Omtay ownay? Itway ouldway ebay absurdway--the enmay ouldway etgay awayway ithway ethay oxbay 
andway evernay ebay oundfay againway. Onay, ehay ouldway ickstay otay eirthay akeway andway ollowfay 
emthay; ehay ouldway usttray otay ethay arknessday orfay ecuritysay omfray iscoveryday. Osay 
ommuningcay ithway imselfhay, Uckhay eppedstay outway andway idedglay alongway ehindbay ethay 
enmay, atcay-like, ithway arebay eetfay, allowingway emthay otay eepkay ustjay arfay enoughway 
aheadway otnay otay ebay invisibleway. 

Eythay ovedmay upway ethay iverray eetstray eethray ocksblay, enthay urnedtay otay ethay eftlay upway 
away ossstreetcray. Eythay entway aightstray aheadway, enthay, untilway eythay amecay otay ethay 
athpay atthay edlay upway Ardiffcay Illhay; isthay eythay ooktay. Eythay assedpay ybay ethay oldway 
Elshmanway's ousehay, alfwayhay upway ethay illhay, ithoutway esitatinghay, andway illstay 
imbedclay upwardway. Oodgay, oughtthay Uckhay, eythay illway urybay itway inway ethay oldway uarryqay. 
Utbay eythay evernay oppedstay atway ethay uarryqay. Eythay assedpay onway, upway ethay ummitsay. 
Eythay ungedplay intoway ethay arrownay athpay etweenbay ethay alltay umachsay ushesbay, andway 
ereway atway onceway iddenhay inway ethay oomglay. Uckhay osedclay upway andway ortenedshay ishay 
istanceday, ownay, orfay eythay ouldway evernay ebay ableway otay eesay imhay. Ehay ottedtray alongway 
awhileway; enthay ackenedslay ishay acepay, earingfay ehay asway aininggay ootay astfay; ovedmay 
onway away iecepay, enthay oppedstay altogetherway; istenedlay; onay oundsay; onenay, avesay atthay 
ehay eemedsay otay earhay ethay eatingbay ofway ishay ownway earthay. Ethay ootinghay ofway anway 
owlway amecay overway ethay illhay--ominous oundsay! Utbay onay ootstepsfay. Eavenshay, asway 
everythingway ostlay! Ehay asway aboutway otay ingspray ithway ingedway eetfay, enwhay away anmay 
earedclay ishay oatthray otnay ourfay eetfay omfray imhay! Uckhay's earthay otshay intoway ishay 
oatthray, utbay ehay allowedsway itway againway; andway enthay ehay oodstay erethay akingshay asway 
ifway away ozenday aguesway adhay akentay argechay ofway imhay atway onceway, andway osay eakway atthay ehay 
oughtthay ehay ustmay urelysay allfay otay ethay oundgray. Ehay ewknay erewhay ehay asway. Ehay 
ewknay ehay asway ithinway ivefay epsstay ofway ethay ilestay eadinglay intoway Idowway Ouglasday' 
oundsgray. Eryvay ellway, ehay oughtthay, etlay emthay urybay itway erethay; itway onway't ebay ardhay 
otay indfay. 

Ownay erethay asway away oicevay--a eryvay owlay oicevay--Injun Oejay's: 

"Amnday erhay, aybemay eshay's otgay ompanycay--there's ightslay, atelay asway itway isway." 

"Iway ancay't eesay anyway." 

Isthay asway atthay angerstray's oicevay--the angerstray ofway ethay auntedhay ousehay. Away 
eadlyday illchay entway otay Uckhay's earthay--this, enthay, asway ethay "evengeray" objay! Ishay 
oughtthay asway, otay yflay. Enthay ehay ememberedray atthay ethay Idowway Ouglasday adhay eenbay 
indkay otay imhay oremay anthay onceway, andway aybemay esethay enmay ereway oinggay otay urdermay 
erhay. Ehay ishedway ehay aredday enturevay otay arnway erhay; utbay ehay ewknay ehay idnday't 
areday--they ightmay omecay andway atchcay imhay. Ehay oughtthay allway isthay andway oremay inway 
ethay omentmay atthay elapsedway etweenbay ethay angerstray's emarkray andway Injunway Oejay's 
extnay--which asway-- 

"Ecausebay ethay ushbay isway inway yourway ayway. Ownay--this ayway--now youway eesay, onday't youway?" 

"Yesway. Ellway, erethay _isway_ ompanycay erethay, Iway eckonray. Etterbay ivegay itway upway." 

"Ivegay itway upway, andway Iway ustjay eavinglay isthay ountrycay oreverfay! Ivegay itway upway andway 
aybemay evernay avehay anotherway ancechay. Iway elltay youway againway, asway Iway've oldtay youway 
eforebay, Iway onday't arecay orfay erhay agsway--you aymay avehay itway. Utbay erhay usbandhay asway 
oughray onway emay--many imestay ehay asway oughray onway emay--and ainlymay ehay asway ethay usticejay 
ofway ethay eacepay atthay uggedjay emay orfay away agrantvay. Andway atthay ainway't allway. Itway ainway't 
away illionthmay artpay ofway itway! Ehay adhay emay _orsewhippedhay_!--horsewhipped inway 
ontfray ofway ethay ailjay, ikelay away iggernay!--with allway ethay owntay ookinglay onway! 
_Orsewhippedhay_!--do youway understandway? Ehay ooktay advantageway ofway emay andway iedday. Utbay 
Iway'll aketay itway outway ofway _erhay_." 

"Ohway, onday't illkay erhay! Onday't oday atthay!" 

"Illkay? Owhay aidsay anythingway aboutway illingkay? Iway ouldway illkay _imhay_ ifway ehay asway 
erehay; utbay otnay erhay. Enwhay youway antway otay etgay evengeray onway away omanway youway onday't 
illkay erhay--bosh! youway ogay orfay erhay ookslay. Youway itslay erhay ostrilsnay--you otchnay erhay 
earsway ikelay away owsay!" 

"Ybay Odgay, atthay's--" 

"Eepkay yourway opinionway otay yourselfway! Itway illway ebay afestsay orfay youway. Iway'll ietay erhay 
otay ethay edbay. Ifway eshay eedsblay otay eathday, isway atthay ymay aultfay? Iway'll otnay ycray, ifway 
eshay oesday. Ymay iendfray, youway'll elphay emay inway isthay ingthay--for _ymay_ akesay--that's 
ywhay youway're erehay--I ightnmay't ebay ableway aloneway. Ifway youway inchflay, Iway'll illkay youway. 
Oday youway understandway atthay? Andway ifway Iway avehay otay illkay youway, Iway'll illkay erhay--and 
enthay Iway eckonray obodynay'll everway owknay uchmay aboutway owhay oneday isthay usinessbay." 

"Ellway, ifway itway's otgay otay ebay oneday, etlay's etgay atway itway. Ethay uickerqay ethay 
etterbay--I'm allway inway away ivershay." 

"Oday itway _ownay_? Andway ompanycay erethay? Ooklay erehay--I'll etgay uspicioussay ofway youway, 
irstfay ingthay youway owknay. Onay--we'll aitway illtay ethay ightslay areway outway--there's onay 
urryhay." 

Uckhay eltfay atthay away ilencesay asway oinggay otay ensueway--a ingthay illstay oremay awfulway 
anthay anyway amountway ofway urderousmay alktay; osay ehay eldhay ishay eathbray andway eppedstay 
ingerlygay ackbay; antedplay ishay ootfay arefullycay andway irmlyfay, afterway alancingbay, 
oneway-legged, inway away ecariouspray ayway andway almostway opplingtay overway, irstfay onway oneway 
idesay andway enthay onway ethay otherway. Ehay ooktay anotherway epstay ackbay, ithway ethay amesay 
elaborationway andway ethay amesay isksray; enthay anotherway andway anotherway, andway--a igtway 
appedsnay underway ishay ootfay! Ishay eathbray oppedstay andway ehay istenedlay. Erethay asway onay 
oundsay--the illnessstay asway erfectpay. Ishay atitudegray asway easurelessmay. Ownay ehay 
urnedtay inway ishay ackstray, etweenbay ethay allsway ofway umachsay ushesbay--turned 
imselfhay asway arefullycay asway ifway ehay ereway away ipshay--and enthay eppedstay uicklyqay utbay 
autiouslycay alongway. Enwhay ehay emergedway atway ethay uarryqay ehay eltfay ecuresay, andway 
osay ehay ickedpay upway ishay imblenay eelshay andway ewflay. Ownday, ownday ehay edspay, illtay ehay 
eachedray ethay Elshmanway's. Ehay angedbay atway ethay oorday, andway esentlypray ethay eadshay 
ofway ethay oldway anmay andway ishay otway alwartstay onssay ereway ustthray omfray indowsway. 

"Atwhay's ethay owray erethay? Owhay's angingbay? Atwhay oday youway antway?" 

"Etlay emay inway--quick! Iway'll elltay everythingway." 

"Ywhay, owhay areway youway?" 

"Uckleberryhay Innfay--quick, etlay emay inway!" 

"Uckleberryhay Innfay, indeedway! Itway ainway't away amenay otay openway anymay oorsday, Iway udgejay! 
Utbay etlay imhay inway, adslay, andway etlay's eesay atwhay's ethay oubletray." 

"Easeplay onday't everway elltay Iway oldtay youway," ereway Uckhay's irstfay ordsway enwhay ehay otgay 
inway. "Easeplay onday't--I'd ebay illedkay, uresay--but ethay idowway's eenbay oodgay iendsfray 
otay emay ometimessay, andway Iway antway otay elltay--I _illway_ elltay ifway youway'll omisepray youway 
onway't everway aysay itway asway emay." 

"Ybay Eorgegay, ehay _ashay_ otgay omethingsay otay elltay, orway ehay ouldnway't actway osay!" 
exclaimedway ethay oldway anmay; "outway ithway itway andway obodynay erehay'll everway elltay, adlay." 

Eethray inutesmay aterlay ethay oldway anmay andway ishay onssay, ellway armedway, ereway upway ethay 
illhay, andway ustjay enteringway ethay umachsay athpay onway iptoetay, eirthay eaponsway inway 
eirthay andshay. Uckhay accompaniedway emthay onay urtherfay. Ehay idhay ehindbay away eatgray 
owlderbay andway ellfay otay isteninglay. Erethay asway away agginglay, anxiousway ilencesay, andway 
enthay allway ofway away uddensay erethay asway anway explosionway ofway irearmsfay andway away ycray. 

Uckhay aitedway orfay onay articularspay. Ehay angspray awayway andway edspay ownday ethay illhay asway 
astfay asway ishay egslay ouldcay arrycay imhay. 




APTERCHAY XXXAY 

ASWAY ethay earliestway uspicionsay ofway awnday appearedway onway Undaysay orningmay, Uckhay amecay 
opinggray upway ethay illhay andway appedray entlygay atway ethay oldway Elshmanway's oorday. Ethay 
inmatesway ereway asleepway, utbay itway asway away eepslay atthay asway etsay onway away airhay-trigger, 
onway accountway ofway ethay excitingway episodeway ofway ethay ightnay. Away allcay amecay omfray away 
indowway: 

"Owhay's erethay!" 

Uckhay's aredscay oicevay answeredway inway away owlay onetay: 

"Easeplay etlay emay inway! Itway's onlyway Uckhay Innfay!" 

"Itway's away amenay atthay ancay openway isthay oorday ightnay orway ayday, adlay!--and elcomeway!" 

Esethay ereway angestray ordsway otay ethay agabondvay oybay's earsway, andway ethay easantestplay 
ehay adhay everway eardhay. Ehay ouldcay otnay ecollectray atthay ethay osingclay ordway adhay everway 
eenbay appliedway inway ishay asecay eforebay. Ethay oorday asway uicklyqay unlockedway, andway ehay 
enteredway. Uckhay asway ivengay away eatsay andway ethay oldway anmay andway ishay acebray ofway alltay 
onssay eedilyspay esseddray emselvesthay. 

"Ownay, ymay oybay, Iway opehay youway're oodgay andway ungryhay, ecausebay eakfastbray illway ebay 
eadyray asway oonsay asway ethay unsay's upway, andway eway'll avehay away ipingpay othay oneway, ootay--make 
yourselfway easyway aboutway atthay! Iway andway ethay oysbay opedhay youway'd urntay upway andway opstay 
erehay astlay ightnay." 

"Iway asway awfulway aredscay," aidsay Uckhay, "andway Iway unray. Iway ooktay outway enwhay ethay istolspay 
entway offway, andway Iway idnday't opstay orfay eethray ilemay. Iway've omecay ownay ecuzbay Iway antedway 
otay owknay aboutway itway, youway owknay; andway Iway omecay eforebay aylightday ecuzbay Iway idnday't 
antway otay unray acrossway emthay evilsday, evenway ifway eythay asway eadday." 

"Ellway, oorpay apchay, youway oday ooklay asway ifway youway'd adhay away ardhay ightnay ofway itway--but 
erethay's away edbay erehay orfay youway enwhay youway've adhay yourway eakfastbray. Onay, eythay 
ainway't eadday, adlay--we areway orrysay enoughway orfay atthay. Youway eesay eway ewknay ightray 
erewhay otay utpay ourway andshay onway emthay, ybay yourway escriptionday; osay eway eptcray alongway 
onway iptoetay illtay eway otgay ithinway ifteenfay eetfay ofway emthay--dark asway away ellarcay atthay 
umachsay athpay asway--and ustjay enthay Iway oundfay Iway asway oinggay otay eezesnay. Itway asway ethay 
eanestmay indkay ofway ucklay! Iway iedtray otay eepkay itway ackbay, utbay onay useway--'twas oundbay otay 
omecay, andway itway idday omecay! Iway asway inway ethay eadlay ithway ymay istolpay aisedray, andway enwhay 
ethay eezesnay artedstay osethay oundrelsscay away-rustling otay etgay outway ofway ethay athpay, 
Iway ungsay outway, 'Irefay oysbay!' andway azedblay awayway atway ethay aceplay erewhay ethay ustlingray 
asway. Osay idday ethay oysbay. Utbay eythay ereway offway inway away iffyjay, osethay illainsvay, andway 
eway afterway emthay, ownday oughthray ethay oodsway. Iway udgejay eway evernay ouchedtay emthay. 
Eythay iredfay away otshay apieceway asway eythay artedstay, utbay eirthay ulletsbay izzedwhay ybay 
andway idnday't oday usway anyway armhay. Asway oonsay asway eway ostlay ethay oundsay ofway eirthay eetfay 
eway uitqay asingchay, andway entway ownday andway irredstay upway ethay onstablescay. Eythay otgay away 
ossepay ogethertay, andway entway offway otay uardgay ethay iverray ankbay, andway asway oonsay asway itway 
isway ightlay ethay eriffshay andway away anggay areway oinggay otay eatbay upway ethay oodsway. Ymay oysbay 
illway ebay ithway emthay esentlypray. Iway ishway eway adhay omesay ortsay ofway escriptionday ofway 
osethay ascalsray--'twould elphay away oodgay ealday. Utbay youway ouldncay't eesay atwhay eythay 
ereway ikelay, inway ethay arkday, adlay, Iway upposesay?" 

"Ohway yesway; Iway awsay emthay owntownday andway olleredfay emthay." 

"Endidsplay! Escribeday emthay--describe emthay, ymay oybay!" 

"Oneway's ethay oldway eafday andway umbday Aniardspay atthay's enbay aroundway erehay onceway orway 
icetway, andway tway'other's away eanmay-looking, aggedray--" 

"Atthay's enoughway, adlay, eway owknay ethay enmay! Appenedhay onway emthay inway ethay oodsway ackbay 
ofway ethay idowway's oneway ayday, andway eythay unkslay awayway. Offway ithway youway, oysbay, andway 
elltay ethay eriffshay--get yourway eakfastbray omorrowtay orningmay!" 

Ethay Elshmanway's onssay epartedday atway onceway. Asway eythay ereway eavinglay ethay oomray Uckhay 
angspray upway andway exclaimedway: 

"Ohway, easeplay onday't elltay _anyway_body itway asway emay atthay owedblay onway emthay! Ohway, 
easeplay!" 

"Allway ightray ifway youway aysay itway, Uckhay, utbay youway oughtway otay avehay ethay editcray ofway atwhay 
youway idday." 

"Ohway onay, onay! Easeplay onday't elltay!" 

Enwhay ethay youngway enmay ereway onegay, ethay oldway Elshmanway aidsay: 

"Eythay onway't elltay--and Iway onway't. Utbay ywhay onday't youway antway itway ownknay?" 

Uckhay ouldway otnay explainway, urtherfay anthay otay aysay atthay ehay alreadyway ewknay ootay 
uchmay aboutway oneway ofway osethay enmay andway ouldway otnay avehay ethay anmay owknay atthay ehay ewknay 
anythingway againstway imhay orfay ethay olewhay orldway--he ouldway ebay illedkay orfay owingknay 
itway, uresay. 

Ethay oldway anmay omisedpray ecrecysay onceway oremay, andway aidsay: 

"Owhay idday youway omecay otay ollowfay esethay ellowsfay, adlay? Ereway eythay ookinglay 
uspicioussay?" 

Uckhay asway ilentsay ilewhay ehay amedfray away ulyday autiouscay eplyray. Enthay ehay aidsay: 

"Ellway, youway eesay, Iway'm away indkay ofway away ardhay otlay,--least everybodyway ayssay osay, andway 
Iway onday't eesay othingnay aginway itway--and ometimessay Iway ancay't eepslay uchmay, onway accountway 
ofway inkingthay aboutway itway andway ortsay ofway yingtray otay ikestray outway away ewnay ayway ofway 
oingday. Atthay asway ethay ayway ofway itway astlay ightnay. Iway ouldncay't eepslay, andway osay Iway 
omecay alongway upstreetway 'outbay idnightmay, away-turning itway allway overway, andway enwhay Iway 
otgay otay atthay oldway acklyshay ickbray orestay ybay ethay Emperancetay Averntay, Iway ackedbay 
upway aginway ethay allway otay avehay anotherway inkthay. Ellway, ustjay enthay alongway omescay 
esethay otway apschay ippingslay alongway oseclay ybay emay, ithway omethingsay underway eirthay 
armway, andway Iway eckonedray eythay'd olestay itway. Oneway asway away-smoking, andway tway'other oneway 
antedway away ightlay; osay eythay oppedstay ightray eforebay emay andway ethay igarscay itlay upway 
eirthay acesfay andway Iway eesay atthay ethay igbay oneway asway ethay eafday andway umbday Aniardspay, 
ybay ishay itewhay iskerswhay andway ethay atchpay onway ishay eyeway, andway tway'other oneway asway away 
ustyray, aggedray-looking evilday." 

"Ouldcay youway eesay ethay agsray ybay ethay ightlay ofway ethay igarscay?" 

Isthay aggeredstay Uckhay orfay away omentmay. Enthay ehay aidsay: 

"Ellway, Iway onday't owknay--but omehowsay itway eemssay asway ifway Iway idday." 

"Enthay eythay entway onway, andway youway--" 

"Olleredfay 'emway--yes. Atthay asway itway. Iway antedway otay eesay atwhay asway upway--they eakedsnay 
alongway osay. Iway oggedday 'emway otay ethay idderway's ilestay, andway oodstay inway ethay arkday andway 
eardhay ethay aggedray oneway egbay orfay ethay idderway, andway ethay Aniardspay earsway ehay'd 
ilespay erhay ookslay ustjay asway Iway oldtay youway andway yourway otway--" 

"Atwhay! Ethay _eafday andway umbday_ anmay aidsay allway atthay!" 

Uckhay adhay ademay anotherway erribletay istakemay! Ehay asway yingtray ishay estbay otay eepkay 
ethay oldway anmay omfray ettinggay ethay aintestfay inthay ofway owhay ethay Aniardspay ightmay ebay, 
andway yetway ishay onguetay eemedsay eterminedday otay etgay imhay intoway oubletray inway itespay ofway 
allway ehay ouldcay oday. Ehay ademay everalsay effortsway otay eepcray outway ofway ishay apescray, 
utbay ethay oldway anmay's eyeway asway uponway imhay andway ehay ademay underblay afterway underblay. 
Esentlypray ethay Elshmanway aidsay: 

"Ymay oybay, onday't ebay afraidway ofway emay. Iway ouldnway't urthay away airhay ofway yourway eadhay orfay 
allway ethay orldway. Onay--I'd otectpray youway--I'd otectpray youway. Isthay Aniardspay isway 
otnay eafday andway umbday; youway've etlay atthay ipslay ithoutway intendingway itway; youway ancay't 
overcay atthay upway ownay. Youway owknay omethingsay aboutway atthay Aniardspay atthay youway antway 
otay eepkay arkday. Ownay usttray emay--tell emay atwhay itway isway, andway usttray emay--I onway't 
etraybay youway." 

Uckhay ookedlay intoway ethay oldway anmay's onesthay eyesway away omentmay, enthay entbay overway andway 
isperedwhay inway ishay earway: 

"'Aintay't away Aniardspay--it's Injunway Oejay!" 

Ethay Elshmanway almostway umpedjay outway ofway ishay airchay. Inway away omentmay ehay aidsay: 

"Itway's allway ainplay enoughway, ownay. Enwhay youway alkedtay aboutway otchingnay earsway andway 
ittingslay osesnay Iway udgedjay atthay atthay asway yourway ownway embellishmentway, ecausebay 
itewhay enmay onday't aketay atthay ortsay ofway evengeray. Utbay anway Injunway! Atthay's away 
ifferentday attermay altogetherway." 

Uringday eakfastbray ethay alktay entway onway, andway inway ethay oursecay ofway itway ethay oldway anmay 
aidsay atthay ethay astlay ingthay ichwhay ehay andway ishay onssay adhay oneday, eforebay oinggay 
otay edbay, asway otay etgay away anternlay andway examineway ethay ilestay andway itsway icinityvay orfay 
arksmay ofway oodblay. Eythay oundfay onenay, utbay apturedcay away ulkybay undlebay ofway-- 

"Ofway _atwhay_?" 

Ifway ethay ordsway adhay eenbay ightninglay eythay ouldcay otnay avehay eapedlay ithway away oremay 
unningstay uddennesssay omfray Uckhay's anchedblay ipslay. Ishay eyesway ereway aringstay 
ideway, ownay, andway ishay eathbray uspendedsay--waiting orfay ethay answerway. Ethay Elshmanway 
artedstay--stared inway eturnray--three econdssay--five econdssay--ten--then epliedray: 

"Ofway urglarbay's oolstay. Ywhay, atwhay's ethay _attermay_ ithway youway?" 

Uckhay anksay ackbay, antingpay entlygay, utbay eeplyday, unutterablyway atefulgray. Ethay 
Elshmanway eyedway imhay avelygray, uriouslycay--and esentlypray aidsay: 

"Yesway, urglarbay's oolstay. Atthay appearsway otay elieveray youway away oodgay ealday. Utbay atwhay 
idday ivegay youway atthay urntay? Atwhay ereway _youway_ expectingway eway'd oundfay?" 

Uckhay asway inway away oseclay aceplay--the inquiringway eyeway asway uponway imhay--he ouldway avehay 
ivengay anythingway orfay aterialmay orfay away ausibleplay answerway--nothing uggestedsay 
itselfway--the inquiringway eyeway asway oringbay eeperday andway eeperday--a enselesssay 
eplyray offeredway--there asway onay imetay otay eighway itway, osay atway away enturevay ehay utteredway 
itway--feebly: 

"Undaysay-school ooksbay, aybemay." 

Oorpay Uckhay asway ootay istressedday otay ilesmay, utbay ethay oldway anmay aughedlay oudlay andway 
oyouslyjay, ookshay upway ethay etailsday ofway ishay anatomyway omfray eadhay otay ootfay, andway 
endedway ybay ayingsay atthay uchsay away aughlay asway oneymay inway away-man's ocketpay, ecausebay 
itway utcay ownday ethay octorday's illbay ikelay everythingway. Enthay ehay addedway: 

"Oorpay oldway apchay, youway're itewhay andway adedjay--you ainway't ellway away itbay--no onderway 
youway're away ittlelay ightyflay andway offway yourway alancebay. Utbay youway'll omecay outway ofway itway. 
Estray andway eepslay illway etchfay youway outway allway ightray, Iway opehay." 

Uckhay asway irritatedway otay inkthay ehay adhay eenbay uchsay away oosegay andway etrayedbay uchsay 
away uspicioussay excitementway, orfay ehay adhay oppeddray ethay ideaway atthay ethay arcelpay 
oughtbray omfray ethay averntay asway ethay easuretray, asway oonsay asway ehay adhay eardhay ethay 
alktay atway ethay idowway's ilestay. Ehay adhay onlyway oughtthay itway asway otnay ethay easuretray, 
oweverhay--he adhay otnay ownknay atthay itway asnway't--and osay ethay uggestionsay ofway away 
apturedcay undlebay asway ootay uchmay orfay ishay elfsay-possession. Utbay onway ethay olewhay 
ehay eltfay adglay ethay ittlelay episodeway adhay appenedhay, orfay ownay ehay ewknay eyondbay allway 
uestionqay atthay atthay undlebay asway otnay _ethay_ undlebay, andway osay ishay indmay asway 
atway estray andway exceedinglyway omfortablecay. Inway actfay, everythingway eemedsay otay ebay 
iftingdray ustjay inway ethay ightray irectionday, ownay; ethay easuretray ustmay ebay illstay 
inway Onay. 2, ethay enmay ouldway ebay apturedcay andway ailedjay atthay ayday, andway ehay andway 
Omtay ouldcay eizesay ethay oldgay atthay ightnay ithoutway anyway oubletray orway anyway earfay ofway 
interruptionway. 

Ustjay asway eakfastbray asway ompletedcay erethay asway away ockknay atway ethay oorday. Uckhay 
umpedjay orfay away idinghay-place, orfay ehay adhay onay indmay otay ebay onnectedcay evenway 
emotelyray ithway ethay atelay eventway. Ethay Elshmanway admittedway everalsay adieslay andway 
entlemengay, amongway emthay ethay Idowway Ouglasday, andway oticednay atthay oupsgray ofway 
itizenscay ereway imbingclay upway ethay illhay--to arestay atway ethay ilestay. Osay ethay ewsnay 
adhay eadspray. Ethay Elshmanway adhay otay elltay ethay orystay ofway ethay ightnay otay ethay 
isitorsvay. Ethay idowway's atitudegray orfay erhay eservationpray asway outspokenway. 

"Onday't aysay away ordway aboutway itway, adammay. Erethay's anotherway atthay youway're oremay 
eholdenbay otay anthay youway areway otay emay andway ymay oysbay, aybemay, utbay ehay onday't allowway emay 
otay elltay ishay amenay. Eway ouldnway't avehay eenbay erethay utbay orfay imhay." 

Ofway oursecay isthay excitedway away uriositycay osay astvay atthay itway almostway elittledbay ethay 
ainmay attermay--but ethay Elshmanway allowedway itway otay eatway intoway ethay italsvay ofway ishay 
isitorsvay, andway oughthray emthay ebay ansmittedtray otay ethay olewhay owntay, orfay ehay 
efusedray otay artpay ithway ishay ecretsay. Enwhay allway elseway adhay eenbay earnedlay, ethay 
idowway aidsay: 

"Iway entway otay eepslay eadingray inway edbay andway eptslay aightstray oughthray allway atthay 
oisenay. Ywhay idnday't youway omecay andway akeway emay?" 

"Eway udgedjay itway arnway't orthway ilewhay. Osethay ellowsfay arnway't ikelylay otay omecay 
againway--they adnhay't anyway oolstay eftlay otay orkway ithway, andway atwhay asway ethay useway ofway 
akingway youway upway andway aringscay youway otay eathday? Ymay eethray egronay enmay oodstay uardgay 
atway yourway ousehay allway ethay estray ofway ethay ightnay. Eythay've ustjay omecay ackbay." 

Oremay isitorsvay amecay, andway ethay orystay adhay otay ebay oldtay andway etoldray orfay away ouplecay 
ofway ourshay oremay. 

Erethay asway onay Abbathsay-school uringday ayday-school acationvay, utbay everybodyway 
asway earlyway atway urchchay. Ethay irringstay eventway asway ellway anvassedcay. Ewsnay amecay 
atthay otnay away ignsay ofway ethay otway illainsvay adhay eenbay yetway iscoveredday. Enwhay ethay 
ermonsay asway inishedfay, Udgejay Atcherthay's ifeway oppeddray alongsideway ofway Mrsay. 
Arperhay asway eshay ovedmay ownday ethay aisleway ithway ethay owdcray andway aidsay: 

"Isway ymay Eckybay oinggay otay eepslay allway ayday? Iway ustjay expectedway eshay ouldway ebay iredtay 
otay eathday." 

"Yourway Eckybay?" 

"Yesway," ithway away artledstay ooklay--"didn't eshay aystay ithway youway astlay ightnay?" 

"Ywhay, onay." 

Mrsay. Atcherthay urnedtay alepay, andway anksay intoway away ewpay, ustjay asway Auntway Ollypay, 
alkingtay isklybray ithway away iendfray, assedpay ybay. Auntway Ollypay aidsay: 

"Oodmorninggay, Mrsay. Atcherthay. Oodmorninggay, Mrsay. Arperhay. Iway've otgay away oybay 
atthay's urnedtay upway issingmay. Iway eckonray ymay Omtay ayedstay atway yourway ousehay astlay 
ightnay--one ofway youway. Andway ownay ehay's afraidway otay omecay otay urchchay. Iway've otgay otay 
ettlesay ithway imhay." 

Mrsay. Atcherthay ookshay erhay eadhay eeblyfay andway urnedtay alerpay anthay everway. 

"Ehay idnday't aystay ithway usway," aidsay Mrsay. Arperhay, eginningbay otay ooklay uneasyway. Away 
arkedmay anxietyway amecay intoway Auntway Ollypay's acefay. 

"Oejay Arperhay, avehay youway eensay ymay Omtay isthay orningmay?" 

"Onay'm." 

"Enwhay idday youway eesay imhay astlay?" 

Oejay iedtray otay ememberray, utbay asway otnay uresay ehay ouldcay aysay. Ethay eoplepay adhay 
oppedstay ovingmay outway ofway urchchay. Isperswhay assedpay alongway, andway away odingbay 
uneasinessway ooktay ossessionpay ofway everyway ountenancecay. Ildrenchay ereway anxiouslyway 
uestionedqay, andway youngway eacherstay. Eythay allway aidsay eythay adhay otnay oticednay 
etherwhay Omtay andway Eckybay ereway onway oardbay ethay erryboatfay onway ethay omewardhay iptray; 
itway asway arkday; onay oneway oughtthay ofway inquiringway ifway anyway oneway asway issingmay. Oneway 
youngway anmay inallyfay urtedblay outway ishay earfay atthay eythay ereway illstay inway ethay avecay! 
Mrsay. Atcherthay oonedsway awayway. Auntway Ollypay ellfay otay yingcray andway ingingwray erhay 
andshay. 

Ethay alarmway eptsway omfray iplay otay iplay, omfray oupgray otay oupgray, omfray eetstray otay 
eetstray, andway ithinway ivefay inutesmay ethay ellsbay ereway ildlyway angingclay andway 
ethay olewhay owntay asway upway! Ethay Ardiffcay Illhay episodeway anksay intoway instantway 
insignificanceway, ethay urglarsbay ereway orgottenfay, orseshay ereway addledsay, iffsskay 
ereway annedmay, ethay erryboatfay orderedway outway, andway eforebay ethay orrorhay asway alfhay 
anway ourhay oldway, otway undredhay enmay ereway ouringpay ownday ighroadhay andway iverray owardtay 
ethay avecay. 

Allway ethay onglay afternoonway ethay illagevay eemedsay emptyway andway eadday. Anymay omenway 
isitedvay Auntway Ollypay andway Mrsay. Atcherthay andway iedtray otay omfortcay emthay. Eythay 
iedcray ithway emthay, ootay, andway atthay asway illstay etterbay anthay ordsway. Allway ethay 
edioustay ightnay ethay owntay aitedway orfay ewsnay; utbay enwhay ethay orningmay awnedday atway 
astlay, allway ethay ordway atthay amecay asway, "Endsay oremay andlescay--and endsay oodfay." 
Mrsay. Atcherthay asway almostway azedcray; andway Auntway Ollypay, alsoway. Udgejay Atcherthay 
entsay essagesmay ofway opehay andway encouragementway omfray ethay avecay, utbay eythay onveyedcay 
onay ealray eerchay. 

Ethay oldway Elshmanway amecay omehay owardtay aylightday, atteredspay ithway 
andlecay-grease, earedsmay ithway ayclay, andway almostway ornway outway. Ehay oundfay Uckhay 
illstay inway ethay edbay atthay adhay eenbay ovidedpray orfay imhay, andway eliriousday ithway 
everfay. Ethay ysiciansphay ereway allway atway ethay avecay, osay ethay Idowway Ouglasday amecay 
andway ooktay argechay ofway ethay atientpay. Eshay aidsay eshay ouldway oday erhay estbay ybay imhay, 
ecausebay, etherwhay ehay asway oodgay, adbay, orway indifferentway, ehay asway ethay Ordlay's, 
andway othingnay atthay asway ethay Ordlay's asway away ingthay otay ebay eglectednay. Ethay 
Elshmanway aidsay Uckhay adhay oodgay otsspay inway imhay, andway ethay idowway aidsay: 

"Youway ancay ependday onway itway. Atthay's ethay Ordlay's arkmay. Ehay onday't eavelay itway offway. 
Ehay evernay oesday. Utspay itway omewheresay onway everyway eaturecray atthay omescay omfray ishay 
andshay." 

Earlyway inway ethay orenoonfay artiespay ofway adedjay enmay eganbay otay agglestray intoway ethay 
illagevay, utbay ethay ongeststray ofway ethay itizenscay ontinuedcay earchingsay. Allway ethay 
ewsnay atthay ouldcay ebay ainedgay asway atthay emotenessesray ofway ethay averncay ereway eingbay 
ansackedray atthay adhay evernay eenbay isitedvay eforebay; atthay everyway ornercay andway 
evicecray asway oinggay otay ebay oroughlythay earchedsay; atthay ereverwhay oneway anderedway 
oughthray ethay azemay ofway assagespay, ightslay ereway otay ebay eensay ittingflay itherhay 
andway itherthay inway ethay istanceday, andway outingsshay andway istolpay-shots entsay eirthay 
ollowhay everberationsray otay ethay earway ownday ethay ombresay aislesway. Inway oneway aceplay, 
arfay omfray ethay ectionsay usuallyway aversedtray ybay ouriststay, ethay amesnay "ECKYBAY & 
OMTAY" adhay eenbay oundfay acedtray uponway ethay ockyray allway ithway andlecay-smoke, andway 
earnay atway andhay away easegray-soiled itbay ofway ibbonray. Mrsay. Atcherthay ecognizedray ethay 
ibbonray andway iedcray overway itway. Eshay aidsay itway asway ethay astlay elicray eshay ouldshay everway 
avehay ofway erhay ildchay; andway atthay onay otherway emorialmay ofway erhay ouldcay everway ebay osay 
eciouspray, ecausebay isthay oneway artedpay atestlay omfray ethay ivinglay odybay eforebay ethay 
awfulway eathday amecay. Omesay aidsay atthay ownay andway enthay, inway ethay avecay, away arfay-away 
eckspay ofway ightlay ouldway immerglay, andway enthay away oriousglay outshay ouldway urstbay 
orthfay andway away orescay ofway enmay ogay oopingtray ownday ethay echoingway aisleway--and enthay away 
ickeningsay isappointmentday alwaysway ollowedfay; ethay ildrenchay ereway otnay erethay; 
itway asway onlyway away earchersay's ightlay. 

Eethray eadfuldray aysday andway ightsnay aggeddray eirthay edioustay ourshay alongway, andway 
ethay illagevay anksay intoway away opelesshay uporstay. Onay oneway adhay earthay orfay anythingway. 
Ethay accidentalway iscoveryday, ustjay ademay, atthay ethay oprietorpray ofway ethay 
Emperancetay Averntay eptkay iquorlay onway ishay emisespray, arcelyscay utteredflay ethay 
ublicpay ulsepay, emendoustray asway ethay actfay asway. Inway away ucidlay intervalway, Uckhay 
eeblyfay edlay upway otay ethay ubjectsay ofway avernstay, andway inallyfay askedway--dimly 
eadingdray ethay orstway--if anythingway adhay eenbay iscoveredday atway ethay Emperancetay 
Averntay incesay ehay adhay eenbay illway. 

"Yesway," aidsay ethay idowway. 

Uckhay artedstay upway inway edbay, ildeyedway: 

"Atwhay? Atwhay asway itway?" 

"Iquorlay!--and ethay aceplay ashay eenbay utshay upway. Ielay ownday, ildchay--what away urntay youway 
idday ivegay emay!" 

"Onlyway elltay emay ustjay oneway ingthay--only ustjay oneway--please! Asway itway Omtay Awyersay 
atthay oundfay itway?" 

Ethay idowway urstbay intoway earstay. "Ushhay, ushhay, ildchay, ushhay! Iway've oldtay youway 
eforebay, youway ustmay _otnay_ alktay. Youway areway eryvay, eryvay icksay!" 

Enthay othingnay utbay iquorlay adhay eenbay oundfay; erethay ouldway avehay eenbay away eatgray 
owwowpay ifway itway adhay eenbay ethay oldgay. Osay ethay easuretray asway onegay oreverfay--gone 
oreverfay! Utbay atwhay ouldcay eshay ebay yingcray aboutway? Uriouscay atthay eshay ouldshay 
ycray. 

Esethay oughtsthay orkedway eirthay imday ayway oughthray Uckhay's indmay, andway underway ethay 
earinessway eythay avegay imhay ehay ellfay asleepway. Ethay idowway aidsay otay erselfhay: 

"Erethay--he's asleepway, oorpay eckwray. Omtay Awyersay indfay itway! Itypay utbay omebodysay 
ouldcay indfay Omtay Awyersay! Ahway, erethay ainway't anymay eftlay, ownay, atthay's otgay opehay 
enoughway, orway engthstray enoughway, eitherway, otay ogay onway earchingsay." 




APTERCHAY IXXXAY 

OWNAY otay eturnray otay Omtay andway Eckybay's areshay inway ethay icnicpay. Eythay ippedtray alongway 
ethay urkymay aislesway ithway ethay estray ofway ethay ompanycay, isitingvay ethay amiliarfay 
ondersway ofway ethay avecay--wonders ubbedday ithway atherray overway-descriptive amesnay, 
uchsay asway "Ethay Awingdray-Room," "Ethay Athedralcay," "Aladdinway's Alacepay," andway 
osay onway. Esentlypray ethay idehay-and-seek olickingfray eganbay, andway Omtay andway Eckybay 
engagedway inway itway ithway ealzay untilway ethay exertionway eganbay otay owgray away ifletray 
earisomeway; enthay eythay anderedway ownday away inuoussay avenueway oldinghay eirthay 
andlescay aloftway andway eadingray ethay angledtay ebworkway ofway amesnay, atesday, 
ostofficepay addressesway, andway ottoesmay ithway ichwhay ethay ockyray allsway adhay eenbay 
escoedfray (inway andlecay-smoke). Illstay iftingdray alongway andway alkingtay, eythay 
arcelyscay oticednay atthay eythay ereway ownay inway away artpay ofway ethay avecay osewhay allsway 
ereway otnay escoedfray. Eythay okedsmay eirthay ownway amesnay underway anway overhangingway 
elfshay andway ovedmay onway. Esentlypray eythay amecay otay away aceplay erewhay away ittlelay eamstray 
ofway aterway, icklingtray overway away edgelay andway arryingcay away imestonelay edimentsay ithway 
itway, adhay, inway ethay owslay-dragging agesway, ormedfay away acedlay andway uffledray Iagaranay 
inway eamingglay andway imperishableway onestay. Omtay ueezedsqay ishay allsmay odybay ehindbay 
itway inway orderway otay illuminateway itway orfay Eckybay's atificationgray. Ehay oundfay atthay 
itway urtainedcay away ortsay ofway eepstay aturalnay airwaystay ichwhay asway enclosedway etweenbay 
arrownay allsway, andway atway onceway ethay ambitionway otay ebay away iscovererday eizedsay imhay. 

Eckybay espondedray otay ishay allcay, andway eythay ademay away okesmay-mark orfay uturefay 
uidancegay, andway artedstay uponway eirthay uestqay. Eythay oundway isthay ayway andway atthay, 
arfay ownday intoway ethay ecretsay epthsday ofway ethay avecay, ademay anotherway arkmay, andway 
anchedbray offway inway earchsay ofway oveltiesnay otay elltay ethay upperway orldway aboutway. Inway 
oneway aceplay eythay oundfay away aciousspay averncay, omfray osewhay eilingcay ependedday away 
ultitudemay ofway iningshay alactitesstay ofway ethay engthlay andway ircumferencecay ofway 
away anmay's eglay; eythay alkedway allway aboutway itway, onderingway andway admiringway, andway 
esentlypray eftlay itway ybay oneway ofway ethay umerousnay assagespay atthay openedway intoway 
itway. Isthay ortlyshay oughtbray emthay otay away ewitchingbay ingspray, osewhay asinbay asway 
incrustedway ithway away ostworkfray ofway itteringglay ystalscray; itway asway inway ethay idstmay 
ofway away averncay osewhay allsway ereway upportedsay ybay anymay antasticfay illarspay ichwhay 
adhay eenbay ormedfay ybay ethay oiningjay ofway eatgray alactitesstay andway alagmitesstay 
ogethertay, ethay esultray ofway ethay easelesscay aterway-drip ofway enturiescay. Underway ethay 
oofray astvay otsknay ofway atsbay adhay ackedpay emselvesthay ogethertay, ousandsthay inway away 
unchbay; ethay ightslay isturbedday ethay eaturescray andway eythay amecay ockingflay ownday ybay 
undredshay, ueakingsqay andway artingday uriouslyfay atway ethay andlescay. Omtay ewknay eirthay 
aysway andway ethay angerday ofway isthay ortsay ofway onductcay. Ehay eizedsay Eckybay's andhay andway 
urriedhay erhay intoway ethay irstfay orridorcay atthay offeredway; andway onenay ootay oonsay, orfay 
away atbay uckstray Eckybay's ightlay outway ithway itsway ingway ilewhay eshay asway assingpay outway 
ofway ethay averncay. Ethay atsbay asedchay ethay ildrenchay away oodgay istanceday; utbay ethay 
ugitivesfay ungedplay intoway everyway ewnay assagepay atthay offeredway, andway atway astlay otgay 
idray ofway ethay erilouspay ingsthay. Omtay oundfay away ubterraneansay akelay, ortlyshay, 
ichwhay etchedstray itsway imday engthlay awayway untilway itsway apeshay asway ostlay inway ethay 
adowsshay. Ehay antedway otay exploreway itsway ordersbay, utbay oncludedcay atthay itway ouldway 
ebay estbay otay itsay ownday andway estray awhileway, irstfay. Ownay, orfay ethay irstfay imetay, ethay 
eepday illnessstay ofway ethay aceplay aidlay away ammyclay andhay uponway ethay iritsspay ofway ethay 
ildrenchay. Eckybay aidsay: 

"Ywhay, Iway idnday't oticenay, utbay itway eemssay everway osay onglay incesay Iway eardhay anyway ofway 
ethay othersway." 

"Omecay otay inkthay, Eckybay, eway areway awayway ownday elowbay emthay--and Iway onday't owknay owhay 
arfay awayway orthnay, orway outhsay, orway eastway, orway icheverwhay itway isway. Eway ouldncay't earhay 
emthay erehay." 

Eckybay ewgray apprehensiveway. 

"Iway onderway owhay onglay eway've eenbay ownday erehay, Omtay? Eway etterbay artstay ackbay." 

"Yesway, Iway eckonray eway etterbay. Pway'raps eway etterbay." 

"Ancay youway indfay ethay ayway, Omtay? Itway's allway away ixedmay-up ookednesscray otay emay." 

"Iway eckonray Iway ouldcay indfay itway--but enthay ethay atsbay. Ifway eythay utpay ourway andlescay 
outway itway illway ebay anway awfulway ixfay. Etlay's ytray omesay otherway ayway, osay asway otnay otay ogay 
oughthray erethay." 

"Ellway. Utbay Iway opehay eway onway't etgay ostlay. Itway ouldway ebay osay awfulway!" andway ethay irlgay 
udderedshay atway ethay oughtthay ofway ethay eadfuldray ossibilitiespay. 

Eythay artedstay oughthray away orridorcay, andway aversedtray itway inway ilencesay away onglay 
ayway, ancingglay atway eachway ewnay openingway, otay eesay ifway erethay asway anythingway amiliarfay 
aboutway ethay ooklay ofway itway; utbay eythay ereway allway angestray. Everyway imetay Omtay ademay anway 
examinationway, Eckybay ouldway atchway ishay acefay orfay anway encouragingway ignsay, andway ehay 
ouldway aysay eerilychay: 

"Ohway, itway's allway ightray. Isthay ainway't ethay oneway, utbay eway'll omecay otay itway ightray 
awayway!" 

Utbay ehay eltfay esslay andway esslay opefulhay ithway eachway ailurefay, andway esentlypray eganbay 
otay urntay offway intoway ivergingday avenuesway atway eershay andomray, inway esperateday opehay ofway 
indingfay ethay oneway atthay asway antedway. Ehay illstay aidsay itway asway "allway ightray," utbay 
erethay asway uchsay away eadenlay eaddray atway ishay earthay atthay ethay ordsway adhay ostlay eirthay 
ingray andway oundedsay ustjay asway ifway ehay adhay aidsay, "Allway isway ostlay!" Eckybay ungclay otay 
ishay idesay inway anway anguishway ofway earfay, andway iedtray ardhay otay eepkay ackbay ethay earstay, 
utbay eythay ouldway omecay. Atway astlay eshay aidsay: 

"Ohway, Omtay, evernay indmay ethay atsbay, etlay's ogay ackbay atthay ayway! Eway eemsay otay etgay 
orseway andway orseway offway allway ethay imetay." 

"Istenlay!" aidsay ehay. 

Ofoundpray ilencesay; ilencesay osay eepday atthay evenway eirthay eathingsbray ereway 
onspicuouscay inway ethay ushhay. Omtay outedshay. Ethay allcay entway echoingway ownday 
ethay emptyway aislesway andway iedday outway inway ethay istanceday inway away aintfay oundsay atthay 
esembledray away ippleray ofway ockingmay aughterlay. 

"Ohway, onday't oday itway againway, Omtay, itway isway ootay orridhay," aidsay Eckybay. 

"Itway isway orridhay, utbay Iway etterbay, Eckybay; eythay ightmay earhay usway, youway owknay," andway 
ehay outedshay againway. 

Ethay "ightmay" asway evenway away illierchay orrorhay anthay ethay ostlyghay aughterlay, itway osay 
onfessedcay away erishingpay opehay. Ethay ildrenchay oodstay illstay andway istenedlay; utbay 
erethay asway onay esultray. Omtay urnedtay uponway ethay ackbay acktray atway onceway, andway urriedhay 
ishay epsstay. Itway asway utbay away ittlelay ilewhay eforebay away ertaincay indecisionway inway ishay 
annermay evealedray anotherway earfulfay actfay otay Eckybay--he ouldcay otnay indfay ishay ayway 
ackbay! 

"Ohway, Omtay, youway idnday't akemay anyway arksmay!" 

"Eckybay, Iway asway uchsay away oolfay! Uchsay away oolfay! Iway evernay oughtthay eway ightmay antway otay 
omecay ackbay! Onay--I ancay't indfay ethay ayway. Itway's allway ixedmay upway." 

"Omtay, Omtay, eway're ostlay! eway're ostlay! Eway evernay ancay etgay outway ofway isthay awfulway 
aceplay! Ohway, ywhay _idday_ eway everway eavelay ethay othersway!" 

Eshay anksay otay ethay oundgray andway urstbay intoway uchsay away enzyfray ofway yingcray atthay Omtay 
asway appalledway ithway ethay ideaway atthay eshay ightmay ieday, orway oselay erhay easonray. Ehay 
atsay ownday ybay erhay andway utpay ishay armsway aroundway erhay; eshay uriedbay erhay acefay inway 
ishay osombay, eshay ungclay otay imhay, eshay ouredpay outway erhay errorstay, erhay unavailingway 
egretsray, andway ethay arfay echoesway urnedtay emthay allway otay eeringjay aughterlay. Omtay 
eggedbay erhay otay uckplay upway opehay againway, andway eshay aidsay eshay ouldcay otnay. Ehay ellfay 
otay amingblay andway abusingway imselfhay orfay ettinggay erhay intoway isthay iserablemay 
ituationsay; isthay adhay away etterbay effectway. Eshay aidsay eshay ouldway ytray otay opehay 
againway, eshay ouldway etgay upway andway ollowfay ereverwhay ehay ightmay eadlay ifway onlyway ehay 
ouldway otnay alktay ikelay atthay anyway oremay. Orfay ehay asway onay oremay otay ameblay anthay eshay, 
eshay aidsay. 

Osay eythay ovedmay onway againway--aimlessly--simply atway andomray--all eythay ouldcay oday 
asway otay ovemay, eepkay ovingmay. Orfay away ittlelay ilewhay, opehay ademay away owshay ofway 
evivingray--not ithway anyway easonray otay ackbay itway, utbay onlyway ecausebay itway isway itsway 
aturenay otay eviveray enwhay ethay ingspray ashay otnay eenbay akentay outway ofway itway ybay ageway andway 
amiliarityfay ithway ailurefay. 

Ybay-and-by Omtay ooktay Eckybay's andlecay andway ewblay itway outway. Isthay economyway eantmay osay 
uchmay! Ordsway ereway otnay eedednay. Eckybay understoodway, andway erhay opehay iedday againway. 
Eshay ewknay atthay Omtay adhay away olewhay andlecay andway eethray orway ourfay iecespay inway ishay 
ocketspay--yet ehay ustmay economizeway. 

Ybay-and-by, atiguefay eganbay otay assertway itsway aimsclay; ethay ildrenchay iedtray otay aypay 
attentionway, orfay itway asway eadfuldray otay inkthay ofway ittingsay ownday enwhay imetay asway 
owngray otay ebay osay eciouspray, ovingmay, inway omesay irectionday, inway anyway irectionday, 
asway atway eastlay ogresspray andway ightmay earbay uitfray; utbay otay itsay ownday asway otay 
inviteway eathday andway ortenshay itsway ursuitpay. 

Atway astlay Eckybay's ailfray imbslay efusedray otay arrycay erhay artherfay. Eshay atsay ownday. 
Omtay estedray ithway erhay, andway eythay alkedtay ofway omehay, andway ethay iendsfray erethay, 
andway ethay omfortablecay edsbay andway, aboveway allway, ethay ightlay! Eckybay iedcray, andway Omtay 
iedtray otay inkthay ofway omesay ayway ofway omfortingcay erhay, utbay allway ishay encouragementsway 
ereway owngray eadthray-bare ithway useway, andway oundedsay ikelay arcasmssay. Atiguefay orebay 
osay eavilyhay uponway Eckybay atthay eshay owseddray offway otay eepslay. Omtay asway atefulgray. 
Ehay atsay ookinglay intoway erhay awndray acefay andway awsay itway owgray oothsmay andway aturalnay 
underway ethay influenceway ofway easantplay eamsdray; andway ybay-and-by away ilesmay awnedday andway 
estedray erethay. Ethay eacefulpay acefay eflectedray omewhatsay ofway eacepay andway ealinghay 
intoway ishay ownway iritspay, andway ishay oughtsthay anderedway awayway otay ygonebay imestay andway 
eamydray emoriesmay. Ilewhay ehay asway eepday inway ishay usingsmay, Eckybay okeway upway ithway away 
eezybray ittlelay aughlay--but itway asway ickenstray eadday uponway erhay ipslay, andway away oangray 
ollowedfay itway. 

"Ohway, owhay _ouldcay_ Iway eepslay! Iway ishway Iway evernay, evernay adhay akedway! Onay! Onay, Iway 
onday't, Omtay! Onday't ooklay osay! Iway onway't aysay itway againway." 

"Iway'm adglay youway've eptslay, Eckybay; youway'll eelfay estedray, ownay, andway eway'll indfay 
ethay ayway outway." 

"Eway ancay ytray, Omtay; utbay Iway've eensay uchsay away eautifulbay ountrycay inway ymay eamdray. Iway 
eckonray eway areway oinggay erethay." 

"Aybemay otnay, aybemay otnay. Eerchay upway, Eckybay, andway etlay's ogay onway yingtray." 

Eythay oseray upway andway anderedway alongway, andhay inway andhay andway opelesshay. Eythay iedtray 
otay estimateway owhay onglay eythay adhay eenbay inway ethay avecay, utbay allway eythay ewknay asway 
atthay itway eemedsay aysday andway eeksway, andway yetway itway asway ainplay atthay isthay ouldcay otnay 
ebay, orfay eirthay andlescay ereway otnay onegay yetway. Away onglay imetay afterway isthay--they 
ouldcay otnay elltay owhay onglay--Tom aidsay eythay ustmay ogay oftlysay andway istenlay orfay 
ippingdray aterway--they ustmay indfay away ingspray. Eythay oundfay oneway esentlypray, andway 
Omtay aidsay itway asway imetay otay estray againway. Othbay ereway uellycray iredtay, yetway Eckybay 
aidsay eshay oughtthay eshay ouldcay ogay away ittlelay artherfay. Eshay asway urprisedsay otay 
earhay Omtay issentday. Eshay ouldcay otnay understandway itway. Eythay atsay ownday, andway Omtay 
astenedfay ishay andlecay otay ethay allway inway ontfray ofway emthay ithway omesay ayclay. Oughtthay 
asway oonsay usybay; othingnay asway aidsay orfay omesay imetay. Enthay Eckybay okebray ethay 
ilencesay: 

"Omtay, Iway amway osay ungryhay!" 

Omtay ooktay omethingsay outway ofway ishay ocketpay. 

"Oday youway ememberray isthay?" aidsay ehay. 

Eckybay almostway iledsmay. 

"Itway's ourway eddingway-cake, Omtay." 

"Yesway--I ishway itway asway asway igbay asway away arrelbay, orfay itway's allway eway've otgay." 

"Iway avedsay itway omfray ethay icnicpay orfay usway otay eamdray onway, Omtay, ethay ayway ownupgray 
eoplepay oday ithway eddingway-cake--but itway'll ebay ourway--" 

Eshay oppeddray ethay entencesay erewhay itway asway. Omtay ividedday ethay akecay andway Eckybay 
ateway ithway oodgay appetiteway, ilewhay Omtay ibblednay atway ishay oietymay. Erethay asway 
abundanceway ofway oldcay aterway otay inishfay ethay eastfay ithway. Ybay-and-by Eckybay 
uggestedsay atthay eythay ovemay onway againway. Omtay asway ilentsay away omentmay. Enthay ehay 
aidsay: 

"Eckybay, ancay youway earbay itway ifway Iway elltay youway omethingsay?" 

Eckybay's acefay aledpay, utbay eshay oughtthay eshay ouldcay. 

"Ellway, enthay, Eckybay, eway ustmay aystay erehay, erewhay erethay's aterway otay inkdray. 
Atthay ittlelay iecepay isway ourway astlay andlecay!" 

Eckybay avegay ooselay otay earstay andway ailingsway. Omtay idday atwhay ehay ouldcay otay omfortcay 
erhay, utbay ithway ittlelay effectway. Atway engthlay Eckybay aidsay: 

"Omtay!" 

"Ellway, Eckybay?" 

"Eythay'll issmay usway andway unthay orfay usway!" 

"Yesway, eythay illway! Ertainlycay eythay illway!" 

"Aybemay eythay're untinghay orfay usway ownay, Omtay." 

"Ywhay, Iway eckonray aybemay eythay areway. Iway opehay eythay areway." 

"Enwhay ouldway eythay issmay usway, Omtay?" 

"Enwhay eythay etgay ackbay otay ethay oatbay, Iway eckonray." 

"Omtay, itway ightmay ebay arkday enthay--would eythay oticenay eway adnhay't omecay?" 

"Iway onday't owknay. Utbay anywayway, yourway othermay ouldway issmay youway asway oonsay asway eythay 
otgay omehay." 

Away ightenedfray ooklay inway Eckybay's acefay oughtbray Omtay otay ishay ensessay andway ehay awsay 
atthay ehay adhay ademay away underblay. Eckybay asway otnay otay avehay onegay omehay atthay ightnay! 
Ethay ildrenchay ecamebay ilentsay andway oughtfulthay. Inway away omentmay away ewnay urstbay ofway 
iefgray omfray Eckybay owedshay Omtay atthay ethay ingthay inway ishay indmay adhay uckstray ershay 
alsoway--that ethay Abbathsay orningmay ightmay ebay alfhay entspay eforebay Mrsay. Atcherthay 
iscoveredday atthay Eckybay asway otnay atway Mrsay. Arperhay's. 

Ethay ildrenchay astenedfay eirthay eyesway uponway eirthay itbay ofway andlecay andway atchedway itway 
eltmay owlyslay andway itilesslypay awayway; awsay ethay alfhay inchway ofway ickway andstay aloneway 
atway astlay; awsay ethay eeblefay ameflay iseray andway allfay, imbclay ethay inthay olumncay ofway 
okesmay, ingerlay atway itsway optay away omentmay, andway enthay--the orrorhay ofway utterway arknessday 
eignedray! 

Owhay onglay afterwardway itway asway atthay Eckybay amecay otay away owslay onsciousnesscay atthay 
eshay asway yingcray inway Omtay's armsway, eithernay ouldcay elltay. Allway atthay eythay ewknay 
asway, atthay afterway atwhay eemedsay away ightymay etchstray ofway imetay, othbay awokeway outway ofway 
away eadday uporstay ofway eepslay andway esumedray eirthay iseriesmay onceway oremay. Omtay aidsay 
itway ightmay ebay Undaysay, ownay--maybe Ondaymay. Ehay iedtray otay etgay Eckybay otay alktay, utbay 
erhay orrowssay ereway ootay oppressiveway, allway erhay opeshay ereway onegay. Omtay aidsay atthay 
eythay ustmay avehay eenbay issedmay onglay agoway, andway onay oubtday ethay earchsay asway oinggay 
onway. Ehay ouldway outshay andway aybemay omesay oneway ouldway omecay. Ehay iedtray itway; utbay inway 
ethay arknessday ethay istantday echoesway oundedsay osay ideouslyhay atthay ehay iedtray itway onay 
oremay. 

Ethay ourshay astedway awayway, andway ungerhay amecay otay ormenttay ethay aptivescay againway. Away 
ortionpay ofway Omtay's alfhay ofway ethay akecay asway eftlay; eythay ividedday andway ateway itway. Utbay 
eythay eemedsay ungrierhay anthay eforebay. Ethay oorpay orselmay ofway oodfay onlyway ettedwhay 
esireday. 

Ybay-and-by Omtay aidsay: 

"SHAY! Idday youway earhay atthay?" 

Othbay eldhay eirthay eathbray andway istenedlay. Erethay asway away oundsay ikelay ethay 
aintestfay, arfay-off outshay. Instantlyway Omtay answeredway itway, andway eadinglay Eckybay ybay 
ethay andhay, artedstay opinggray ownday ethay orridorcay inway itsway irectionday. Esentlypray 
ehay istenedlay againway; againway ethay oundsay asway eardhay, andway apparentlyway away ittlelay 
earernay. 

"Itway's emthay!" aidsay Omtay; "eythay're omingcay! Omecay alongway, Eckybay--we're allway 
ightray ownay!" 

Ethay oyjay ofway ethay isonerspray asway almostway overwhelmingway. Eirthay eedspay asway owslay, 
oweverhay, ecausebay itfallspay ereway omewhatsay ommoncay, andway adhay otay ebay uardedgay 
againstway. Eythay ortlyshay amecay otay oneway andway adhay otay opstay. Itway ightmay ebay eethray 
eetfay eepday, itway ightmay ebay away undredhay--there asway onay assingpay itway atway anyway ateray. 
Omtay otgay ownday onway ishay eastbray andway eachedray asway arfay ownday asway ehay ouldcay. Onay 
ottombay. Eythay ustmay aystay erethay andway aitway untilway ethay earcherssay amecay. Eythay 
istenedlay; evidentlyway ethay istantday outingsshay ereway owinggray oremay istantday! 
away omentmay orway otway oremay andway eythay adhay onegay altogetherway. Ethay earthay-sinking 
iserymay ofway itway! Omtay oopedwhay untilway ehay asway oarsehay, utbay itway asway ofway onay useway. Ehay 
alkedtay opefullyhay otay Eckybay; utbay anway ageway ofway anxiousway aitingway assedpay andway onay 
oundssay amecay againway. 

Ethay ildrenchay opedgray eirthay ayway ackbay otay ethay ingspray. Ethay earyway imetay aggeddray 
onway; eythay eptslay againway, andway awokeway amishedfay andway oeway-stricken. Omtay elievedbay 
itway ustmay ebay Uesdaytay ybay isthay imetay. 

Ownay anway ideaway uckstray imhay. Erethay ereway omesay idesay assagespay earnay atway andhay. Itway 
ouldway ebay etterbay otay exploreway omesay ofway esethay anthay earbay ethay eightway ofway ethay 
eavyhay imetay inway idlenessway. Ehay ooktay away itekay-line omfray ishay ocketpay, iedtay itway otay 
away ojectionpray, andway ehay andway Eckybay artedstay, Omtay inway ethay eadlay, unwindingway ethay 
inelay asway ehay opedgray alongway. Atway ethay endway ofway entytway epsstay ethay orridorcay endedway 
inway away "umpingjay-off aceplay." Omtay otgay ownday onway ishay eesknay andway eltfay elowbay, 
andway enthay asway arfay aroundway ethay ornercay asway ehay ouldcay eachray ithway ishay andshay 
onvenientlycay; ehay ademay anway effortway otay etchstray yetway away ittlelay artherfay otay ethay 
ightray, andway atway atthay omentmay, otnay entytway yardsway awayway, away umanhay andhay, oldinghay 
away andlecay, appearedway omfray ehindbay away ockray! Omtay iftedlay upway away oriousglay outshay, 
andway instantlyway atthay andhay asway ollowedfay ybay ethay odybay itway elongedbay otay--Injun 
Oejay's! Omtay asway aralyzedpay; ehay ouldcay otnay ovemay. Ehay asway astlyvay atifiedgray ethay 
extnay omentmay, otay eesay ethay "Aniardspay" aketay otay ishay eelshay andway etgay imselfhay outway 
ofway ightsay. Omtay onderedway atthay Oejay adhay otnay ecognizedray ishay oicevay andway omecay
