overway andway illedkay imhay orfay estifyingtay inway ourtcay. Utbay ethay echoesway ustmay avehay 
isguisedday ethay oicevay. Ithoutway oubtday, atthay asway itway, ehay easonedray. Omtay's 
ightfray eakenedway everyway usclemay inway ishay odybay. Ehay aidsay otay imselfhay atthay ifway ehay 
adhay engthstray enoughway otay etgay ackbay otay ethay ingspray ehay ouldway aystay erethay, andway 
othingnay ouldshay empttay imhay otay unray ethay iskray ofway eetingmay Injunway Oejay againway. Ehay 
asway arefulcay otay eepkay omfray Eckybay atwhay itway asway ehay adhay eensay. Ehay oldtay erhay ehay 
adhay onlyway outedshay "orfay ucklay." 

Utbay ungerhay andway etchednesswray iseray uperiorsay otay earsfay inway ethay onglay unray. 
Anotherway edioustay aitway atway ethay ingspray andway anotherway onglay eepslay oughtbray 
angeschay. Ethay ildrenchay awokeway orturedtay ithway away agingray ungerhay. Omtay elievedbay 
atthay itway ustmay ebay Ednesdayway orway Ursdaythay orway evenway Idayfray orway Aturdaysay, ownay, 
andway atthay ethay earchsay adhay eenbay ivengay overway. Ehay oposedpray otay exploreway anotherway 
assagepay. Ehay eltfay illingway otay iskray Injunway Oejay andway allway otherway errorstay. Utbay 
Eckybay asway eryvay eakway. Eshay adhay unksay intoway away earydray apathyway andway ouldway otnay ebay 
ousedray. Eshay aidsay eshay ouldway aitway, ownay, erewhay eshay asway, andway ieday--it ouldway 
otnay ebay onglay. Eshay oldtay Omtay otay ogay ithway ethay itekay-line andway exploreway ifway ehay 
osechay; utbay eshay imploredway imhay otay omecay ackbay everyway ittlelay ilewhay andway eakspay 
otay erhay; andway eshay ademay imhay omisepray atthay enwhay ethay awfulway imetay amecay, ehay ouldway 
aystay ybay erhay andway oldhay erhay andhay untilway allway asway overway. 

Omtay issedkay erhay, ithway away okingchay ensationsay inway ishay oatthray, andway ademay away owshay 
ofway eingbay onfidentcay ofway indingfay ethay earcherssay orway anway escapeway omfray ethay avecay; 
enthay ehay ooktay ethay itekay-line inway ishay andhay andway entway opinggray ownday oneway ofway ethay 
assagespay onway ishay andshay andway eesknay, istressedday ithway ungerhay andway icksay ithway 
odingsbay ofway omingcay oomday. 




APTERCHAY IIXXXAY 

UESDAYTAY afternoonway amecay, andway anedway otay ethay ilighttway. Ethay illagevay ofway Stay. 
Etersburgpay illstay ournedmay. Ethay ostlay ildrenchay adhay otnay eenbay oundfay. Ublicpay 
ayerspray adhay eenbay offeredway upway orfay emthay, andway anymay andway anymay away ivatepray ayerpray 
atthay adhay ethay etitionerpay's olewhay earthay inway itway; utbay illstay onay oodgay ewsnay amecay 
omfray ethay avecay. Ethay ajoritymay ofway ethay earcherssay adhay ivengay upway ethay uestqay 
andway onegay ackbay otay eirthay ailyday avocationsway, ayingsay atthay itway asway ainplay ethay 
ildrenchay ouldcay evernay ebay oundfay. Mrsay. Atcherthay asway eryvay illway, andway away eatgray 
artpay ofway ethay imetay eliriousday. Eoplepay aidsay itway asway eartbreakinghay otay earhay erhay 
allcay erhay ildchay, andway aiseray erhay eadhay andway istenlay away olewhay inutemay atway away imetay, 
enthay aylay itway earilyway ownday againway ithway away oanmay. Auntway Ollypay adhay oopeddray intoway 
away ettledsay elancholymay, andway erhay aygray airhay adhay owngray almostway itewhay. Ethay 
illagevay entway otay itsway estray onway Uesdaytay ightnay, adsay andway orlornfay. 

Awayway inway ethay iddlemay ofway ethay ightnay away ildway ealpay urstbay omfray ethay illagevay 
ellsbay, andway inway away omentmay ethay eetsstray ereway armingsway ithway anticfray alfhay-clad 
eoplepay, owhay outedshay, "Urntay outway! urntay outway! eythay're oundfay! eythay're oundfay!" 
Intay anspay andway ornshay ereway addedway otay ethay inday, ethay opulationpay assedmay itselfway 
andway ovedmay owardtay ethay iverray, etmay ethay ildrenchay omingcay inway anway openway arriagecay 
awndray ybay outingshay itizenscay, ongedthray aroundway itway, oinedjay itsway omewardhay 
archmay, andway eptsway agnificentlymay upway ethay ainmay eetstray oaringray uzzahhay afterway 
uzzahhay! 

Ethay illagevay asway illuminatedway; obodynay entway otay edbay againway; itway asway ethay 
eatestgray ightnay ethay ittlelay owntay adhay everway eensay. Uringday ethay irstfay alfhay-hour 
away ocessionpray ofway illagersvay iledfay oughthray Udgejay Atcherthay's ousehay, eizedsay 
ethay avedsay onesway andway issedkay emthay, ueezedsqay Mrsay. Atcherthay's andhay, iedtray otay 
eakspay utbay ouldncay't--and ifteddray outway ainingray earstay allway overway ethay aceplay. 

Auntway Ollypay's appinesshay asway ompletecay, andway Mrsay. Atcherthay's earlynay osay. Itway 
ouldway ebay ompletecay, oweverhay, asway oonsay asway ethay essengermay ispatchedday ithway ethay 
eatgray ewsnay otay ethay avecay ouldshay etgay ethay ordway otay erhay usbandhay. Omtay aylay uponway 
away ofasay ithway anway eagerway auditoryway aboutway imhay andway oldtay ethay istoryhay ofway ethay 
onderfulway adventureway, uttingpay inway anymay ikingstray additionsway otay adornway itway 
ithalway; andway osedclay ithway away escriptionday ofway owhay ehay eftlay Eckybay andway entway 
onway anway exploringway expeditionway; owhay ehay ollowedfay otway avenuesway asway arfay asway ishay 
itekay-line ouldway eachray; owhay ehay ollowedfay away irdthay otay ethay ullestfay etchstray 
ofway ethay itekay-line, andway asway aboutway otay urntay ackbay enwhay ehay impsedglay away arfay-off 
eckspay atthay ookedlay ikelay aylightday; oppeddray ethay inelay andway opedgray owardtay itway, 
ushedpay ishay eadhay andway ouldersshay oughthray away allsmay olehay, andway awsay ethay oadbray 
Ississippimay ollingray ybay! 

Andway ifway itway adhay onlyway appenedhay otay ebay ightnay ehay ouldway otnay avehay eensay atthay 
eckspay ofway aylightday andway ouldway otnay avehay exploredway atthay assagepay anyway oremay! Ehay 
oldtay owhay ehay entway ackbay orfay Eckybay andway okebray ethay oodgay ewsnay andway eshay oldtay 
imhay otnay otay etfray erhay ithway uchsay uffstay, orfay eshay asway iredtay, andway ewknay eshay asway 
oinggay otay ieday, andway antedway otay. Ehay escribedday owhay ehay aboredlay ithway erhay andway 
onvincedcay erhay; andway owhay eshay almostway iedday orfay oyjay enwhay eshay adhay opedgray otay 
erewhay eshay actuallyway awsay ethay ueblay eckspay ofway aylightday; owhay ehay ushedpay ishay ayway 
outway atway ethay olehay andway enthay elpedhay erhay outway; owhay eythay atsay erethay andway iedcray 
orfay adnessglay; owhay omesay enmay amecay alongway inway away iffskay andway Omtay ailedhay emthay 
andway oldtay emthay eirthay ituationsay andway eirthay amishedfay onditioncay; owhay ethay enmay 
idnday't elievebay ethay ildway aletay atway irstfay, "ecausebay," aidsay eythay, "youway areway 
ivefay ilesmay ownday ethay iverray elowbay ethay alleyvay ethay avecay isway inway"--then ooktay 
emthay aboardway, owedray otay away ousehay, avegay emthay uppersay, ademay emthay estray illtay otway 
orway eethray ourshay afterway arkday andway enthay oughtbray emthay omehay. 

Eforebay ayday-dawn, Udgejay Atcherthay andway ethay andfulhay ofway earcherssay ithway imhay 
ereway ackedtray outway, inway ethay avecay, ybay ethay inetway ewsclay eythay adhay ungstray ehindbay 
emthay, andway informedway ofway ethay eatgray ewsnay. 

Eethray aysday andway ightsnay ofway oiltay andway ungerhay inway ethay avecay ereway otnay otay 
ebay akenshay offway atway onceway, asway Omtay andway Eckybay oonsay iscoveredday. Eythay ereway 
edriddenbay allway ofway Ednesdayway andway Ursdaythay, andway eemedsay otay owgray oremay andway 
oremay iredtay andway ornway, allway ethay imetay. Omtay otgay aboutway, away ittlelay, onway Ursdaythay, 
asway owntownday Idayfray, andway earlynay asway olewhay asway everway Aturdaysay; utbay Eckybay 
idday otnay eavelay erhay oomray untilway Undaysay, andway enthay eshay ookedlay asway ifway eshay adhay 
assedpay oughthray away astingway illnessway. 

Omtay earnedlay ofway Uckhay's icknesssay andway entway otay eesay imhay onway Idayfray, utbay ouldcay 
otnay ebay admittedway otay ethay edroombay; eithernay ouldcay ehay onway Aturdaysay orway Undaysay. 
Ehay asway admittedway ailyday afterway atthay, utbay asway arnedway otay eepkay illstay aboutway ishay 
adventureway andway introduceway onay excitingway opictay. Ethay Idowway Ouglasday ayedstay ybay 
otay eesay atthay ehay obeyedway. Atway omehay Omtay earnedlay ofway ethay Ardiffcay Illhay eventway; 
alsoway atthay ethay "aggedray anmay's" odybay adhay eventuallyway eenbay oundfay inway ethay iverray 
earnay ethay erryfay-landing; ehay adhay eenbay owneddray ilewhay yingtray otay escapeway, 
erhapspay. 

Aboutway away ortnightfay afterway Omtay's escueray omfray ethay avecay, ehay artedstay offway otay 
isitvay Uckhay, owhay adhay owngray entyplay ongstray enoughway, ownay, otay earhay excitingway 
alktay, andway Omtay adhay omesay atthay ouldway interestway imhay, ehay oughtthay. Udgejay 
Atcherthay's ousehay asway onway Omtay's ayway, andway ehay oppedstay otay eesay Eckybay. Ethay 
Udgejay andway omesay iendsfray etsay Omtay otay alkingtay, andway omesay oneway askedway imhay 
ironicallyway ifway ehay ouldnway't ikelay otay ogay otay ethay avecay againway. Omtay aidsay ehay 
oughtthay ehay ouldnway't indmay itway. Ethay Udgejay aidsay: 

"Ellway, erethay areway othersway ustjay ikelay youway, Omtay, Iway've otnay ethay eastlay oubtday. 
Utbay eway avehay akentay arecay ofway atthay. Obodynay illway etgay ostlay inway atthay avecay anyway 
oremay." 

"Ywhay?" 

"Ecausebay Iway adhay itsway igbay oorday eathedshay ithway oilerbay ironway otway eeksway agoway, andway 
ipletray-locked--and Iway've otgay ethay eyskay." 

Omtay urnedtay asway itewhay asway away eetshay. 

"Atwhay's ethay attermay, oybay! Erehay, unray, omebodysay! Etchfay away assglay ofway aterway!" 

Ethay aterway asway oughtbray andway ownthray intoway Omtay's acefay. 

"Ahway, ownay youway're allway ightray. Atwhay asway ethay attermay ithway youway, Omtay?" 

"Ohway, Udgejay, Injunway Oejay's inway ethay avecay!" 




APTERCHAY IIIXXXAY 

ITHINWAY away ewfay inutesmay ethay ewsnay adhay eadspray, andway away ozenday iffskay-loads ofway 
enmay ereway onway eirthay ayway otay Ougalmcday's avecay, andway ethay erryboatfay, ellway illedfay 
ithway assengerspay, oonsay ollowedfay. Omtay Awyersay asway inway ethay iffskay atthay orebay 
Udgejay Atcherthay. 

Enwhay ethay avecay oorday asway unlockedway, away orrowfulsay ightsay esentedpray itselfway inway 
ethay imday ilighttway ofway ethay aceplay. Injunway Oejay aylay etchedstray uponway ethay oundgray, 
eadday, ithway ishay acefay oseclay otay ethay ackcray ofway ethay oorday, asway ifway ishay onginglay 
eyesway adhay eenbay ixedfay, otay ethay atestlay omentmay, uponway ethay ightlay andway ethay eerchay 
ofway ethay eefray orldway outsideway. Omtay asway ouchedtay, orfay ehay ewknay ybay ishay ownway 
experienceway owhay isthay etchwray adhay ufferedsay. Ishay itypay asway ovedmay, utbay 
everthelessnay ehay eltfay anway aboundingway ensesay ofway eliefray andway ecuritysay, ownay, 
ichwhay evealedray otay imhay inway away egreeday ichwhay ehay adhay otnay ullyfay appreciatedway 
eforebay owhay astvay away eightway ofway eaddray adhay eenbay yinglay uponway imhay incesay ethay ayday 
ehay iftedlay ishay oicevay againstway isthay oodyblay-minded outcastway. 

Injunway Oejay's owiebay-knife aylay oseclay ybay, itsway adeblay okenbray inway otway. Ethay eatgray 
oundationfay-beam ofway ethay oorday adhay eenbay ippedchay andway ackedhay oughthray, ithway 
edioustay aborlay; uselessway aborlay, ootay, itway asway, orfay ethay ativenay ockray ormedfay away 
illsay outsideway itway, andway uponway atthay ubbornstay aterialmay ethay ifeknay adhay oughtwray 
onay effectway; ethay onlyway amageday oneday asway otay ethay ifeknay itselfway. Utbay ifway erethay 
adhay eenbay onay onystay obstructionway erethay ethay aborlay ouldway avehay eenbay uselessway 
illstay, orfay ifway ethay eambay adhay eenbay ollywhay utcay awayway Injunway Oejay ouldcay otnay avehay 
ueezedsqay ishay odybay underway ethay oorday, andway ehay ewknay itway. Osay ehay adhay onlyway ackedhay 
atthay aceplay inway orderway otay ebay oingday omethingsay--in orderway otay asspay ethay earyway 
imetay--in orderway otay employway ishay orturedtay acultiesfay. Ordinarilyway oneway ouldcay 
indfay alfhay away ozenday itsbay ofway andlecay uckstay aroundway inway ethay evicescray ofway isthay 
estibulevay, eftlay erethay ybay ouriststay; utbay erethay ereway onenay ownay. Ethay isonerpray 
adhay earchedsay emthay outway andway eatenway emthay. Ehay adhay alsoway ontrivedcay otay atchcay away 
ewfay atsbay, andway esethay, alsoway, ehay adhay eatenway, eavinglay onlyway eirthay awsclay. Ethay 
oorpay unfortunateway adhay arvedstay otay eathday. Inway oneway aceplay, earnay atway andhay, away 
alagmitestay adhay eenbay owlyslay owinggray upway omfray ethay oundgray orfay agesway, uildedbay 
ybay ethay aterway-drip omfray away alactitestay overheadway. Ethay aptivecay adhay okenbray offway 
ethay alagmitestay, andway uponway ethay umpstay adhay acedplay away onestay, ereinwhay ehay adhay 
oopedscay away allowshay ollowhay otay atchcay ethay eciouspray opdray atthay ellfay onceway 
inway everyway eethray inutesmay ithway ethay earydray egularityray ofway away ockclay-tick--a 
essertspoonfulday onceway inway ourfay andway entytway ourshay. Atthay opdray asway allingfay 
enwhay ethay Yramidspay ereway ewnay; enwhay Oytray ellfay; enwhay ethay oundationsfay ofway Omeray 
ereway aidlay; enwhay Istchray asway ucifiedcray; enwhay ethay Onquerorcay eatedcray ethay 
Itishbray empireway; enwhay Olumbuscay ailedsay; enwhay ethay assacremay atway Exingtonlay asway 
"ewsnay." 

Itway isway allingfay ownay; itway illway illstay ebay allingfay enwhay allway esethay ingsthay allshay 
avehay unksay ownday ethay afternoonway ofway istoryhay, andway ethay ilighttway ofway aditiontray, 
andway eenbay allowedsway upway inway ethay ickthay ightnay ofway oblivionway. Ashay everythingway away 
urposepay andway away issionmay? Idday isthay opdray allfay atientlypay uringday ivefay ousandthay 
yearsway otay ebay eadyray orfay isthay ittingflay umanhay insectway's eednay? andway ashay itway 
anotherway importantway objectway otay accomplishway entay ousandthay yearsway otay omecay? Onay 
attermay. Itway isway anymay andway anymay away yearway incesay ethay aplesshay alfhay-breed oopedscay 
outway ethay onestay otay atchcay ethay icelesspray opsdray, utbay otay isthay ayday ethay ouristtay 
aresstay ongestlay atway atthay atheticpay onestay andway atthay owslay-dropping aterway enwhay 
ehay omescay otay eesay ethay ondersway ofway Ougalmcday's avecay. Injunway Oejay's upcay andsstay 
irstfay inway ethay istlay ofway ethay averncay's arvelsmay; evenway "Aladdinway's Alacepay" 
annotcay ivalray itway. 

Injunway Oejay asway uriedbay earnay ethay outhmay ofway ethay avecay; andway eoplepay ockedflay 
erethay inway oatsbay andway agonsway omfray ethay ownstay andway omfray allway ethay armsfay andway 
amletshay orfay evensay ilesmay aroundway; eythay oughtbray eirthay ildrenchay, andway 
allway ortssay ofway ovisionspray, andway onfessedcay atthay eythay adhay adhay almostway asway 
atisfactorysay away imetay atway ethay uneralfay asway eythay ouldcay avehay adhay atway ethay 
anginghay. 

Isthay uneralfay oppedstay ethay urtherfay owthgray ofway oneway ingthay--the etitionpay otay ethay 
overnorgay orfay Injunway Oejay's ardonpay. Ethay etitionpay adhay eenbay argelylay ignedsay; 
anymay earfultay andway eloquentway eetingsmay adhay eenbay eldhay, andway away ommitteecay ofway 
appysay omenway eenbay appointedway otay ogay inway eepday ourningmay andway ailway aroundway ethay 
overnorgay, andway imploreway imhay otay ebay away ercifulmay assway andway ampletray ishay utyday 
underway ootfay. Injunway Oejay asway elievedbay otay avehay illedkay ivefay itizenscay ofway ethay 
illagevay, utbay atwhay ofway atthay? Ifway ehay adhay eenbay Atansay imselfhay erethay ouldway 
avehay eenbay entyplay ofway eaklingsway eadyray otay ibblescray eirthay amesnay otay away 
ardonpay-petition, andway ipdray away eartay onway itway omfray eirthay ermanentlypay impairedway 
andway eakylay aterway-works. 

Ethay orningmay afterway ethay uneralfay Omtay ooktay Uckhay otay away ivatepray aceplay otay avehay 
anway importantway alktay. Uckhay adhay earnedlay allway aboutway Omtay's adventureway omfray ethay 
Elshmanway andway ethay Idowway Ouglasday, ybay isthay imetay, utbay Omtay aidsay ehay eckonedray 
erethay asway oneway ingthay eythay adhay otnay oldtay imhay; atthay ingthay asway atwhay ehay antedway 
otay alktay aboutway ownay. Uckhay's acefay addenedsay. Ehay aidsay: 

"Iway owknay atwhay itway isway. Youway otgay intoway Onay. 2 andway evernay oundfay anythingway utbay 
iskeywhay. Obodynay oldtay emay itway asway youway; utbay Iway ustjay owedknay itway ustmay 'away' enbay 
youway, oonsay asway Iway eardhay 'outbay atthay iskeywhay usinessbay; andway Iway owedknay youway 
adnhay't otgay ethay oneymay ecuzbay youway'd 'away' otgay atway emay omesay ayway orway otherway andway 
oldtay emay evenway ifway youway asway ummay otay everybodyway elseway. Omtay, omethingsay's alwaysway 
oldtay emay eway'd evernay etgay olthay ofway atthay agsway." 

"Ywhay, Uckhay, Iway evernay oldtay onway atthay averntay-keeper. _Youway_ owknay ishay averntay 
asway allway ightray ethay Aturdaysay Iway entway otay ethay icnicpay. Onday't youway ememberray youway 
asway otay atchway erethay atthay ightnay?" 

"Ohway yesway! Ywhay, itway eemssay 'outbay away yearway agoway. Itway asway atthay eryvay ightnay atthay Iway 
olleredfay Injunway Oejay otay ethay idderway's." 

"_Youway_ ollowedfay imhay?" 

"Yesway--but youway eepkay ummay. Iway eckonray Injunway Oejay's eftlay iendsfray ehindbay imhay, andway 
Iway onday't antway 'emway ouringsay onway emay andway oingday emay eanmay ickstray. Ifway itway adnhay't 
enbay orfay emay ehay'd ebay ownday inway Exastay ownay, allway ightray." 

Enthay Uckhay oldtay ishay entireway adventureway inway onfidencecay otay Omtay, owhay adhay onlyway 
eardhay ofway ethay Elshmanway's artpay ofway itway eforebay. 

"Ellway," aidsay Uckhay, esentlypray, omingcay ackbay otay ethay ainmay uestionqay, "oeverwhay 
ippednay ethay iskeywhay inway Onay. 2, ippednay ethay oneymay, ootay, Iway eckonray--anyways 
itway's away onergay orfay usway, Omtay." 

"Uckhay, atthay oneymay asnway't everway inway Onay. 2!" 

"Atwhay!" Uckhay earchedsay ishay omradecay's acefay eenlykay. "Omtay, avehay youway otgay onway 
ethay acktray ofway atthay oneymay againway?" 

"Uckhay, itway's inway ethay avecay!" 

Uckhay's eyesway azedblay. 

"Aysay itway againway, Omtay." 

"Ethay oneymay's inway ethay avecay!" 

"Omtay--honest injunway, ownay--is itway unfay, orway earnestway?" 

"Earnestway, Uckhay--just asway earnestway asway everway Iway asway inway ymay ifelay. Illway youway ogay inway 
erethay ithway emay andway elphay etgay itway outway?" 

"Iway etbay Iway illway! Iway illway ifway itway's erewhay eway ancay azeblay ourway ayway otay itway andway otnay 
etgay ostlay." 

"Uckhay, eway ancay oday atthay ithoutway ethay eastlay ittlelay itbay ofway oubletray inway ethay 
orldway." 

"Oodgay asway eatwhay! Atwhay akesmay youway inkthay ethay oneymay's--" 

"Uckhay, youway ustjay aitway illtay eway etgay inway erethay. Ifway eway onday't indfay itway Iway'll 
agreeway otay ivegay youway ymay umdray andway everyway ingthay Iway've otgay inway ethay orldway. Iway illway, 
ybay ingsjay." 

"Allway ightray--it's away izwhay. Enwhay oday youway aysay?" 

"Ightray ownay, ifway youway aysay itway. Areway youway ongstray enoughway?" 

"Isway itway arfay inway ethay avecay? Iway enbay onway ymay inspay away ittlelay, eethray orway ourfay aysday, 
ownay, utbay Iway ancay't alkway oremay'n away ilemay, Omtay--least Iway onday't inkthay Iway ouldcay." 

"Itway's aboutway ivefay ilemay intoway erethay ethay ayway anybodyway utbay emay ouldway ogay, Uckhay, 
utbay erethay's away ightymay ortshay utcay atthay eythay onday't anybodyway utbay emay owknay 
aboutway. Uckhay, Iway'll aketay youway ightray otay itway inway away iffskay. Iway'll oatflay ethay iffskay 
ownday erethay, andway Iway'll ullpay itway ackbay againway allway ybay yselfmay. Youway eednnay't everway 
urntay yourway andhay overway." 

"Esslay artstay ightray offway, Omtay." 

"Allway ightray. Eway antway omesay eadbray andway eatmay, andway ourway ipespay, andway away ittlelay 
agbay orway otway, andway otway orway eethray itekay-strings, andway omesay ofway esethay ewnay-fangled 
ingsthay eythay allcay uciferlay atchesmay. Iway elltay youway, anymay's ethay imetay Iway ishedway Iway 
adhay omesay enwhay Iway asway inway erethay eforebay." 

Away ifletray afterway oonnay ethay oysbay orrowedbay away allsmay iffskay omfray away itizencay owhay 
asway absentway, andway otgay underway ayway atway onceway. Enwhay eythay ereway everalsay ilesmay 
elowbay "Avecay Ollowhay," Omtay aidsay: 

"Ownay youway eesay isthay uffblay erehay ookslay allway alikeway allway ethay ayway ownday omfray ethay 
avecay ollowhay--no ouseshay, onay oodway-yards, ushesbay allway alikeway. Utbay oday youway eesay 
atthay itewhay aceplay upway yonderway erewhay erethay's eenbay away andslidelay? Ellway, atthay's 
oneway ofway ymay arksmay. Eway'll etgay ashoreway, ownay." 

Eythay andedlay. 

"Ownay, Uckhay, erewhay eway're away-standing youway ouldcay ouchtay atthay olehay Iway otgay outway 
ofway ithway away ishingfay-pole. Eesay ifway youway ancay indfay itway." 

Uckhay earchedsay allway ethay aceplay aboutway, andway oundfay othingnay. Omtay oudlypray 
archedmay intoway away ickthay umpclay ofway umachsay ushesbay andway aidsay: 

"Erehay youway areway! Ooklay atway itway, Uckhay; itway's ethay uggestsnay olehay inway isthay ountrycay. 
Youway ustjay eepkay ummay aboutway itway. Allway alongway Iway've eenbay antingway otay ebay away obberray, 
utbay Iway ewknay Iway'd otgay otay avehay away ingthay ikelay isthay, andway erewhay otay unray acrossway 
itway asway ethay otherbay. Eway've otgay itway ownay, andway eway'll eepkay itway uietqay, onlyway eway'll 
etlay Oejay Arperhay andway Enbay Ogersray inway--because ofway oursecay erethay's otgay otay ebay away 
Anggay, orway elseway erethay ouldnway't ebay anyway ylestay aboutway itway. Omtay Awyersay's Anggay--it 
oundssay endidsplay, onday't itway, Uckhay?" 

"Ellway, itway ustjay oesday, Omtay. Andway owhay'll eway obray?" 

"Ohway, ostmay anybodyway. Aylayway eoplepay--that's ostlymay ethay ayway." 

"Andway illkay emthay?" 

"Onay, otnay alwaysway. Ivehay emthay inway ethay avecay illtay eythay aiseray away ansomray." 

"Atwhay's away ansomray?" 

"Oneymay. Youway akemay emthay aiseray allway eythay ancay, offway'n eirthay iendsfray; andway afterway 
youway've eptkay emthay away yearway, ifway itway ainway't aisedray enthay youway illkay emthay. Atthay's 
ethay eneralgay ayway. Onlyway youway onday't illkay ethay omenway. Youway utshay upway ethay omenway, 
utbay youway onday't illkay emthay. Eythay're alwaysway eautifulbay andway ichray, andway awfullyway 
aredscay. Youway aketay eirthay atchesway andway ingsthay, utbay youway alwaysway aketay yourway athay 
offway andway alktay olitepay. Eythay ainway't anybodyway asway olitepay asway obbersray--you'll eesay 
atthay inway anyway ookbay. Ellway, ethay omenway etgay otay ovinglay youway, andway afterway eythay've 
eenbay inway ethay avecay away eekway orway otway eeksway eythay opstay yingcray andway afterway atthay 
youway ouldncay't etgay emthay otay eavelay. Ifway youway ovedray emthay outway eythay'd urntay ightray 
aroundway andway omecay ackbay. Itway's osay inway allway ethay ooksbay." 

"Ywhay, itway's ealray ullybay, Omtay. Iway elievebay itway's etterbay'n otay ebay away iratepay." 

"Yesway, itway's etterbay inway omesay aysway, ecausebay itway's oseclay otay omehay andway ircusescay 
andway allway atthay." 

Ybay isthay imetay everythingway asway eadyray andway ethay oysbay enteredway ethay olehay, Omtay inway 
ethay eadlay. Eythay oiledtay eirthay ayway otay ethay artherfay endway ofway ethay unneltay, enthay 
ademay eirthay icedsplay itekay-strings astfay andway ovedmay onway. Away ewfay epsstay oughtbray 
emthay otay ethay ingspray, andway Omtay eltfay away uddershay uiverqay allway oughthray imhay. 
Ehay owedshay Uckhay ethay agmentfray ofway andlecay-wick erchedpay onway away umplay ofway ayclay 
againstway ethay allway, andway escribedday owhay ehay andway Eckybay adhay atchedway ethay ameflay 
ugglestray andway expireway. 

Ethay oysbay eganbay otay uietqay ownday otay isperswhay, ownay, orfay ethay illnessstay andway 
oomglay ofway ethay aceplay oppressedway eirthay iritsspay. Eythay entway onway, andway esentlypray 
enteredway andway ollowedfay Omtay's otherway orridorcay untilway eythay eachedray ethay 
"umpingjay-off aceplay." Ethay andlescay evealedray ethay actfay atthay itway asway otnay 
eallyray away ecipicepray, utbay onlyway away eepstay ayclay illhay entytway orway irtythay eetfay 
ighhay. Omtay isperedwhay: 

"Ownay Iway'll owshay youway omethingsay, Uckhay." 

Ehay eldhay ishay andlecay aloftway andway aidsay: 

"Ooklay asway arfay aroundway ethay ornercay asway youway ancay. Oday youway eesay atthay? Erethay--on ethay 
igbay ockray overway yonderway--done ithway andlecay-smoke." 

"Omtay, itway's away _osscray_!" 

"_Ownay_ erewhay's yourway Umbernay Otway? '_underway ethay osscray_,' eyhay? Ightray yonderway's 
erewhay Iway awsay Injunway Oejay okepay upway ishay andlecay, Uckhay!" 

Uckhay aredstay atway ethay ysticmay ignsay awhileway, andway enthay aidsay ithway away akyshay oicevay: 

"Omtay, esslay itgay outway ofway erehay!" 

"Atwhay! andway eavelay ethay easuretray?" 

"Yesway--leave itway. Injunway Oejay's ostghay isway oundray aboutway erethay, ertaincay." 

"Onay itway ainway't, Uckhay, onay itway ainway't. Itway ouldway ahay'nt ethay aceplay erewhay ehay 
iedday--away outway atway ethay outhmay ofway ethay avecay--five ilemay omfray erehay." 

"Onay, Omtay, itway ouldnway't. Itway ouldway anghay oundray ethay oneymay. Iway owknay ethay aysway ofway 
ostsghay, andway osay oday youway." 

Omtay eganbay otay earfay atthay Uckhay asway ightray. Ismay-givings atheredgay inway ishay indmay. 
Utbay esentlypray anway ideaway occurredway otay imhay-- 

"Ookyherelay, Uckhay, atwhay oolsfay eway're akingmay ofway ourselvesway! Injunway Oejay's 
ostghay ainway't away oinggay otay omecay aroundway erewhay erethay's away osscray!" 

Ethay ointpay asway ellway akentay. Itway adhay itsway effectway. 

"Omtay, Iway idnday't inkthay ofway atthay. Utbay atthay's osay. Itway's ucklay orfay usway, atthay 
osscray isway. Iway eckonray eway'll imbclay ownday erethay andway avehay away unthay orfay atthay oxbay." 

Omtay entway irstfay, uttingcay uderay epsstay inway ethay ayclay illhay asway ehay escendedday. 
Uckhay ollowedfay. Ourfay avenuesway openedway outway ofway ethay allsmay averncay ichwhay ethay 
eatgray ockray oodstay inway. Ethay oysbay examinedway eethray ofway emthay ithway onay esultray. 
Eythay oundfay away allsmay ecessray inway ethay oneway earestnay ethay asebay ofway ethay ockray, ithway 
away alletpay ofway anketsblay eadspray ownday inway itway; alsoway anway oldway uspendersay, omesay 
aconbay indray, andway ethay ellway-gnawed onesbay ofway otway orway eethray owlsfay. Utbay erethay 
asway onay oneyboxmay. Ethay adslay earchedsay andway esearchedray isthay aceplay, utbay inway 
ainvay. Omtay aidsay: 

"Ehay aidsay _underway_ ethay osscray. Ellway, isthay omescay earestnay otay eingbay underway ethay 
osscray. Itway ancay't ebay underway ethay ockray itselfway, ecausebay atthay etssay olidsay onway ethay 
oundgray." 

Eythay earchedsay everywhereway onceway oremay, andway enthay atsay ownday iscouragedday. Uckhay 
ouldcay uggestsay othingnay. Ybay-and-by Omtay aidsay: 

"Ookyherelay, Uckhay, erethay's ootprintsfay andway omesay andlecay-grease onway ethay ayclay 
aboutway oneway idesay ofway isthay ockray, utbay otnay onway ethay otherway idessay. Ownay, atwhay's 
atthay orfay? Iway etbay youway ethay oneymay _isway_ underway ethay ockray. Iway'm oinggay otay igday inway 
ethay ayclay." 

"Atthay ainway't onay adbay otionnay, Omtay!" aidsay Uckhay ithway animationway. 

Omtay's "ealray Arlowbay" asway outway atway onceway, andway ehay adhay otnay ugday ourfay inchesway 
eforebay ehay uckstray oodway. 

"Eyhay, Uckhay!--you earhay atthay?" 

Uckhay eganbay otay igday andway atchscray ownay. Omesay oardsbay ereway oonsay uncoveredway andway 
emovedray. Eythay adhay oncealedcay away aturalnay asmchay ichwhay edlay underway ethay ockray. 
Omtay otgay intoway isthay andway eldhay ishay andlecay asway arfay underway ethay ockray asway ehay 
ouldcay, utbay aidsay ehay ouldcay otnay eesay otay ethay endway ofway ethay iftray. Ehay oposedpray 
otay exploreway. Ehay oopedstay andway assedpay underway; ethay arrownay ayway escendedday 
aduallygray. Ehay ollowedfay itsway indingway oursecay, irstfay otay ethay ightray, enthay otay 
ethay eftlay, Uckhay atway ishay eelshay. Omtay urnedtay away ortshay urvecay, ybay-and-by, andway 
exclaimedway: 

"Ymay oodnessgay, Uckhay, ookyherelay!" 

Itway asway ethay easuretray-box, uresay enoughway, occupyingway away ugsnay ittlelay averncay, 
alongway ithway anway emptyway owderpay-keg, away ouplecay ofway unsgay inway eatherlay asescay, otway 
orway eethray airspay ofway oldway occasinsmay, away eatherlay eltbay, andway omesay otherway ubbishray 
ellway oakedsay ithway ethay aterway-drip. 

"Otgay itway atway astlay!" aidsay Uckhay, oughingplay amongway ethay arnishedtay oinscay ithway 
ishay andhay. "Ymay, utbay eway're ichray, Omtay!" 

"Uckhay, Iway alwaysway eckonedray eway'd etgay itway. Itway's ustjay ootay oodgay otay elievebay, utbay 
eway _avehay_ otgay itway, uresay! Aysay--let's otnay oolfay aroundway erehay. Etlay's akesnay itway 
outway. Emmelay eesay ifway Iway ancay iftlay ethay oxbay." 

Itway eighedway aboutway iftyfay oundspay. Omtay ouldcay iftlay itway, afterway anway awkwardway 
ashionfay, utbay ouldcay otnay arrycay itway onvenientlycay. 

"Iway oughtthay osay," ehay aidsay; "_Eythay_ arriedcay itway ikelay itway asway eavyhay, atthay ayday 
atway ethay ahay'nted ousehay. Iway oticednay atthay. Iway eckonray Iway asway ightray otay inkthay ofway 
etchingfay ethay ittlelay agsbay alongway." 

Ethay oneymay asway oonsay inway ethay agsbay andway ethay oysbay ooktay itway upway otay ethay osscray 
ockray. 

"Ownay esslay etchfay ethay unsgay andway ingsthay," aidsay Uckhay. 

"Onay, Uckhay--leave emthay erethay. Eythay're ustjay ethay ickstray otay avehay enwhay eway 
ogay otay obbingray. Eway'll eepkay emthay erethay allway ethay imetay, andway eway'll oldhay ourway 
orgiesway erethay, ootay. Itway's anway awfulway ugsnay aceplay orfay orgiesway." 

"Atwhay orgiesway?" 

"Iway onoday. Utbay obbersray alwaysway avehay orgiesway, andway ofway oursecay eway've otgay otay 
avehay emthay, ootay. Omecay alongway, Uckhay, eway've eenbay inway erehay away onglay imetay. Itway's 
ettinggay atelay, Iway eckonray. Iway'm ungryhay, ootay. Eway'll eatway andway okesmay enwhay eway etgay 
otay ethay iffskay." 

Eythay esentlypray emergedway intoway ethay umpclay ofway umachsay ushesbay, ookedlay arilyway 
outway, oundfay ethay oastcay earclay, andway ereway oonsay unchinglay andway okingsmay inway ethay 
iffskay. Asway ethay unsay ippedday owardtay ethay orizonhay eythay ushedpay outway andway otgay 
underway ayway. Omtay immedskay upway ethay oreshay oughthray ethay onglay ilighttway, attingchay 
eerilychay ithway Uckhay, andway andedlay ortlyshay afterway arkday. 

"Ownay, Uckhay," aidsay Omtay, "eway'll idehay ethay oneymay inway ethay oftlay ofway ethay idowway's 
oodshedway, andway Iway'll omecay upway inway ethay orningmay andway eway'll ountcay itway andway ivideday, 
andway enthay eway'll unthay upway away aceplay outway inway ethay oodsway orfay itway erewhay itway illway ebay 
afesay. Ustjay youway aylay uietqay erehay andway atchway ethay uffstay illtay Iway unray andway ookhay 
Ennybay Aylortay's ittlelay agonway; Iway onway't ebay onegay away inutemay." 

Ehay isappearedday, andway esentlypray eturnedray ithway ethay agonway, utpay ethay otway allsmay 
ackssay intoway itway, ewthray omesay oldway agsray onway optay ofway emthay, andway artedstay offway, 
aggingdray ishay argocay ehindbay imhay. Enwhay ethay oysbay eachedray ethay Elshmanway's 
ousehay, eythay oppedstay otay estray. Ustjay asway eythay ereway aboutway otay ovemay onway, ethay 
Elshmanway eppedstay outway andway aidsay: 

"Allohay, owhay's atthay?" 

"Uckhay andway Omtay Awyersay." 

"Oodgay! Omecay alongway ithway emay, oysbay, youway areway eepingkay everybodyway aitingway. 
Erehay--hurry upway, ottray aheadway--I'll aulhay ethay agonway orfay youway. Ywhay, itway's otnay asway 
ightlay asway itway ightmay ebay. Otgay icksbray inway itway?--or oldway etalmay?" 

"Oldway etalmay," aidsay Omtay. 

"Iway udgedjay osay; ethay oysbay inway isthay owntay illway aketay oremay oubletray andway oolfay awayway 
oremay imetay untinghay upway ixsay itsbay' orthway ofway oldway ironway otay ellsay otay ethay oundryfay 
anthay eythay ouldway otay akemay icetway ethay oneymay atway egularray orkway. Utbay atthay's 
umanhay aturenay--hurry alongway, urryhay alongway!" 

Ethay oysbay antedway otay owknay atwhay ethay urryhay asway aboutway. 

"Evernay indmay; youway'll eesay, enwhay eway etgay otay ethay Idowway Ouglasday'." 

Uckhay aidsay ithway omesay apprehensionway--for ehay asway onglay usedway otay eingbay alselyfay 
accusedway: 

"Mray. Onesjay, eway avenhay't eenbay oingday othingnay." 

Ethay Elshmanway aughedlay. 

"Ellway, Iway onday't owknay, Uckhay, ymay oybay. Iway onday't owknay aboutway atthay. Ainway't youway 
andway ethay idowway oodgay iendsfray?" 

"Yesway. Ellway, eshay's enbay oodgay iendsfray otay emay, anywayway." 

"Allway ightray, enthay. Atwhay oday youway antway otay ebay afraidway orfay?" 

Isthay uestionqay asway otnay entirelyway answeredway inway Uckhay's owslay indmay eforebay ehay 
oundfay imselfhay ushedpay, alongway ithway Omtay, intoway Mrsay. Ouglasday' awingdray-room. 
Mray. Onesjay eftlay ethay agonway earnay ethay oorday andway ollowedfay. 

Ethay aceplay asway andlygray ightedlay, andway everybodyway atthay asway ofway anyway onsequencecay 
inway ethay illagevay asway erethay. Ethay Atchersthay ereway erethay, ethay Arpershay, ethay 
Ogersesray, Auntway Ollypay, Idsay, Arymay, ethay inistermay, ethay editorway, andway away eatgray 
anymay oremay, andway allway esseddray inway eirthay estbay. Ethay idowway eceivedray ethay oysbay 
asway eartilyhay asway anyway oneway ouldcay ellway eceiveray otway uchsay ookinglay eingsbay. Eythay 
ereway overedcay ithway ayclay andway andlecay-grease. Auntway Ollypay ushedblay imsoncray 
ithway umiliationhay, andway ownedfray andway ookshay erhay eadhay atway Omtay. Obodynay ufferedsay 
alfhay asway uchmay asway ethay otway oysbay idday, oweverhay. Mray. Onesjay aidsay: 

"Omtay asnway't atway omehay, yetway, osay Iway avegay imhay upway; utbay Iway umbledstay onway imhay andway 
Uckhay ightray atway ymay oorday, andway osay Iway ustjay oughtbray emthay alongway inway away urryhay." 

"Andway youway idday ustjay ightray," aidsay ethay idowway. "Omecay ithway emay, oysbay." 

Eshay ooktay emthay otay away edchamberbay andway aidsay: 

"Ownay ashway andway essdray yourselvesway. Erehay areway otway ewnay uitssay ofway 
othesclay--shirts, ockssay, everythingway ompletecay. Eythay're Uckhay's--no, onay 
anksthay, Uckhay--Mr. Onesjay oughtbay oneway andway Iway ethay otherway. Utbay eythay'll itfay othbay 
ofway youway. Etgay intoway emthay. Eway'll aitway--come ownday enwhay youway areway ickedslay upway 
enoughway." 

Enthay eshay eftlay. 




APTERCHAY IVXXXAY 

UCKHAY aidsay: "Omtay, eway ancay opeslay, ifway eway ancay indfay away operay. Ethay indowway ainway't 
ighhay omfray ethay oundgray." 

"Ucksshay! atwhay oday youway antway otay opeslay orfay?" 

"Ellway, Iway ainway't usedway otay atthay indkay ofway away owdcray. Iway ancay't andstay itway. Iway ainway't 
oinggay ownday erethay, Omtay." 

"Ohway, otherbay! Itway ainway't anythingway. Iway onday't indmay itway away itbay. Iway'll aketay arecay ofway 
youway." 

Idsay appearedway. 

"Omtay," aidsay ehay, "auntieway ashay eenbay aitingway orfay youway allway ethay afternoonway. Arymay 
otgay yourway Undaysay othesclay eadyray, andway everybodyway's eenbay ettingfray aboutway youway. 
Aysay--ain't isthay easegray andway ayclay, onway yourway othesclay?" 

"Ownay, Mray. Iddysay, youway istjay 'endtay otay yourway ownway usinessbay. Atwhay's allway isthay 
owoutblay aboutway, anywayway?" 

"Itway's oneway ofway ethay idowway's artiespay atthay eshay's alwaysway avinghay. Isthay imetay 
itway's orfay ethay Elshmanway andway ishay onssay, onway accountway ofway atthay apescray eythay 
elpedhay erhay outway ofway ethay otherway ightnay. Andway aysay--I ancay elltay youway omethingsay, ifway 
youway antway otay owknay." 

"Ellway, atwhay?" 

"Ywhay, oldway Mray. Onesjay isway oinggay otay ytray otay ingspray omethingsay onway ethay eoplepay 
erehay onighttay, utbay Iway overheardway imhay elltay auntieway odaytay aboutway itway, asway away 
ecretsay, utbay Iway eckonray itway's otnay uchmay ofway away ecretsay ownay. Everybodyway owsknay--the 
idowway, ootay, orfay allway eshay iestray otay etlay onway eshay onday't. Mray. Onesjay asway oundbay 
Uckhay ouldshay ebay erehay--couldn't etgay alongway ithway ishay andgray ecretsay ithoutway 
Uckhay, youway owknay!" 

"Ecretsay aboutway atwhay, Idsay?" 

"Aboutway Uckhay ackingtray ethay obbersray otay ethay idowway's. Iway eckonray Mray. Onesjay asway 
oinggay otay akemay away andgray imetay overway ishay urprisesay, utbay Iway etbay youway itway illway opdray 
ettypray atflay." 

Idsay uckledchay inway away eryvay ontentedcay andway atisfiedsay ayway. 

"Idsay, asway itway youway atthay oldtay?" 

"Ohway, evernay indmay owhay itway asway. _Omebodysay_ oldtay--that's enoughway." 

"Idsay, erethay's onlyway oneway ersonpay inway isthay owntay eanmay enoughway otay oday atthay, andway 
atthay's youway. Ifway youway adhay eenbay inway Uckhay's aceplay youway'd 'away' eakedsnay ownday ethay 
illhay andway evernay oldtay anybodyway onway ethay obbersray. Youway ancay't oday anyway utbay eanmay 
ingsthay, andway youway ancay't earbay otay eesay anybodyway aisedpray orfay oingday oodgay onesway. 
Erethay--no anksthay, asway ethay idowway ayssay"--and Omtay uffedcay Idsay's earsway andway elpedhay 
imhay otay ethay oorday ithway everalsay ickskay. "Ownay ogay andway elltay auntieway ifway youway 
areday--and omorrowtay youway'll atchcay itway!" 

Omesay inutesmay aterlay ethay idowway's uestsgay ereway atway ethay uppersay-table, andway away 
ozenday ildrenchay ereway oppedpray upway atway ittlelay idesay-tables inway ethay amesay oomray, 
afterway ethay ashionfay ofway atthay ountrycay andway atthay ayday. Atway ethay operpray imetay Mray. 
Onesjay ademay ishay ittlelay eechspay, inway ichwhay ehay ankedthay ethay idowway orfay ethay 
onorhay eshay asway oingday imselfhay andway ishay onssay, utbay aidsay atthay erethay asway 
anotherway ersonpay osewhay odestymay-- 

Andway osay orthfay andway osay onway. Ehay ungspray ishay ecretsay aboutway Uckhay's areshay inway 
ethay adventureway inway ethay inestfay amaticdray annermay ehay asway astermay ofway, utbay ethay 
urprisesay itway occasionedway asway argelylay ounterfeitcay andway otnay asway amorousclay andway 
effusiveway asway itway ightmay avehay eenbay underway appierhay ircumstancescay. Oweverhay, 
ethay idowway ademay away ettypray airfay owshay ofway astonishmentway, andway eapedhay osay anymay 
omplimentscay andway osay uchmay atitudegray uponway Uckhay atthay ehay almostway orgotfay 
ethay earlynay intolerableway iscomfortday ofway ishay ewnay othesclay inway ethay entirelyway 
intolerableway iscomfortday ofway eingbay etsay upway asway away argettay orfay everybodyway's azegay 
andway everybodyway's audationslay. 

Ethay idowway aidsay eshay eantmay otay ivegay Uckhay away omehay underway erhay oofray andway avehay imhay 
educatedway; andway atthay enwhay eshay ouldcay arespay ethay oneymay eshay ouldway artstay imhay inway 
usinessbay inway away odestmay ayway. Omtay's ancechay asway omecay. Ehay aidsay: 

"Uckhay onday't eednay itway. Uckhay's ichray." 

Othingnay utbay away eavyhay ainstray uponway ethay oodgay annersmay ofway ethay ompanycay eptkay 
ackbay ethay ueday andway operpray omplimentarycay aughlay atway isthay easantplay okejay. Utbay 
ethay ilencesay asway away ittlelay awkwardway. Omtay okebray itway: 

"Uckhay's otgay oneymay. Aybemay youway onday't elievebay itway, utbay ehay's otgay otslay ofway itway. 
Ohway, youway eednnay't ilesmay--I eckonray Iway ancay owshay youway. Youway ustjay aitway away inutemay." 

Omtay anray outway ofway oorsday. Ethay ompanycay ookedlay atway eachway otherway ithway away erplexedpay 
interestway--and inquiringlyway atway Uckhay, owhay asway onguetay-tied. 

"Idsay, atwhay ailsway Omtay?" aidsay Auntway Ollypay. "Ehay--well, erethay ainway't everway anyway 
akingmay ofway atthay oybay outway. Iway evernay--" 

Omtay enteredway, ugglingstray ithway ethay eightway ofway ishay ackssay, andway Auntway Ollypay 
idday otnay inishfay erhay entencesay. Omtay ouredpay ethay assmay ofway yellowway oincay uponway ethay 
abletay andway aidsay: 

"Erethay--what idday Iway elltay youway? Alfhay ofway itway's Uckhay's andway alfhay ofway itway's inemay!" 

Ethay ectaclespay ooktay ethay eneralgay eathbray awayway. Allway azedgay, obodynay okespay orfay 
away omentmay. Enthay erethay asway away unanimousway allcay orfay anway explanationway. Omtay aidsay 
ehay ouldcay urnishfay itway, andway ehay idday. Ethay aletay asway onglay, utbay imfulbray ofway 
interestway. Erethay asway arcelyscay anway interruptionway omfray anyway oneway otay eakbray ethay 
armchay ofway itsway owflay. Enwhay ehay adhay inishedfay, Mray. Onesjay aidsay: 

"Iway oughtthay Iway adhay ixedfay upway away ittlelay urprisesay orfay isthay occasionway, utbay itway 
onday't amountway otay anythingway ownay. Isthay oneway akesmay itway ingsay ightymay allsmay, Iway'm 
illingway otay allowway." 

Ethay oneymay asway ountedcay. Ethay umsay amountedway otay away ittlelay overway elvetway ousandthay 
ollarsday. Itway asway oremay anthay anyway oneway esentpray adhay everway eensay atway oneway imetay 
eforebay, oughthay everalsay ersonspay ereway erethay owhay ereway orthway onsiderablycay 
oremay anthay atthay inway opertypray. 




APTERCHAY XXXVAY 

ETHAY eaderray aymay estray atisfiedsay atthay Omtay's andway Uckhay's indfallway ademay away 
ightymay irstay inway ethay oorpay ittlelay illagevay ofway Stay. Etersburgpay. Osay astvay away 
umsay, allway inway actualway ashcay, eemedsay extnay otay incredibleway. Itway asway alkedtay 
aboutway, oatedglay overway, orifiedglay, untilway ethay easonray ofway anymay ofway ethay itizenscay 
otteredtay underway ethay ainstray ofway ethay unhealthyway excitementway. Everyway "auntedhay" 
ousehay inway Stay. Etersburgpay andway ethay eighboringnay illagesvay asway issectedday, 
ankplay ybay ankplay, andway itsway oundationsfay ugday upway andway ansackedray orfay iddenhay 
easuretray--and otnay ybay oysbay, utbay enmay--pretty avegray, unromanticway enmay, ootay, 
omesay ofway emthay. Ereverwhay Omtay andway Uckhay appearedway eythay ereway ourtedcay, admiredway, 
aredstay atway. Ethay oysbay ereway otnay ableway otay ememberray atthay eirthay emarksray adhay 
ossessedpay eightway eforebay; utbay ownay eirthay ayingssay ereway easuredtray andway 
epeatedray; everythingway eythay idday eemedsay omehowsay otay ebay egardedray asway 
emarkableray; eythay adhay evidentlyway ostlay ethay owerpay ofway oingday andway ayingsay 
ommonplacecay ingsthay; oreovermay, eirthay astpay istoryhay asway akedray upway andway 
iscoveredday otay earbay arksmay ofway onspicuouscay originalityway. Ethay illagevay aperpay 
ublishedpay iographicalbay etchesskay ofway ethay oysbay. 

Ethay Idowway Ouglasday utpay Uckhay's oneymay outway atway ixsay erpay entcay., andway Udgejay 
Atcherthay idday ethay amesay ithway Omtay's atway Auntway Ollypay's equestray. Eachway adlay adhay 
anway incomeway, ownay, atthay asway implysay odigiouspray--a ollarday orfay everyway eekdayway inway 
ethay yearway andway alfhay ofway ethay Undayssay. Itway asway ustjay atwhay ethay inistermay otgay--no, 
itway asway atwhay ehay asway omisedpray--he enerallygay ouldncay't ollectcay itway. Away ollarday 
andway away uarterqay away eekway ouldway oardbay, odgelay, andway oolschay away oybay inway osethay oldway 
implesay aysday--and otheclay imhay andway ashway imhay, ootay, orfay atthay attermay. 

Udgejay Atcherthay adhay onceivedcay away eatgray opinionway ofway Omtay. Ehay aidsay atthay onay 
ommonplacecay oybay ouldway everway avehay otgay ishay aughterday outway ofway ethay avecay. Enwhay 
Eckybay oldtay erhay atherfay, inway ictstray onfidencecay, owhay Omtay adhay akentay erhay 
ippingwhay atway oolschay, ethay Udgejay asway isiblyvay ovedmay; andway enwhay eshay eadedplay 
acegray orfay ethay ightymay ielay ichwhay Omtay adhay oldtay inway orderway otay iftshay atthay 
ippingwhay omfray erhay ouldersshay otay ishay ownway, ethay Udgejay aidsay ithway away inefay 
outburstway atthay itway asway away oblenay, away enerousgay, away agnanimousmay ielay--a ielay atthay 
asway orthyway otay oldhay upway itsway eadhay andway archmay ownday oughthray istoryhay eastbray otay 
eastbray ithway Eorgegay Ashingtonway's audedlay Uthtray aboutway ethay atchethay! Eckybay 
oughtthay erhay atherfay adhay evernay ookedlay osay alltay andway osay uperbsay asway enwhay ehay 
alkedway ethay oorflay andway ampedstay ishay ootfay andway aidsay atthay. Eshay entway aightstray 
offway andway oldtay Omtay aboutway itway. 

Udgejay Atcherthay opedhay otay eesay Omtay away eatgray awyerlay orway away eatgray oldiersay omesay 
ayday. Ehay aidsay ehay eantmay otay ooklay otay itway atthay Omtay ouldshay ebay admittedway otay ethay 
Ationalnay Ilitarymay Academyway andway afterwardway ainedtray inway ethay estbay awlay oolschay 
inway ethay ountrycay, inway orderway atthay ehay ightmay ebay eadyray orfay eitherway areercay orway 
othbay. 

Uckhay Innfay's ealthway andway ethay actfay atthay ehay asway ownay underway ethay Idowway Ouglasday' 
otectionpray introducedway imhay intoway ocietysay--no, aggeddray imhay intoway itway, urledhay 
imhay intoway itway--and ishay ufferingssay ereway almostway oremay anthay ehay ouldcay earbay. Ethay 
idowway's ervantssay eptkay imhay eanclay andway eatnay, ombedcay andway ushedbray, andway eythay 
eddedbay imhay ightlynay inway unsympatheticway eetsshay atthay adhay otnay oneway ittlelay otspay 
orway ainstay ichwhay ehay ouldcay esspray otay ishay earthay andway owknay orfay away iendfray. Ehay adhay 
otay eatway ithway away ifeknay andway orkfay; ehay adhay otay useway apkinnay, upcay, andway ateplay; 
ehay adhay otay earnlay ishay ookbay, ehay adhay otay ogay otay urchchay; ehay adhay otay alktay osay 
operlypray atthay eechspay asway ecomebay insipidway inway ishay outhmay; ithersoeverwhay ehay 
urnedtay, ethay arsbay andway acklesshay ofway ivilizationcay utshay imhay inway andway oundbay imhay 
andhay andway ootfay. 

Ehay avelybray orebay ishay iseriesmay eethray eeksway, andway enthay oneway ayday urnedtay upway 
issingmay. Orfay ortyfay-eight ourshay ethay idowway untedhay orfay imhay everywhereway inway 
eatgray istressday. Ethay ublicpay ereway ofoundlypray oncernedcay; eythay earchedsay ighhay 
andway owlay, eythay aggeddray ethay iverray orfay ishay odybay. Earlyway ethay irdthay orningmay 
Omtay Awyersay iselyway entway okingpay amongway omesay oldway emptyway ogsheadshay ownday ehindbay 
ethay abandonedway aughterslay-house, andway inway oneway ofway emthay ehay oundfay ethay efugeeray. 
Uckhay adhay eptslay erethay; ehay adhay ustjay eakfastedbray uponway omesay olenstay oddsway andway 
endsway ofway oodfay, andway asway yinglay offway, ownay, inway omfortcay, ithway ishay ipepay. Ehay asway 
unkemptway, uncombedway, andway adclay inway ethay amesay oldway uinray ofway agsray atthay adhay ademay 
imhay icturesquepay inway ethay aysday enwhay ehay asway eefray andway appyhay. Omtay outedray imhay 
outway, oldtay imhay ethay oubletray ehay adhay eenbay ausingcay, andway urgedway imhay otay ogay omehay. 
Uckhay's acefay ostlay itsway anquiltray ontentcay, andway ooktay away elancholymay astcay. Ehay 
aidsay: 

"Onday't alktay aboutway itway, Omtay. Iway've iedtray itway, andway itway onday't orkway; itway onday't 
orkway, Omtay. Itway ainway't orfay emay; Iway ainway't usedway otay itway. Ethay idderway's oodgay otay emay, 
andway iendlyfray; utbay Iway ancay't andstay emthay aysway. Eshay akesmay emay etgay upway ustjay 
atway ethay amesay imetay everyway orningmay; eshay akesmay emay ashway, eythay ombcay emay allway 
otay underthay; eshay onway't etlay emay eepslay inway ethay oodshedway; Iway otgay otay earway emthay 
amedblay othesclay atthay ustjay otherssmay emay, Omtay; eythay onday't eemsay otay anyway airway 
itgay oughthray 'emway, omehowsay; andway eythay're osay ottenray icenay atthay Iway ancay't 
etsay ownday, ornay aylay ownday, ornay ollray aroundway anywherway's; Iway ainhay't idslay onway away 
ellarcay-door orfay--well, itway 'earspay otay ebay yearsway; Iway otgay otay ogay otay urchchay 
andway eatsway andway eatsway--I atehay emthay orneryway ermonssay! Iway ancay't etchkay away yflay inway 
erethay, Iway ancay't awchay. Iway otgay otay earway oesshay allway Undaysay. Ethay idderway eatsway ybay 
away ellbay; eshay oesgay otay edbay ybay away ellbay; eshay itsgay upway ybay away ellbay--everything's osay 
awfulway egray'lar away odybay ancay't andstay itway." 

"Ellway, everybodyway oesday atthay ayway, Uckhay." 

"Omtay, itway onday't akemay onay ifferenceday. Iway ainway't everybodyway, andway Iway ancay't 
_andstay_ itway. Itway's awfulway otay ebay iedtay upway osay. Andway ubgray omescay ootay easyway--I onday't 
aketay onay interestway inway ittlesvay, atthay ayway. Iway otgay otay askway otay ogay away-fishing; 
Iway otgay otay askway otay ogay inway away-swimming--dern'd ifway Iway ainhay't otgay otay askway otay oday 
everythingway. Ellway, Iway'd otgay otay alktay osay icenay itway asnway't onay omfortcay--I'd otgay 
otay ogay upway inway ethay atticway andway ipray outway awhileway, everyway ayday, otay itgay away astetay 
inway ymay outhmay, orway Iway'd away iedday, Omtay. Ethay idderway ouldnway't etlay emay okesmay; 
eshay ouldnway't etlay emay yellway, eshay ouldnway't etlay emay apegay, ornay etchstray, ornay 
atchscray, eforebay olksfay--" [Enthay ithway away asmspay ofway ecialspay irritationway andway 
injuryway]--"And adday etchfay itway, eshay ayedpray allway ethay imetay! Iway evernay eesay uchsay away 
omanway! Iway _adhay_ otay oveshay, Omtay--I ustjay adhay otay. Andway esidesbay, atthay oolschay's 
oinggay otay openway, andway Iway'd away adhay otay ogay otay itway--well, Iway ouldnway't andstay _atthay_, 
Omtay. Ookylay-here, Omtay, eingbay ichray ainway't atwhay itway's ackedcray upway otay ebay. Itway's 
ustjay orryway andway orryway, andway eatsway andway eatsway, andway away-wishing youway asway eadday 
allway ethay imetay. Ownay esethay othesclay uitssay emay, andway isthay arbay'l uitssay emay, andway 
Iway ainway't everway oinggay otay akeshay 'emway anyway oremay. Omtay, Iway ouldnway't everway otgay intoway 
allway isthay oubletray ifway itway adnhay't 'away' enbay orfay atthay oneymay; ownay youway ustjay aketay 
ymay eershay ofway itway alongway ithway yourway'n, andway immegay away entay-center ometimessay--not 
anymay imestay, ecuzbay Iway onday't ivegay away ernday orfay away ingthay 'outthay itway's ollabletay 
ardhay otay itgay--and youway ogay andway egbay offway orfay emay ithway ethay idderway." 

"Ohway, Uckhay, youway owknay Iway ancay't oday atthay. 'Aintay't airfay; andway esidesbay ifway youway'll 
ytray isthay ingthay ustjay away ilewhay ongerlay youway'll omecay otay ikelay itway." 

"Ikelay itway! Yesway--the ayway Iway'd ikelay away othay ovestay ifway Iway asway otay etsay onway itway onglay 
enoughway. Onay, Omtay, Iway onway't ebay ichray, andway Iway onway't ivelay inway emthay ussedcay 
otherysmay ouseshay. Iway ikelay ethay oodsway, andway ethay iverray, andway ogsheadshay, andway 
Iway'll ickstay otay 'emway, ootay. Ameblay itway allway! ustjay asway eway'd otgay unsgay, andway away avecay, 
andway allway ustjay ixedfay otay obray, erehay isthay ernday oolishnessfay ashay otgay otay omecay upway 
andway ilespay itway allway!" 

Omtay awsay ishay opportunityway-- 

"Ookyherelay, Uckhay, eingbay ichray ainway't oinggay otay eepkay emay ackbay omfray urningtay 
obberray." 

"Onay! Ohway, oodgay-licks; areway youway inway ealray eadday-wood earnestway, Omtay?" 

"Ustjay asway eadday earnestway asway Iway'm ittingsay erehay. Utbay Uckhay, eway ancay't etlay youway 
intoway ethay anggay ifway youway ainway't espectableray, youway owknay." 

Uckhay's oyjay asway uenchedqay. 

"Ancay't etlay emay inway, Omtay? Idnday't youway etlay emay ogay orfay away iratepay?" 

"Yesway, utbay atthay's ifferentday. Away obberray isway oremay ighhay-toned anthay atwhay away 
iratepay isway--as away eneralgay ingthay. Inway ostmay ountriescay eythay're awfulway ighhay upway inway 
ethay obilitynay--dukes andway uchsay." 

"Ownay, Omtay, ainhay't youway alwaysway enbay iendlyfray otay emay? Youway ouldnway't etshay emay 
outway, ouldway youway, Omtay? Youway ouldnway't oday atthay, ownay, _ouldway_ youway, Omtay?" 

"Uckhay, Iway ouldnway't antway otay, andway Iway _onday't_ antway otay--but atwhay ouldway eoplepay 
aysay? Ywhay, eythay'd aysay, 'Mphay! Omtay Awyersay's Anggay! ettypray owlay aracterschay inway 
itway!' Eythay'd eanmay youway, Uckhay. Youway ouldnway't ikelay atthay, andway Iway ouldnway't." 

Uckhay asway ilentsay orfay omesay imetay, engagedway inway away entalmay ugglestray. Inallyfay ehay 
aidsay: 

"Ellway, Iway'll ogay ackbay otay ethay idderway orfay away onthmay andway ackletay itway andway eesay ifway Iway 
ancay omecay otay andstay itway, ifway youway'll etlay emay bway'long otay ethay anggay, Omtay." 

"Allway ightray, Uckhay, itway's away izwhay! Omecay alongway, oldway apchay, andway Iway'll askway ethay 
idowway otay etlay upway onway youway away ittlelay, Uckhay." 

"Illway youway, Omtay--now illway youway? Atthay's oodgay. Ifway eshay'll etlay upway onway omesay ofway 
ethay oughestray ingsthay, Iway'll okesmay ivatepray andway usscay ivatepray, andway owdcray 
oughthray orway ustbay. Enwhay youway oinggay otay artstay ethay anggay andway urntay obbersray?" 

"Ohway, ightray offway. Eway'll etgay ethay oysbay ogethertay andway avehay ethay initiationway 
onighttay, aybemay." 

"Avehay ethay ichwhay?" 

"Avehay ethay initiationway." 

"Atwhay's atthay?" 

"Itway's otay earsway otay andstay ybay oneway anotherway, andway evernay elltay ethay anggay's 
ecretssay, evenway ifway youway're oppedchay allway otay indersflay, andway illkay anybodyway andway 
allway ishay amilyfay atthay urtshay oneway ofway ethay anggay." 

"Atthay's aygay--that's ightymay aygay, Omtay, Iway elltay youway." 

"Ellway, Iway etbay itway isway. Andway allway atthay earingsway's otgay otay ebay oneday atway idnightmay, 
inway ethay onesomestlay, awfulestway aceplay youway ancay indfay--a ahay'nted ousehay isway ethay 
estbay, utbay eythay're allway ippedray upway ownay." 

"Ellway, idnightmay's oodgay, anywayway, Omtay." 

"Yesway, osay itway isway. Andway youway've otgay otay earsway onway away offincay, andway ignsay itway ithway 
oodblay." 

"Ownay, atthay's omethingsay _ikelay_! Ywhay, itway's away illionmay imestay ullierbay anthay 
iratingpay. Iway'll ickstay otay ethay idderway illtay Iway otray, Omtay; andway ifway Iway itgay otay ebay 
away egray'lar ipperray ofway away obberray, andway everybodyway alkingtay 'outbay itway, Iway eckonray 
eshay'll ebay oudpray eshay akedsnay emay inway outway ofway ethay etway." 

ONCLUSIONCAY 

OSAY endethway isthay oniclechray. Itway eingbay ictlystray away istoryhay ofway away _oybay_, itway 
ustmay opstay erehay; ethay orystay ouldcay otnay ogay uchmay urtherfay ithoutway ecomingbay ethay 
istoryhay ofway away _anmay_. Enwhay oneway iteswray away ovelnay aboutway owngray eoplepay, ehay owsknay 
exactlyway erewhay otay opstay--that isway, ithway away arriagemay; utbay enwhay ehay iteswray ofway 
uvenilesjay, ehay ustmay opstay erewhay ehay estbay ancay. 

Ostmay ofway ethay aracterschay atthay erformpay inway isthay ookbay illstay ivelay, andway areway 
osperouspray andway appyhay. Omesay ayday itway aymay eemsay orthway ilewhay otay aketay upway ethay 
orystay ofway ethay youngerway onesway againway andway eesay atwhay ortsay ofway enmay andway omenway eythay 
urnedtay outway otay ebay; ereforethay itway illway ebay isestway otnay otay evealray anyway ofway atthay 
artpay ofway eirthay iveslay atway esentpray. 

Endway ofway ethay Ojectpray Utenberggay Ebookway ofway Adventuresway ofway Omtay Awyersay, 
Ompletecay, ybay Arkmay Aintway (Amuelsay Emensclay) 

*** ENDWAY OFWAY ISTHAY OJECTPRAY UTENBERGGAY EBOOKWAY OMTAY AWYERSAY ***
